# 朔日手记 - Notes on Shuori

- NS-08 十万个问答 / Questions and Answers
- NS-09 街市狂澜 / Chaos on Streets

## NS-01 启程的祷声 / Safe Travel

家乡的灰尘总使身处其中的人感到愉快和甜蜜，在有人即将再度远行的清晨更是如此。\
"The smoke of the fatherland is sweet and pleasant to us," especially in the early morning when someone is about to travel far from home.

至少，正要启程的人是这样认为的。\
However, it's not obvious to this complaining lady.

**贵族女性**：——报纸？驿马车早就不过来了，说是价码不高，人手不够……都跟那些农民似的，一样贪心，恨不得把别人的舌头都吞进自己肚皮里去。\
**Noble Lady**: Newspaper? Their cart hasn't been here for a long time. They said the price was too low and they were short-handed. Those vendors are as greedy as a bottomless pit, like those farmers.

**贵族女性**：这城里什么都缺，就是不缺烟尘和见风使舵的人。\
**Noble Lady**: The smoke, the dust, and the opportunists are the last things needed in this poor town.

**贵族女性**：……唉……\
**Noble Lady**: *sighs*

**贵族女性**：上次出去转头就是一整年，中间半点消息也没有，这么快又要走。还要去那些地方，去跟摇蚊、虱子和流放犯交朋友。\
**Noble Lady**: Last time, she was away for a whole year and didn't write a single letter back. Now, she's leaving again, to the places where she can only make friends with mosquitos, lice, and exiles!

**贵族女性**：……圣母保佑她不会落得一身病，或者像那个女人一样弄瞎了眼被赶回来。\
**Noble Lady**: Sweet Mary forbid she should get sick or come back blind, like that woman.

**贵族女性**：哦，您说陛下的奖章。可铜打的奖章能值多少个卢布？不如来说说前一年她错过的那些舞会吧。许多年轻的近卫军都来了，可她却一个也没见过……\
**Noble Lady**: Oh, you mean the medal awarded by His Majesty. It's made of bronze. Who knows how many rubles it's worth? Not to mention the balls she had missed. Young cavaliers had come and gone, but she hadn't had the chance to meet any of them ...

这些反对的声音很容易顺势飘进房间里，就像窗外的灰尘一样。\
The grumbles easily sneak into the room through the window with the floating dust.

只有拉上门，得到一个足够安静平和的环境，被谈论的主角才好继续收拾行李，使整理的思绪不被打断。毕竟每样东西对远行来说都足够重要，不能忘记。\
The one being complained about closes the door. She needs to pack carefully in a room free of noise and interruptions. For a long journey, everything is too essential to forget.

**？？？**：……路线确认……\
**???**: ... Route confirmed ...

**？？？**：衣物、地图。车马券、介绍信、玻璃瓶、地质锤……\
**???**: Clothes, maps, carriage ticket, reference letter, glass bottles, rock hammer ...

**？？？**：小刀在身上……纸质的东西要裹起来。\
**???**: And the knife, in my pocket. Oh, I need to waterproof the papers.

**？？？**：亚麻布，我记得——啊。在这儿。\
**???**: Linen, it's emm ... Oh, here it is.

上次旅行前裁切的布料，幅面比记忆中宽大，在仅需承载一人使用的纸张时，更因空旷而显得慷慨了。\
The fabric, left from the last trip, has a broader width than remembered. Perhaps because it is holding paper for only one user this time, it seems much more empty than it had been.

她很少有这样大手笔的时刻。\
Using such a large fabric is a luxury for her.

**？？？**：新的羊皮纸可以多带一些了。\
**???**: I can bring more new parchment this time.

**？？？**：……\
**???**: ...

**？？？**：嗯？奇怪，这上面怎么有……\
**???**: Hmm? Wait, why is it ...

**？？？**：……这么多的字？\
**???**: ... already used?

隐藏在空白纸张中间的文字记录，字迹不一，但排列整齐。似乎被人刻意遗忘，直到现在重新发掘。\
A written document is hidden between blank sheets of paper. The handwriting is inconsistent but neatly penned. It seems to have been deliberately forgotten and is now being rediscovered at this very moment.

——幸运的是，她能在边角处找到签名，就像每页的一枚谨慎脚注。\
—Fortunately, there are signatures in the margins, left as a discreet footnote on each page.

“记录人”——\
"Recorded by"

“小叶尼塞”。\
"Yenisei"

**小叶尼塞**：这是……我的听写稿件。\
**Yenisei**: It's a record I wrote from dictation.

**小叶尼塞**：笔迹看起来像野外速记，页边磨损，已经干燥保存一年以上……\
**Yenisei**: Judging from the handwriting, I must have done it in the wilds. The edge is ragged, so probably it's been stored for over a year since it was dried.

**小叶尼塞**：一年……噢，这是别斯米尔女士曾委托我记录的游记。\
**Yenisei**: Over a year ... Oh, it's the travel diary Madam Bessmert asked me to write down for her.

**小叶尼塞**：或者说，应该叫“手记”？哈哈……\
**Yenisei**: Maybe I should call it travel "notes"? Haha ...

**小叶尼塞**：无论是什么，我都应该已经整理完成，寄给她了才对。\
**Yenisei**: Either way, I think I had completed the arrangement and sent the original to her.

**小叶尼塞**：我不会忘记这种事。它怎么会还在这里？\
**Yenisei**: There's no way I forgot such an important thing. So what is it doing here?

**小叶尼塞**：上面的记录也断了几天——\
**Yenisei**: And it's ... it's missing a few days of records.

**小叶尼塞**：十月十日，十月十六，十月十七……\
**Yenisei**: October 10, October 16, October 17 ...

**小叶尼塞**：“……十月十七日，天气阴。我们卖掉马车，改租当地农民的船只，以顺利渡过尚未进入结冰期的鄂木河……”\
**Yenisei**: "... October 17, cloudy. We sold the carriage and rented boats from the local farmers to sail along the Om River before it froze ..."

**小叶尼塞**：“这样我们便能找到另一种可能，规避掉从鄂木斯克北门进城的路线。”\
**Yenisei**: "In this way, we might be able to enter the city of Omsk without passing the north gate."

**小叶尼塞**：“毕竟在远东的旅行者口中……那里防备森严，如同堡垒；守卫从不放过任何说辞与文书不匹配的细节。”\
**Yenisei**: "After all, the travelers from the Far East had said ... the city was heavily guarded like a fortress, and the guards would not overlook the slightest inconsistency between people's stories and their documents."

**小叶尼塞**：“之所以这样大费周章，都是由于出行匆忙，我们临时拼凑起的证明文书—— ”\
**Yenisei**: "We had to go through this trouble because we were in such a rush when we set off that we had little time ..."

**？？？**：“——根本经不起那样严格的检验。”\
**???**: "... to prepare the documents. They were far from authentic enough to convince the guards."

**？？？**：“为了筹集行程经费，我多次召开游说演讲。我还记得最后一次演讲的地方，正位于鄂木河下游的新建公园之中。”\
**???**: "Before we left, I gave several speeches to raise funds for the travel. The last speech was in a new park in the downstream area of the Om River."

**？？？**：“据我的助手描述，那里生有一片高耸的堆积岩，上面遍布正处于茂盛期的欧洲俄罗斯植被。”\
**???**: "My assistant described to me that the park was crowned by a large pile of cumulate rock, which was burdened with the European Russian vegetation, all in its best time of year."

**？？？**：“这便是十七日的记述。那么，第二天后……”\
**???**: "This is the note on the 17th. The day after ..."

**？？？**：“唔，十月十八日”……这天我缺少印象。小叶尼塞，你还记得吗？\
**???**: "Emm, October 18th ..." I have almost no recollection of that day. Child, do you recall anything?

女孩忙于检查自己的记录，一小会儿后才终于出声回答。\
The girl is busy checking her records, but after a while, she opens her mouth to respond.

**小叶尼塞**：十月十八日……我记得。在适当休整和获取补给之后，您与总督进行了面谈。\
**Yenisei**: October 18 ... I do. After we took a break and collected the supplies we needed, you talked to the governor.

**小叶尼塞**：他将负责历史研究的文员介绍给您，并派遣测绘员——\
**Yenisei**: He introduced you to a historian and sent a land surveyor ...

**？？？**：噢，我想起来了，都是不重要的事情。那让我们跳过它吧。\
**???**: Oh. Yes, I remember it now. Bits of trivia. Let's skip that day for now.

**小叶尼塞**：……好的。\
**Yenisei**: Yes, Madam.

**？？？**：“十月十九日，天气较为晴朗。我在公园里正式阐述了我的计划，所用论据中，就包含着部分我所了解的东方‘度朔节’传说。”\
**???**: "October 19, partly sunny. I elaborated on my plan in my speech in the park. One of my arguments mentioned the Dùshuò Festival in the Eastern Land."

**小叶尼塞**：“度朔节”，传说……\
**Yenisei**: Legend ... of the Dùshuò Festival ...

**？？？**：“……里面那些与亚洲土地崇拜相关的古代地质学猜想，和对佚散神秘术的考察资料，都成功引发了听众的兴趣。”\
**???**: "... I was gratified to see that the audience was drawn to the relations between land worship and the historical geological features in Asia and the investigation materials about a long-lost arcane skill."

**？？？**：“土地崇拜会随‘保护神’的更替有所不同，而类似‘所求必应’的东方神秘术，却在行脚商人的口口相传中长久地存在。”\
**???**: "While the forms of land worship vary from one religion to another, the stories about an Eastern arcane skill known to the merchants as Ask and Acquire are almost identical."

**？？？**：“在那些绘声绘色的描述里，主角们常怀着用至高信念换取答案的决心，飞跃高山，横跨天堑……”\
**???**: "In those stories, men and women with determined minds overcame the highest mountain and the deepest canyon to seek an answer ..."

**？？？**：“……他们一如苦行僧般企望着摄提神的怜悯，亟待自身所求能够灵验。”\
**???**: "... They patiently endured the suffering like the ascetics, pleading for the Gods of Shètí's motherly mercy and hoping to be given what they asked."

年轻人快速地记录下这些关键词。从陌生到熟悉，她已经与这些名字相识长久。\
The girl quickly makes a note of these important words. From unknown to familiar, she has known these names for a long time.

**？？？**：“即使那人从此失去踪迹，神明也从未显露真身……但从枯寂中复现丰润的大地上，我们仍能窥见，‘所求必应’这一古老神秘术确实施行起效。”\
**???**: "Even till this day, after the seekers are long gone, the god has never shown Itself to any one of us ... But we know It was there, for there is no better proof of the Ask and Acquire than this revived land."

**？？？**：“毕竟他们的语调就像是地质学家研究河滩低地后，认为其土质与大部分山地有显著不同一样笃定。”\
**???**: "There is a sureness in people's remarks on Ask and Acquire. They are certain about its authenticity, like any geologist would not doubt the difference of soils in flood plains and mountains."

**？？？**：“没错。人们没有亲手触摸过沉积岩，却不能因此便认为它不存在……”\
**???**: "That's right. Do we really have to see it to believe it? None of us have ever touched one sedimentary rock, but we can infer that such a thing exists ..."

年轻人记录的速度已经能与口述者的话语保持相当的同步。但即使如此，到此处她还是迟疑了。\
The girl's speedy transcription follows in close synchronization with the speaker's words. But even so, she hesitates at this moment.

**小叶尼塞**：别斯米尔女士，这个类比……\
**Yenisei**: Madam, your analogy ...

**别斯米尔**：嗯？有什么问题吗？\
**Bessmert**: Is there a problem?

**小叶尼塞**：低地沉积岩是可以被验证的，“失落的神秘术”似乎并不是。\
**Yenisei**: The existence of sedimentary rock can be verified, but that of the "lost arcane skill" cannot.

**别斯米尔**：所以我才更应该亲自找到它。\
**Bessmert**: Which is what I'm going to do now—to find the last piece of the jigsaw puzzle.

**？？？**：请原谅我，女士们……\
**???**: Pardon me, ladies.

第三人的话音响起，戴眼镜的青年整理着衣服，往两人所在的方向走来。\
A third voice rings out. A young man in glasses tidies up his clothes and walks towards them.

**？？？**：我们确实应该“找到”些什么，否则如何度过这在躲避中被浪费的数日呢？\
**???**: She's right. We do need to find something; otherwise, how are we supposed to make up for this time we've spent running and waiting?

**小叶尼塞**：什么？\
**Yenisei**: What?

**？？？**：睁开眼睛看看吧。\
**???**: Take a good look around you.

女孩意识到今天不会再有东西可记了，于是依言将纸笔收好，站了起来，好去完整地看到骤雨狂风肆虐后的草原。\
The girl realizes that there will be nothing more for her to record today, and puts away her pen and paper. Then she stands to take in a complete view of the steppes now that the roaring wind and rain had ceased.

与大地呈现同样黑棕色彩的秃鹫于头顶盘旋，平等地凝视底下所有疑似不再动弹的生物。\
Vultures, the same color as the dark earth, hover above their heads, gazing with a scavenger's intent at all the creatures below them that seem to have stopped moving.

**小叶尼塞**：……雨停了。\
**Yenisei**: The rain has stopped.

**？？？**：别表现得好像完全没注意到似的，小姐。\
**???**: Don't act like you just noticed it, Miss.

**？？？**：我们究竟还要等多久？等到那些秃鹫来啃掉我们的皮肉和骨头？\
**???**: How much longer are we going to wait? Long enough for the vultures to eat our flesh and bones?

**小叶尼塞**：你——\
**Yenisei**: You ...

**别斯米尔**：克罗利克先生，您的担忧是没有必要的。\
**Bessmert**: Mr. Krolik. You're troubled by unnecessary concerns.

**别斯米尔**：秃鹫食腐，如果它们一直在不远处盘旋，应当是为了寻找被风暴卷去后坠落的小动物，而不会来招惹我们。\
**Bessmert**: The vultures are scavengers. They are here only for the animal corpses brought by the thunderstorm. They will leave us alone.

**克罗利克**：既然没有任何威胁，那我们还在等什么？\
**Krolik**: So they don't pose a threat. Then what's with the waiting?

急促的吐字方式显露出他的紧张。小叶尼塞却不明白那是为什么。\
His hurried speech reveals his nervousness. Though Yenisei doesn't understand why.

**小叶尼塞**：如果您想赶快继续上路，是可以直接提出来的。\
**Yenisei**: If you are trying to get us back on the road, you have the right to propose it directly.

**小叶尼塞**：队伍一直都这样商量着前进，并不是我们在刻意拖延。\
**Yenisei**: The team discusses to decide the next step. That's how things have worked all the way. We are not trying to waste your time.

**克罗利克**：这就是我想说的。我认为我们应该继续上路了。\
**Krolik**: That's what I mean. We should get going now.

**小叶尼塞**：我明白了。像之前一样，我们会给出之后的方向，然后所有人投票表决——\
**Yenisei**: I see. We will suggest the directions as usual, and everyone will vote to decide ...

**克罗利克**：哦，不，你没明白。没有表决和讨论的必要。\
**Krolik**: Oh, no, you don't get it. There's no need to discuss or vote.

**小叶尼塞**：嗯？\
**Yenisei**: Hmm?

**克罗利克**：因为我们会往回走，而不是向前。这就是唯一的方向。\
**Krolik**: Because we are not going forward, but going back! That's the only direction available.

小叶尼塞沉默地注视克罗利克。她不赞同，却也会礼貌地等待对方说完。\
Yenisei stares silently at Krolik. She disagrees, but politely waits for him to finish speaking.

**克罗利克**：这不仅是我的想法，别斯米尔女士。\
**Krolik**: I'm not the only one with this idea, Ms. Bessmert.

**克罗利克**：那些东方的传说，度朔节的狂欢？或者“所求必应”的神秘学把戏……\
**Krolik**: Those legends from the East, that ... Dùshuò Festival, is it? And the arcane trick you call "Ask and Acquire" ...

**克罗利克**：没有哪一件能比我们的命重要。\
**Krolik**: None of them matter more than our lives!

道理的确是这样，女孩只能无言转过头去。更远处，一片寂寥无边的无雪冬景，是枯草散落后的温带大地。\
He is right. The girl can only turn her head in silence further away, to that desolate, boundless, snowless winter landscape, all that remained of the temperate land after its withered grass scattered with the wind.

一行人先前遭遇的那场风暴，几乎席卷了此地所有能够喘息的生命体。\
The storm they had encountered had blown through here as well, sweeping away almost every living thing.

而青年人的目的就像眼前这片空旷的草地一样一览无余。\
And the young man's purpose is as clear as the open land that lies in front of them.

**克罗利克**：——谁能保证不会再遇上一次这样的突发情况？如果下次我们找不到这样能遮蔽风雨的石林呢？\
**Krolik**: Can anyone promise there won't be another emergency like this? What if we can't find a shelter next time?

**克罗利克**：找不到，下一次变成外面那些死物的就是我们。\
**Krolik**: Yeah, we'll be lying dead out there, just like those corpses.

**别斯米尔**：……我知道了。\
**Bessmert**: I hear you.

这是离开鄂木斯克向南而去的第三十七天。也是队伍在这片缺乏活水的草原上逗留的第五天。\
It has been 37 days since they left Omsk heading south. The fifth day on these steppes they have gone without fresh water.

如果一切都按照计划进行，此时，所有人都应该已经坐在补给站的房屋内喝着热茶。\
If everything had gone according to plan, they would've already been sitting in the supply station drinking tea.

前提是，队伍没有遇上突如其来的风暴天气——\
If they hadn't encountered this sudden storm ...

即使如此，最初召集起队伍的两人，也不会对这样的时刻有所准备。\
Yet, the two people, who put this very team together, did not anticipate such an eventuality.

**别斯米尔**：鉴于我们先前的遭遇，您的诉求是合理的。\
**Bessmert**: Given what happened earlier, it is only reasonable that you would wish to return.

**小叶尼塞**：……\
**Yenisei**: ...

这种标志半途而废的分歧时刻。\
This marks a moment of disagreement, when all the half-met measures sow the seeds of discord.

## NS-02 柔板 / Adagio

近处的其他同行者中，没有人表达支持，也没有人出声反对。\
There is neither a single voice of opposition nor one of support from their fellow travelers.

假如别斯米尔能瞧见他们的表情，就会意识到那种沉默的“不约而同”实则意味着早有预谋。\
If Bessmert could see their expressions, she might realize that this silent assent had actually been the sound of plotting minds.

**克罗利克**：那么，我们达成共识了？\
**Krolik**: So, are we on the same page?

**别斯米尔**：我是说，我知道您的想法，也认同您提出诉求的合理性。\
**Bessmert**: I fully understand where you're coming from, and I acknowledge your reasoning.

**克罗利克**：有什么不同——\
**Krolik**: What are you trying to ...

**别斯米尔**：但我们依然需要投票表决。\
**Bessmert**: But we still need a vote to decide.

克罗利克睁大了眼睛，喜悦在其中闪烁。他正等待着眼前人说出这句话。\
Krolik opens his eyes wide, pure joy flickering within them, and waits for the person in front of him to utter the words he longs to hear.

**小叶尼塞**：——等等——\
**Yenisei**: Wait!!

小叶尼塞阻拦不及。擅长游说的探险家对自己劝服他人的能力深信不疑。\
Yenisei couldn't stop the inevitable. The explorer, with a knack for speeches, always seems to have a strong belief in her own persuasiveness.

**克罗利克**：没问题，当然。这是文明的做法。\
**Krolik**: No problem, of course. It's the civilized way to solve it.

**克罗利克**：但我要求——跳过发言环节。因为时间紧迫，我们没有空闲听您长篇大论。\
**Krolik**: But I require we skip the speech. We have no time to waste on your monologue.

**别斯米尔**：……可以。\
**Bessmert**: Alright.

**小叶尼塞**：女士！\
**Yenisei**: Madam!

**克罗利克**：好，先生们。选择原路返回的，请举手表决。\
**Krolik**: Alright, gentlemen. If you agree to go back, please raise your hand.

话音落下，他身后不远处，几人缓缓抬手，中食两指交叉放至耳旁。\
As these words land on the listeners not far behind him, the people slowly begin to raise their hands to their ears, fingers crossed.

到最后，才是克罗利克。他面对着两人，同样只举起手，却仿佛是在示威一样扩大了脸上笑容的胜利意味。\
In the end, Krolik has it. He faces both of them, simply raising his hands, as though grandstanding somewhat, and a victorious smile stretches across his face.

**克罗利克**：四对二。您看，这样不就很快有结果了？\
**Krolik**: Four to two. See, we can make decisions in no time, right?

**别斯米尔**：……\
**Bessmert**: ...

**小叶尼塞**：女士，他们早就商量好了！我们不能就这么——难道您真的要这样回去吗？\
**Yenisei**: This is their trap, Madam! We can't just ... Are you really fine with going back empty-handed like this?

**克罗利克**：这是别斯米尔女士自己要求的投票，可不是我。\
**Krolik**: The vote was required by Ms. Bessmert, not me.

**克罗利克**：至于你……如果再不停止对我的污蔑，那我将认为这是你要求决斗的信号。\
**Krolik**: And you, I'll take it that you're challenging me to a duel if you continue with the slander.

**别斯米尔**：不，先生，那不是她的意思。我们没有动武的必要。\
**Bessmert**: No, good sir, please don't take her the wrong way. We don't have to go physical.

**小叶尼塞**：——尤利恩先生呢？他还没有投票，结果还是无效的！\
**Yenisei**: What about Mr. Jurien? He has not voted yet, so the vote is not over!

少女认为自己找到了事情的关键，哪怕她的理智知道再多一票也于事无补。\
The girl believes she has reached the heart of the matter, even if her rational mind knows that a single vote would be of no use.

她仍然坚持。\
Still, she insists.

**克罗利克**：哦，他很累，所以没有过来。不过他的想法肯定与我们一致，毕竟……\
**Krolik**: Oh, he's too tired to show up, but I'm sure he shares the same idea with us, because ...

**克罗利克**：我们都是人类。他当然会站在我们这边。\
**Krolik**: We are all humans. Of course, he's on our side.

小叶尼塞并不打算与青年男子多说，决定越过眼前这群人，去寻找剩下的那个投票者。\
Yenisei doesn't intend to say much to the young man, and decides to cross over to the group of people ahead to search for their final voter.

直到另一个高大的男子站了出来，似有若无地挡住了她的去路。\
That is until another tall man stands up, seemingly to block her path.

**考察队员Ⅰ**：不用多说了，克罗利克。收拾物资，我们往回走。\
**Team Member I**: Say no more, Krolik. Pack your things. Let's head back.

**小叶尼塞**：……！\
**Yenisei**: ...!

**小叶尼塞**：那我们就在这里分头行动——\
**Yenisei**: Fine. We'll split up from here, then.

**考察队员Ⅰ**：我们会带走剩下的所有物资，才能保障顺利返回。这没得商量。\
**Team Member I**: We'll take all the supplies with us, or we can't make our way back. No discussion.

**小叶尼塞**：……\
**Yenisei**: ...

他比他们派出的沟通者更为强硬，说完就与小叶尼塞在狭窄的岩石缝隙中擦身而过，率先走向两人身后的物资箱。\
He looks even tougher than the communicators they sent, and after saying his piece, he brushes past Yenisei down through the narrow rock crevice and leads the way toward the supply box behind them.

片刻前，她们都还在那里总结着先前的旅途。\
A moment ago, they were all there, recounting their previous journey together.

**别斯米尔**：先生们，大家都是自愿加入这趟旅途的，也许我们应该好好谈谈，而不是——\
**Bessmert**: Gentlemen, the team was put together in good faith. Perhaps we should negotiate, not ...

小叶尼塞的回答是快步追过去，用身体拦在了男人与别斯米尔之间。\
Yenisei's solution is to chase after him and plant herself between the man and Bessmert.

**小叶尼塞**：指南针失效，你们需要我来指出回去的方向。\
**Yenisei**: The compass doesn't work here. You need me to find the way back.

**小叶尼塞**：留下我们那份物资，我可以给你方向。\
**Yenisei**: Leave our supplies, and I'll show you the way.

**考察队员Ⅰ**：……看来你还是选择了决斗。\
**Team Member I**: You have to do this the hard way.

男人摇头，显然并不接受这个交易。\
The man shakes his head, clearly unwilling to accept the proposal.

小叶尼塞惊愕地护住身后人，意识到武力的对峙似乎不可避免。\
In her shock, Yenisei instinctively protects the person behind her, realizing that confrontation seems inevitable.

**？？？**：——咳咳……这样太野蛮了，朋友们。\
**???**: *coughs* That, my friends, is not how civilized people solve their problem.

这声音沉稳，平静，其中的分量却恰好能够介入这场儿戏一样的“决斗”。\
The voice is calm and composed, but its gravity brings a swift end to the playful duel.

**别斯米尔**：啊，尤利恩先生！\
**Bessmert**: Mr. Jurien!

在这样一支临时组成的队伍里，最年长的人通常有着阅历赋予的天然威信。\
In a makeshift team of this sort, the eldest member is often bestowed a special prestige based on their experience.

**克罗利克**：尤利恩先生……\
**Krolik**: Mr. Jurien ...

**尤利恩**：克罗利克先生。我还以为您要与别斯米尔女士谈重新分配每日物资的问题。但我没想到……\
**Jurien**: Mr. Krolik. I thought you were here to discuss the reallocation of supplies with Madam Bessmert. I didn't expect this ...

**克罗利克**：呃……\
**Krolik**: Well ...

**尤利恩**：您的确不是自愿来的，但您也肩负着总督授予的重要使命。\
**Jurien**: It's true that you didn't choose to be here. You are here because you have an important mission given by the governor to complete.

**尤利恩**：既然已经出发了，为什么又在半途中放弃完成任务的信念？\
**Jurien**: We have come this far. Do you really want to give up now?

被点到名的人缩了缩身子。“沟通”的假意暴露无遗，年长者的每一句话都令他无法反驳。\
The man's frame visibly shrinks. Their pretense of "communication" has been exposed, and every word spoken by his elder makes it more and more impossible for him to offer a rebuttal.

**尤利恩**：至于这几位先生……竟然连你也不愿继续前进了，彼得洛夫。\
**Jurien**: As for you gentlemen ... Petrov, I'm surprised you're here too.

**尤利恩**：只是一点谁也无法预料的风险，就把你吓得不敢动弹了？我记得演讲时，你对南方那些古老地层表现出了相当的兴趣。\
**Jurien**: It's a risk that none of us expected, but it shouldn't have broken your will. I remember you showed a great interest in those ancient strata in the South when we were at the speech.

**考察队员Ⅰ**：我们也只是需要一些保障。\
**Team Member I**: All we need is safety.

**考察队员Ⅰ**：极端天气过后通常有缓冲期，能在此期间回去是更好的选择。\
**Team Member I**: There will always be a buffer period after extreme weather. We should seize the chance and head back.

**考察队员Ⅰ**：不过……如果您能让别斯米尔定下一个足够往返的期限，且在期限内找到活水，我们也能按原计划不变。\
**Team Member I**: If you persuade Ms. Bessmert to give us a confirmed date, before which we can find the running water and come back, we can stick to the original plan.

**尤利恩**：别斯米尔女士？\
**Jurien**: Madam Bessmert?

**别斯米尔**：没问题，您瞧，这都是可以商议的……\
**Bessmert**: Certainly. You see, these are all negotiable.

**小叶尼塞**：等等。还有一点，这个期限要等我们清点完剩余物资才能决定。\
**Yenisei**: Wait. About the date, we can only decide after making an inventory.

听见这话，男人掏出怀里的袖珍钟，晃了两下，展示给小叶尼塞现在的时间。\
Upon hearing these words, the man takes out his pocket watch, shakes it twice, and shows Yenisei the current time.

**考察队员Ⅰ**：……给你三十分钟。\
**Team Member I**: You have 30 minutes.

**小叶尼塞**：足够了。\
**Yenisei**: That's enough.

短暂的共识达成，其他人回到原先分散的地方，将物资箱收拢到一起，等待两人给出答复。\
A brief consensus is reached, and the others scatter back to their former places, gathering supply boxes together and waiting for a response from the two in charge.

别斯米尔小心翼翼触碰那些木箱，年轻的女孩也带着纸笔来到她的身边，安静地记录起来。\
Bessmert cautiously touches the wooden boxes. The young girl comes to her side with a pen and paper, making a quiet record of things.

一时间，周围只剩下纸笔动作的声响。\
For a moment, the only sound between them is of pen on paper.

**别斯米尔**：其实……\
**Bessmert**: You know ...

**小叶尼塞**：嗯？\
**Yenisei**: Hmm?

**别斯米尔**：尤利恩先生对神秘学家和神秘术很感兴趣。他本来就是除总督之外最支持这趟旅途的人类。\
**Bessmert**: Mr. Jurien is very interested in arcanum and arcanists. He is the keenest supporter of our journey, besides the governor.

**别斯米尔**：即使他对“所求必应”的认知和理解，与我有很大的不同……\
**Bessmert**: Even if his understanding of Ask and Acquire is significantly different from mine ...

少女没有停下手中翻找和记录的动作，同时也轻声回应着别斯米尔像往常一样突然展开的话题。\
The girl continues her rummaging and recording, while responding gently and deftly to Bessmert's habitual broaching of this parallel topic.

**别斯米尔**：那些商人提到过，“所求必应”的实现需要付出代价。但这个代价并不是固定的。只是在民间传说中，多数都需要以身犯险。\
**Bessmert**: The legend of Ask and Acquire, as told by many merchants, always involves a certain price. The price takes different forms in the stories, but mostly it is a great danger.

**小叶尼塞**：我以为那些无法越过的悬崖，和难以攀登的高山，就是这个意思。\
**Yenisei**: I believe that refers to "the highest mountain and deepest canyon" in those stories.

**别斯米尔**：它理应是。而尤利恩先生作为一名研究神秘术的历史学家，则认为这是神秘学家与自然进行的某种交换仪式……\
**Bessmert**: I reckon so. But Mr. Jurien, as a human historian studying the arcane skill, believes it's a form of exchange that arcanists make with nature ...

**小叶尼塞**：嗯。但您认为，这是错的？\
**Yenisei**: Mm-hmm. And you think he's wrong?

**别斯米尔**：在无法验证的阶段，所有的猜想都可以被认定为可疑。只是我们越靠近这片大陆，我对那神秘知识的渴求，便变得越强烈。\
**Bessmert**: At this stage, we can't verify anything, so all these assumptions will have to remain assumptions. However, as we are getting closer to that mysterious land, my craving for its knowledge is also becoming stronger.

话语间，别斯米尔绕到另一个箱子的面前，发觉越靠近放置仪器的部分，便越能闻见掺水的酒精。\
Between these words, Bessmert walks around to another box and notices that the closer the instrument is placed to it, the more distinctly she can smell the alcohol.

显然，为测量沸点所准备的纯酒精，已经在气温骤降的夜里被当作“应急物资”使用了。\
It is obvious that the alcohol prepared for boiling point measurements had been used as an "emergency resource" during the night when the temperature dropped drastically.

……对这样一支中途拼凑起来的队伍实在不应苛求太多。\
We shouldn't ask too much from such a ragtag team.

**别斯米尔**：物资的情况怎么样了？\
**Bessmert**: What do we know about the supplies?

**小叶尼塞**：刨去饮用水，所有人常量使用大概最少八天，紧凑再加四天。如果能猎到小型动物，或者遇上牧民，还能坚持更久。\
**Yenisei**: Put aside the water problem, the supplies can feed everyone for eight days, maybe twelve if we economize. We can hold even longer if there are any preys or herders along the way.

**别斯米尔**：补给站呢？\
**Bessmert**: Are there any supply stations?

**小叶尼塞**：这片草原上没有我们的补给站。至少地图上没有。\
**Yenisei**: Our supply stations are not on these plains, at least not on the map.

**别斯米尔**：饮用水和酒精还有多少？\
**Bessmert**: How much drinking water and alcohol do we have left?

**小叶尼塞**：应该有——\
**Yenisei**: Approximately ...

**小叶尼塞**：哦，好极了。他们疯到把水倒进纯酒精里，现在我们两样都缺了。\
**Yenisei**: Oh, great. These idiots put water in the alcohol. Now we are short of both.

**别斯米尔**：至少，喝酒可以取暖。\
**Bessmert**: At least the alcohol has kept them warm.

**小叶尼塞**：他们也能直接喝酒精。\
**Yenisei**: They could have just drunk the alcohol.

**别斯米尔**：不是这样的，孩子。比起追究这些东西，或许我们更应该先定下路线。\
**Bessmert**: Alright, alright, child. Now we should focus on the direction for the next step, not these bits of trivia.

**别斯米尔**：事先声明，我目前的想法只比“毫无头绪”好上一点。\
**Bessmert**: Regarding which, just to be clear, what I have in mind is only slightly better than nothing.

**小叶尼塞**：哪一点？\
**Yenisei**: Better how?

**别斯米尔**：湿润的气息，和土质。发现了吗？对于风暴过后，腐料还没深入土壤的阶段来说，这里的土质过于黏稠了。\
**Bessmert**: The moist air and the soil. Have you noticed? The soil beneath our feet is way too sticky, even for a land after a thunderstorm.

**别斯米尔**：虽然不是准确判断……但我倾向于认为，这是有地下水的标志。\
**Bessmert**: I'm not entirely sure about this ... But I tend to think that there is groundwater beneath us.

**别斯米尔**：有地下水，就会有活水。\
**Bessmert**: Which means we are close to running water.

**小叶尼塞**：好吧，让我想想。\
**Yenisei**: Alright. Let me think about how to get us there.

**别斯米尔**：你的神秘术不能用吗？\
**Bessmert**: Can't you use your arcane skill?

**小叶尼塞**：什么？您不能像他们一样，因为一无所知就把希望都寄托在这上面。\
**Yenisei**: What?! Just because you don't know what to do doesn't mean you should count on this thing. You are not like them!

**别斯米尔**：我只是需要把可能性都考虑进去……\
**Bessmert**: I just want to make use of everything we have ...

**小叶尼塞**：好吧。我向您解释过它的运作方式，现在没有新的活水可用，这些瓶子里的东西，在最好的情况下，能指出的也只有回去的方向。\
**Yenisei**: Fine. I told you how it works. Without new running water, the old samples in the bottles can only show us the way back. That's the best they can do.

为了证明，女孩从身上取下一枚玻璃瓶，放到对方的手中。\
To prove this, the girl takes a glass bottle from her person and places it in the waiting, doubtful hand.

**小叶尼塞**：这是鄂木河下游的水。里面可用于占卜方向的活跃气息已经很淡了。\
**Yenisei**: This one is from the lower course of the Om River. The arcane energy I can use for divination has almost faded away.

**小叶尼塞**：跟着它走回去？能做到，但这不是我们想要的。只有克罗利克先生他们会高高兴兴上路。\
**Yenisei**: Can it show us the way back? Sure, but that's not what we want. Only Mr. Krolik and his men would be happy to hear that.

听到这儿，年长的女人直起身来。虽然看不见眼神，但她沉默时的姿态，总是看上去在进行快速的思考。\
Upon hearing this, Bessmert stands up straight. Although she cannot see her eyes, her silent posture alone seems to affect an aura of rapid thought.

小叶尼塞抬头望她，几乎能听到那些齿轮在头壳中转动咬合的声音。\
Yenisei looks up at her and can almost hear the sound of gears spinning in her skull.

**别斯米尔**：往好处想，这确保了我们能够回去。\
**Bessmert**: To think on the bright side, we still have a chance to go home.

**小叶尼塞**：可我离开不是为了回去，女士。\
**Yenisei**: But I didn't leave my homeland to go back there, Madam.

**别斯米尔**：是的，我知道，我知道。因为我也一样。这并不意味着现在就往回走，它只是一份保障。\
**Bessmert**: Yes, yes, I know. I feel the same. I'm not suggesting we turn back immediately. It's just an option.

**别斯米尔**：那种润湿量的土质，印象中最接近温带山地河滩，一般位于那种覆盖森林植物的黑土草原，和我们踏入这里所认识的地貌不同。\
**Bessmert**: To the best of my recollection, such moist soil is often found in the mountains and floodplains of the temperate zone, especially in the forest steppes covered with chernozem. The landscape is very different from where we are now.

**别斯米尔**：在我们找到躲避的位置前，你曾向我描述过东南方有一座山切断了地平线，对吗？\
**Bessmert**: Before we sheltered from the thunderstorm, you told me about a mountain in the southeast. It blocked the horizon from our sight, right?

听到这句话，女孩睁大了眼睛。那是逐渐意识到关窍的惊喜表情。\
The girl's eyes widen upon hearing these words—the expression of a hopeful epiphany.

**别斯米尔**：由此可以假设，我们遇上的风暴，正是强对流翻山而来的结果，在草原上，如果要形成这么大团的云雨，必须有足够的活水——\
**Bessmert**: Based on this, I would assume, the thunderstorm was the result of a stronger convection coming from the other side of the mountain. Now, on the steppe, to form a cloud large enough to bring a thunderstorm would require a large amount of running water ...

**小叶尼塞**：而活水的来源可能就在那个方向！！\
**Yenisei**: And the source of the running water is probably on the other side of the mountain!

**别斯米尔**：没错……有了这个大致方向，我们就能继续前进。\
**Bessmert**: Exactly ... We can set off in that general direction.

**别斯米尔**：而且，即使得到最坏的结果，翻过山去，我们没有找到活水，你的神秘术也能带我们回来。\
**Bessmert**: We might not find any water there. That's the worst result. In that case, we can still return here with the help of your arcane skill.

**别斯米尔**：只要玻璃瓶还在。\
**Bessmert**: As long as we have that glass bottle with us.

**小叶尼塞**：是的。\
**Yenisei**: That's right.

**别斯米尔**：然后，我们定下五天的期限……\
**Bessmert**: We tell them we need another five days ...

别斯米尔抓紧了手中的玻璃瓶，像是抓住了最后一点希望。\
Bessmert grips the glass bottle in her hand as though clinging on to one final trace of hope.

**别斯米尔**：这可能也是他们能接受的最大期限。就算不行，我也会像游说时那样，再次说服他们。\
**Bessmert**: They won't accept more days than that. If they won't even settle for this, I will convince them, like I did when I first got them on the team.

## NS-03 仙子草地 / The Fairyland

别斯米尔的确做到了。\
Bessmert did indeed succeed.

一方面，当她肯定地指明方向，并给出判断来由和论据的时候，人类同伴其实是容易被说服的。\
On one hand, as she clearly points out the direction of her thinking and provides reasons and arguments for her judgment, her human companions are easily convinced.

另一方面，一切别的担忧也很快都不再成为问题——\
On the other hand, all other concerns soon cease to be of significance—

两日后\
Two days later

**小叶尼塞**：——！！！\
**Yenisei**: ...!!!

年轻的女孩瞪大了眼睛，难以置信地望着不远处几乎凭空出现的活水溪流，好像瞪视就能使它恢复原状一样。\
The girl's eyes widen as she looks blinking at the flowing stream appearing seemingly from thin air not far from them—as though staring at it might restore it all to its original state.

她清晰记得，昨天傍晚在身后一俄里处驻扎下来时，四周可没有任何东西能向他们展示这样的“奇迹”。\
She remembers clearly when she was only a mile from here yesterday evening, there was nothing to indicate the presence of such a miraculous hidden feature.

**尤利恩**：两位女士……\
**Jurien**: Ladies ...

**尤利恩**：这可真是令人印象深刻，不是吗？还好我们先前没有选择返回。\
**Jurien**: This is a miracle. I'm glad we didn't give up and go back.

**小叶尼塞**：奇怪，请稍等……我……\
**Yenisei**: Wait, something's not right ... I ...

**克罗利克**：等什么？\
**Krolik**: What-what are we waiting for?

他并不打算等待一个回答，便焦躁地奔向溪流。这是于荒原上长途跋涉后必然出现的情境。\
Not intending to wait for an answer, he runs toward the stream. An unheeded reaction to the long labors of their journey through the desolate wilderness.

**克罗利克**：既然看起来方向没错，那我也没什么可说的了。\
**Krolik**: We are on the right path. I have nothing to say.

同行的人类都向涌动的溪流快步走去。\
The humans move briskly toward the rushing stream.

一时之间，竟然只有两位神秘学家对眼前的状况保持怀疑。\
For a moment, only the two arcanists remain skeptical about this new variable.

**别斯米尔**：不对……等等，请先不要！\
**Bessmert**: No ... Wait! Please don't ... !

他们当然听不见这无力的呼喊，很快踏入了溪流之中。将脸埋进水里又拔出来时，他们快活得像第一次步入野外的城市之子。\
Unable or unwilling to heed her shouts, they rush into the stream. Sinking their faces into the water and pulling them out, with smiles as wide as if they had never seen such natural beauty before.

在阻止不及的别斯米尔身边，红发女孩警惕地后退了，与这些热情投向活水怀抱的人类相反。\
Standing beside Bessmert, who had failed to stop their advance, the red-haired girl cautiously retreats as well, marking a sharp contrast with the humans who embrace the water like a fish too long in the air.

**小叶尼塞**：这、这是……\
**Yenisei**: Wh-What ...

**小叶尼塞**：女士，昨天我们驻扎的时候，您似乎没有提到这么近的地方存在活水。\
**Yenisei**: Madam, you didn't tell us the running water was right on the side when we pitched camp yesterday.

**别斯米尔**：是的，因为我根本就没有发现。\
**Bessmert**: Yes, because I didn't notice any signs of water.

**小叶尼塞**：我还以为是您做了什么！\
**Yenisei**: I thought it was your doing!

**别斯米尔**：很遗憾，我什么也没做。我的神秘术也做不到这个。我甚至不确定我们是否还走在先前决定的道路上。\
**Bessmert**: I wish it was, but, sadly, this is beyond my power. I'm not even sure if we are still staying on the planned route.

这显然不是一个好消息，小叶尼塞的沉默显示了这点，别斯米尔也立刻意识到了自己话语的歧义。\
This is obviously not good news, as Yenisei's silence reveals. Bessmert immediately realizes the ambiguity of her words.

**别斯米尔**：我是说，我能听见它现在的声音，那些撞击岩石和浅滩的响动，但也仅此而已。\
**Bessmert**: Indeed, I can hear the river flowing and running against the stones and shores.

**小叶尼塞**：您是不是还察觉到了其他的事情？\
**Yenisei**: Have you noticed anything else?

**别斯米尔**：我并非这方面的专家，但……\
**Bessmert**: Yes, um, I'm not an expert, though.

**别斯米尔**：这里的草地也很湿润，却是春季经常落雨才会有的那种短暂情况，与土质无关。\
**Bessmert**: The soil here is moist too, but it feels different, like just dampened by frequent spring rains.

**别斯米尔**：早前那种干枯的，像野火过后烧焦草垛一样的冬日气息，已经完全消失了。\
**Bessmert**: The dry air of winter has completely gone.

**小叶尼塞**：而且这里草地的颜色，也不像我们应经历的温带草原的十二月，而是四月、五月，那样的绿色。\
**Yenisei**: And the grass here looks nothing like the temperate grass we should be seeing in December. It's so green, as if it were April or May now.

**别斯米尔**：可我们没有走那么远，那么久，所以……\
**Bessmert**: But we haven't gone that far. Is this ...

**别斯米尔**：这难道是某种神秘术制造的幻觉？\
**Bessmert**: Is this some kind of illusion brought by arcane power?

**小叶尼塞**：如果这是幻觉，或者其他的异常，那他们喝下的那些水就会有问题。\
**Yenisei**: Whether it's an illusion or something else, there must be something wrong with the water they drank.

**别斯米尔**：……你说得对，这样不行——\
**Bessmert**: You're right. We can't let them drink it.

理智的接连否认，也不能改变此时同伴已经饮下异常流水的事实。\
Yet, their rational repudiations could not change the fact that their companions had already drunk from the abnormal water.

别斯米尔下意识向前跑去，想要在事情进一步恶化之前，及时止损。\
Bessmert instinctively runs forward, wishing to minimize the damage before things get worse.

**别斯米尔**：先生们，请听我说！那些水——\
**Bessmert**: Gentlemen, please listen! The water ...

**小叶尼塞**：女士！他们已经跑得太远了！\
**Yenisei**: Hold on, Madam! It's too late!

小叶尼塞拉住她的手，试图防止年长者因慌乱而在奔跑中跌倒。\
Yenisei grabs her hand, trying to prevent Bessmert from running in a panic and potentially suffering a fall.

别斯米尔仍要向前，却发现自己挣脱不开。\
Bessmert still wishes to rush forward, but finds herself unable to break free.

**别斯米尔**：但这可能是因为我指出的方向有问题，我必须去啊。\
**Bessmert**: I have to tell them. I am the reason why they are here.

**小叶尼塞**：您看，他们已经装完水，上岸开始往回走了。\
**Yenisei**: Listen. They have filled the water bags and are coming back.

能够继续前进的喜悦被异常很快地冲淡。\
Their momentary joy at finally being able to move forward is rapidly diluted.

唯一的安慰是，此时正在朝两人走回来的同伴，看上去并无异常。\
The only consolation is that the human walking back toward the two of them still appears to be normal.

**考察队员Ⅰ**：怎么了？你们不去补充水袋吗？\
**Team Member I**: What's wrong? Are you not going to fill your water bags?

**小叶尼塞**：……不，没事。我们会去的。\
**Yenisei**: Nothing. We'll go later.

**考察队员Ⅰ**：这水很清澈，里面甚至有鳟鱼。只可惜带不走太多。\
**Team Member I**: The water is clean. You can even see the trouts swimming. Too bad, we need to keep our packs light.

**小叶尼塞**：……\
**Yenisei**: ...

**别斯米尔**：谢谢您。我们想先确定接下来的方向，再补充水源。\
**Bessmert**: Thank you. We'll fill our bags once we figure out which way we should go next.

**考察队员Ⅰ**：克罗利克还在水边，看上去渴坏了。你们是因为他才不愿意过去？\
**Team Member I**: Krolik is still by the river. He seems parched. Is he the reason you didn't go there?

**小叶尼塞**：不是。\
**Yenisei**: No.

**考察队员Ⅰ**：那就没关系。我先去补充其他的水袋了。\
**Team Member I**: Alright, no problem, then. I'll go check and fill the rest.

高大的同行者在点头后，与两人错身而过，往先前被放下的辎重走去。\
Their tall companion nods and walks past the two of them, and toward the previously set-down baggage.

等到他完全离开之后，小叶尼塞才再度开口。\
Once he is gone, Yenisei speaks once more.

**小叶尼塞**：女士，请您等在这里，我会过去查看——\
**Yenisei**: Please wait here, Madam. I'll go check ...

**尤利恩**：——别斯米尔女士。\
**Jurien**: Madam Bessmert.

**别斯米尔**：嗯？尤利恩先生，您——您也去那边喝水了吗？\
**Bessmert**: Mm? Mr. Jurien, did, did you drink the water?

**尤利恩**：哦，是的。就像彼得洛夫那小子说的那样，水很清澈，甚至有些甜味。\
**Jurien**: Oh, we ... I did. Just like Petrov said, the water is clean, a bit sweet to taste, even.

**别斯米尔**：……好的，好的。那么，您叫我，是有什么问题吗？\
**Bessmert**: That's good, that's good then. You were looking for me. Is there a problem?

**尤利恩**：也许夸赞对你来说是不必要的。但现在我们的确找到了活水，你用能力赢回了大家的信任。\
**Jurien**: No, no. Look, I know you don't need any compliments, but thank you for leading us to the running water. I'm glad you once again earned their trust.

**别斯米尔**：又或许只是因为“所求必应”听见了我的渴望。\
**Bessmert**: Maybe we should thank the "Ask and Acquire."

**尤利恩**：哈哈，也许是吧。\
**Jurien**: Haha, perhaps.

**尤利恩**：总之，现在我们可以重新确定方向，继续向前，去寻找你说的东方神秘术了。\
**Jurien**: Now, it's time for us to set out again for the Eastern arcane skill you mentioned.

**尤利恩**：而在这之前……我的记忆告诉我，你在游说时提起过你的助手。她的神秘术似乎与水有关，能指引方向？\
**Jurien**: But before we do that ... I remember you once mentioned your assistant during your speech, saying her arcane skill was related to water and could find directions in the wild.

**别斯米尔**：是的，您的记忆一点儿也没错。\
**Bessmert**: Yes, you remember it correctly.

得到确认的喜悦笑容出现在中年人的脸上，热忱驱使着他接连发问。\
A glad smile of acknowledgment appears on the face of the middle-aged man, his enthusiasm compelling him to ask one question after another.

**尤利恩**：啊，那真是太好了！先前，你还说过这是一道保险，当时却没有继续详细说明，这个保险要怎样运作……\
**Jurien**: Ah, that is so wonderful! Earlier, you said that this was a safeguard, but at the time you did not explain in detail how it would work ...

**尤利恩**：现在我们能有幸看到了吗？她怎样通过这样的流水获取指引，需不需要请灵上身？\
**Jurien**: Now, may I have the honor to witness it? How does she communicate with water? Will she be possessed?

**尤利恩**：是否就像皇宫里的那些法师一样——\
**Jurien**: Or like those mystics in the Palace ...

**小叶尼塞**：先生，我的神秘术并非精准预言，也不通过“降灵”施行。\
**Yenisei**: Sir, my arcane skill cannot predict what will happen precisely, and it is not cast through "possession."

**小叶尼塞**：您不能把全部的希望都寄托在自己无法理解的事物之上。\
**Yenisei**: Please do not overestimate what you don't understand and simply count on it.

**尤利恩**：我知道，孩子。我只是感兴趣，想亲眼看一看——\
**Jurien**: I know, child. I'm only curious and hoping to see it with my own eyes ...

**小叶尼塞**：不行，先生。这不是什么观赏品，也不是剧院里的演出。\
**Yenisei**: No, Sir. It is not an exhibit in the museum or a play in the theater.

**尤利恩**：是吗……\
**Jurien**: Oh ...

少女摇头，笃定地再次拒绝了尤利恩的要求。\
The girl shakes her head and firmly refuses Jurien's request once again.

但年长的人类并不在意。他已得到比预想更多的答案，在离开时微笑着再次整理自己的领口，向两人分别致意。\
But he doesn't care. He has received more of an answer than he expected, and as he leaves, he smiles and straightens his collar again, bidding goodbye to both of them, respectively.

**小叶尼塞**：……他们看上去可没什么问题。\
**Yenisei**: They look alright.

**别斯米尔**：也许只是暂时的，我还是很担心，我得去——\
**Bessmert**: For now, yes. I feel uneasy about it. I have to go there ...

**小叶尼塞**：您的眼睛不方便，过去的作用实在不大。我会去那边查看一下他们每个人的状况。\
**Yenisei**: There's little you can do even if you go there, given the condition of your eyes. I will go check them, one by one.

**别斯米尔**：等等，还有。刚才尤利恩先生提到你的神秘术……或许现在的确正是合适的时机。\
**Bessmert**: Wait. Mr. Jurien just asked about your arcane power. Maybe now it's a good time.

**小叶尼塞**：什么？\
**Yenisei**: What?

**别斯米尔**：你过去查看后，可以施展你的神秘术，在占卜方向的同时，也实际验证那水，是不是真的活水。\
**Bessmert**: When you look for the direction with your arcane skill, check if the "water" is real.

**小叶尼塞**：如果不是呢？\
**Yenisei**: What if it's not?

**别斯米尔**：……\
**Bessmert**: ...

**别斯米尔**：那么，好孩子，你就继续用玻璃瓶中原来的水，占卜出回去的方向。\
**Bessmert**: In that case, child, we have no choice but to divine our way back, with the water in your bottle.

别斯米尔忧虑而无奈的话语，在小叶尼塞耳边阵阵作响。\
Bessmert's worried and helpless words echo in Yenisei's ears.

**小叶尼塞**：……\
**Yenisei**: ...

**小叶尼塞**：好，我来。\
**Yenisei**: Fine. I'll do it.

**小叶尼塞**：我会占卜方向，验证活水，确定是否异常。\
**Yenisei**: I will find the direction through divination, verify if the water is running, and check if anything's wrong.

女孩迈步，走向似乎凭空出现的潺潺河流。\
The girl takes a step forward and walks toward the strange babbling stream that seems to have come from nowhere.

小叶尼塞赤足步入河流中。\
Yenisei walks barefoot into the river.

温带高原上理应冰冷的流水，没过小腿，轻柔拍打着。\
Flowing water on a temperate plateau like this should naturally be cold. It gently laps at her, just beneath her calves.

她闭上眼，仿佛对温度丝毫没有察觉。\
She closes her eyes, trying to make herself unaware of the temperature.

**小叶尼塞**：——神圣之水，请您奔涌，奔涌——\
**Yenisei**: Sacred water, please flow and flow ...

**小叶尼塞**：请令您慈爱的轻抚，随奔涌的泡沫漂向远方。\
**Yenisei**: May your love and care drift far away with the flowing foam.

**小叶尼塞**：沿途您可灌溉根系，湿润草地，泼洒灵魂的蜜。\
**Yenisei**: May you water the roots, moisten the grass, and sweeten the souls.

**小叶尼塞**：就像从海浪扑打的礁岸捧起一个潺潺流淌的尽头。\
**Yenisei**: Like lifting a current from a reef where waves are breaking.

光点汇集，逐渐充盈空落的玻璃瓶。\
The light spots gather and gradually fill the empty glass bottle.

**小叶尼塞**：而我——\
**Yenisei**: And I ...

**小叶尼塞**：我将走上那个尽头。\
**Yenisei**: I will go to that current.

**小叶尼塞**：一切都将如我所说那般成为现实。\
**Yenisei**: Everything will be as I said.

**小叶尼塞**：……\
**Yenisei**: ...

**小叶尼塞**：东南。\
**Yenisei**: Southeast.

空玻璃瓶从松开的手中坠落。\
The empty glass bottle falls from her loosened grip.

女孩神色恍惚，从水中拾起潮湿沉重的脚步，向着东南迈去。\
The girl looks dazed as she picks up her damp and heavy feet from the water, heading to the southeast.

**别斯米尔**：——\
**Bessmert**: ...

**别斯米尔**：——嘿——\
**Bessmert**: HEY!

**别斯米尔**：——你要去哪儿？\
**Bessmert**: Where are you going?

**小叶尼塞**：嗯……\
**Yenisei**: Hmm ...

**小叶尼塞**：……嗯？我——\
**Yenisei**: Mmm? I ...

她的精神仍有一半处于谵妄的地界。恍惚中听见的声音都碎成数片，难以拼凑。\
Half of her mind is still in the realm of delirium. The sounds she hears are fragmented into pieces that she can only attempt to fit together.

要听清旁人实在有些困难，但她仍然努力着。\
Yet, through the difficulty of her present state of mind, she tries her best to make sense of what Bessmert is saying.

**小叶尼塞**：呃……\
**Yenisei**: Mmm ...

**别斯米尔**：有结果，对吗？\
**Bessmert**: You've found something, haven't you?

**小叶尼塞**：我，唔……\
**Yenisei**: I, emm ...

**别斯米尔**：孩子，你慢慢说。\
**Bessmert**: Easy, Yeni, take your time.

**小叶尼塞**：……是的。\
**Yenisei**: Yes.

**小叶尼塞**：是的。有结果了。\
**Yenisei**: Yes. The sign has come out.

**小叶尼塞**：这条河在诸多道路中，选择了东南。我请它指向的是神秘术气息最浓厚的地方……\
**Yenisei**: I asked the river to show me the place with the strongest arcane energy. Then, it pointed at the southeast among all the other directions.

**小叶尼塞**：它很可能就是我们所想要寻找的方位。\
**Yenisei**: That is probably the direction we are looking for.

**小叶尼塞**：……嗯，这的确是活水，它很有生命力。\
**Yenisei**: And yes, this river is real running water. It is flowing with vitality.

**别斯米尔**：好吧。也许是我判断失误。\
**Bessmert**: Alright. Perhaps I was wrong.

**小叶尼塞**：考虑多种可能性总是没错的，女士。\
**Yenisei**: It's never wrong to consider all the possibilities, Madam.

**小叶尼塞**：请在此等候吧。我去做标记，然后通知其他人。\
**Yenisei**: Please wait here. I will mark the direction and inform everyone of it.

**别斯米尔**：……好。\
**Bessmert**: Sure.

## NS-04 俯身旷野 / Strange Horses

草原的春色一路延展。\
The spring scenery of the steppes stretches out to the edge of the horizon.

考察小队沿着河流所指方向前行，继续跋涉。\
The expedition team continues to trek in the direction indicated by the river.

地形逐渐变化，众人已经不知不觉在裸露的山石中穿行许久。\
As they do, they scarcely notice as the terrain beneath them changes. Until the party at last finds themselves walking across bare rock.

高低不平的绿岩衔接着灰紫色斑岩，崎岖嶙峋。风滚草和沙蓬从中间洞穿，翻卷过去，再直直坠下峭壁。\
The uneven green rocks merge with grayish and purple granite, rough and jagged. In spots, tumbleweed and sand rice plants pierce through the jagged stone, billowing and cascading, and then plummeting down the cliff.

人们也感觉自己在向下。随着周围异样的增加，呼吸却越来越被收紧。\
The travelers also feel as though they are moving downward. As the surrounding peculiarities increase, so too does their breathing, which becomes increasingly restricted.

**小叶尼塞**：呼……\
**Yenisei**: *pants*

**克罗利克**：你们先前……已经证明了自己，带我们找到了活水……\
**Krolik**: You proved yourself right by ... finding running water for us ...

**克罗利克**：所以，我不愿总是成为提出质疑的那个。但是——\
**Krolik**: So, I'm not ... judging you ... this time, but ...

**克罗利克**：我们是不是走错路了？\
**Krolik**: Are we going the wrong way?

**小叶尼塞**：是这个方向没错。\
**Yenisei**: No. This is the right direction.

**克罗利克**：可我觉得呼吸越来越困难了，就算这分明——分明是在下山。\
**Krolik**: But it's getting harder and harder to breathe, even if we are going down the mountain.

**小叶尼塞**：女士，您呢？您感觉还好吗？\
**Yenisei**: What about you, Madam? Are you feeling alright?

**别斯米尔**：或许是我常常登山的缘故，还没有什么感觉。\
**Bessmert**: I feel fine. Perhaps because I'm used to climbing mountains.

**别斯米尔**：但这地方的海拔绝对超过3000米了，你们或许是不适应这种高度。如果我们还有酒精……\
**Bessmert**: But we are definitely 3000 meters above the sea level now. It's normal if you're feeling unwell at this height. If only we still had alcohol ...

**别斯米尔**：好吧，只是想想。如果没有那几口酒，我甚至可能爬不上刚才那道窄坡。\
**Bessmert**: Well, it's just a thought. I wouldn't have gathered enough courage to climb up that slope if I hadn't taken the last few sips.

别斯米尔摇头，驱散了多余的想法，改为追寻另一种可能。\
Bessmert shakes her head, dispelling unnecessary thoughts, and instead pursues another possibility.

**别斯米尔**：只是……孩子，你确定我们的方向是对的吗？\
**Bessmert**: But, child, are you sure we are on the right path?

**小叶尼塞**：我认为不会有错。占卜的指向越清晰，准确性就越高。\
**Yenisei**: I don't think it's wrong. The clearer the sign, the higher the accuracy.

**小叶尼塞**：这次的指向，恰好明晰得十分少见。\
**Yenisei**: And the sign I just saw happened to be exceptionally clear.

**别斯米尔**：其他人有没有出现身体不适？我们是否需要停下来暂时休整？\
**Bessmert**: What about the others? Are you feeling alright? Shall we stop and take a short break?

**克罗利克**：感觉不太对劲。比起休整，我们更需要改变方向。比如往回走。\
**Krolik**: I have a bad feeling. Instead of a break, we need a new direction. Back home, for example.

**尤利恩**：或者，能不能至少先休整一下？我已经头痛有一阵子了，还以为这是在高原上的通常情况。\
**Jurien**: Before we do anything, can we have some rest? My head has been pounding for a while. I thought it was common in the mountains and you all felt the same.

**别斯米尔**：是的，头痛在高原是常见情况，先生。\
**Bessmert**: Yes, headache is a common altitude sickness, Sir.

**小叶尼塞**：等等，那些是刺蓟吗？刺蓟好像不应该出现在这种地方。\
**Yenisei**: Wait, is that tumbleweed?! I don't think it belongs here.

小叶尼塞终于留意到了不远处滚动的巨大物体。\
Yenisei finally notices a large bundle trundling on not far away.

**别斯米尔**：我听到的……就是它们在翻滚的声音？你确定吗？\
**Bessmert**: I hear ... Are they rolling nearby? Are you sure?

**别斯米尔**：可现在不是它们播种的季节。\
**Bessmert**: This is not the right season for them to roll and spread seeds.

**小叶尼塞**：我应该没有看错，但是我不明白。还有那些花——\
**Yenisei**: I'm not seeing things, I guess, but I don't know why they are here. And those flowers ...

缀在队伍末尾的队员停下了脚步。于是他身旁的其他人也一起停下了。\
The team members at the end of their procession stop in their tracks. The others beside him also stop as a result.

队伍彻底陷入了停滞。\
Until the entire team comes to a standstill.

**考察队员Ⅰ**：这不对劲。\
**Team Member I**: Something's wrong.

**考察队员Ⅱ**：——嘿，你们……你们究竟想把我们带去哪儿？\
**Team Member II**: Hey you ... where are you taking us?

**考察队员Ⅱ**：你们难道一点也看不见周围这些岩石吗？这些奇怪的颜色，我从没见过，也不在任何的资料记录里……\
**Team Member II**: Haven't you noticed the rocks around us? Their color is abnormal. I've never seen anything like this, not even in books ...

**考察队员Ⅱ**：那些石头上的水蚀洞也绝对不是这个气候应该出现的！\
**Team Member II**: And look at the holes in the rocks! They were made by water erosion! And that's not supposed to happen in this climate!

**小叶尼塞**：先生，请冷静。也许我们只是走到了不存在于其他旅行者记录上的地方——\
**Yenisei**: Calm down, Sir. Perhaps we have reached somewhere beyond other adventurers' records, but that's all ...

**考察队员Ⅱ**：那这个呢！这个要怎么解释？\
**Team Member II**: What about this?! How are you going to explain it?!

**考察队员Ⅱ**：用你们那该死的神秘术吗？\
**Team Member II**: Another one of your stupid arcane skill tricks?

小叶尼塞低头看去，只看到貌似普通的黄色花束。\
Yenisei lowers her head to look at what seem to be ordinary yellow flowers.

但这鲜花却自盛开后便立刻枯萎，要说不是神迹，就实在难以描述这样的情景。\
But these flowers wither almost immediately after blooming. It would be difficult to describe such a scene as anything less than a miracle or a curse.

**小叶尼塞**：什么？这……这是……\
**Yenisei**: What? This is ...

**别斯米尔**：怎么了？解释什么？\
**Bessmert**: What is it? Explain what?

**小叶尼塞**：……我不认识这种花，它看起来像迷你的葵花。但是它——\
**Yenisei**: I don't know what species it is. It looks like a mini sunflower, but ...

**克罗利克**：我说了，我们应该往回走。这鬼地方不对劲。\
**Krolik**: Told you we should head back. Something's wrong with this dump.

**考察队员Ⅰ**：我支持。遇上异常状况，在退路没有被封死的情况下，我们应该往回走。\
**Team Member I**: Agree. We have a situation now. We should go back while we still can.

**尤利恩**：女士，我得说这确实……有些超出想象了。\
**Jurien**: Ladies, I have to say this is beyond my imagination.

**小叶尼塞**：……\
**Yenisei**: ...

**别斯米尔**：只是花，怎么都像被吓到了一样？我看不见，但是——\
**Bessmert**: It's just a flower, yes? Why are you all so scared? I can't see, but ...

别斯米尔茫然地伸手握住花朵，花瓣也在她指尖迅速干枯。即使试图继续往前触摸完整的花簇，却都只能捉到一撮枯尽的碎末。\
Bessmert reaches out to grasp the flowers again, but the petals wither beneath her fingertips. Now more puzzled, she tries touching a complete cluster, but only ends up with a handful of withered husks.

枯萎的气息在清香消失后都接近腐烂，人所能做的，仅是捕捉这“香味”的后调。\
The scent of these withered fragments turns rotten as their sweet fragrance disappears, leaving her having captured only the base note of their "perfume."

**别斯米尔**：嗯？这是……\
**Bessmert**: Emm? The smell ...

**克罗利克**：这一切都违反常理……根本不应该出现在这个纬度的湿雾、怪异的地貌，还有这转瞬即逝的植物——！\
**Krolik**: Everything is wrong here. The fog is not supposed to form at this latitude, the terrain is strange, and the plants … they wither in an instant!

**考察队员Ⅰ**：我不想这么说，但是，这里就像是遭到了诅咒。\
**Team Member I**: I don't want to say this, but this place seems to be cursed.

**考察队员Ⅰ**：这些东西……说不通。这次我们必须得往回走了。\
**Team Member I**: These phenomena make no sense. We have to go back now.

青年男人的声音比以往的所有时候都更加不可撼动。\
The voice of the young man is more resolute than ever before.

面对这样不合常理的情况，“逃走”的确是最为理性的选择。\
Faced with such a bizarre situation, escape is unarguably the most rational choice.

**小叶尼塞**：别斯米尔女士，他们说往回走，您觉得应该怎么办？现在的情况确实很奇怪——\
**Yenisei**: You heard them, Madam. What do you say? Things are indeed weird.

**别斯米尔**：不，不是的。我们连草原风暴都熬过了，这不会是什么比自然灾害更加危在旦夕的情况。\
**Bessmert**: No, we are not returning. We have made it through the thunderstorm. What could be more dangerous than that?

**别斯米尔**：也许我们就快到了，这是那些商人说过的，实现“所求必应”的考验……对，尤利恩先生，您当时还向我提问了，您也不记得了吗？\
**Bessmert**: Perhaps we are getting close, like those merchants said, there will be a "price" we must pay for the Ask and Acquire. Mr. Jurien, you also asked me about it, don't you remember?

**尤利恩**：正好相反，女士。我记得，记得清清楚楚……后来我也告诉了你，我认为那是神秘学家与自然进行某种交易的仪式。\
**Jurien**: On the contrary, Madam, I remember it clearly. I have also told you my suspicion—it could be an exchange made between the arcanists and nature.

**别斯米尔**：什么？那当然不是——\
**Bessmert**: What? Of course not.

**尤利恩**：看看现在周围这些异象，我的猜想难道不是确有其事吗？你追逐着神秘术，却带我们来到了这种地方……\
**Jurien**: Look around you—all these bizarre phenomena! You know I wasn't making things up. You set out to pursue that arcane skill, yet we ended up here ...

**克罗利克**：我不知道你们还有什么谋划，总之我不会继续参与了。\
**Krolik**: I don't know what your next plan is, but count me out.

受到异常与“献祭仪式”猜想刺激的年轻人毫不犹豫地推开别斯米尔，去与队伍后面的其他人站到一起。\
Agitated by this abnormal phenomenon and talk of a possible sacrifice, the young man pushes Bessmert aside and stands with the others at the back of the group.

一幕先前对立的重演。\
A previous scene of division and opposition repeats itself.

**别斯米尔**：不，我发誓，我绝对没有那样的想法！\
**Bessmert**: No, I swear on my life, that is not my intention!

**小叶尼塞**：别斯米尔女士不会那样做的。\
**Yenisei**: Madam Bessmert would never do that.

**小叶尼塞**：而且，没有我，也没有指南针，你们不会辨别中途的方向。\
**Yenisei**: The point is, the compass doesn't work here. You will get lost on the way back without me.

**克罗利克**：这当然也是你们算计的一环。\
**Krolik**: There's no doubt this is part of your scheme.

**小叶尼塞**：你说什么？\
**Yenisei**: Excuse me?

**克罗利克**：尤利恩先生早就告诉我们了，你那遮遮掩掩的神秘术——却是指南针失效之后，唯一能带我们往回赶路的方法。\
**Krolik**: Mr. Jurien already told us about your secret arcane skill. It's our last hope of getting home in this plight.

**别斯米尔**：……\
**Bessmert**: ...

**克罗利克**：我们相信他的判断，既然是这样，那你就必须跟我们走了。\
**Krolik**: We trust him. That being the case, you must come with us.

**小叶尼塞**：不。我是同别斯米尔女士一起来的，她不回去，我也不会走。\
**Yenisei**: No. I came here with Madam Bessmert. I'm not leaving without her.

小叶尼塞也清晰地表达了自己的选择。她从来不是一个容易被外力改变的人，除非——\
Yenisei also expresses her intentions clearly. Never having been one to be swayed by external forces, unless ...

**别斯米尔**：我们……\
**Bessmert**: Let's ...

**小叶尼塞**：女士，没关系，我们自己继续前进——\
**Yenisei**: It's fine, Madam. We can keep going on our own ...

**别斯米尔**：我们往回走吧。\
**Bessmert**: Let's go back.

**小叶尼塞**：——？！\
**Yenisei**: ...?!

——除非她所支持的人先一步低头。\
… Unless the person she is supporting lowers her head first.

**别斯米尔**：没关系，虽然我看不见，但我可以想象眼前的景象有多么令人惊讶。\
**Bessmert**: It's alright. Though I can't see, I can imagine how shocking it must be to make you so uneasy.

**别斯米尔**：等我们回到牧区——\
**Bessmert**: When we get back to the pastureland ...

**克罗利克**：不，女士，很遗憾，我们不能带上你。\
**Krolik**: I'm sorry, Madam. We are not taking you.

**克罗利克**：我认为物资已经不足以支撑我们所有人顺利返回，当然有人需要被放弃。\
**Krolik**: I don't think we have enough supplies for everyone to make it back, so certainly someone must be abandoned.

小叶尼塞往前更近一步，直到将失魂落魄的别斯米尔完全挡住。\
Yenisei takes a step closer until she is completely blocking the depressed Bessmert's path.

**小叶尼塞**：那么，请允许我拒绝。如果不带上别斯米尔女士，我是不会为你们指路的。\
**Yenisei**: Then, allow me to say no. I will not show you the way without Madam Bessmert in the team.

**别斯米尔**：……不，孩子。你要和他们走。\
**Bessmert**: No, Yeni. You're going with them.

**小叶尼塞**：可他们要抛下您！\
**Yenisei**: But they are leaving you behind!

**克罗利克**：看来您的助手有自己的决断。真可惜，原本我还希望我们不会走到这一步——\
**Krolik**: Looks like your assistant has made her own decision. Sorry, but I never thought it would end up like this ...

**考察队员Ⅰ**：不必多说。抱歉了，女士们。\
**Team Member I**: Enough with the talking. My apologies, ladies.

**小叶尼塞**：你们——你们要做什么？！\
**Yenisei**: What ... What are you doing?!

人们对峙着，决定将争执以武力压制作结。\
They are now facing each other, seeming to have decided to end their dispute through force.

他们显然都清楚放弃一个能拯救更多。\
They are acutely aware that sacrificing one might save the many.

简单的算术题。\
It is a simple matter of arithmetic.

直立是人所专属的行为，它是人们摆脱大地，执着朝向天空而诞生的奇迹。\
Standing upright is a phenomenon exclusive to humans. It is a miracle born of a desire to break free from the earth and move upward towards the sky.

变故发生于所有人的意料之外。\
The outcome unfolds quite apart from everyone's expectations.

**小叶尼塞**：……什么？\
**Yenisei**: What?

**斑纹马？**：咴咴——咴——\
**Striped Horse?**: *neighs*

**小叶尼塞**：我不理解，你们、你们这是——发生了什么？！\
**Yenisei**: I-I don't understand. What is ... What is going on?!

而即使人们已经意识到内斗的不合时宜，却也只能目睹和解的可能在瞬间化为乌有。\
Even though they acknowledge the untimely nature of their dispute, they are left to witness all hope of reconciliation disintegrate before them.

小叶尼塞得不到回答，是因为眼前的人们已经失去用言语回答的能力。\
Yenisei receives no answer, as the people standing in front of her now have lost the ability to reply.

## NS-05 巴别塔消融 / Language Barrier

**斑纹马？**：——咴——咴——\
**Striped Horse?**: *neighs*

**小叶尼塞**：……为什么……\
**Yenisei**: No way ...

转过身去，却发现同行者从双脚站立的人类，突然变成四肢着地的奇蹄目动物。\
Turning around, she finds that her companion has transformed in an instant from a human on two feet to a strange hoofed animal on all fours.

作为唯一清楚地目睹了全程的人，她却感到现状实在难以理解，只能把疑惑的目光投向年长者。\
As the only person to have witnessed the entire process in detail, with every aspect too difficult to comprehend, she can only turn her puzzled gaze toward her elder.

但别斯米尔也浑然不觉。\
But Bessmert is also in the dark.

**别斯米尔**：这是什么声音？……克罗利克先生？\
**Bessmert**: What's this noise? Mr. Krolik?

回答她的只有奇蹄目踩踏草皮的不耐烦动静。\
The only answer she receives is the impatient stirring of the odd-toed ungulate as it tramples the grass.

**别斯米尔**：尤利恩先生？\
**Bessmert**: Mr. Jurien?

**斑纹马？**：咴——\
**Striped Horse?**: *neighs*

**别斯米尔**：不对。我听到了动物的声音。有什么东西出现了？\
**Bessmert**: Strange. I heard animals. What happened?

**小叶尼塞**：……这……\
**Yenisei**: Emm ...

**别斯米尔**：小叶尼塞，我看不见。我需要你的帮助。\
**Bessmert**: Yenisei, I can't see. I need your help.

**小叶尼塞**：天啊，让、让我想想……呃，看起来，尤利恩先生他们变成了——斑纹马？\
**Yenisei**: Oh dear, give me a minute ... Emm, looks like they turned into ... I don't know, striped horses?

**小叶尼塞**：抱歉，我不知道。我只在画册上见过这些动物。\
**Yenisei**: I ... Sorry, I'm not sure. I've only seen similar animals in books.

**小叶尼塞**：它们看起来比马要小一些，又比驴的体型更大、更高，身上有一些黄色的斑纹。\
**Yenisei**: They look a bit smaller than horses, but taller and bigger than donkeys. And they have yellow stripes on their skin.

**别斯米尔**：也许是某种温带草原上特有的动物……你确定是尤利恩先生他们自行变成了马，而不是附近出现了牧民？\
**Bessmert**: Perhaps some local species on the temperate steppe? Are you certain they're transformed from Mr. Jurien and others? Not the livestock of nearby herders?

**别斯米尔**：我刚才并没有采取过激的举措，你也没有。而且，我并没有感受到神秘术的波动——\
**Bessmert**: I didn't cast any violent arcane skills on them, nor did you. Besides, I didn't sense any fluctuations of arcane energy ...

**小叶尼塞**：对不起，女士，我也毫无头绪。\
**Yenisei**: I'm sorry, Madam. I have no idea.

**别斯米尔**：我想，如果不是因为我们的行动，就说明这地方可能还有其他人。\
**Bessmert**: I think ... if this wasn't because of us, there must be someone else around.

**别斯米尔**：你靠近我，不要走散。\
**Bessmert**: Stay close to me.

事实证明，迅速地聚拢且时刻保持警惕是必要的。\
The importance of rallying together and remaining vigilant has already been proven to them.

猛禽翅膀急速划破空气的声音，朝着两人与马群所在方向直直冲来。\
The sound of raptor wings rapidly slicing through the air rushes towards the two travelers and their horses.

**别斯米尔**：来了，当心！\
**Bessmert**: It's here. Watch out!

**小叶尼塞**：天哪，那是什么——\
**Yenisei**: What is it?!

**别斯米尔**：是不是某种猛禽？它翅膀的振幅剧烈，说明速度很快。我们得站到尤利恩先生他们前面去，动物袭击的目标很可能是他们……\
**Bessmert**: Some bird of prey? It's fast, judging from the flapping sound of its wings. We must go up front to protect Mr. Jurien and the others. They might be its target ...

**别斯米尔**：对了，火石，把火石拿出来！然后找团沙蓬点燃来驱赶它！\
**Bessmert**: Oh, yes, the flint! Take out the flint! Kindle the sand rice to drive it away!

**小叶尼塞**：不，等等……\
**Yenisei**: No, wait ...

**小叶尼塞**：我觉得那看起来像是一个长着翅膀的人，而不是普通的猛禽！\
**Yenisei**: I don't think that's a bird of prey, but a human with wings!

**小叶尼塞**：……而且它也没有继续前进？\
**Yenisei**: And it's not coming any closer?

女孩犹豫是因为乐声。\
The girl hesitates upon hearing the sound of music.

起初也有乐声。只是巨大翅膀搅动空气震颤更响，更剧烈，乐声就理所当然地被遮盖了。\
The music had been playing for only a short while. When those huge wings stirred the air into a violent storm, it was totally drowned out.

等到它并没有打算继续向前，逐渐缓慢的振翅声才被乐声所覆盖。\
It wasn't until it gave up on advancing that the slow flapping of wings was covered up by the music.

——被某种乐声覆盖，可音色却并不被此地任何人所知。\
But the tune of the music is unknown to all present.

音乐声从人耳能够捕捉到振翅声音的方位开始蔓延，像急雨一样，笼罩了地面不安的棕色动物。\
The music starts from the bird and spreads around, like a torrential rain, enveloping the restless brown animals on the ground below.

马群随旋律抬头，和剩下的两人一样都在聆听着。\
The horses look up in search of the source of this melody, as do the two other listeners.

分明是简单的重复旋律，却似乎攥住了别斯米尔全部的注意力。\
It is a simple and repetitive melody, but more than enough to consume Bessmert's full attention.

**？？？**：——\
**???**: ...

**小叶尼塞**：女士——！那是……！\
**Yenisei**: Madam! That thing is a creature with a human's head and a bird's body ...!

草原上的风吹散了她的呼喊。\
The fierce steppe winds carry off her cries.

**别斯米尔**：——什么？你说什么？我听不清——\
**Bessmert**: What? What did you say? I can't hear ...

**小叶尼塞**：我说，那看起来像是一个长着翅膀的人!\
**Yenisei**: I said, that thing looks like a human with wings!

**别斯米尔**：人？你是指人面？音乐声是从它那边传出来的？\
**Bessmert**: A human? You mean it has the face of a human? Is the music also coming from it?

**小叶尼塞**：是的！\
**Yenisei**: Yes!

**别斯米尔**：会奏乐，人面的带翅生物。听起来相当耳熟，不是吗？\
**Bessmert**: The music-playing winged creature with a human's face. Sounds familiar, don't you think?

**小叶尼塞**：……天使？！您在开玩笑吗？\
**Yenisei**: ... An angel?! You are not serious!

**小叶尼塞**：可天使吹奏的是号角！而且那个正在发出声音的，究竟是一根术杖还是某种乐器？\
**Yenisei**: But angels blow trumpets! That stick it uses to play music—I'm not sure whether it's a wand or some instrument.

女孩的声音藏不住疑惑。她拉住别斯米尔，想要向后退去，却又牢记不能离开马群太远。\
The girl's voice cannot conceal her doubt. She grabs Bessmert, wishing to step back, but remembers not to stray too far from the horses.

对本能与理智两种选择的犹豫，在她话语里显露得支离破碎。\
This conflict between her instinct and reason is revealed in her fragmented words.

她努力理解现状，可这实在有些困难。\
She tries to understand the current situation, but finds it strangely difficult.

**小叶尼塞**：女士，我……我们——\
**Yenisei**: Madam, we, I, we ...

**别斯米尔**：——冷静，孩子。\
**Bessmert**: Calm down, child.

**别斯米尔**：你再瞧仔细些，然后告诉我：它和那个术杖都长什么样子？\
**Bessmert**: Look closer and tell me. What does it look like? What about its wand?

**小叶尼塞**：它……它长着人的脑袋，披着衣服，看起来灰扑扑的，但双手却是黑色的猛禽翅膀，像是某种——某种巨大的鸟类……\
**Yenisei**: It ... It has a human's head, dressed in gray, with black wings instead of arms. Looks … looks like a huge bird of prey ...

**小叶尼塞**：至于那个术杖，我不知道。\
**Yenisei**: While the wand, I don't know how to describe it ...

女孩又匆忙抬起头确认，好为自己表述不清的部分增加抗辩似的补充。\
The girl hurriedly lifts her head again to confirm, and add a supplementary defense to that which she still cannot clearly express.

**小叶尼塞**：它甚至没用手抓着它！那东西似乎是隔空在发出声音。\
**Yenisei**: But that thing is not even holding it! It's making the sound in mid-air.

**别斯米尔**：抛开术杖的部分，听起来像鹰身女妖。\
**Bessmert**: Sounds like a Harpy, if there wasn't a wand.

**小叶尼塞**：可它羽毛的颜色，和这里的环境……和书上说的不一样。\
**Yenisei**: But it doesn't quite fit the descriptions in the book ... Neither the color of its feathers nor the environment does.

地上的两人还在尝试解读变故，几匹棕色的斑纹马早已从草地上抬头，轻快地原地迈步，都列队望向声音的来源。\
As they're trying to figure out what's going on, the horses, effecting a brisk piaffe, look up to the source of the sound.

片刻后，“鹰身女妖”转身，扇动翅膀缓缓飞离，马群就仿佛受到感召一般紧随其后。\
After a brief moment, the "Harpy" turns around, flapping its wings and slowly flying away, with the horses following closely behind as if compelled.

**小叶尼塞**：他们——他们跟着它走了！\
**Yenisei**: Mr. Jurien ... They are leaving after that thing!

**别斯米尔**：……冷静，孩子。\
**Bessmert**: Stay calm, Yenisei.

**别斯米尔**：他们一定被控制了，但我不确定——不确定鹰身女妖是不是有这种隔空操纵行为的能力。\
**Bessmert**: They must be under its control, but I'm not sure if ... if a Harpy can manipulate its subjects from a distance.

别斯米尔努力从脑海中挖掘着信息，希望能找到一点可用的东西，好解释眼前荒唐的变故。\
Bessmert strains to extract something useful from her mind, hoping to find anything that might explain the absurdities before her.

结果是，她毫无收获，疑问仍然像一把铁锤一样敲打着脑袋。\
In the end, she gains nothing, and the doubt strikes at her head again like a well-paced hammer.

**别斯米尔**：呃，好吧，让我们祈祷……\
**Bessmert**: Err, alright, let's hope that ...

**小叶尼塞**：祈祷他们不会被吃掉？女士，我们不能坐以待毙——\
**Yenisei**: Hope that "Harpy" doesn't eat horses? Madam, we can't just stand here and hope ...

**别斯米尔**：当然不是！是祈祷这是某种可以控制思维的神秘术，他们都是被控制了……\
**Bessmert**: Nonsense. Hope that this is just a mind-controlling arcane skill, and they're just affected by it.

**别斯米尔**：对，没错。我们需要追上去，打断施术者的行动。\
**Bessmert**: That's right. We must follow that creature and break the spell on them.

**别斯米尔**：所以你先——\
**Bessmert**: Now you need to ...

别斯米尔抓住小叶尼塞，另一手则坚定地指向马群奔向的上游。\
Bessmert grabs Yenisei, while her other hand points firmly upstream toward the herd of horses.

小叶尼塞几乎立刻理解了她的意思，逐渐镇定下来。\
Yenisei takes only a moment to understand her intentions and calms down.

**小叶尼塞**：……好，我明白了。\
**Yenisei**: Alright. I see what you mean.

**小叶尼塞**：我先追上去。请您留意我的脚步声，尽快赶上来。\
**Yenisei**: I'll go first. Please listen carefully to my footsteps and find us as soon as possible.

然而，很遗憾。\
Unfortunately ...

它似乎不用回头就知道身后发生的事，只需抬手就能接下小叶尼塞所有的攻击。\
They quickly realize the creature doesn't need to look back to know what's going on behind it. It merely raises its talons to deftly parry Yenisei's attacks.

换句话说，它的力量超出了两人的想象。\
That is to say, they realize soon enough that its power is far beyond what the two of them had imagined.

**小叶尼塞**：——停下！你到底要做什么！\
**Yenisei**: Hold there! What on earth do you want!

**小叶尼塞**：回答我！\
**Yenisei**: Answer me!

**？？？**：……\
**???**: ...

或许是力量实在悬殊，不必放在眼里，“鹰身女妖”在天上回过身来。\
Perhaps it is because of this disparity in strength that the "Harpy" seems not to feel any need to pay attention. It whirls around in midair.

但小叶尼塞很难看清它那张酷似人形的脸上有任何的表情。\
However, Yenisei struggles to see any discernible expression on its human face.

**？？？**：归去。\
**???**: Turn thee back.

**？？？**：此处并无尔等所寻之物。\
**???**: Seek what thou desire elsewhere.

**小叶尼塞**：什么？\
**Yenisei**: What?

**？？？**：既如此，不如归去。\
**???**: Turn thee back, there is naught to find here.

**别斯米尔**：这声音是它在说话，还是在唱歌？为什么听起来更像青年男子的音色？\
**Bessmert**: What is this sound? Speaking or singing? Sounds like a young man, how so?

**别斯米尔**：不过，也许可以认为它不是鹰身女妖了。\
**Bessmert**: Well, at least it's definitely not a Harpy.

**小叶尼塞**：也许它是在说话。可声调很奇怪，我从没听过这种语言。\
**Yenisei**: Perhaps it's talking, but the tone sounds strange. I've never heard any language like this.

小叶尼塞徒劳地想要继续上前，直到“巨鸟”警告似的在空中摇晃脑袋。\
Yenisei tries in vain to continue forward, but the "giant bird" shakes its head in the air as though issuing a warning.

**？？？**：若执着于此……便是光阴蹉跎，前程惘然。\
**???**: Thine pursuit will cost thee greatly, and yet little will be thy reward.

**？？？**：勿要上前了。\
**???**: Tread not one step more.

随“巨鸟”翅膀抬起而动作的，除了那古怪的乐器，还有蓦然回头的马群。\
As the wings of the "giant bird" rise and heave, in addition to the strange instrument, the horses also turn around.

失去控制的同伴拦在路中，乐声也陡然由悠扬转向尖锐。\
Their unhinged companions stand in the way as the music suddenly shifts from a melodious tone to a piercing frenzy.

它谱了一出无奈的冲突。\
It paints the scene of a hopeless conflict.

同伴变作的斑纹马被“巨鸟”驱遣着，掉转头来挡住她的去路。\
The striped horses are driven by the giant bird, turning their heads to block her path.

小叶尼塞只能在围堵中抬起手来，继续向上发动攻击。\
Yenisei can only lift her hands against the encirclement and continue launching her attacks upward.

**斑纹马？**：*愤怒的叫声*\
**Striped Horse?**: *neighs angrily*

**小叶尼塞**：呃！\
**Yenisei**: Ugh!

**小叶尼塞**：呃……你们……让开。让开！\
**Yenisei**: Ugh ... Gentlemen ... Get out of the way. Out!

**小叶尼塞**：还有你，天上的那个！你会说话，是吗？虽然我听不明白——\
**Yenisei**: And you, hey, the flying one! You can talk, right? I don't know your language, but ...

**小叶尼塞**：但你如果坚持要选他们做食物的话，我建议你还是好好考虑一下。\
**Yenisei**: If you are going to eat them, you'd better think twice.

**小叶尼塞**：马肉的味道很腥。\
**Yenisei**: Horse meat has a bad smell.

**？？？**：……\
**???**: ...

巨鸟没再出声。小叶尼塞留意到一枚细长白色的短杖自它身上飞出。\
The bird remains silent. Yenisei notices a slender, white stick poking out from his feathers.

像骨头，也像术杖。\
Like a bone, but yet also like a wand.

**小叶尼塞**：不……女士，快躲开！\
**Yenisei**: No ... Madam, watch out!

**别斯米尔**：什么？我没有感觉到攻击性——\
**Bessmert**: What? I don't sense any hostility ...

这“攻击”显示，它是术杖。\
This "attack" indicates that it is, in fact, a wand.

然而理应受到“攻击”的两人，看上去毫无变化。无论身体或精神，都与先前如出一辙。\
However, the two individuals supposedly subjected to this attack seem unchanged. Both physically and mentally, they are exactly as they were before.

**小叶尼塞**：……嗯？\
**Yenisei**: Hmm?

**别斯米尔**：没事。我没事，这不是一次攻击。\
**Bessmert**: Don't worry. I'm fine. It wasn't an attack.

就在两人惊疑不定时，空中挥舞着翅膀的人却再次开口了。\
As the two of them begin to explore their uncertainty, the figure flapping its wings in the air speaks once again.

这一次，有什么东西不一样了。\
This time, though, something is different.

**？？？**：你们所寻之人……自走入此地，饮下流水起，就已与你们无关。\
**???**: Those whom you chase are no longer related to you once they walked in here and moistened their throats with the flowing water.

**？？？**：此事需交由职祠处理。\
**???**: They are the Zhící's concern.

**？？？**：休要再追。\
**???**: No more chasing.

**小叶尼塞**：职祠是什么？我实在难以理解你说的……\
**Yenisei**: What is a Zhící? I don't understand ...

**小叶尼塞**：啊，不对，我、我能听懂了？\
**Yenisei**: No, wait, I-I understand his words now. What?

**小叶尼塞**：可是——这——发生了什么？难道是我产生了幻觉？\
**Yenisei**: But ... What is happening? Am I seeing illusions again?

**小叶尼塞**：女士，你——\
**Yenisei**: Madam, what about ...

**别斯米尔**：不，不是幻觉，我也能听懂。\
**Bessmert**: No, it's not an illusion. I can understand it, too.

**小叶尼塞**：太奇怪了。是他能使用多种语言，还是说，他能快速学习我们说的话——\
**Yenisei**: Unbelievable. Is he able to speak different languages, or can he learn from our conversation in no time?

**别斯米尔**：刚才我们以为的“攻击”，应该是他的神秘术。\
**Bessmert**: The "attack" he just made could be his arcane skill.

**别斯米尔**：我能感觉到神秘术波动的气息。如果是真的，那这个术相当奇特。它似乎能使人语言相通……\
**Bessmert**: I can sense the fluctuation of his arcane energy. It's a wondrous power that allows people to communicate.

**？？？**：揣测是无用的。回去吧。\
**???**: Speculation is unhelpful to your situation. Go back ...

**？？？**：回来处去。\
**???**: ... To where you came from.

此时语义清晰。但无论是劝告的话语，还是拒绝的语气，都无法动摇两人执着的念头。\
This time, its meaning is clear. But neither these words of advice nor its tone of refusal can shake their resolve.

之前她们不考虑回头，此时当然也不会答应。\
Turning back had never been a consideration before, so of course, they wouldn't consider it now.

**小叶尼塞**：不。\
**Yenisei**: No.

**小叶尼塞**：你需要把他们变回来。回不回去，是我们之间的事，与你无关。\
**Yenisei**: First, you must turn them back. Second, to go back or not is our decision to make, not yours.

**？？？**：……此事非我之祸。\
**???**: That was not my doing.

小叶尼塞试图理解这只巨鸟话中潜藏的真实含义。她的头脑飞速转动起来，无数个问题要争先跳出舌苔。\
Yenisei attempts to understand the true meaning hidden in the giant bird's words. Her mind spins rapidly, and countless questions clamber up, desperate to leap from her tongue.

**小叶尼塞**：你停了下来，而且对我们使用了能通人言的神秘术，这代表你默认了沟通选择的存在。\
**Yenisei**: You stopped here and cast that arcane skill for us to talk, which means you think communication is an available choice between us.

**小叶尼塞**：你刚才说的“饮下流水”，是指我们先前路过的河流吗？\
**Yenisei**: You just mentioned "the flowing water." Do you mean the river we passed by?

**小叶尼塞**：而且，这些斑纹马是我们的同伴。你说要将他们带到“职祠”处去，我需要知道那儿究竟是哪里。\
**Yenisei**: And you said these striped horses are "Zhící's concern." I need to know where that place is because they are my teammates.

**小叶尼塞**：还有……你究竟是谁？\
**Yenisei**: Besides ... who on earth are you?

**？？？**：……\
**???**: ...

**？？？**：你所问，皆非我所能答。\
**???**: What you ask, I have no answer.

**小叶尼塞**：……那你能回答什么？\
**Yenisei**: Then what do you know?

**？？？**：四书五经，堪舆风水，谶纬天地。\
**???**: The Four Books and Five Classics, Geomancy and Feng Shui, Chen-Wei Divination.

**小叶尼塞**：那都是什么东西？！\
**Yenisei**: What are you talking about?!

**？？？**：嗯？自然是解惑之道。\
**???**: Mm? The answers to many questions, naturally.

他语气里的疑惑听起来竟然是发自内心的真诚。\
The doubt in his tone seems to come straight from the bottom of his heart.

**别斯米尔**：孩子，听我说。我们也许不应该这样向他提问。\
**Bessmert**: Yenisei, listen to me. We might be asking the wrong questions.

**小叶尼塞**：可我们总得知道些什么，或者拖延时间，总之——总之不能就这样让他离开。\
**Yenisei**: But we need to collect more information or buy more time. Whatever we are going to do, we can't just let him go.

**小叶尼塞**：他会带走尤利恩先生他们！\
**Yenisei**: He will take Mr. Jurien and the team away from us!

**别斯米尔**：可他听起来，显然也不愿正面回答这些问题。\
**Bessmert**: But clearly, he is reluctant to answer these questions.

**别斯米尔**：也许我们应该考虑，能不能用物资和他交换我们的同伴？\
**Bessmert**: Perhaps he'd be willing to exchange them for our supplies?

**别斯米尔**：他要带走马群，更有可能是因为现在的尤利恩先生他们身上，有他想要的东西。\
**Bessmert**: He is trying to take them away, perhaps because they are carrying the supplies he needs.

**小叶尼塞**：食物？还是什么？那我们——\
**Yenisei**: You mean food, or what? Let's ...

**？？？**：既无所问，两位这便留步罢。\
**???**: Stop, there's nothing else for you here.

**？？？**：毕竟……\
**???**: And I need nothing ...

**？？？**：我所欲，渺然远矣，不知亦不可追。\
**???**: What I yearn for is beyond even my own grasp.

**别斯米尔**：等等，先生——\
**Bessmert**: Wait, good sir ...!

巨鸟回身振翅，比先前更快地飞远了。\
The bird turns around and flaps its wings, flying away much faster than before.

而这次甚至没有了乐声。奇蹄目在翅膀挥舞所带动的风声中，仍然紧跟其后。\
This time, there is no music. Yet the odd creatures follow closely in the wake of the wind raised by the motion of its wings.

**小叶尼塞**：你——\
**Yenisei**: Hey!

**小叶尼塞**：该死，他又飞走了！\
**Yenisei**: Darn. He flew away!

**别斯米尔**：……是我说错了什么吗？\
**Bessmert**: ... Did I say anything wrong?

**小叶尼塞**：不是您的错，女士。他看起来就是个反复无常的家伙。\
**Yenisei**: Don't blame yourself, Madam. He appeared to be the unpredictable type.

**小叶尼塞**：您还能走吗？我们得快点追上去——\
**Yenisei**: Do you still have the strength to walk? We need to hurry up and go after him ...

别斯米尔挽住小叶尼塞的手臂，快步朝着凛冽的风声追去。\
Bessmert grabs Yenisei's arm and quickly chases after the piercing sound of the wind.

## NS-06 黄沙道 / The Yellow Sand Road

两足在与四足的追逐战中，一开始就落了下风。\
In the battle between two legs and four, they find themselves on the back foot from the beginning.

不必负重的斑纹马在草原上狂奔，巨鸟也在更远的空中逐渐缩小成一个断续变化的点。 早已疲倦的两人很快就因体力不支而被甩在后方。\
The burdenless horses gallop wildly as the giant bird flies further and further, leaving exhausted Bessmert and Yenisei far behind.

**小叶尼塞**：……呼……哈……\
**Yenisei**: *pants*

**小叶尼塞**：别斯米尔……女士……\
**Yenisei**: Madam ...

力气比先前在平原上时更快地从周身溜走。\
Their stamina slips away faster than it did before on the plains.

两人的行动愈发艰难，脚步也逐渐停滞。\
Their actions become increasingly labored, and their steps slow to a plodding halt.

**别斯米尔**：我们是向着河水上游跑吗？\
**Bessmert**: Are we going upstream?

**别斯米尔**：如果是上游，那么他要带猎物回到栖息地……难道、难道上游有森林？！\
**Bessmert**: If we are, he must be taking his preys back to his nest. Is-Is there a forest there?

**小叶尼塞**：对不起，女士，我的脑子——转不动。\
**Yenisei**: I'm sorry, Madam. I can't ... I can't think right now.

**小叶尼塞**：我的眼前……只有重影，什么也……看不清。\
**Yenisei**: I can't see ... anything. Only ... stars ...

**小叶尼塞**：……呼……\
**Yenisei**: *exhales*

女孩突然发现，自己再也拉不动年长者。\
The girl suddenly realizes that she can no longer pull Bessmert along.

一泄力，突然的停顿只让她陷入迷惑。\
With her energy dwindling, the sudden pause only leaves her more flustered.

**小叶尼塞**：唔……？\
**Yenisei**: Huh?

**小叶尼塞**：您为什么……呃……为什么停下了？\
**Yenisei**: Why ... *pants* ... Why stop?

**小叶尼塞**：呼，呼……\
**Yenisei**: *pants*

**别斯米尔**：……\
**Bessmert**: ...

**别斯米尔**：马的声音，就在前面。\
**Bessmert**: I hear horses, right in front of us.

**别斯米尔**：……还有许多人的声音。\
**Bessmert**: And people.

不仅是单纯的人声。\
And not just people.

市集的吵嚷，旋律的铮鸣，马车负重，滚轮碾地，土石上的踢踏声随之而来……\
The clamor of commerce, a melody in the trundling of carriages, rolling wheels on the ground, and the sound of footsteps on the soil and stones soon follow ...

无论那上面究竟是什么——\
No matter what lies ahead ...

**别斯米尔**：——不。上游不是森林。\
**Bessmert**: No. It's not a forest.

**小叶尼塞**：这些墙、这些人……我、我不明白，等等……难道是……\
**Yenisei**: There are walls and people ... I-I don't understand. Wait ... Could it be ...

——土石组成的坚硬城墙和结构前所未见的高耸门楼，将人影绰绰的热闹城镇囊括其中。\
Hard city walls made of earth and stone, and a soaring gate tower, the likes of which they have never seen before, encompass the bustling town and the vivid figures within.

大门洞开，行人往来，身着银盔的守卫伫立在城门的入口。\
The gate is opened wide. Pedestrians pass under it, as guards wearing silver armor stand at the entrance to the city.

**小叶尼塞**：……呃，这里是……补给站？\
**Yenisei**: Emm, is it ... a supply station?

**小叶尼塞**：……不，不是……\
**Yenisei**: No, no ...

**小叶尼塞**：我们——我们究竟在哪儿？！\
**Yenisei**: Where ... Where on earth are we?!

**别斯米尔**：孩子，现在我需要你告诉我，我们大概走到什么地方了。\
**Bessmert**: Child, please tell me where we are.

**别斯米尔**：我听不到沙蓬翻滚，但有一些其他的声响。我在想，我们是不是走到有人聚居的地方了？\
**Bessmert**: I can't hear the rustling of the sand rice anymore, but there are other noises. I'm thinking ... is this a settlement?

女孩晃了晃脑袋，没有马上回答别斯米尔的问题。\
The girl shakes her head, failing to answer Bessmert's question.

她从未见过，也因此对眼前的一切产生怀疑。\
Having never seen such a place before, she is naturally apprehensive of all that stands before her.

**小叶尼塞**：不是……至少，它看起来不像。它看起来不像任何我们见过的，那些城镇、村庄……\
**Yenisei**: No. At least it doesn't look like one. Not like any towns or villages we've seen.

**小叶尼塞**：我，我觉得我出现了幻觉。我看到——荒漠植被和黄色的城墙，还有城墙上木头做的阁楼。\
**Yenisei**: I-I think I'm seeing another illusion. I see a desert, some plants, and a wooden pavilion on the yellow walls.

**小叶尼塞**：阁楼的屋顶就像鸟的翅膀，城墙下面的那些人看上去也不一样——\
**Yenisei**: The roof of the pavilion looks like bird wings, and the people down the walls are quite different from us ...

**别斯米尔**：有城墙，也有人，是吗？那么城墙之后，就应该是城镇，这与我听到的人声环境一致，也许并不是你的幻觉。\
**Bessmert**: Walls and people, right? Only a city has walls around it. I also hear those noises. It's not an illusion.

**小叶尼塞**：不，请听我说，不是那样的。那些黄色的城墙和门，看上去根本不像真的！\
**Yenisei**: No, you don't understand. Those yellow walls and the gates don't look real at all!

**小叶尼塞**：我从来没见过这样的建筑，在土石城墙上建起阁楼，四角就像飞在半空里一样……\
**Yenisei**: I've never seen any buildings like this. A pavilion on the stone walls with four pointy tips around the roof. They seem to be flying in the mid-air ...

**别斯米尔**：听起来，也可能只是另一种文明的建筑方式。\
**Bessmert**: Perhaps it's just a foreign architectural style.

**小叶尼塞**：而且，就算这是城镇，我们也不可能走了那么远。除非——除非这是假的。\
**Yenisei**: Besides, we couldn't have gone far enough to reach a city, unless ... unless it's a fake one.

**小叶尼塞**：我们不能贸然过去。\
**Yenisei**: We must not go there rashly.

**别斯米尔**：但是，甚至早在前头的人声出现之前，我们就已经跟丢了那个巨鸟和尤利恩先生他们，只知道扇动翅膀的声音，最后出现在正南方。\
**Bessmert**: We've lost track of the giant bird and the others long before we heard the noises of this city. The last thing I can recall is that the flapping of the huge wings disappeared in the south.

女孩紧紧抓住了年长者的衣袖，她发觉事情正在滑向自己完全无法控制的方向。\
The girl tightly clasps Bessmert's sleeve, realizing that things are sliding in a direction beyond her control.

**别斯米尔**：而你眼前的城墙就在正南方，对吗？\
**Bessmert**: The city wall before you is also to the south, is it not?

别斯米尔安静地以面庞朝向小叶尼塞。即使对方知道那被布料遮住的眼睛看不清任何东西，这个动作也具备了凝视应有的力量。\
Bessmert quietly turns her face toward Yenisei. Even though the girl knows her eyes are covered by fabric and are unable to see a thing, this gesture still possesses the power of a gaze.

那种安抚、稳定，却同时代表了执着叩问的力量。\
A kind of soothing, stable, but at the same time questioning power.

**小叶尼塞**：您……您总是这样。您一定不会听我的意见了。\
**Yenisei**: Madam ... you are doing it again. You never listen to me.

**别斯米尔**：孩子，我们已经在这里了。\
**Bessmert**: Child, we are standing in the right place.

**别斯米尔**：并且尤利恩先生他们，极有可能是因为我们的选择，才遭受了这样的灾难。\
**Bessmert**: Behind these walls, our teammates might be suffering due to my misjudgment.

小叶尼塞沉默了。片刻后，她做出了一个决定。\
Yenisei pauses a brief moment, before she makes up her mind.

**小叶尼塞**：……城门的确开着，能看到里面的人影。\
**Yenisei**: The gate is open. I can see the people in the city.

**小叶尼塞**：可门口有守卫，拿着一些矛一样的冷兵器。最前面的那个人看起来……\
**Yenisei**: But there are guards patrolling around. They are holding some spear-like weapons, and the one in the front looks ...

**小叶尼塞**：和我们很不一样。\
**Yenisei**: Quite different from us.

**小叶尼塞**：即使我们想进去，他们也不一定能听懂我们说的话……还记得那些牧民吗？没有来自当地的翻译，通常很难沟通。\
**Yenisei**: I don't think they understand our language, even if we ask them to let us in ... Remember those herders? Almost impossible to communicate with them without an interpreter!

**别斯米尔**：……那就希望我们的“通关文书”能派上用场吧。\
**Bessmert**: Hope our "travel documents" can get us through that gate.

## NS-07 远来是客 / The Guests From Afar

据小叶尼塞描述，样貌奇特的守城者都穿着银色的盔甲，手中握有锐利的冷兵器。\
According to Yenisei's description, the peculiar-looking city defenders are all clad in silver armor and bear sharp weapons in their hands.

乍一听像中世纪的光景。由于已经从鄂木斯克一路过来，别斯米尔以为这样的守备力量比起她们顺利通过的那些严苛关隘，应该是不足看的。\
It sounds like a scene from the medieval era. Having passed every barrier smoothly all the way from Omsk, they think the garrison here is also a piece of cake.

但很显然，她们错了。\
But as it becomes clear, they are wrong to underestimate them.

即使双方都奇迹般地仍然能够听懂彼此语义，这里的关卡仍然死守严防。\
Even though both sides miraculously understand each other's words, the passes here are still well-guarded.

**小叶尼塞**：……\
**Yenisei**: ...

**城门郎**：请出示过所。\
**Gate Keeper**: Please show me your Pass.

**小叶尼塞**：我们所有的通行文书都已经给你了。\
**Yenisei**: You have all our documents.

**城门郎**：这不是过所。\
**Gate Keeper**: This is not a Pass.

**别斯米尔**：先生，文书就在您的手上，请再看看吧。\
**Bessmert**: Sir, you have the documents. Please, take a closer look at them.

**城门郎**：我不是先生。\
**Gate Keeper**: I'm not a Sir.

**城门郎**：烦请出示准确过所，上面会写清楚你从哪里来，要到哪里去。\
**Gate Keeper**: Please show me the right Pass, which shows where you come from and where you are going.

**小叶尼塞**：……如果我知道这个问题的答案，我就不会在这里了。\
**Yenisei**: I wouldn't have been here if I knew the answers.

**城门郎**：没有过所不能进城。\
**Gate Keeper**: No Pass, no entry.

问题似乎出在双方旗鼓相当的鸡同鸭讲身上。\
The problem seems to lie in both parties failing in the art of effective communication.

在毫无用处的嘴仗上“打得有来有回”，无疑浪费着所有人的时间。\
This bickering back and forth over useless technical pitfalls undoubtedly wastes everyone's time.

**别斯米尔**：唉。我认为这张通行证上都写得很清楚了。\
**Bessmert**: *sighs* I think it has been clearly stated on our documents.

**别斯米尔**：您瞧，协会印发的过关文书，在北边的周边关隘都适用，没有理由在您这里不行。\
**Bessmert**: The documents were issued by the association. They worked in all the borders in the North. What makes the difference here?

**城门郎**：它不行。我不知道你用这个经过了哪里的关卡，况且这上面的记录，无论文字还是印章都不合规制。\
**Gate Keeper**: It's not verified. I don't know which pass let you pass with this Pass, let alone the writing and the seal on it cannot be recognized.

**城门郎**：我不能放你们进去，这是玩忽职守。\
**Gate Keeper**: If I let you in, it would be my negligence.

**小叶尼塞**：能不能换个人来跟我们说？你听不懂我们的话。\
**Yenisei**: Can we talk to someone else? You don't understand what we are talking about.

**城门郎**：我明白你们在说什么。\
**Gate Keeper**: I understand every word you say.

**别斯米尔**：好吧，如果你的确能听懂，事情实际上是这样的，朋友。\
**Bessmert**: Very well, if you do, friend, this is what happened:

**别斯米尔**：我们的同伴被变成了马一样的动物，又被一个长着翅膀的人带走了。我们怀疑他们进了城，所以才需要进去找到他们。\
**Bessmert**: Our teammates were transformed into "horses" and taken away by a winged man. We think they might have been brought here, so we need to get into the city to find them.

**别斯米尔**：这很紧急，希望你能理解——\
