**Bessmert**: This is urgent. I hope you can understand ...

**城门郎**：我今日值守此门已逾三个时辰，从没见过什么长着翅膀的人。\
**Gate Keeper**: I've been on duty for over six hours. There was no such thing as a "winged man."

**城门郎**：编故事是无用的。像你们这样想要浑水摸鱼的家伙，我见过太多了。\
**Gate Keeper**: You can't fool me with your stupid story. I've seen too many of these little tricks.

**城门郎**：规矩就是，没有过所不能进城。\
**Gate Keeper**: The rule is, no Pass, no entry.

身着银盔的守城者无论从哪个角度打量都像是一堵铁墙。\
The defender in silver armor looks like a wall of iron from whichever angle he's seen.

小叶尼塞抬头，看到砖石之上木制的屋檐，往天空直直翘起，给地面投下一片阴影。她想起那只“巨鸟”，突然希望自己也生有翅膀。\
Yenisei looks up and sees the wooden eaves above the masonry, rising straight into the sky to cast a shadow over the ground. She remembers the "giant bird" and suddenly wishes she too had wings.

**小叶尼塞**：……好吧，看来这家伙是听得懂，但听不进去。\
**Yenisei**: Fine. This man understands our language, but he won't buy it.

**别斯米尔**：小叶尼塞？\
**Bessmert**: Yeni?

可惜她没有翅膀，只能尝试一些别的办法。\
Unfortunately, she doesn't have wings, and so she must find some other way to deal with their predicament.

**小叶尼塞**：我要试试，没有你说的这东西，究竟能不能进去。\
**Yenisei**: Then I'll see if we can make it in without this Pass.

**城门郎**：……你们要强行闯关？这是不自量力。\
**Gate Keeper**: Trying to break in? You're overestimating yourself.

**小叶尼塞**：我只是要试一试，因为我们也没有别的办法了，先生。\
**Yenisei**: Just trying, because we are not given any choices, Sir.

**别斯米尔**：等等，小叶尼塞——！\
**Bessmert**: Wait, Yenisei ...!

玻璃瓶逐个空掉，小叶尼塞身上能用的“武器”已经很快见底。\
Emptying the glass bottles one by one, Yenisei's "weapons" are quickly depleted.

两人对面，一堵干燥的铁墙变成了一堵湿淋淋的铁墙。\
Across from them, the dry iron wall—the poor guard—has become a wet iron wall.

**城门郎**：——\
**Gate Keeper**: ...

**城门郎**：——报——有人正试图强行闯入——\
**Gate Keeper**: Warning! Intruders!

**城门郎**：关城门——！\
**Gate Keeper**: Close the gate!!

城门墙楼上的卫兵立即响应，极富节奏地奔跑起来。\
The guards on the wall above the city gates respond in a quick and rhythmic step.

下方，城门内的脚步声蹭动沙地，门上沉重的缆索被规整而迅速地收绞，在手中挽紧，只等一声令下。\
Below, those within the city gates scuff the sand, as the gates' heavy cables are twisted in reply, held tightly in expectant hands awaiting their next command.

**别斯米尔**：他们要关门了！\
**Bessmert**: They are closing the gate!

**别斯米尔**：糟了，我们、我们得进去，否则再也找不到尤利恩先生他们了！我们不能把他们丢在里面——\
**Bessmert**: This is bad! We, we have to get in, or how are we going to get them back? We can't just leave them here ...

**别斯米尔**：还有、还有那些“度朔节”与东方神秘术的线索……\
**Bessmert**: Neither can I just turn away from the clues to the Dùshuò Festival and the mysterious Eastern arcane power ...

**别斯米尔**：先生，我请求您！\
**Bessmert**: Sir, I beg of you!

别斯米尔冲上前去，试图以一己之力拉住正在后退的守卫与缓缓关闭的城门。\
Bessmert rushes forward, attempting to pull back the guards and city gates with all her might.

可她什么也看不见，当然也发现不了不平的沙土道路上隐藏的危险。\
But her lack of sight impedes her, unable to detect the hidden dangers on the uneven, packed-sand road.

——一颗石头也足以绊倒她，令她摔下去，甚至一时之间难以再次爬起。\
—A loose stone is enough to trip her, and despite the demands of the moment, it takes her time to get back up again.

**城门郎**：……不要上前了。\
**Gate Keeper**: Don't get any closer.

**小叶尼塞**：别斯米尔女士！您怎么样了！\
**Yenisei**: Madam! Are you alright?!

她着急地搀扶起别斯米尔，另一只手，紧紧攥着那枚空掉的玻璃瓶。\
She anxiously helps Bessmert to her feet, with her other hand tightly gripping an empty glass bottle.

这一路上经历的不可测的事故已数不胜数，足以撰写出一部荒诞的冒险小说，更足以击倒任何一位经验丰富探险家的意志。\
They've had countless unpredictable mishaps along the way, enough to write an adventure story few would believe, and experienced more than enough to exhaust the will of any explorer.

也许，就这样任由城门关闭，的确是更为妥当与安全的做法。\
Perhaps simply allowing the city gates to close is a safer and more appropriate approach.

**小叶尼塞**：女士，我们或许真的该放弃了……我甚至怀疑，这一切是否只是一场可耻的幻觉。\
**Yenisei**: Maybe we should just give up, Madam ... I'm even thinking if all these things we've been through are just illusions.

**小叶尼塞**：那些怪异的地貌，那些变成斑纹马的队友，还有眼前这、这些……\
**Yenisei**: The unusual terrains, the teammates turned into striped horses, and now this nonsense ...

**小叶尼塞**：我不能眼睁睁地看着您用自己的安危去冒险……！\
**Yenisei**: I won't let you go in there and risk your life!

别斯米尔看不见对方的表情，却能从声音中读出那种犹豫。于是她挣扎着起身。\
Bessmert cannot see her companion's expression, but can hear the hesitation in her voice. It proves enough to add to her struggle to get up again.

**别斯米尔**：不，恰恰相反，我的孩子。\
**Bessmert**: No, on the contrary, child.

**别斯米尔**：这些闻所未闻的风土人情，距离我们所追寻的东西已经非常接近了——那些我们生来便要追寻的新奇而伟大的事物。\
**Bessmert**: The unknown people, the uncharted city ... We are very close to what we've been chasing. We were born to run after these exciting and amazing things.

**别斯米尔**：而且，你不也有问题，期望着“所求必应”能够给出答案吗？\
**Bessmert**: You're also looking for an answer from Ask and Acquire, right?

**别斯米尔**：更不必说还有尤利恩先生他们不明的去向……与这些相比，我们的安全简直不值一提。\
**Bessmert**: Besides, we have no idea how Mr. Jurien and the others are doing ... There is more to consider other than our own safety.

**？？？**：说得好。若论安全……\
**???**: Well said. Speaking of which ...

**？？？**：城内应比城外安全许多。我可以向两位保证。\
**???**: The city is much safer than the wild. You have my word.

**里正**：至于我……我在这城中最大的金市任里正一职，两位称呼我为里正即可。\
**Lizheng**: As for me, I am the Lǐzhèng of the biggest merchants hub in this city. You can address me by my title. *Lǐzhèng: A low-ranking government official responsible for taxation and household registrations.

**小叶尼塞**：里正……？\
**Yenisei**: Lǐzhèng ...?

**别斯米尔**：听起来是一位体面的先生。\
**Bessmert**: He sounds like a decent gentleman.

**城门郎**：里正，这两人要强行冲关入城。\
**Gate Keeper**: Lǐzhèng, they are the intruders!

**里正**：我已知悉，情况可控，不必关城门了。这两位似是胡商，正在我职责范围之内。\
**Lizheng**: Noted. The situation is under control. No need to close the gate. The ladies look like foreign merchants. Their business is within my purview.

**里正**：况且正值节日，亦或许只是前来参加庆典的人。不必如此严苛。\
**Lizheng**: Besides, it's holiday time. They could be here for the celebration. Don't be so harsh on them.

**城门郎**：……喏。\
**Gate Keeper**: Understood.

守城者把两只手往身前一抱，做了个小叶尼塞看不懂的手势，就退回一边了。\
The guard holds his hands in front of him and makes a gesture that Yenisei cannot understand before retreating to one side.

似是厄运散去，小叶尼塞与别斯米尔心中重新燃起了微微的期望。\
A glimmer of expectation is reignited in the hearts of Yenisei and Bessmert, as if their misfortune might have at last dissipated.

**里正**：我瞧两位，似乎丢了过所文书？\
**Lizheng**: If I'm correct, you have lost your Pass, right?

**别斯米尔**：我们有文书，只是好像不能在这里使用。\
**Bessmert**: We do have a Pass, but it seems it doesn't work here.

**里正**：远道而来，难免错漏。\
**Lizheng**: Well, just an understandable mistake for people from afar.

**里正**：不过，即使两位来此或为经商，或为度朔节，这缺了过所，却仍是麻烦。\
**Lizheng**: However, either for business or the Dùshuò Festival, it is troublesome without a proper Pass.

**别斯米尔**：度朔节？您是说，现在就是度朔节期间吗？\
**Bessmert**: Dùshuò Festival? Is it taking place now?

**里正**：正是？我还以为你们是清楚这一点，才来到沛城。\
**Lizheng**: That's what I said. I thought that is why you're here in Pèi City.

**别斯米尔**：啊，是的！我们知道，但我们从来没有真正参与过，所以不了解，也不确定。\
**Bessmert**: Uh, yes! We were told of it, but we've never been to one. We are not sure.

**别斯米尔**：我们只是听过这个传说。\
**Bessmert**: We all heard of the legend about it.

**里正**：哦？度朔节，难道在你们的部族当中被当作童谣传唱了？\
**Lizheng**: Hmm. So, is the festival sung as a nursery rhyme in your tribe?

**别斯米尔**：啊，“部族”。不是那样的，我们来自……北方。\
**Bessmert**: Uh, "tribe"? We are not tribal people. We come from the North.

**里正**：北人？我还以为，两位都是西边乌孙族的后人。\
**Lizheng**: Northerners? Oh, I mistook you for the descendants of the Wūsūn from the westward.

**里正**：我听闻他们早已失落于折罗漫关外，此前都无人得见……加之你们的服饰也相当奇特，这才贸然猜测了，实在抱歉。\
**Lizheng**: It is said that they have migrated outside the Zhéluómàn Mountain. No one has ever met them until now. Your clothes also have a unique style. I should apologize for my mistake.

**里正**：况且，您的同伴红发碧眼，貌色白皙，恰好符合史书上的记载……\
**Lizheng**: What's more, this lady by your side has red hair, green eyes, and a fair complexion. The features match the records in history books ...

**别斯米尔**：史书？里正先生，你们的史书上——\
**Bessmert**: History books? Mr. Lǐzhèng, in your history books, do you have ...

**里正**：我说过了，称我为“里正”即可。\
**Lizheng**: Like I said, you may just call me Lǐzhèng.

**里正**：书中有言：“乌孙于西域诸戎其形最异。今之胡人青眼、赤须，状类猕猴者，本其种也。”\
**Lizheng**: The book says, "Wūsūn, one of the tribes in the Western Regions, has the most unusual appearance. The present foreigners are their descendants with features of green eyes, red hair, and the looks of macaque monkeys."

**小叶尼塞**：猴、猴子吗……\
**Yenisei**: M-Monkeys ...

**里正**：哈哈……或许书中所言也不可尽信，两位听过便罢。\
**Lizheng**: Heh heh ... Maybe we can't believe every word in the book. No matter.

**里正**：至于先前，我们说到何处了？是否……\
**Lizheng**: Where were we just now? Was it ...

**别斯米尔**：度朔节。我们是为度朔节来的。\
**Bessmert**: Dùshuò Festival. We are here for the festival.

**里正**：哦，正是！\
**Lizheng**: Oh, right. Exactly!

眼前老者貌似兴致盎然，双手一合就拾起了刚才的话题。\
The old man in front of her seems to be full of interest, and with his hands clasped, he resumes his topic.

**里正**：沛城度朔节的氛围与仪典，曾经最鼎盛时，每年都能吸引许多不远万里赶来的人。\
**Lizheng**: The Pèi City is famous for its grand celebration and joyful spirit during the festival. It attracts countless travelers from far away every year.

**里正**：想必两位自北而来，路途遥远，亦是如此。辛苦了。\
**Lizheng**: I could only imagine how hard it was for you to arrive here. Well done.

**里正**：不过，我尚有最后一问。你这眼，是双目皆盲？\
**Lizheng**: However, forgive me for being offensive. It seems you have lost sight in both eyes ...?

**别斯米尔**：嗯，您说的没错……请问，这会有什么影响吗？\
**Bessmert**: Yes. Would that be a problem?

**里正**：对缺少过所文书的旅人来说，身有疾残或许并非坏事。\
**Lizheng**: Under this city's caring policy, you have the privilege of traveling without a Pass.

**里正**：今日当值的城门郎新才到任，或有冒犯之处，还请两位海涵。\
**Lizheng**: The gate guard is new here. I sincerely apologize for his offense.

他微微鞠躬，略表歉意，将二人向城内引去。\
He bows slightly, implying a subtle apology, and leads the two toward the city proper.

**里正**：这便随我来吧，逗留城外并不安全。\
**Lizheng**: Come, follow me. It's not safe to stay outside of the city.

**里正**：最近人口失踪案频发，须得四方走动巡查，才能确保不会有人因被拦在门外而失踪。\
**Lizheng**: There have been many missing persons cases recently. We intensified the patrol, in case someone is blocked out of the city and goes missing.

**小叶尼塞**：失踪案……\
**Yenisei**: Missing persons cases ...

更多交谈的话题间，两人跟随里正的指引，身影没入城门之中。\
Between further topics of conversation, the two follow Lǐzhèng's guidance and, at last, pass through the city gates.

## NS-08 十万个问答 / Questions and Answers

里正引着两人登上城墙，来到阁楼中的一处内室。\
Lǐzhèng leads the two of them up the city wall to a connected inner chamber.

小叶尼塞一路都怀揣着下一步就将踏空的不真实感，直到进入房间之内才放下心来。\
Yenisei cannot shake the notion that her next step will land on thin air, until they at last enter the room, and she can let go.

即使与先前城外的景象全然不同，这短暂路途也足以使人印象再度深刻。\
From the city gate to the room, the scenery is completely different from outside the city. Though it's a short distance, she is very impressed.

**小叶尼塞**：……请问……\
**Yenisei**: Emm ...

**里正**：都先坐下来吧。\
**Lizheng**: Have a seat.

**别斯米尔**：好。\
**Bessmert**: Thank you.

**小叶尼塞**：女士，在这边。\
**Yenisei**: Here, Madam.

**别斯米尔**：我没有摸到座椅，要怎么……\
**Bessmert**: I don't feel any chairs around me. How am I going to ...

**小叶尼塞**：似乎是跪坐的方式。来，这里有软垫。\
**Yenisei**: It seems the people here sit on their heels. Here, cushion.

**里正**：两位随心坐下即可。\
**Lizheng**: Just make yourself comfortable.

两人磕磕绊绊地学着老者的样子，在矮桌边跪坐下来。\
The two of them hobble onward, imitating the old man's unfamiliar posture as he kneels down beside a low table.

**里正**：小娘子面色好些了。方才想问什么？\
**Lizheng**: You ladies look better now. What were you going to ask?

疑问自然有很多。不过最先溜出口的，却是这样一句冷不丁的话。\
There are many fears and doubts in their hearts that beg expression. However, the first to break the silence is nothing more than an odd query.

**小叶尼塞**：我想问，你们的城墙……难道不会塌下来吗？\
**Yenisei**: Your walls ... Won't they collapse?

**里正**：嗯？为什么这么说？\
**Lizheng**: Hmm? Why do you think that?

**小叶尼塞**：因为，我看见城墙似乎是黄色的纯土石结构。它们应该经不起雨水冲刷和大风侵蚀……\
**Yenisei**: Because they seem to be made of only earth and stone. I don't think these materials can stand the weathering ...

**小叶尼塞**：更不用说，上面还有用木头架起来的阁楼。\
**Yenisei**: Not to mention the wooden pavilion on the walls.

**里正**：哈哈。你独见其外，不知其中木桩已沉沉嵌入大地，土石仅为依凭与外壳。无需担忧，即使墙砖剥落，它也存在久矣，与整座城的年岁相仿。\
**Lizheng**: Haha. You draw the conclusion only by its appearance. In fact, the stakes are deeply driven into the ground and stand firmly. No need to worry about the peeling bricks and clay. It's just the sign of the city's longevity.

**小叶尼塞**：与整座城的年岁相仿……那这座城，存在多久了？\
**Yenisei**: The city's longevity. So how old is this city?

**里正**：据我所知，数百年。县志占据了书库的一整片书架，十载为一本，数百年是一个比实际更轻描淡写的概括。\
**Lizheng**: As I recall, hundreds of years. Its annals take up most of the library. Each volume records a decade. Considering the large quantity, "hundreds" may not be the best quantifier.

**里正**：城中多有历史遗迹，或许之后可带令慈前去游赏。\
**Lizheng**: There are many historical sites in the city. You may take your mother for a sight tour.

**小叶尼塞**：别斯米尔女士不是我的母亲。\
**Yenisei**: Madam Bessmert is not my mother.

**里正**：别女士——？哦，抱歉。我还忘了她的眼疾。\
**Lizheng**: Ms. Be- ... Oh, I apologize. I forgot about her sight ...

话语间，里正下意识朝别斯米尔所在的方向投去饱含歉意的一眼。\
Between his words, Lǐzhèng instinctively casts an apologetic glance in Bessmert's direction.

她看不见，但似有所感，转过头来。\
Though she cannot see, she seems to feel something and turns her head towards his voice.

**别斯米尔**：没关系。也许是因为我看上去行动太过自如，人们常常忽略这一点。\
**Bessmert**: That's alright. People often mistake me for having good eyesight because I walk around freely like others.

**里正**：宽心些，此事亦有好的一面。即使你行动无碍，我们依然会施以援手。\
**Lizheng**: The silver lining is, we have a caring policy in this regard. We're here to help, whether you need assistance or not.

**别斯米尔**：我可以问一下，这是为什么吗？对于我是盲人这件事，你们似乎很在意。\
**Bessmert**: You keep talking about my eyesight. May I ask why?

**里正**：双目失明为笃疾，残疾者受官府庇护。北人没有这样的惯例么？\
**Lizheng**: The government is obliged to provide help to people with severe impairments, including those who have lost their sights in both eyes. Isn't it the same with the Northerners?

**里正**：啊，这问题若令你感到冒犯——\
**Lizheng**: Oh, if my question is offensive ...

**别斯米尔**：不，这很好。不如说，相当好……\
**Bessmert**: No. That's fine. More than fine, actually ...

**别斯米尔**：在北方，我需要付出更多才能得到和寻常人一样的待遇。\
**Bessmert**: In the North, I have to do more to be treated like an ordinary person.

**里正**：竟是如此……北边弱肉强食，我有所耳闻。却不成想连疾残者也得不到应有庇护。\
**Lizheng**: I see. I've heard that people in the North idolize the strong and pay little attention to the weak. Little did I know the disabled enjoy no privilege.

**里正**：既然今日，你们已经来到沛城，就放下心来吧。\
**Lizheng**: But now you're here with us in Pèi City. Please rest at ease.

**里正**：而且，两位的汉话听起来十分流利，这会令你们在城中方便许多。\
**Lizheng**: Moreover, you speak fluent Hanese. I'm sure your stay here will go swimmingly.

**小叶尼塞**：……！您指的是，我们现在说的正是“汉话”么？\
**Yenisei**: ...! You mean we are speaking the "Hanese" right now?

小叶尼塞感到自己的手被别斯米尔轻轻按了一下。\
Yenisei feels her hand being pressed lightly by Bessmert's own.

**里正**：自然？小娘子此言，倒是当真有趣。在金市记册中，言语流利的胡人多数都在中原生活已久。\
**Lizheng**: Are you not? It's interesting you ask. According to the records of the hub, most of the foreign merchants with fluent Hanese have lived a long time in the Central Plains. *Central Plains: the name given to China by the ancient Chinese.

**里正**：而你们看上去，显然并非如此。并且也没有频繁地出入中原，否则——\
**Lizheng**: While you are obviously not one of them, neither have you paid frequent visits here, otherwise ...

**里正**：就不会连过所也忘记了。\
**Lizheng**: You wouldn't have forgotten a proper Pass.

这句不知是否别有深意的玩笑话，令别斯米尔的心头一惊。\
This somewhat insightful witticism surprises Bessmert.

**别斯米尔**：我得说，您猜得没错。\
**Bessmert**: You're a man of sharp wit, I have to say.

**别斯米尔**：我们在家乡时，常年与那些会讲“汉话”的商人打交道。正如您说的那样，他们总是日夜兼程，穿梭于不同的城乡之间。\
**Bessmert**: Back where we are from, merchants come and go, including those who speak your tongue. We've dealt with them a lot throughout the years.

**别斯米尔**：如果不是有他们分享给我们的经验，像我们这样首次出行的商队，恐怕还会遭遇更大的危机。\
**Bessmert**: If it weren't for their advice, we wouldn't have made it this far on our first journey as a new caravan.

**里正**：嗯。胡商见多识广，沛城也一向乐于与他们贸易往来。哦，对了，金市之中有些胡商，若无落脚处，也可去那边寻个旅店……\
**Lizheng**: I see. Foreign merchants are well-informed and welcomed by the citizens in Pèi City. Oh, there are other foreign merchants in the hub. If you have no place to stay, the caravanserai there might be a good choice ...

话语间，里正从厚实的书简纸堆中取出了其中一张。\
As he speaks, Lǐzhèng takes out a sheet of paper from a large stack.

**里正**：那么，还需此物。两位需备齐此类过所文书，以作身份证明。\
**Lizheng**: Take this with you. It is the Pass to verify your identities.

**里正**：由此才好在城中行走，否则，仍有可能被驱逐出去。\
**Lizheng**: You can enjoy your stay here with it, or you might end up being expelled.

**别斯米尔**：好的，那请问我们要怎么……\
**Bessmert**: Thank you. Then how are we going to ...

**里正**：请两位将现下携有的文书予我一观。\
**Lizheng**: Please show me the documents you have now.

**别斯米尔**：没问题，让我翻翻那东西在哪儿……\
**Bessmert**: Certainly. Let me just ...

**小叶尼塞**：在我这里。一直都在我这里，女士。\
**Yenisei**: I have them. I always have them with me, Madam.

**别斯米尔**：噢，可靠的好孩子。\
**Bessmert**: Oh. Thank you. You are reliable as always, child.

她们递去一份牛皮纸信封袋装着的文书。\
They hand over a document in a brown paper envelope.

**里正**：好，我来看看。\
**Lizheng**: Thank you. I will take a look.

**里正**：稍等。\
**Lizheng**: Hold on a second.

**里正**：……\
**Lizheng**: ...

“文书”之上，除开一枚图样红章能勉强看出用途以外，剩下的表述性字迹都像鬼画符一般，句句之间首尾相连，仓促而不留一丝空隙。\
On this "document," besides a drawn red seal that roughly illustrates its purpose, the remaining descriptive handwriting looks like scrawled symbols, with the beginnings and ends of sentences connected hastily without leaving any gaps.

这实在有些令人为难。\
The embarrassment between reader and writer grows like a bubble waiting to pop.

**里正**：呃……\
**Lizheng**: Er ...

**里正**：它们看起来像突厥文。这是突厥文吗？\
**Lizheng**: Looks like it's written in Turkic. Is it Turkic?

**小叶尼塞**：什么？不——\
**Yenisei**: What? No ...

年长的女性抢在小叶尼塞能够说完之前有了动作。她拍拍女孩的背，示意下面由自己来说。\
Bessmert makes a move before Yenisei finishes speaking. She pats the girl's back and gestures for her to allow her to explain.

尽管疑惑，女孩还是习惯性地听从了。\
Despite her doubts, the girl habitually follows her lead.

**别斯米尔**：是的，可以说它是突厥文。我们北方也使用这种文字。\
**Bessmert**: Yes, a variation of it. This is the written language in the North.

**小叶尼塞**：……\
**Yenisei**: ...

**别斯米尔**：孩子，这是你家乡的文字，也叫叶尼塞文，不是吗？\
**Bessmert**: Yeni, this is the written language in your hometown, also known as Yeniseic, isn't it?

小叶尼塞怀疑自己是否真的看见对方眨了两下眼睛，毕竟那是被遮住的部分。\
Yenisei is almost certain that her companion is winking at her, despite her eyes being covered.

又或许只是一种感应和提醒，她随即福至心灵地意识到。在目前尚且不明状况的险境中，也许她需要学会迅速接受这些偶尔的谎言。\
Or perhaps it is just her own intuition prompting her. She realizes then, in a moment of enlightenment, that in their precarious situation, she may well need to learn how to quickly accommodate these occasional lies.

**小叶尼塞**：……哦，是的。没错。\
**Yenisei**: Oh, yes. That's right.

**别斯米尔**：抱歉，我们应该考虑到这种文字在“中原”不那么常见。\
**Bessmert**: My apologies. I should have known that our language is a rare kind in the Central Plains.

**里正**：我了解了。无妨，只是需得两位自己写出来历了。\
**Lizheng**: I understand. It's alright, but I'm afraid you have to write it down yourself, including where you came from.

**里正**：具体行文，参见此书。\
**Lizheng**: Please take this file as a reference.

**小叶尼塞**：好的，我来写。\
**Yenisei**: Thank you. I'll do it.

**小叶尼塞**：……\
**Yenisei**: ...

**小叶尼塞**：呃，不好意思，我好像也不认识这上面的字。\
**Yenisei**: Emm, sorry, but I don't think I can read it.

**里正**：嗯？\
**Lizheng**: Hmm?

**里正**：哦，是我考虑不周。汉话读写，的确比听说更困难。\
**Lizheng**: Oh, my mistake. I should have realized the paper work is much harder than oral communication.

**里正**：小童今日不在……\
**Lizheng**: But the servant is not here today ...

**里正**：既如此，那便你们说，我来写，例如……此处。两位入城，所为何事？\
**Lizheng**: Alright, you can tell me, and I'll write it down. Like ... this one. What did you come to the city for?

**别斯米尔**：经商。\
**Bessmert**: For business.

**里正**：商队几人？\
**Lizheng**: How many of you are there in the team?

**别斯米尔**：算我们在内，七个人。\
**Bessmert**: Seven, including us.

**小叶尼塞**：原本有七个人。\
**Yenisei**: There WERE seven of us.

**里正**：原本？他们现在何处？\
**Lizheng**: Were? Where are they now?

**别斯米尔**：这也是我们想要知道的。\
**Bessmert**: This is also what we are trying to find out.

**别斯米尔**：在来到这里的路上，他们变成了马一样的动物，然后被一只巨鸟带走了。\
**Bessmert**: On our way here, they were transformed into "horses" and taken away by a giant bird.

**里正**：被变成了马？这……那两位如何幸免于难？\
**Lizheng**: Transformed into horses? Um ... Then how come you didn't get transformed?

**小叶尼塞**：我不知道。也许因为别斯米尔女士与我是神秘学家，而他们是人类。\
**Yenisei**: We have no idea. Perhaps because Madam Bessmert and I are arcanists, while the others are humans.

**里正**：何出此言？\
**Lizheng**: What do you mean?

**里正**：难道巨鸟只袭击人类？可他又如何分辨呢？\
**Lizheng**: Does the giant bird only attack humans? Then how does he identify them?

**里正**：毕竟，人类与神秘学家并无太大分别。\
**Lizheng**: There is no huge difference between humans and arcanists, after all.

**小叶尼塞**：什么？这……\
**Yenisei**: What? Emm ...

**别斯米尔**：……没有太大区别？\
**Bessmert**: No huge difference?

这是她们从未设想过的回答。\
This is an answer they had never considered before.

或者说，能这样自然以为的前提，在两人的认知中，从未存在。\
Or rather, it was a premise that seemed so distant to their own views that it defied being considered.

钻石与泥土如何等同？人类与神秘学家又如何等同？\
As if saying a diamond was no different from a clump of soil.

**里正**：怎么？\
**Lizheng**: Is that a problem?

**别斯米尔**：不，没事。\
**Bessmert**: No, not at all.

**别斯米尔**：先不论……神秘学家与人类的区别。\
**Bessmert**: Let's go back to the difference between humans and arcanists later.

**别斯米尔**：我认为，问题也有可能出在水上。\
**Bessmert**: My guess is, there might be something wrong with the water.

**别斯米尔**：穿越草原时，我们发现了一条活水河流。当时其他人由于长途跋涉的疲累，在我们发现异常之前，就喝下了那条河中的水。\
**Bessmert**: We found a river when crossing the steppe. Our teammates were too thirsty and drank the water in haste. Then we realized something was wrong.

**小叶尼塞**：是的，那是一条在草原上自西北方延伸出来的河。流量不大，但很清澈。\
**Yenisei**: Yes. It came from the northwest. Not a big one, but quite clean.

**里正**：你们所见的河流，也许是我们的母亲河，沛霖川。\
**Lizheng**: That might be the main river of Pèi City, called Pèilín River.

**里正**：但近来她已经濒临枯竭，也不会导致这般变化……那巨鸟长什么模样？\
**Lizheng**: But it has been shrinking these past years. Also, there are no cases of people drinking it and turning into horses ... What were the features of that giant bird?

**小叶尼塞**：黑色或棕色的翅膀，红色的尾羽。面目像人。\
**Yenisei**: He has black or brown wings, red tail feathers, and a man's face.

**别斯米尔**：还有，在我的回忆中，那位巨鸟具有青年男子的嗓音。\
**Bessmert**: Also, as I recall it, he has the voice of a young man.

**里正**：人面鸟身，那么，便是羽人。他能否奏乐？\
**Lizheng**: A giant bird with a man's face. A feather man. Did he play a musical instrument?

**小叶尼塞**：他使用一种能发出声音的长条形乐器，还能用那乐器奏乐来控制动物随它前进。\
**Yenisei**: He played a stick-like instrument. His music could lead the horses to where he went.

**里正**：他是否还带着像骨头的短杖？\
**Lizheng**: Was there a bone-like wand with him?

**小叶尼塞**：有相似的东西，但我不确定。当时他与我们的距离实在是太远了。\
**Yenisei**: Could be, but I'm not sure. He was so far away from us.

**里正**：既如此，我大约知晓这羽人身份了。\
**Lizheng**: I have a rough idea now.

**里正**：……\
**Lizheng**: ...

**里正**：若真如我所想，即使他本就并非“祥瑞”，这也实在——唉！\
**Lizheng**: If that's what I think it is, even though he is not a Xiángruì, I have to say ... *sighs*

他似乎感到万分遗憾。\
He seems to be overcome with regret.

别斯米尔轻轻地调整跪坐的姿势。她敏锐地感知到，新的进展似乎出现了。\
Bessmert demurely adjusts her kneeling position, keenly sensing a new development.

**别斯米尔**：听起来，似乎还发生过什么事情。\
**Bessmert**: Sounds like something happened when you last met.

**里正**：你们所见巨鸟，或为我们城中所传的羽人。他曾被城中少许居民视为“祥瑞”，皆因其大致身形，与传说中的句芒相似。\
**Lizheng**: The giant bird, or the feather man, as we say, was considered the Xiángruì by some citizens. It is because he looks like the legendary Gōumáng.

**别斯米尔**：“祥瑞”是一种类似“保护神”的存在吗？\
**Bessmert**: What is this Xiángruì? Is it some kind of guardian?

**里正**：不，并非如此。“祥瑞”多为妖类，但常与人为善，施术解难，福佑天地。\
**Lizheng**: Not exactly. In most cases, Xiángruì is just Yāo, but in the good way. They are benevolent, using their power to help people and bless the area.

**里正**：在你们来报之前，城中亦有人侧面目击过持有骨杖的羽人。据传他曾将动物牵引至职祠，声称所带动物实则为人所变。\
**Lizheng**: Before your report, there was someone else witnessing a feather man with a bone wand. He once brought some animals to the Zhící and claimed they were transformed from humans.

**别斯米尔**：这……这和我们同伴的遭遇，是一样的。\
**Bessmert**: This ... this is exactly what happened to our teammates.

**里正**：假使确为同一人所为，那便足以怀疑他与城内失踪案有关了。\
**Lizheng**: If these two are the same feather man, then he is very likely involved in these missing persons cases.

**小叶尼塞**：原来之前说的失踪案……是这件事。\
**Yenisei**: Oh, the cases you mentioned ... I see.

**里正**：可惜，我们那位侧面目击者，甚至无法凭记忆给出一张画像，此后也无人佐证她的说法，自然被当作是胡言乱语了。\
**Lizheng**: Too bad, that witness couldn't remember anything, even the slightest feature, for us to draw a picture. Since no one could provide other evidence, her word was considered nonsense.

**里正**：为此，法曹甚至以为她中了邪，建议她趁节日回乡歇去。\
**Lizheng**: The Fǎcáo thought she was "possessed" and suggested she take a break in her hometown during the holiday.

**别斯米尔**：我们还能找到她吗？\
**Bessmert**: We want to pay her a visit. Will she come back?

里正摆了摆手。好不容易找到的线索，显然是断了。\
Lǐzhèng waves his hand. There is little value to be gleamed from such a faulty clue.

**里正**：她是于职祠工作的执礼，虽非官府要人，可这年节里也不能出现这样的差错。现下是其他人在职祠帮忙。\
**Lizheng**: I'm afraid not. She worked as the Zhílǐ in the Zhící. It's not a crucial position, but clearly not suitable for a possessed person. There is someone filling in for her now.

小叶尼塞捏紧了膝上的布料。她总是像个执行命令的士兵般执着，而这次也是一样。\
Yenisei grips the fabric on her knee. She is as persistent as a soldier when executing orders, and this time is no different.

**小叶尼塞**：如果，如果——我还能给出羽人的画像呢？\
**Yenisei**: What if ... What if I can offer a drawing of the feather man?

**小叶尼塞**：虽然他当时飞在半空，看不清细节，只记得廓形和翅膀的颜色。但我学过素描！而且有画地图的经验。\
**Yenisei**: He was far away in mid-air at the time. I couldn't see the details, but I remember his outline and the color of his wings. Besides, I have experience in making sketches and maps.

**小叶尼塞**：我能画出来。\
**Yenisei**: I can totally make a drawing of him.

**里正**：素描？地图……唔……即使你能画出来，我们也只能暂且发令通缉，捉不得他下狱。一切还需得等到当庭对质才行。\
**Lizheng**: Sketch? Map? Hmm ... But we can only attach your drawing to the wanted poster for the moment. We can't put him in prison without solid evidence. Everything is yet to be confirmed by the court.

**里正**：不过，既然你能画，便试试吧。\
**Lizheng**: But a drawing is better than nothing. Please give it a try.

**里正**：此处有毛笔与砚台。请。\
**Lizheng**: Here is the brush and the ink. Help yourself.

小叶尼塞靠近桌前，拿起刚才里正记录用过的笔状物。\
Yenisei approaches the table and picks up the brush that was used to write just moments ago.

**小叶尼塞**：这是刚才您用的那种很长的笔，对吗？\
**Yenisei**: This is the same long pen you just used?

**里正**：是。\
**Lizheng**: That's right.

**小叶尼塞**：这上面的，就是墨水？可我似乎蘸不起来。\
**Yenisei**: And this is ... the ink? But it won't adhere to the pen.

**里正**：……墨需得新研后蘸取。罢了，我来替你研磨，你尽管画。\
**Lizheng**: To get the liquid ink, you need to rub the ink stick on the ink stone first. It's fine. I'll rub it for you. You can focus on the drawing.

老人挽起袖口，利落地研出一些墨汁来，让小叶尼塞能够蘸取。\
The old man rolls up his sleeves and deftly grinds out some ink for Yenisei to dip the brush in.

而女孩落笔确实也毫不迟疑——\
And the girl does not hesitate to write—

**小叶尼塞**：咦？这个笔落在纸上，笔迹怎么这么粗……\
**Yenisei**: Huh? The lines it draws are really heavy ...

**小叶尼塞**：而且这个墨水，只有黑色吗？\
**Yenisei**: And do we only have the black ink?

**里正**：……\
**Lizheng**: ...

**里正**：不，旁的颜色也是有的。\
**Lizheng**: No, there are different colors.

**小叶尼塞**：红色可以吗？\
**Yenisei**: May I have the red one?

**里正**：……稍等，我去取。\
**Lizheng**: Please hold on. I'll get it for you.

缓慢而稳定的脚步声逐渐远离。\
The slow and steady footsteps gradually move away.

## NS-09 街市狂澜 / Chaos on Streets

**里正**：如此甚好。有这画像，我们尽可以通缉羽人了。\
**Lizheng**: This is great. With your drawing, we can issue wanted posters to find the feather man.

**小叶尼塞**：……\
**Yenisei**: ...

**里正**：小娘子沉默不语，可是还有其他顾虑？\
**Lizheng**: You stay silent. Any questions or concerns?

**小叶尼塞**：您先前，提到职祠有一位已经离开的工作人员……或者说，“执礼”？\
**Yenisei**: You mentioned a former employee of the Zhící ... Or should I call her the Zhílǐ?

**小叶尼塞**：您说那位执礼曾经见到了羽人，和他带来的动物。那也许他今天也会来，如果他带着我们同伴变成的那些斑纹马——\
**Yenisei**: You said she had seen the feather man and the animals he brought. Then maybe he will come again today. If he shows up with our horse teammates ...

**里正**：……意味着前任执礼目击的羽人，与你们所见，确为同一人。\
**Lizheng**: That is to say, the feather man she saw is the same person you met.

老者很快跟上思路，皱眉思索间，从笔架上再次取下了毛笔。\
The old man follows his train of thought to its destination, frowns and ponders, before taking the brush from its holder yet again.

他利落地铺开一张白纸，研墨落笔，从容而迅速。\
He neatly spreads out a new piece of paper, rubs an ink stick on the slab, and begins to write with a calm and swift hand.

**里正**：那么，或许两位应去一趟职祠。\
**Lizheng**: In this case, a visit to the Zhící might be a good choice for you.

**里正**：我修书一封，劳两位带去职祠，交予现在的执礼曲娘。若是真有羽人来过，你们也好接手那些被他带来的动物。\
**Lizheng**: I will write a letter for you. Please take it to the Zhící and show it to Jiǔ Niángzǐ, the current Zhílǐ. If the feather man has been there, you can take over the animals he brought to her.

**里正**：假使没来，两位也能将信转交，请新任执礼多多留意。曲娘是个热心的孩子，此刻约莫正在职祠，两位自去寻她便是。\
**Lizheng**: Even if he hasn't, you can still proceed with the letter, since Jiǔ Niángzǐ is very warm-hearted. She should be in the Zhící right now. You can find her there.

**小叶尼塞**：……好。\
**Yenisei**: Thank you.

少许希望的出现，终于暂时锚定了两人初入异域的动荡心情。\
With this glimmer of hope, the turbulent emotions of these two strangers in a strange land find themselves anchored, temporarily at least.

领了书信，异域的来客才终于真正去到城中。只见彩色的绸缎高悬于指向天空的飞檐间，东方面孔的人们视若无睹地穿行其下。\
After receiving their pass, they are finally permitted into the city. Colorful silks hanging between pointed eaves. People bustle around, taking no notice of the extraordinary beauty around them.

而道路两旁……各户门前或银或铜的炭盆里有着更细微的爆裂声。一团团无光的火，在寒日里捧起热切的温度。\
On both sides of the street, there is a silver or copper charcoal pot in front of every house, crackling subtly and bringing spots of warmth to the cold day.

**小叶尼塞**：……\
**Yenisei**: ...

**别斯米尔**：走吧，孩子。\
**Bessmert**: We should go, Yeni.

两人向着里正所指方向，从石砖铺就的寂寥门前，走向沙石翻飞，人语与噼啪声齐响的热闹街市。\
They walk in the direction indicated by Lǐzhèng, from the silent neighborhood, to the dusty and bustling market.

摊贩与表演者岿然不动地占去部分空间，流动的行人都被逐渐收拢至干道中央。\
The peddlers and street performers lay a steady claim to their spaces, forming eddies in the stream of pedestrians that flows toward the center of the main boulevard.

汇聚到交集路口的行人越多，便越拥挤。这显然滞缓了急于行路者的速度。\
The more people flow toward that intersection, the more crowded it becomes. Until it becomes a slow-moving throng, impeding anyone wishing to move through it.

**小叶尼塞**：如果这样一直推挤着彼此前进，就太慢了……\
**Yenisei**: This is going to take forever if we have to follow the crowd.

**小叶尼塞**：女士，我们能不能从房屋与房屋之间穿过去？当然，如果能问到更快的路径会更好——\
**Yenisei**: Madam, do you think we can take the gaps between the houses? Or find a shortcut. That'd be even better ...

**城中居民Ⅰ**：——啊！\
**Citizen I**: Ahh!

要在拥挤人群中强求面对面说话的礼貌，就会发生这样的事故。\
Insisting on politeness in a crowded space like this can often lead to such accidents.

**别斯米尔**：小心。怎么了？\
**Bessmert**: Careful. What's wrong?

**小叶尼塞**：抱歉……我们急着赶路——您还好吗？\
**Yenisei**: Sorry, we were in a hurry. Are you alright?

**城中居民Ⅰ**：无妨，不过略微磕碰罢了。两位是胡人吧？还从没在城中见过你这头发色式的，真是漂亮。\
**Citizen I**: No problem. Don't worry about the bumping. Oh, aren't you the foreigners? I've never seen any red hair in the city. It's pretty.

**城中居民Ⅰ**：现下各处都在过节，摩擦是常有的，不过你们这样着急，是要去哪里呢？\
**Citizen I**: It's holiday time. It's fine to stumble into people. But what's with the rush? Where are you going?

**小叶尼塞**：我们是要去职祠。\
**Yenisei**: We are going to the Zhící.

**城中居民Ⅰ**：原来如此……可现在去职祠的路上游人却是太多了。或许，两位能从别的路过去——\
**Citizen I**: Oh. But the way there is crowded with visitors. Maybe you can take the other road.

衣着艳丽的女子皱起了眉，似乎思考着如何描述，却很快被喧哗声转移了注意力。\
The gaudily-dressed woman frowns, clearly pondering how to describe it, but is just as soon distracted by a commotion.

只见一群黑色奇异生物，拖着长尾自不远处腾空而起。\
A group of strange black creatures appear from somewhere nearby, dragging their long tails before soaring into the air.

**城中居民Ⅰ**：——嗯？那是——天哪，烛夜怎么会白日里出现在大街上？！\
**Citizen I**: Huh? They are ... Oh no, they are Zhúyès! What are they doing in the street during the daytime?!

**小叶尼塞**：烛夜是什么？一种魔精吗？\
**Yenisei**: Zhúyè? What's that? Some kind of critter?

**烛夜？**：吱……咕叽……吱吱！\
**Zhuye the Monster?**: Squeak ... Coo ... Squeak!

它们自屋檐跃下，挥动潮湿的小翅膀卖力掀起一阵飞扬尘土，连带着洒落香味莫名的水点。\
They jump down from the eaves, flapping their sticky little wings and violently raising a wave of flying dust accompanied by strangely fragrant drops of water.

**别斯米尔**：唔，好香啊。我似乎闻到了一股酒香味儿。\
**Bessmert**: Umm, an extraordinary smell. Like liquor.

街上的游人则连连奔逃，被那四处振翅的动物折腾得不轻。\
The travelers on the street run away, harangued by the creatures flapping their wings at them everywhere they turn.

**城中居民Ⅱ**：这儿哪儿来的烛夜！好大的一股酒味儿！\
**Citizen II**: Why are they here? Oh! I smell liquor. A lot of liquor!

**城中居民Ⅱ**：谁家的酒坛子翻了招的烛夜！\
**Citizen II**: Who broke the liquor jar and attracted them here?!

**？？？**：——诸位！烛夜白日跃市，乃喜兆也，勿要惊慌！\
**???**: People! A Zhúyè in the street during daytime is a sign of auspiciousness. Stay calm!

**小叶尼塞**：……它朝我们来了，别斯米尔女士，小心！\
**Yenisei**: It's coming our way! Watch out, Madam!

似乎是因为发觉了自己被轻视的现实，闹剧元凶扑腾的动作看上去愈发有分量。\
It seems as though the ringleader's movements are even more exaggerated than the others, perhaps realizing that it is being underestimated.

它径直地朝人群中心飞扑而来，扬起了钩爪。\
It flies straight toward the center of the crowd, readying its talons.

**烛夜**：咕——！！！\
**Zhuye the Monster**: Coo!

**烛夜**：咕咕咕！吱！！\
**Zhuye the Monster**: Coo! Squeak! Squeak!

烛夜的称霸之路被一群突然闯入的牲畜所终结。\
The Zhúyè's ambition to dominate the street is ended by the sudden intrusion of rampaging livestock that burst into the scene.

或许是这景象看起来太过混乱，以至于几乎所有人都没能反应过来究竟发生了什么。\
The milieu of beasts, pedestrians, and fliers soon becomes so entirely chaotic, that no one present seems to have any grasp of what is happening beyond the end of their nose.

**？？？**：呃——抱……抱歉！\
**???**: Um ... S-sorry!

**？？？**：你们……你们——给我——回来——！\
**???**: You ... You guys! COME BACK!

**？？？**：坏东西！\
**???**: Bad boys and girls!

**烛夜**：咕咕——咕——咕！\
**Zhuye the Monster**: Coo coo! Coo! Coo!

**别斯米尔**：——怎么了？吵嚷声好像不仅没有减弱，反而越发纷扰了。\
**Bessmert**: What's going on? All this shouting and running about ...?!

**别斯米尔**：我闻到了酒，还有尘土扬起的呛人气。发生什么事了？\
**Bessmert**: I smell liquor and dust. What happened?

**小叶尼塞**：路上突然出现了一种被称为“烛夜”的当地神秘学动物，我不知道——图鉴上没有那样的东西。它似乎身带酒香。\
**Yenisei**: A kind of local animal named Zhúyè popped up in the street. Maybe they are arcane creatures? I don't know. I've never seen one in books. The liquor smell probably comes from them.

**小叶尼塞**：还有……更远处似乎是冲进来了一群牲畜，但我没能看清。\
**Yenisei**: And ... I think a herd of livestock rushed out of the fence over there, but I can't see it clearly.

**小叶尼塞**：抱歉，女士，我们本来不该停在这里的。\
**Yenisei**: Sorry, Madam. We are not supposed to stop here.

顾不上眼前的闹剧，两人决定在人越聚越多之前离开。\
Ignoring the chaos around them, the two travelers decide to leave before even more commotion starts.

围观鸡飞狗跳的混乱场面从不在她们的计划列表中。\
This bizarre scene of animals, critters and people leaping every which way and everywhere was never part of their plan.

**城中居民Ⅰ**：烛夜就算了，这会儿又是谁家的年节动物跑出来了——\
**Citizen I**: We are already having enough trouble with the Zhúyè. Who let out these Festive Animals now?

除非计划的确赶不上变化。\
It seems life has seen fit to frustrate their plans yet again.

**城中居民Ⅰ**：等等……\
**Citizen I**: Wait ...

**城中居民Ⅰ**：这不是曲娘吗？！\
**Citizen I**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ?!

——熟悉的名字在小叶尼塞脑中嗡的一声响起。\
—The familiar name hums in Yenisei's mind.

**城中居民Ⅰ**：曲娘，你、你不应该在职祠吗——你这是……？\
**Citizen I**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ, aren't you supposed to be in the Zhící during work hours? What are you ...

**曲娘**：……呃……我现在……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Um ... I ...

**曲娘**：没法解释！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: No time for explaining!

**曲娘**：总之——它们——跑了……！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Anyway ... They're escaping!

**曲娘**：……而且我要……我要拽不住啦！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: And I'm ... I'm losing them!!

**小叶尼塞**：“曲娘”？这不是里正让我们去找的那个人吗？\
**Yenisei**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ? That's the one Lǐzhèng told us to talk to, isn't it?

被称为“曲娘”的女孩努力使自己的话听起来轻松，但眼前的景象显然逐渐要脱离她的控制。\
The girl named Jiǔ Niángzǐ tries to sound as relaxed as possible in reply, but the scene before her is one obviously and rapidly spiraling out of her control.

她额角沁下汗珠，越发地惊慌失措起来。\
A panicked sweat drips down her forehead.

如果这时候放手，这些得到自由以至于癫狂的动物们，将会是市集道路上所有人的灾难。\
If she lets go now, these wild creatures will wreak havoc on the market street and everyone on it.

**小叶尼塞**：女士，我……\
**Yenisei**: Madam, I ...

小叶尼塞下意识想要上前去。她望了望远处还看不见的职祠，又回头看着别斯米尔。\
Yenisei's instincts tell her to step forward. She looks toward the Zhící, still out-of-sight in the distance, then turns back to look at Bessmert.

年长者能感受到她的视线，轻轻地点头。\
Bessmert can feel her gaze and nods gently.

**别斯米尔**：去吧，我会在这里等你。\
**Bessmert**: Go. I will wait here.

**曲娘**：呃……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Er ...

其中两匹马突然狠狠地往前蹿去，似乎试探着身后人的力气。\
Two of the horses suddenly bolt forward, as if testing the strength of the people behind them.

**曲娘**：——呀！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Whoa!

**曲娘**：拜托、拜托大家……我这次真的要，拽不住啦！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Please, please, guys ... I can't hold on anymore!

位于人群视线中心的女孩，继续试图牵住那一大群明显超过她力气大小的动物。\
The girl in the center of the crowd strains to keep her eyes fixed on the horde of animals more than outmatching her strength.

力气不断流失，让牵制这件事变得越发困难。她只能把麻绳用力在掌心绞紧，一圈，又一圈，紧到虎口都渗出血来。\
Her obviously waning control does nothing to contain the chaos. All she can do is twist the hemp rope tightly in her hand, winding it one hoop after another, until it is so tight that rough-edged rope cuts into her hand.

**城中居民Ⅳ**：……哦，我来帮你！\
**Citizen IV**: Oh, let me help!

**城中居民Ⅱ**：呀！我来，我也来帮帮忙！\
**Citizen II**: Yeah! I'll help, too!

**城中居民Ⅱ**：不过，这些家伙怎么跑出来的……\
**Citizen II**: I wonder how these animals got out ...

到此刻终于——在第一个回过神来的居民的呼吁下，人们逐渐开始涌上前去。\
It is at this moment that finally—heeding the call to come to their senses, the crowd begins to rush forward to assist.

**曲娘**：——谢谢、谢谢……大家！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Thank you! Thanks ... everyone ...

**曲娘**：劳烦……再帮我……牵紧一些……！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Please ... help me ... pull harder!

**曲娘**：拽住呀——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Hold on!

**曲娘**：我会请你们喝酒的！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: You all get a drink on the house!

片刻后，在围观者的帮助下，她终于将扎着彩带奔逃而出的节庆动物们控制住了。\
After a short while, with help from the other streetgoers, she manages to get the rampaging, if festively decorated, animals back under control.

绿衣女孩手脚利索地把冷静下来的动物都拴在了彩旗柱子上，又将多出来的末端握在手中，才终于松出一口气。\
She deftly ties the quelled animals to the flagpole, then, breathing a well-earned sigh of relief, lets the rope finally slack down from her hands.

**曲娘**：天呀，谢谢你们——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Oh dear, thank you so much ...

**曲娘**：要不然，我可真不知道该怎么办……上任第一天就出这么大的岔子！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I couldn't do this without you ... Making so much trouble on the first day of work ...

她气喘吁吁的，如同经过一场浩大的战役——保卫家乡的战役。\
She pants heavily, still recovering from her battle—a battle to defend her hometown.

**城中居民Ⅰ**：曲娘打哪儿来呀，早些时候在酒坊没瞧见你。\
**Citizen I**: Where were you, Jiǔ Niángzǐ? I didn't see you in the tavern.

**曲娘**：我？我就在那边，在职祠里。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Me? I was in the Zhící.

**城中居民Ⅲ**：曲娘在职祠做什么？\
**Citizen III**: What were you doing there?

**城中居民Ⅰ**：哎，柳郎，你又忘啦？原先的执礼回乡去了。现在呀，曲娘已是新的执礼了。\
**Citizen I**: Oh, Mr. Liǔ, did you forget again? The former Zhílǐ went back to her hometown. Jiǔ Niángzǐ is the new Zhílǐ now.

**曲娘**：不不，不是的，我只是，呃，代班！我刚才清点节庆动物的数量时，听到了外面的动静……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: No, no, that's not it. I'm just, um, covering for her! I was counting the Festive Animals, and then I heard the noise outside ...

**城中居民Ⅱ**：哈哈哈，是听到了说书先生的声音吧？今日是他最后一讲，你定是不会错过。\
**Citizen II**: Haha, you must have been distracted by the Storyteller, huh? He was telling the end of the story today, so you would never miss it.

**曲娘**：是啊，我想着，他可能会讲祥瑞的故事，才着急出来。兴许是没有关好围栏的门，唔……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Well, yeah. I thought he might tell the story of Xiángruì, so I hurried out and forgot to lock the fence. Hmm ...

**城中居民Ⅰ**：总是惦记着“祥瑞”、“祥瑞”的，不晓得的，还以为你是要写书呢。\
**Citizen I**: You're talking about Xiángruì again. People would think you were another Storyteller if they didn't know you just really like these tales.

**城中居民Ⅲ**：也看看手掌有无擦伤，若是有恙，一会儿可随我去医馆取药。\
**Citizen III**: Are your palms bruised? Go to my clinic for medicine if it hurts.

**城中居民Ⅱ**：晚些时候还要请大伙喝酒～\
**Citizen II**: Remember the drinks on the house!

**曲娘**：好的呀，那是一定的！真是谢谢你们啦！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Of course, I will! Thank you so so much!

她熟络地与居民叙话，却又不住地向茶馆的方向张望——似乎想确认之前那位说书先生是否还在原地。\
She speaks with warm familiarity to the other residents, but keeps an eye in the direction of the tea house—as though anxious to confirm whether the Storyteller from before is still there.

当看到远处那摇头晃脑的身影后，她终于露出释然和欢欣的神色。\
After seeing his swaying figure in the distance, a look of joy lightens up her face.

**小叶尼塞**：……\
**Yenisei**: ...

小叶尼塞安静观察，慢慢退后，转身朝别斯米尔走去。刚才人们的对话流进她的耳朵，使她确定了一个事实。\
Yenisei quietly observes the scene and retreats, turning around to walk toward Bessmert. The conversations among the locals flow into her ears, allowing her to confirm a crucial fact.

**小叶尼塞**：女士，请跟我来。那位应该就是……里正所说的“执礼”。\
**Yenisei**: Please follow me, Madam. That lady must be the "Zhílǐ" that Lǐzhèng mentioned.

**小叶尼塞**：请您留神脚下，现在地面上有些乱糟糟的。我们得继续跟上去看看，或许能与她搭上话。\
**Yenisei**: Please mind your steps, as we are walking in a mess now. We need to follow the crowd and see if we will have a chance to talk to her.

**说书先生**：——先不论——烛夜如何——\
**Storyteller**: Let's put aside the Zhúyè for now ...

**小叶尼塞**：……？\
**Yenisei**: ...?

两人一走到茶馆前，没等拾到一个好位置，便发现人潮都追着石台上的声音向前涌去。\
Little sooner than they reach the tea house, do they notice the crowd rushing toward a stone platform, filling up every nearby space before they have a chance to find a seat.

他们更紧地聚拢在茶店前的空地，以至于身在其中的两人也被裹挟到那人面前。\
The crowd fills the tea house tightly. The surge of people pushes Bessmert and Yenisei right in front of the Storyteller.

**说书先生**：且说那帝尧，亦是多见此类异兽——\
**Storyteller**: ... And talk about Emperor Yáo. He had seen strange beasts like this many times ...

他的声音娓娓道来，的确带着某种奇异的魔力，连并不为此而来的人都自然被吸引。\
He speaks with eloquence, as if possessing some strange magic that naturally attracts even those who didn't go there to hear him.

**说书先生**：其在位日久，及至七年。有使者前来献宝。此使乃结匈国人，样貌精奇，胸脯尖削，自称从玉门关外万万里处来。\
**Storyteller**: It was the seventh year of his reign. Yáo granted an audience to an envoy offering a treasure from the Jiéxiōng Kingdom. The envoy had a strange face and a bulgy chest. He claimed to have come from somewhere millions of miles away from the Yùmén Pass.

**说书先生**：“有鸟生来即通人言，鸣若凤啸，吾人引以为祥瑞，特此献上人主！”\
**Storyteller**: "This bird is born with the talent for human languages and the phoenix's voice. Our people see it as a Xiángruì, and I am here to offer it to you, Your Majesty!"

**说书先生**：帝尧诸臣见证，结匈使者所献宝物果真为一巨鸟。其貌壮如山峦，有凤凰之姿，青身红尾，神貌不凡！\
**Storyteller**: Then Yáo and his people saw a real giant bird. It was as huge as a mountain and as dazzling as a phoenix. It had an azure body and red tail feathers!

**城中居民Ⅱ**：难道真的是凤凰？\
**Citizen II**: Was it really a phoenix?

**说书先生**：哎，非也，非也。此鸟唤作灭蒙鸟，云是能勘骨相，改命貌，禳异灾！\
**Storyteller**: Oh no, no. The bird was called Mièméng. It was said to be able to read one's bones, change their fate, and even remove misfortune!

**说书先生**：于是帝尧甚悦，故另辟山头饲之。今人所见灭蒙，盖度朔山始祖之后也。\
**Storyteller**: Yáo was pleased with the gift and kept the bird in Dùshuò Mountain. Naturally, that very bird was the ancestor of all the Mièméngs nowadays.

先前那位绿衣姑娘眼中盈满了艳羡的神色。\
The envy in the eyes of the girl clad in green matches her attire completely.

**曲娘**：您、您有亲眼见过灭蒙鸟吗？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: H-have you seen a Mièméng with your own eyes?

**说书先生**：莫急莫急。灭蒙鸟生性喜静好洁，古今之人常将门前扫净，盼望祥瑞禽鸟停留聚集。虽时不定，长此以往，或可见之。\
**Storyteller**: Be patient and listen. Mièméngs tend to inhabit silent and clean environments, so since the ancient times, the people have always cleaned their yards carefully from time to time, hoping the Xiángruìs will gather and stay beside them. It may not work immediately, but it makes things possible in the long term.

**城中居民Ⅲ**：我们朔日需得扫门，原是这么个道理？\
**Citizen III**: So that's why we have the tradition of cleaning the yards on Shuòrì?

**说书先生**：正是。亦有人将金玉珠宝刻成灭蒙模样，装点家宅以求平安。是以诸位仰头望去，今日屋头檐上所刻时夜，其非时夜也，其真灭蒙也，家户所裁门笺亦是。\
**Storyteller**: Exactly. Some even make Mièméng statues with jewelry and use them to decorate their homes, hoping the Mièméngs will bless the family. Remember the "chicken" statues on your roof? Actually, they are not chickens but Mièméngs, so are those birds you see in the paper-cutouts on the doors.

说罢，他举起一张红色的门笺，上面剪刻了某种鸟类的形状。\
After saying this, he lifts a piece of red paper, carved in the shape of a peculiarly familiar bird.

**说书先生**：此鸟即为——灭蒙鸟。\
**Storyteller**: Look, everyone. This is the Mièméng.

众人露出了失望的神色。\
The crowd expresses an underwhelmed disappointment.

**曲娘**：唔。可这个，看起来像普通的鸡……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Hmm. But this looks like a normal chicken ...

**小叶尼塞**：这看起来像松鸡。\
**Yenisei**: More like a capercaillie to me.

**小叶尼塞**：……也像我刚才画的巨鸟？\
**Yenisei**: And like the bird I just drew, isn't it?

**别斯米尔**：他说话的方式和语调很有韵律感，像是在唱歌。只可惜没有伴奏，清唱似乎令这些歌词失去了一些味道。\
**Bessmert**: The way he is speaking is interesting, rhythmic, like singing. It would be great if there was some music to accompany him. Something is missing in his story without the music.

**别斯米尔**：如果他能——\
**Bessmert**: If he could ...

别斯米尔话音未落，红色的纸张瞬间在灰衣男子手中自燃，又于触到手指之前尽数化为灰烬，簌簌落到石台之上。\
Before Bessmert can finish speaking, the red paper instantly ignites in the hands of the Storyteller, and before touching his fingers, it becomes ashes and falls onto the stone platform.

一旁侍立的小童则登时踮起脚来，利落地接手，将那些灰烬扫进了下方的炭盆中。\
The little boy standing beside him stands on his tiptoes, quickly taking the initiative to sweep the ashes into the charcoal pot below.

**说书先生**：灭蒙属火，庭燎燃春，此即为喻。而话又说回——\
**Storyteller**: Among the Five Elements, Mièméng belongs to the Fire. That's why people set fire in spring to drive away misfortunes. Speaking of ...

小叶尼塞的注意力被转移了。她目睹小童那一切动作，却不明白其中的含义，只是注视，直到噼啪的爆炸声在身后响起。\
Yenisei's attention is diverted. She witnesses the child's movements, but doesn't yet understand the meaning behind them, choosing to stare ahead until a crackling sound explodes behind her.

**别斯米尔**：这是——什么声音——？\
**Bessmert**: What is this noise?

然而几乎身边所有人都对这动静见怪不怪，以至于此时与两人一同回过头去的，只有先前在闹市中力挽狂澜的曲娘。\
It seems no one cares about the noise of the cracker. Only Jiǔ Niángzǐ, who had previously worked so hard to restore order to the bustling city, turns around with the two of them.

她回头时，一种突然记起早前遗忘之事的懊恼神色，也逐渐浮现在她脸上。\
As she turns around, she seems to remember something and shows a remorseful look.

**曲娘**：庭燎爆竿……糟了。天哪，我差点忘了正事！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: The cracker ... Shoot. I almost forgot!

**曲娘**：抱歉、抱歉！请让开一下，我得出去——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Sorry, excuse me! Please let me go out ...

**城中居民Ⅱ**：这就不继续听啦？时辰还早着呢，急着回去酿酒吗？\
**Citizen II**: You won't listen to the rest? It's still early. Oh, are you going back to the tavern to make our drinks?

**曲娘**：不是酿酒，但也还有事呢……明天，明天一定请你们喝酒！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Not drinks, but other stuff! Oh, and "drinks on the house" tomorrow!

人们低声调笑着，为曲娘让开一条小道来。小叶尼塞也牵住别斯米尔，以防跟过去时，她落在了身后。\
Everyone chuckles warmly, making way for Jiǔ Niángzǐ. Yenisei holds onto Bessmert to prevent her from falling behind.

她们这回很轻易地跟上去了。无人对发色醒目的异乡人投以别样注视，所有人的注意力都集中在这位讲述传奇的“歌唱家”身上。\
This time, they follow her without incident. Despite the strangers' otherwise eye-catching hair, everyone's attention seems focused intently on the Storyteller telling the legend.

## NS-10 异乡人关怀 / Treat Them Right

不远处，能大致瞧见曲娘在先前拴动物的桩子前停了下来，仿佛对它们私语着什么。\
Not far away, Jiǔ Niángzǐ can be seen stopping near the post where the animals were tied, vaguely moving as if whispering something to them.

**曲娘**：嗯，你们能听懂我说的话吗……？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Um, can you understand me?

**曲娘**：可不可以告诉我，你们是从哪里来的？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Can you tell me where you are from?

**小叶尼塞**：请问……\
**Yenisei**: Hello ...

小叶尼塞等待了片刻才走上前去，试着拍了拍她的肩膀。\
Yenisei waits for a moment before walking forward and attempting to pat her shoulder.

而后少女回过头来，展露一副年轻而热切的面庞。\
The girl turns around to reveal her young and eager face.

**曲娘**：咦？怎么啦？娘子面生，我们从前见过吗？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Hmm? What's wrong? I don't know you. Have we met before?

**小叶尼塞**：……应该没有。我们才到城里。\
**Yenisei**: I don't think so. We just arrived here.

**曲娘**：真的吗？天哪，欢迎你们来沛城玩！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Really? Oh, welcome to Pèi City!

小叶尼塞没忍住，用余光看了眼这女孩手里拽住的一把麻绳，和麻绳尽头的许多动物。\
Yenisei cannot help but hold her eyes on the bundled hemp rope the girl is holding in her hand, and the many animals now tied at the end of it.

被称作“曲娘”的女孩眨眼，又眨眼，似乎终于发现了对方正在看着什么。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ blinks, then blinks again, as though realizing what the other girl is staring at.

红晕很快像两朵火烧云一样浮上她的脸颊。\
A blush quickly rises to her cheeks like two sunset clouds.

**曲娘**：……啊，你们……你们刚才也在街上吗？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Oh ... Y-you were on the street, weren't you?

**曲娘**：真不好意思……一来就让你们看见这种混乱的情况。我保证，这只是一场意外！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I am so sorry. I didn't mean to make such a scene there. I promise, it was just an accident!

**别斯米尔**：可以想象的意外。您的反应很及时，避免了一场灾难的发生。\
**Bessmert**: I can imagine. You reacted quickly and saved us from more trouble.

**曲娘**：没有没有，都是我应该做的。而且大家也帮了很多忙。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: No, no, no, it was my responsibility. And the people on the street also gave me a hand there!

**曲娘**：你们找我是有什么事情吗？如果有什么能帮上忙的，请尽管告诉我。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: How can I help you? Please feel free to let me know.

看来是一位相当好说话的姑娘。\
She seems to be a warm-hearted type.

**小叶尼塞**：是这样的。我先前听见他们叫你“曲娘”，你是曲娘，在职祠工作，是吗？\
**Yenisei**: Here's the case: The people call you Jiǔ Niángzǐ, and you work in the Zhící, right?

**曲娘**：嗯，是的！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Ng, ng. Yes!

**小叶尼塞**：我们从里正那里过来，之前恰好听见了你们在街上的对话……\
**Yenisei**: Lǐzhèng told us to find you, and we happened to hear your conversation on the street.

**小叶尼塞**：请问羽人今日来过职祠了吗？\
**Yenisei**: So did the feather man come here today?

**曲娘**：羽人？你说城外那位“祥瑞”？唔，我听说他以前好像来过，今天就不知道了。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Feather man? You mean the Xiángruì out of the city? Um, I heard that he had been here. As for today, I have no idea.

**小叶尼塞**：……那职祠有没有今天才新送到的动物？\
**Yenisei**: What about the animals in the fence? Any new ones?

**曲娘**：这，我也不清楚……今天我到职祠点卯的时候，围栏里就已经有很多年节动物了。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I-I'm not sure about that either. When I arrived at the Zhící this morning, there were already many Festive Animals in the fence.

**曲娘**：真奇怪啊，为什么越来越多了呢……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: They're getting more and more ... How weird is that!

曲娘嘟囔着转过身去，以食指将先前闹事的那些罪魁祸首指给两人瞧。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ mutters inaudibly before turning around, pointing out the culprits who caused her so much trouble earlier with her index finger.

小叶尼塞顺眼望去，的确没看出来什么不同。这里几乎是一个常见牲畜的博览会，各种牛羊马都争相露出个脸来。\
Yenisei inspects the creatures briefly but doesn't seem to notice any difference. It seems to be a show for common livestock, where various cattle, sheep, and horses might compete to show their worth.

**曲娘**：你看，它们都长得差不多，我不知道哪些是今天送到的。清点的时候也很麻烦，经常忘记自己刚才数到哪里了。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: See, they all look alike. I can't tell which of them were brought here today. Counting is troublesome as well. I always think, "where am I?"

**曲娘**：如果我识字就好了。能写下来，就不会算错。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: If only I could read and write. You write them down, then you won't miscount.

**小叶尼塞**：……我们的同伴就变成了这种有斑纹的马。\
**Yenisei**: Our teammates have been turned into striped horses, like these.

**小叶尼塞**：是这样的，我们原本是一支商队，走到城外的时候，同伴被变成了马，还被一只巨鸟带走了。\
**Yenisei**: Actually, we are a team of merchants. When we reached the outskirts of the city, our teammates were turned into horses and brought away by a giant bird.

**小叶尼塞**：里正告诉我们，那只巨鸟很可能就是他们正在追寻的羽人，而他曾经在职祠附近出没过。\
**Yenisei**: Lǐzhèng said that bird was probably the feather man they've been looking for, and he appeared around the Zhící once.

**小叶尼塞**：所以，我们想来职祠寻求帮助。\
**Yenisei**: That's why we are here to ask for help.

**曲娘**：它们……它们应该不是马。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: They're-They're not horses, I suppose.

曲娘似乎有些欲言又止。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ seems hesitant to say anything further.

**曲娘**：但是——怎么可能呢？你们的意思好像是说，羽人能把人变成……变成马？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: But-but how is that possible? Are you saying that the feather man can turn people into ... into horses ...?

**曲娘**：我不明白。难道因为他是“祥瑞”，就会有这样的能力吗？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I don't understand. How did he get this power? Is it because he is the Xiángruì?

再次听到“祥瑞”这个词，别斯米尔燃起了兴趣。\
Upon hearing the word "Xiángruì" again, Bessmert's interest is immediately captured.

**别斯米尔**：我们刚刚也在说书先生那儿听到了关于“祥瑞”的故事，“祥瑞”听起来确实很像具有地域特征的保护神。\
**Bessmert**: We've also heard about the Xiángruì from the Storyteller. It does sound like some kind of local guardian.

**曲娘**：什么神？我只知道摄提神。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Guardian? Is it the Gods of Shètí we're talking about?

**别斯米尔**：噢。是的，摄提神。这应该才是你们供奉的东西。\
**Bessmert**: Oh, yes, the Gods of Shètí. These are the gods you serve.

**别斯米尔**：我猜“祥瑞”应该更类似一种本地的信仰，传奇的神秘学家之类的。这里神秘术的使用听起来相当常见，或许神秘学家也一样。\
**Bessmert**: I guess Xiángruì is closer to a local legend, like a reputed arcanist in this area. The use of arcane skills seems common here. Perhaps there are also many arcanists around.

**别斯米尔**：不过，既然说到这里，您能告诉我，摄提神究竟是什么吗？\
**Bessmert**: But, could you please tell us more about the Gods of Shètí?

**曲娘**：我只知道摄提神有十二……还是十三位，的样子？但那些名字，很多我都不认识。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: There are 12 ... or 13 of them, I guess? That's all I know. I can't read most of their names.

**曲娘**：哦，我知道今年是摄提神执徐的生辰年！我们会请很多的年节动物去断桥供奉祂。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Oh, but I know this year is the year of Zhíxú! We will bring lots of Festive Animals to the broken bridge to worship It.

**曲娘**：走吉和跃桥是最有趣的。我们会带着年节动物去到悬崖上的断桥前，一起数着步数摆动身子，像跳舞一样，最后再尝试跳过去——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: The Fortune Walk and Bridge Leap are the most fun parts! We go to the broken bridge on the cliff with the animals, count our steps, and swing our bodies, like dancing. And at last, we will try to jump over it!

**小叶尼塞**：跳过悬崖上的断桥？这听起来不仅危险，而且还相当的……耳熟。\
**Yenisei**: Jump over a broken bridge on the cliff? It sounds dangerous and quite ... familiar.

别斯米尔知道小叶尼塞在暗示什么。传闻中“所求必应”的规则不约而同浮现在她们的脑海里，但没有一个人真的问出声来。\
Bessmert knows exactly what Yenisei is hinting at. The familiar rule of "Ask and Acquire" resurfaces in their minds, but no one attempts to ask it out loud.

而曲娘的解释也及时打断了她们的联想。\
So that Jiǔ Niángzǐ's explanation interrupts their thoughts with perfect timing.

**曲娘**：不不不，跳不过去的！还没听说有谁能跳过去呢，连最厉害的山羊都跳不过去，更别说人了。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: No, no, no, we can't do that. No one has even done that! Even the goats can't do that, let alone humans.

**曲娘**：我们还会提前用神秘术进行保护，防止真的有人或者动物掉下去。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: We'll also cast arcane skills as safety measures to protect anyone from falling.

**曲娘**：山谷很深。掉下去，就再也回不来了。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: The valley is deeeep down there. Once you fall down, you're not coming back.

**别斯米尔**：真有意思。那些提前的神秘术设置，都是由什么人负责的？\
**Bessmert**: Intriguing. And who's in charge of the safety measures, may I ask?

**曲娘**：嗯，就是职祠负责的。职祠是负责管理沛城神秘术事务的地方哦。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: The staff in the Zhící. It's the place to manage arcane affairs in the Pèi City.

**曲娘**：不过，我并不负责那些……我只是新来的，在上任执礼回乡后，暂时兼任这个工作而已。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: But not me ... I'm new here, filling in for the former Zhílǐ after she went back to her hometown.

**曲娘**：他们跟我说，我只需要这几天把职祠照看好就可以了！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: They told me to take care of Zhící for a couple of days. That's good enough for me!

她似乎对能帮上忙感到很高兴。\
Her eagerness to be able to help is clear.

**小叶尼塞**：所以简单来说，您是看门的。\
**Yenisei**: So, simply put, you're a doorkeeper?

预料不到的结论令曲娘惊讶地涨红了脸。\
The barb of her conclusion makes Jiǔ Niángzǐ fluster into a red blush.

**曲娘**：我——我不是——我不站在门口呀。我也有其他事要做的。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I-I'm not-I'm not just keeping the door safe! I do stuff too!

**曲娘**：比如，嗯，我还要安抚那些被爆竿声音吓到的人，有一种被神秘术加强过的爆竿，声音很大的！比刚才茶馆外面的动静，都还要大很多……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Like, um, take good care of those startled by the fire crackers! There is a kind of firecracker enhanced by arcane skill. It can make a huuuge sound! Much more louder than what you heard in the tea house!

**别斯米尔**：请您原谅，她并不是对您有恶意，只是我们来自北方，说话都会直率一些。\
**Bessmert**: Please forgive her. She didn't mean to hurt your feelings. We speak bluntly in the North.

**曲娘**：没关系，没关系。我能感觉到，她只是有点着急。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Oh, it's alright. I can tell she's a bit anxious.

**曲娘**：但现在着急也没用呀。就像，呃，野猪上树？也不是说会就会的……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: But it's not getting us anywhere. Like, um, pigs can't learn how to climb in a day ...

**小叶尼塞**：……\
**Yenisei**: ...

**曲娘**：或者，你们能从这些马里面，认出来哪些是你们的同伴吗？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Or, let's think another way. Can you recognize your teammates from these horses?

**曲娘**：我看看，这里有一、二、三……三只“斑纹马”。来，你们也瞧瞧。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Let me see, there are one, two, three ... three striped horses. Come see for yourself.

**小叶尼塞**：……我认不出来，当时太匆忙了，我不记得样貌的差别。而且，即使这几只都是，也还差了两只。\
**Yenisei**: I can't. There was little time for me to memorize the difference. Besides, even if they are my teammates, two of them are still missing.

**曲娘**：你们的同伴比三个还多？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: More than three teammates?

**曲娘**：三加二——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: When three plus two ...

曲娘掰着指头就要仔细算来。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ counts out the numbers on her fingers, calculating with great care.

**别斯米尔**：……这样吧，我们先等等里正那边的消息。\
**Bessmert**: How about we wait and see what Lǐzhèng has found out?

**别斯米尔**：对了，小叶尼塞，里正不是给了我们一封书信么？\
**Bessmert**: That's right, child, didn't Lǐzhèng leave us with a letter?

**小叶尼塞**：噢，是的，我差点忘记了……来，曲娘小姐，请你看看这个。也许里面有关于羽人的线索。\
**Yenisei**: Oh, right. I almost forgot. Please read this, Ms. Jiǔ Niángzǐ. It may have clues about the feather man.

她掏出那张信函。\
She produces the letter, offering it to the girl.

曲娘接过后，毫不防备地当面打开，但小叶尼塞只看见几枚图画留在上面。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ opens it in front of them without a moment's hesitation, but all Yenisei can see on it are several images.

**曲娘**：唔……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Um ...

**曲娘**：加高围栏……早些放班……回酒坊……？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Make the fence taller ... Get off work earlier and ... go back to the tavern?

**曲娘**：什么跟什么呀。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: What is he trying to say?

**曲娘**：这些都跟羽人有什么关系？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: What do these have to do with the feather man?

**小叶尼塞**：嗯？\
**Yenisei**: Hmm?

**别斯米尔**：……\
**Bessmert**: ...

曲娘对着满是图画的信件自言自语，皱眉又舒展，半晌才把它乱七八糟地叠好，夹到腰绳上。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ mutters to herself as she stares at the pictures on the letter, before frowning and smoothing it out. She clumsily folds it and clips it to her waist.

**曲娘**：别担心，这几天我会帮你们多多留意新来的马的！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Well, don't worry! I'll pay close attention to the new horses for you!

**曲娘**：一旦有什么好消息，里正一定会转告你们。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: If there's any good news, I'll ask Lǐzhèng to tell you.

**别斯米尔**：谢谢您的好意。不过，我们今日才入城，还没有找到住的地方。要怎么才能让里正知道我们在哪里呢？\
**Bessmert**: You're so kind. But we just got here and haven't decided where to stay for the night. How are we going to keep Lǐzhèng informed once we find a place to rest?

**曲娘**：啊，这样啊……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Oh ... I see ...

她很快便想到了答案。\
An answer leaps to her mind, bursting through and out at the same time.

**曲娘**：对，你们可以住在我的酒坊里！刚才忘了和你们介绍了，我正在经营一家酒坊。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: How about staying in my tavern? I forgot to tell you that I'm the owner of a tavern.

**曲娘**：而且……生意还挺不错的。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: And I'm doing it well!

曲娘笑了起来，似乎想到这个，便能令她感到安心。\
She laughs, as though just the saying of it might render it true.

**曲娘**：酒坊就在离职祠两坊距离的金市中，里正会知道的。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: It is located in the merchants hub, two streets away from the Zhící. Lǐzhèng will know your whereabouts since he's in charge of the hub.

**曲娘**：我还可以顺路把这些家伙都送回职祠。你们也去看一看其他的年节动物吧！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I'll take you back to the tavern, also escort these animals back to the Zhící. You can check out other animals there as well!

**小叶尼塞**：我赞成。\
**Yenisei**: Good idea.

**别斯米尔**：这太好了，也不必在外面摸索到天黑了。\
**Bessmert**: That'd be great. Saves us from all the trouble sleeping on the streets.

**曲娘**：是呀。不过等晚些入夜了，街市上会更好看。度朔节有金灯和庭燎，照得天上和地上都亮堂堂。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Let's go then. Oh, the street looks beautiful later in the night. You can't miss the golden lanterns and bonfires lit on Dùshuò Festival! They light up the sky and the street as if it's daytime.

**曲娘**：在晚上，感觉什么都是特别亮的。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Everything seems brighter at night.

## NS-11 廊下夜话 / Night Talk

职祠中的动物多得令人眼花缭乱，对她们确认同伴并无帮助。\
A breathtaking number of animals lie within the Zhící—a fact that only hinders their efforts to find their companions.

权衡之下，两人决定先跟随曲娘到酒坊中落脚，似乎终于得以卸下急行数日的疲惫。\
After weighing their options, they decide to follow Jiǔ Niángzǐ and settle in at the tavern first. The weary travelers are more than eager to relieve their fatigue after journeying non-stop for so long.

前提是没有那么多怪异的事情接连发生。\
And they've more than earned it, because strange things have indeed happened to them, non-stop for several days.

**小叶尼塞**：女士……\
**Yenisei**: Madam ...

**小叶尼塞**：您觉得白天曲娘说的，有可能是“所求必应”吗？\
**Yenisei**: What do you think about Jiǔ Niángzǐ's words? Could that be "Ask and Acquire"?

**别斯米尔**：跃过断桥就像跃过悬崖，攀爬高山，就像商人们说的那样，一个不可能达成的条件。\
**Bessmert**: Jumping over a broken bridge is like "jumping over a canyon or climbing over a mountain." It's a condition that cannot be met, like those merchants said.

**小叶尼塞**：一种绝对的代价？\
**Yenisei**: An inevitable price?

两人都因为陷入思索而沉默。\
Both of them fall silent, lost in thought.

别斯米尔的疑问却没有因此落在地上，被正从酒坊里走出来的曲娘轻轻拾起。\
However, Bessmert's doubts do not seem to have fallen on deaf ears, as Jiǔ Niángzǐ responds while walking out from the tavern.

**曲娘**：——你们是在说城外的断桥吗？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Are you talking about the broken bridge outside the city?

**曲娘**：不好意思，大堂里的座椅都还没擦洗，要委屈你们先坐在这里……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I'm so sorry. The chairs in the lobby have not been cleaned yet. Please take a seat here, just for now.

**别斯米尔**：哦，没关系，谢谢您的收留。\
**Bessmert**: Oh, don't worry about it. Thank you for letting us stay here.

**别斯米尔**：关于我们刚才说的那座断桥……您知道些什么吗？\
**Bessmert**: As for the broken bridge we talked about ... can you tell me more about it?

**曲娘**：断桥嘛，反正在我到城里的时候，就已经断掉很久了。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Hmm, when I first got here, the bridge was already broken.

**曲娘**：在它下面是高高的悬崖，对面是一个叫渊庙的地方，但被雾气遮盖了。所以我也不知道那个庙是不是真的存在。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Beneath that is a deeeep canyon. Across that canyon stands the Yuān Temple. You can't see it from the other side of the bridge. It's surrounded by fog. So, I'm not sure if there really is a temple there or not.

**小叶尼塞**：渊庙……\
**Yenisei**: The Yuān Temple ...

**曲娘**：据说在渊庙里，你能和执徐对话。有什么问题，你虔诚地问祂，祂就会回答。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: They said you can talk to Zhíxú in the Yuān Temple. Be faithful and ask It. It will answer you.

**曲娘**：他们管这叫什么来着？好像是“问卜”？而且据说那里的雾气有些奇异，不能久留，否则会让人昏迷，或者变得过于兴奋……我是没有见过的。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: What did they call this? "The Divination," I think? They also said that the fog was strange. You can't stay there for long, or you'll pass out or get overexcited ... Well, I haven't seen such things so far.

**别斯米尔**：……！\
**Bessmert**: ...!

**曲娘**：就算会这样，以前的人们都还是会去渊庙，就说明问卜确实有效呀。在桥被洪水冲断之后，可就再也没有这样的好事了。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: But even so, people of that time still rushed there and prayed. Doesn't it mean that The Divination is for real? After the bridge was broken, no one's wish was ever granted.

**别斯米尔**：这是有些奇怪。按理说，如果最开始这座桥能修建起来，那就没有道理不能重建。\
**Bessmert**: Seems odd. There was already a bridge in the first place. Why wouldn't people rebuild it in all these years?

**曲娘**：这个我知道！是因为水变少了，人们不能游过去到对岸，也没办法跳过去，因为山和山之间的悬崖很高，很危险。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I can answer this one! The river dried out. People couldn't swim across, and the cliffs between the mountains were too dangerous to jump over.

**曲娘**：人跳不过去，不过，如果能成为新的“祥瑞”，或许就能跳过去了。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: But, if one can be the new Xiángruì, the problem will be solved.

**曲娘**：它们是很厉害的，八面威风，还能守护一方，为众人排忧解难，什么事情都能做到……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: The Xiángruìs are awesome! They protect the city, help the people ... There's nothing they can't do ...

说着说着，她自顾自地陷入了低落的沉思。\
As she speaks, she sinks into her own personal contemplation.

**小叶尼塞**：没关系。明天，明天我们再去职祠看看那些斑纹马。\
**Yenisei**: Never mind. We'll check the striped horses in the Zhící again tomorrow.

**曲娘**：嗯，我和你们一起去！现在就先歇息吧，我在楼上收拾出了房间。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Alright, I'll go with you! It's time to rest now. I got the rooms cleaned for you upstairs.

**曲娘**：这里呢，还有助眠的浊酒，能帮你们睡个好觉——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: And here, take the liquor with you. They can help you sleep tight!

**曲娘**：来一些吧。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: You got to have some.

**小叶尼塞**：抱歉，曲娘小姐，我不喝酒……别斯米尔女士也不喝酒。\
**Yenisei**: Sorry, Ms. Jiǔ Niángzǐ. I don't drink, neither does Madam Bessmert.

**曲娘**：为什么要叫我“小姐小姐”？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Why did you call me "Ms." twice?

**曲娘**：唔，水的话，要等一下。水缸在院子另一头，我去打。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Um, if you want some water, wait a second, please. The water jars are on the other side of the yard. I'll get it for you.

**小叶尼塞**：啊。那我自己去，不用麻烦你——\
**Yenisei**: Oh, I can do it myself. You don't have to ...

**曲娘**：晚上水缸那边没有点灯，还要过一条小溪，我怕你找不着地方——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: It's fine. There is no light near the jar. You need to cross a stream. I'm afraid you might get lost ...

**小叶尼塞**：……好的。\
**Yenisei**: Thank you.

在少女的声音与身形都被黑夜隐没之后，小叶尼塞转头望向年长者。\
Once the girl's voice and figure are obscured by the night, Yenisei turns to look at Bessmert.

似乎疑惑，又似乎只是单纯的疲倦。\
She seems puzzled, or perhaps, just tired.

**小叶尼塞**：今天在职祠看到的那些斑纹马，花色众多，完全难以分辨……\
**Yenisei**: There were so many different striped horses in the Zhící. I couldn't recognize them at all.

**小叶尼塞**：明天还要早起，您喝些水再去休息吧。\
**Yenisei**: We are going to get up early tomorrow. Please have some water and go to bed.

**别斯米尔**：其实我不渴，只是累了。\
**Bessmert**: I'm not thirsty, thank you. But I do feel like some rest.

**小叶尼塞**：……好。那我扶您去休息。\
**Yenisei**: Okay. I'll take you to the room.

少女打水归来，却只在廊下找到另一名少女。\
The girl returns from fetching water, only to find Yenisei alone in the hallway.

四处张望无果，她走过去，自然坐到先前年长女子坐过的地方。\
Looking around and not seeing Bessmert, she walks over and naturally sits where Bessmert sat earlier.

**曲娘**：远远的，我瞧你们不见，还以为都歇去了呢。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I didn't see you from there. I thought you went to sleep.

**小叶尼塞**：……啊，抱歉。别斯米尔女士太累了，所以……\
**Yenisei**: Oh, sorry. Madam Bessmert is tired, so ...

**小叶尼塞**：谢谢你帮助我们。\
**Yenisei**: Thank you for helping us.

**曲娘**：这些话就不必说啦。喏，这是你要的水。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Don't bother. Here's the water.

接过那个陶土材质的杯子时，小叶尼塞有些微的惊讶。\
As she takes up the ceramic cup, Yenisei is slightly surprised.

在她的印象中，这种材质一般只与粗糙和精致两种极端关联，前者是一些农家手制的碗盆，后者是贵族专用的珍品——\
In her mind, a material like this is one of two extremes—crudeness and finesse, one of handmade rough bowls used by the populace, and the latter of delicate treasures owned only by the rich nobles ...

总之都不是眼前这个显然供平民日常使用，还带着良好审美和品味的成熟工艺制品。\
Yet this cup is a combination of the two extremes—it's used by an ordinary tavern owner, but it is marked by a refined, tasteful aesthetic.

**小叶尼塞**：……\
**Yenisei**: ...

她用手指摩挲杯壁，轻轻擦过那些彩绘的纹路，像感受一枚复活节瓷胎。\
She rubs the side of the cup with her fingers, gently brushing across the painted patterns, as if feeling a fine porcelain vase.

**小叶尼塞**：这个杯子……\
**Yenisei**: The cup ...

**曲娘**：怎么啦？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: What's wrong?

**小叶尼塞**：它看起来很昂贵。\
**Yenisei**: It looks expensive.

**曲娘**：啊，这是别人给我的。我不知道它贵不贵，但它很漂亮，是吧。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: It's a gift I received. I don't know how much it costs, but it's delicate, isn't it?

**小叶尼塞**：是的，它很漂亮。\
**Yenisei**: Yes, it is delicate.

小叶尼塞反复摩挲着陶杯的表面，似乎对这触感爱不释手，又似乎若有所思。\
Yenisei feels compelled to rub the surface of the ceramic cup again, as though she cannot bear to part from it, and loses herself in thought.

**曲娘**：上面画的是鹿蜀，一种祥瑞。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: The pattern is a Lùshǔ, also a kind of Xiángruì.

**曲娘**：你看，它好雄伟的，尾鬃就像傍晚的云霞一样……我很喜欢它，也希望你会喜欢。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: See? It's majestic. The tail is like the sunset clouds. I really like it. I hope you do too.

**小叶尼塞**：是很威风。仔细看，它和职祠里那些斑纹马还有点相近，或许因为都是马一样的动物吧。\
**Yenisei**: Majestic indeed. And it looks a bit like those striped horses in the Zhící. Both of them are similar to horses.

**曲娘**：嗯……但大家还是觉得它们是马，不是吗？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Hmm ... but people still think they are horses. Don't they?

**小叶尼塞**：当然了，我想，它们应该是沛城特有的物种。这很有意思，对我们的风物记录很有帮助。\
**Yenisei**: Sure, they do. I think this species is native to Pèi City. It's an interesting discovery and will help enrich our travel notes.

曲娘低头看向她自己手里的杯子。小叶尼塞能够闻到一股发酵的香气从里面散发，就像格瓦斯，却并没有属于小麦的香甜气息。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ lowers her head to look at the cup in her own hand. Yenisei can smell a fermented aroma emanating from within, like kvass, but without the sweet aroma of wheat.

**曲娘**：她去睡了，那这杯就只好归我啦。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: She is in bed now. I can only drink it for her.

**小叶尼塞**：你的杯子里很香。这个，就是你说的助眠酒吗？\
**Yenisei**: Your drink smells good. Is this the liquor that helps one sleep tight?

**曲娘**：不是哦，这就是普通的浊酒。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Not exactly. It's just unfiltered liquor.

**小叶尼塞**：听起来在你们这里酒有很多的分类。\
**Yenisei**: Sounds like you have a lot of different kinds of liquor here.

**曲娘**：当然呀。酒有很多不同的，有浊酒、清酒、药酒、露酒……好多好多。助眠酒就是一种加了酸枣仁的药酒。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Sure, we do. There are a lot of different liquors. The unfiltered ones, the clear ones, the ones made of herbs, the fine ones ... and on and on. Bedtime liquor is made of herbs with Spine Date Seeds.

**小叶尼塞**：我还以为酒就只是酒而已。至少，在我们那里……没有这么多的分别。\
**Yenisei**: I thought liquor was just liquor. At least there aren't so many types in my hometown.

**曲娘**：好吧，其实我也不明白，为什么酒有这么多不同的名字，却都还是酒。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Well, to be honest, I too have no idea why they are still "liquor," though they have different names.

**曲娘**：如果是因为它们颜色不同，那我换了一件颜色不一样的衣服，我就不叫曲娘了吗？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: If the color is the standard to classify them, then what am I when I'm wearing different colored clothes? Am I not Jiǔ Niángzǐ anymore?

**小叶尼塞**：……哈哈。\
**Yenisei**: Haha.

小叶尼塞一愣，忍不住发笑起来。\
Shocked, Yenisei cannot help but break into a laugh.

看到对方露出了笑容，曲娘眼睛也变得闪闪发亮。她点点头，决定更进一步地说出自己的想法。\
Seeing the other girl smile, Jiǔ Niángzǐ's eyes begin to sparkle. She nods and decides to go one step further and express her thoughts.

**曲娘**：——没错。如果你的同伴变成了马，或者别的什么颜色的动物，那就不是你的同伴了吗？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: That is to say, if your teammates are turned into horses or other animals in different colors, are they not your teammates anymore?

**小叶尼塞**：不是那样的，他们当然……\
**Yenisei**: They are, of course ...

小叶尼塞止住了话头。这样孩子气的对话能让她短暂地笑出声来，但她仍然清醒着，清醒地感受到内心的忧虑。\
Yenisei stops talking. This childish conversation might have caused her to erupt with laughter, but the weight of the situation is still acute, and her worries swell deep within her.

寒夜的鸟鸣轻易盖过了呼吸声。\
The chirping of birds in the cold night gently blankets the sound of her anxious breathing.

**小叶尼塞**：其实我很担心。\
**Yenisei**: I'm worried, actually.

**小叶尼塞**：……或者说不仅仅是担忧，我不知道。\
**Yenisei**: Well, maybe not just worried. I don't know.

**曲娘**：嗯，你看起来，真的很想念你的同伴。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Looks like you really miss your teammates.

**小叶尼塞**：“想念”？\
**Yenisei**: "Miss" them?

**小叶尼塞**：我……不会这样描述这种心情。\
**Yenisei**: I ... I won't use this word to describe my feeling.

**小叶尼塞**：我只是认为，他们会被变成动物，都是由于我指错了方向。\
**Yenisei**: All I'm thinking is, they were turned into animals because I gave them the wrong direction.

**小叶尼塞**：如果——如果他们再也变不回来了，那……\
**Yenisei**: What if ... What if they can't turn back to who they really are ...

这叩问将小叶尼塞自进入这座奇异城市以来的不安，全部表露无遗。\
The frankness of her own inquiry unmasks the long unease Yenisei had been harboring since entering this strange city.

说完，她就屏住呼吸，控制回头去看别斯米尔所在方向的冲动。话语吐露后有一瞬间，她甚至不确定自己身在何处。\
After speaking, she holds her breath and controls the impulse to turn back and look toward Bessmert. For a moment she is no longer even sure of where she is.

**曲娘**：唔。我觉得，不会这样的，事情一定不会变得更糟糕。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: But I don't think that will happen! Things won't get any worse.

**小叶尼塞**：嗯？\
**Yenisei**: Hmm?

**曲娘**：——我觉得，一定会有办法的！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: There must be a way. I promise!

**曲娘**：就像天空出现彩色的云朵，池水变得如醇酒般甘美一样……天地之间，还有许多吉祥的征兆没有显现。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Like the clouds turn colorful, pool water gets sweet like liquor ... There are many signs of auspiciousness. They just need time.

**曲娘**：你想想，也许渊庙是真的呢？也许，也许会有别的办法，让你能认出你的同伴……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Think about it, what if the story about the Yuān Temple is real? Maybe, maybe there will be another way for you to recognize your teammates.

**曲娘**：而且，就算羽人不是祥瑞，这城里却还有别的祥瑞。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Even if the feather man is not a Xiángruì, there are other Xiángruìs in the city.

**曲娘**：总之——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: All in all ...

曲娘试图找到更多的角度来劝说小叶尼塞，却被对方打住。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ racks her brain to find another way to persuade Yenisei, but is stopped by the other girl before she can begin.

尽管双方文化并不相通，但小叶尼塞已从她战栗、短促的话语中感受到一股热流。\
Despite the cultural differences between the two of them, Yenisei feels a surge of warmth from her brief trembling words.

**小叶尼塞**：……谢谢你，曲娘小姐……曲娘。\
**Yenisei**: Thank you, Ms. ... No, Jiǔ Niángzǐ.

**小叶尼塞**：我明白，我明白。\
**Yenisei**: I see what you mean. I really do.

小叶尼塞深吸一口气，然后让松动的心情与话语一同呼出，变成一股白烟飘散。\
Yenisei takes a deep breath and exhales both calm emotions and words together, so that like a light white smoke they soon drift away.

**小叶尼塞**：谢谢你。\
**Yenisei**: Thank you.

**曲娘**：这有什么！我一定会帮你们的！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: It's nothing! I will definitely help you!

**曲娘**：哦，我口袋里还有一些干酸枣仁。你快把水喝掉，我去给你泡酸枣水，也有助眠效果——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Oh, here are some other Spine Date seeds. Drink the water, and I'll go make you a cup of tea with the seeds. It also helps you sleep ...

曲娘忙忙碌碌地站起来，在身侧的袋子里不停往外掏着什么，一边催促着小叶尼塞赶快喝掉手中的水。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ shoots up to immediately rummage around in the bag beside her as she urges Yenisei to drain what is left in her cup.

小叶尼塞于是饮尽了冰凉但甘甜的清水，将漂亮杯子递还——\
Yenisei drinks down all of the cold, sweet water and hands the still-compelling cup back to her ...

然后注视曲娘踩上门廊，小步跑着回到大厅里去了。\
She then watches Jiǔ Niángzǐ step onto the porch and run back into the hall at a trot.

**小叶尼塞**：……呼……\
**Yenisei**: *exhales*

她长舒一口气，回头望向干燥的夜空。\
She takes a long breath and turns to look at the arid night sky.

即使陌生的城市也与草原享有同一片月色。\
It seems even in a strange city like this, she can enjoy the same bright moonlight as the steppes.

## NS-12 倾杯舞 / Dancing Dolls

夜幕早已沉沉地降下，即使喝下了据说有助眠功效的茶水，小叶尼塞也始终没能睡着。\
The curtain of night has already fallen, but even after drinking another cup of tea promised to induce drowsiness, Yenisei finds that sleep evades her.

按理说，常人在她们先前那样累重的疲倦之下，得到机会便迅速入睡，几乎是一种本能。可对她来说却并非如此。\
In theory, someone so heavily fatigued, should fall fast asleep the very moment the opportunity presents itself. But not for her.

相反，她满怀心事，在黑暗中不需费力就保持着清醒。\
On the contrary, her mind, so sick with worries, seems to run faster now than ever in the stillness of night.

**小叶尼塞**：……\
**Yenisei**: ...

**别斯米尔**：……\
**Bessmert**: ...

**小叶尼塞**：呼……\
**Yenisei**: *sighs*

她起身，离开榻上，轻手轻脚地走向楼下。\
She stands up, steps away from the couch, and treads lightly down the stairs.

因为连梦境也不收留，除了游荡之外，她无处可去。\
Unwelcome in even her own dreams, she wanders around without direction.

**小叶尼塞**：花园在……下楼后，穿过主厅……\
**Yenisei**: The yard ... Go downstairs and through the main hall ...

她在黑暗中摸索着栏杆，踩上下楼的阶梯。\
Groping around for the railing in the darkness, she walks up and then down the steps.

一级，一级。随她向下的，还有悉窣的响动，如同挥之不去的清醒一样在黑夜里包裹了她。\
One step, another step ... As she descends, a rustling sound envelops her in the darkness, like an indelible point that demands her whole focus.

**小叶尼塞**：……嗯？有声音……\
**Yenisei**: Hmm? What's that sound ...

**小叶尼塞**：在哪里——\
**Yenisei**: Where does it come from?

**？？？**：两岸山花——似雪开——家家春酒——满银杯——\
**???**: By the flowers in the snow, raise a toast and don't say no.

**小叶尼塞**：……\
**Yenisei**: ...

**小叶尼塞**：那是……？谁在——\
**Yenisei**: Who is it? Someone's ...

**小叶尼塞**：……唱歌？\
**Yenisei**: ... singing?

不知不觉间，她离开二楼，循着声音踏进了整洁而空旷的酒坊大堂。\
Without realizing it, she departs the second floor and follows the sound into the spacious hall of the tavern.

月光扑撒，歌声悠然，而眼前真正是从未想象过的一幕。\
With the cascading moonlight and melodious singing, the scene laid out before her is one that defies description.

**？？？**：两岸山花——似雪开——家家春酒——满银杯——\
**???**: By the flowers in the snow, raise a toast and don't say no.

**小叶尼塞**：……什么……\
**Yenisei**: What ...

**小叶尼塞**：——这些斑纹马，怎么会……在发光？！\
**Yenisei**: The striped horses—how come they are ... glowing?!

**小叶尼塞**：……这……\
**Yenisei**: What ...

**小叶尼塞**：这都是什么东西？！\
**Yenisei**: What on earth is happening?!

**小叶尼塞**：我——\
**Yenisei**: I ...

**小叶尼塞**：天哪。\
**Yenisei**: Gosh!

那有着红色鬃毛与发光斑纹的“马”站在院中，向她回过头来。\
With its red mane and luminous stripes, the "horse" stands there in the courtyard and turns gently toward her.

歌声仍在持续，把小叶尼塞几乎凝滞在原地。她用力转身，想要逃离声音的包围，才发觉自己早已受到了围困。\
The singing continues, almost freezing Yenisei in place. She turns around sharply, trying to escape the sound, only to realize that she has already been surrounded ...

——被一群刚才还在酒碗中的木头小人。\
… by the group of wooden dolls who were in her cup earlier.

**木头小人群**：家家春酒——满银杯——\
**Wooden Dolls**: By the flowers in the snow, raise a toast and don't say no.

**小叶尼塞**：——？\
**Yenisei**: ...?

**木头小人群**：请满上，请满上！\
**Wooden Dolls**: Fill your cup, fill your cup!

**小叶尼塞**：它们这是……邀请我喝酒……？\
**Yenisei**: Are they ... asking me to drink?

**小叶尼塞**：……曲娘——曲娘在哪儿？？\
**Yenisei**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ! Where are you?

**小叶尼塞**：她会不会——\
**Yenisei**: Is she ...

现在，就连原本浸在院外河水中的木头小人也缓缓地爬上了岸。\
Now, the wooden dolls, originally submerged in the stream in the courtyard, have begun to climb up the bank.

它们围着她，转圈，欢唱，扭动，身体明显有着木头不应拥有的柔软程度。\
They surround her, spinning, singing, and contorting, with bodies clearly possessing a flexibility beyond what wood should possess.

依靠着这种柔软，它们不断向小叶尼塞举起手中满盈的杯盏。\
Using this odd flexibility, they repeatedly lift their full cups toward Yenisei.

**木头小人群**：莫辞，莫辞！\
**Wooden Dolls**: No turning down, no turning down!

**小叶尼塞**：不——\
**Yenisei**: No ...

本应热情的邀请，在这样的浓夜中越发显露出它的不合时宜。\
This invitation, perhaps initially hospitable, turns increasingly creepy in the dark night.

做出选择几乎不用太多思考，小叶尼塞跳出包围圈，向着院子另一头，也向着水缸的所在跑去。\
Making a choice now requires next to no thought. Yenisei jumps out from their enclosure and runs toward the other end of the yard—toward the water jar.

好在，她的确清晰记得曲娘指过的位置。\
Fortunately, she clearly remembered the location pointed out by Jiǔ Niángzǐ.

**小叶尼塞**：不能回楼上去，得引开它们——\
**Yenisei**: I can't go back to my room. Need to lead them away.

木头小人们依然欢唱，以为这是一场追逐的游戏。\
The wooden dolls still sing happily, as if they are only playing a game of tag.

**小叶尼塞**：——呃！\
**Yenisei**: Ugh!

木头小人的攻击毫无章法，歌声刺耳，屡次带偏小叶尼塞对周围环境的准确感知。\
The wooden dolls stage a disorganized offensive, with a piercing song that twists Yenisei's perception of her surroundings.

她只能站在水缸周围，不断后退，几乎已经被逼至绝路。\
She can only stand by the water jar, in a constant retreat, consciously nearing a dead end.

**木头小人群**：咯——咯——\
**Wooden Dolls**: *sound of wood rubbing*

**木头小人群**：咚、咚、咚。\
**Wooden Dolls**: Clack. Clack. Clack.

**小叶尼塞**：……不……\
**Yenisei**: No ...

**小叶尼塞**：不行，还要——还要再远。\
**Yenisei**: Can't stop here. I must go ... farther.

**小叶尼塞**：……过来！来这边！\
**Yenisei**: Come here! This way!

木头没有耳朵，自然听不见，也听不懂。\
The wooden figures have no ears, so it seems unlikely they hear or understand her.

所幸，它们的确受到吸引，继续向前跳动。\
Nonetheless, they are lured in, leaping forward with strange enthusiasm.

永不疲倦，充满热情。如同它们始终被高高举起，不停洒出又重新满溢的杯盏。\
Never tiring. Just like those cups, always lifted high, constantly spilling and overflowing.

**木头小人群**：咯——咯咯——\
**Wooden Dolls**: *sound of wood rubbing*

**？？？**：——\
**???**: ...

看似粗糙的木头造物比人更早警觉第三者的介入。\
It seems these crude wooden creations are quick to be alert to sudden interlopers.

它们立刻停止对小叶尼塞的围攻，突兀地转投院中树木伫立的方向。\
They immediately stop their siege of Yenisei and abruptly turn toward the tall trees in the courtyard.

**小叶尼塞**：……嗯？它们是要……去哪儿？\
**Yenisei**: Hmm? Where are they going?

**木头小人群**：咚！咚！\
**Wooden Dolls**: Clack! Clack!

**木头小人群**：咚咚！咚咚！

逼迫的节奏比先前走得更重更急，它们几步蹦跳，去往树下——\
The coercive rhythm plays heavier and faster than before, as they jump a few more hops toward the bottom of the tree—

**？？？**：……退！\
**???**: Be off!

骨杖飞出，酒水泼散，木头小人应声破碎成块。\
A wand of bone flies out from the darkness, scattering liquor and shattering the wooden figures into pieces.

**？？？**：……\
**???**: ...

一切似乎就这样归于平静，结束得如同转机出现一般突然。\
Serenity comes back to the scene, the end coming as swiftly as its beginning.

**？？？**：这造物……\
**???**: They are conjured ...

**？？？**：竟如此羸弱。\
**???**: ... so feebly.

**小叶尼塞**：谁——是谁？！\
**Yenisei**: Who ... Who is it?!

**？？？**：……嗯？\
**???**: Hmm?

**？？？**：只你一人？\
**???**: It's you?

**小叶尼塞**：……是你？你是偷走我们马匹的羽人——\
**Yenisei**: You? The feather man who stole our horses!

**？？？**：罢了，也须得与我走。\
**???**: No matter. You're leaving with me.

**小叶尼塞**：别过来！这到底是怎么回事——\
**Yenisei**: Leave me alone! What is going on?

**？？？**：噤声。此地危险，多说无益。\
**???**: Silence. It's dangerous here, and words are no help to us.

不由分说，巨鸟将小叶尼塞的双臂抓起，飞快带离了院落。\
Without hesitation, the giant bird grabs Yenisei's arms quickly, lifting her up and away from the courtyard.

她的挣扎在呼啸的天空下愈发徒劳无功。\
Her struggle proves futile in the howling wind.

**小叶尼塞**：啊——！\
**Yenisei**: Aaaah!

振翅的响动与尖叫逐渐远离，只留下此处院中一片狼藉。\
The sound of flapping wings punctuated by the shrieking girl gradually fades in the distance, leaving only a disordered mess as evidence in the courtyard.

清晨，曲娘迈入院子里的狼藉中。\
In the morning, Jiǔ Niángzǐ walks into the shambolic scene.

一个完整的木头小人正蹦跳着，将它同类的残骸拢作一团。\
A still-intact wooden doll bounces around, gathering the remains of its kind into a ball.

**木头小人**：——兄兄，缺了一只手，拼不回来了。\
