**Wooden Doll**: Alas, alas. An arm is missing. Can't put them together, anymore.

**曲娘**：……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: ...

**木头小人**：来晚了，你。\
**Wooden Doll**: Late. You are late.

**曲娘**：怎么回事？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: What's going on?

**曲娘**：是让你们看家，不是让你们拆家。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I told you to keep the house, not to tear it down.

**木头小人**：只是想尽地主之谊，请喝酒。\
**Wooden Doll**: Being, a, good host. Offering, a drink.

**曲娘**：你们要请谁喝？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Offer a drink to whom?

**曲娘**：昨天来的两位，还在楼上睡着呀……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Those two ladies should be soundly asleep upstairs.

**木头小人**：一个，晚上在楼下。那个鸟人也在。\
**Wooden Doll**: One, was downstairs, at night. Bird man, with her.

**曲娘**：什么鸟人……？你是说羽人？他来过了？！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Bird man ... You mean that feather man? He had been here?!

**曲娘**：他来做什么？他都不是祥瑞，也没有在做好事。不许你们请他喝酒！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: What was he doing here? He's not even a Xiángruì, nor is he doing anything good. Do not offer a drink to him!

**曲娘**：哼，要让我见到他，我一定——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Humph. If I were the one treating him, I would ...

**木头小人**：他把一个带走了。\
**Wooden Doll**: He took one, with him.

**曲娘**：——等等，什么？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I would ... I, wait, what?

**曲娘**：谁被他带走了？？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Took whom with him??

**木头小人**：绛色的。茶色带走了绛色。\
**Wooden Doll**: The scarlet. The brown, took away, the scarlet.

**曲娘**：什么茶色和……绛色？什么颜色？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Brown? Scarlet? What color is that?

**曲娘**：唉，我怎么越听越糊涂了。下次我一定给你们多做一张嘴，你看看，这都是在说什么呀——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: *sighs* You're just confusing me. I'll make you one more mouth next time. What on earth are you talking about.

**别斯米尔**：嘶……\
**Bessmert**: Hiss ...

曲娘闻声回头，看见年长的女性跌倒在门槛上。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ turns around to see Bessmert fall over the threshold.

她赶紧提着裙角迎过去，木头小人正好蹦跳着，躲进她身后。\
She quickly approaches with her skirt held up, and the wooden doll jumping up and down, hiding behind her.

**曲娘**：请小心一些！来，我扶你。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Be careful! I'll help you.

**别斯米尔**：谢谢，谢谢您。\
**Bessmert**: Thank you. Thank you so much.

**别斯米尔**：小叶尼塞，她不在楼上，也不在院子里吗？\
**Bessmert**: Where's Yenisei? Did you see her upstairs or in the yard?

**曲娘**：是你红头发的朋友吗？我没看见她。她是不是先出门了？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Are you talking about your red-haired friend? Did she go out?

**别斯米尔**：不，不会的。她如果要出门去，一定会告诉我。或者至少通过您告诉我。\
**Bessmert**: No, not very likely. She would have told me if she was going out. Or at least ask someone to pass on the message.

**别斯米尔**：您真的没有见到她吗？\
**Bessmert**: Did you really not see her today?

曲娘绞尽脑汁地回忆了一下，声音更加认真而坚定。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ racks her brain, her voice coming out serious and resolute.

**曲娘**：没有，早上真的没有呀。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: No, not this morning, no.

**别斯米尔**：……\
**Bessmert**: ...

**别斯米尔**：失踪案。城里的失踪案，是不是也都是这样的情况？\
**Bessmert**: The missing persons cases! Is this how they happened?!

**曲娘**：我、我不知道，里正没有和我讲过……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I-I don't know. Lǐzhèng didn't make it in time to tell me the details ...

别斯米尔陷入了沉默。这是她难以接受的损失。\
Bessmert falls into silence. This is a loss that she finds difficult to accept.

**别斯米尔**：如果，只是如果，这就是所谓的失踪案，那也一定会留下什么蛛丝马迹。\
**Bessmert**: If—I'm only saying—if this is another missing case, there must be a clue or two telling us what happened.

**别斯米尔**：请您帮忙看一看，院子里有没有留下什么东西？她不是在二楼被掠走的，否则我不会一点声音也没听见。\
**Bessmert**: Could you please look around and see if she has left anything in the yard? She must have been taken from there, or I would have definitely heard the noises.

别斯米尔着急地握住了曲娘的手。那是两双略有风霜的手，一双曾饱经日晒，另一双，兴许做过不少手工活儿。\
Bessmert anxiously grasps Jiǔ Niángzǐ's hands. Their hands are equally coarse—one pair exposed to age and sun, and the other exposed to grueling work.

**曲娘**：你先别急，我们可以去找里正——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Stay calm. Let's go ask Lǐzhèng.

**别斯米尔**：等等……\
**Bessmert**: Wait ...

**曲娘**：怎么了？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: What's wrong?

**别斯米尔**：神秘术。这院子里有使用过神秘术的痕迹。\
**Bessmert**: I sense an arcane energy. Someone cast a skill in the yard.

**别斯米尔**：跟着我。\
**Bessmert**: Follow me.

**曲娘**：你要去哪儿？你看不见呀，你告诉我，我带你去。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Where are you going? You can't see! Just tell me. I'll take you there.

**别斯米尔**：不，请跟着我就好。\
**Bessmert**: No, please follow me.

**曲娘**：再往前走就是水缸了，昨晚我来这里打过水。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: You're heading toward the water jar. I was here last night to get water.

**别斯米尔**：就在水缸的附近。我能很清晰地感受到。\
**Bessmert**: It's somewhere close to the water jar. I sense it clearly.

别斯米尔蹚过溪水，在水缸斜前方停住。她蹲下身，在面前地上散落的树叶中，准确地摸出一样东西。\
Bessmert wades through the stream and stops in front of the water jar. She crouches down to find something among the scattered leaves in front of her.

**曲娘**：这是……一根骨头？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Is this a bone?

**别斯米尔**：那就对了。里正说，羽人也拿着像骨头的术杖。而小叶尼塞看见巨鸟也有这样的东西。\
**Bessmert**: That makes sense. Lǐzhèng told us that the feather man uses a bone wand. Yenisei also saw something similar in that giant bird's hand when we faced him outside the city.

**曲娘**：我就知道！这下我们有证据了，我们可以——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I knew it! Now, we have the proof, we can ...

**别斯米尔**：这不够。而且小叶尼塞失踪了。\
**Bessmert**: No, it's not enough. And Yenisei is missing.

**曲娘**：为什么？我觉得这就够了呀，羽人的骨杖都掉在这里了，这说明他来过，而且你的同伴不见了，那不就说明是他干的吗？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Why not enough? He left his bone wand, which means he was here before. And your friend is missing! Still not enough to prove his guilt?

**别斯米尔**：但只有小叶尼塞先前亲眼看见了巨鸟，巨鸟的画像也是她提供的。\
**Bessmert**: But only Yenisei knows what the giant bird looks like. She also drew the picture of that bird.

**别斯米尔**：没有她，我们依然无法证明，巨鸟与羽人就是同一人……\
**Bessmert**: Without her, we cannot confirm that the feather man and the giant bird are the same creature.

**曲娘**：我听不懂……是说就算我们找到了他的骨头，也不能用这个证明任何东西吗？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I don't understand. You're saying that, even if we have his bone wand, we can't prove anything?

**别斯米尔**：……是的，没错。\
**Bessmert**: Exactly.

**曲娘**：但是，我觉得不需要想这么多。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: But, I think you're overthinking.

别斯米尔稍微抬起头来，用动作传达茫然。\
Bessmert raises her head slightly, conveying her confusion in unsubtle movements.

**曲娘**：就是——就是这个证据够不够，能不能证明，不是我们说了算的。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I-I mean, whether enough or not, it's not up to us, right?

**曲娘**：我也不懂，但感觉，这样不对……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I know nothing about the law. It ... it just doesn't feel right.

女孩的声音渐渐小了下去，终于也生出一点不确定的犹疑。\
The girl's voice quietens down, giving rise to her own hesitation.

**曲娘**：……我只是觉得，我们应该做些什么。因为你很难过。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I'm just thinking ... we should do something, because you are sad.

但别斯米尔已经明白了。\
But Bessmert already understands.

**别斯米尔**：……\
**Bessmert**: ...

**别斯米尔**：您说得对。那我们——\
**Bessmert**: You have a point. Then we ...

**曲娘**：嗯！我们先去职祠吧，今天里正也会在，他要跟我说些度朔节的事……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Let's go to the Zhící now! Lǐzhèng will be there today. He is supposed to tell me something about the Dùshuò Festival.

**曲娘**：我们正好可以告诉他。里正会有办法的！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Let's tell him what happened today. He will know what to do!

**别斯米尔**：……好。\
**Bessmert**: Sure.

她们决定离开酒坊，前往职祠。别斯米尔收好骨杖，亦步亦趋地跟随曲娘的脚步。\
They decided to head towards the Zhící. Bessmert puts away the bone wand and follows Jiǔ Niángzǐ's footsteps carefully, one at a time.

留下木头小人伫立原地，与另一些残骸一起。\
They leave the wooden doll standing in place, a sentinel atop the rest of the debris.

## NS-13 葛生 / Gesheng

里正翻阅着往年的年节用度账册，心下踌躇。\
Lǐzhèng is flipping through annual expense account records from previous years, worries written on his heart and wizened face.

曲娘会准时过来点卯，而他需要在对方到达之前，做出一个决定。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ is sure to report for duty on time, and he must have a decision ready before she does.

**里正**：……往年走吉与跃桥，所用年节动物，皆不超过三只。\
**Lizheng**: In past years, the Festive Animals used in the Fortune Walk and the Bridge Leap were less than three.

**里正**：“一牛，一羊，一驴，未有例外。”\
**Lizheng**: "A cow, a goat, and a donkey. Without exception."

**里正**：收成愈差，城内少有可用的青壮成驴，以至于用马代替。可现今——\
**Lizheng**: The poorer the harvest, the less food for the animals and less well-fed donkeys, so people had to use horses instead. However ...

**里正**：即使庆贺执徐生辰，职祠之内的年节动物也过多了。其中还有为人所变，断不可一视同仁。\
**Lizheng**: Aren't there too many Festive Animals this time? Even if it is for celebrating the birth of Zhíxú? Not to mention some of them are transformed from humans! We shall act prudently.

**里正**：若要取消跃桥之仪，岁除后便是朔日，须得尽早决断……\
**Lizheng**: If we have to cancel the ceremony, we must make the decision before New Year's Eve ...

他在手中账册的空白处，写上“走吉”、“跃桥”几字，又洗墨沾红，轻轻用圈勾住。一个提醒。\
He writes the words "Fortune Walk" and "Bridge Leap" into a blank space on the account records in his hand, then circles them in red ink to serve as his reminder.

写下这些，里正思索着，将视线移向一旁的“巨鸟画像”。\
As he does, he ponders and shifts his gaze nearby to the portrait of a giant bird.

**里正**：……\
**Lizheng**: ...

**里正**：巨鸟……羽人……\
**Lizheng**: A giant bird ... a feather man ...

**里正**：偏生是在这年节关头……烦扰从来都接踵而至。\
**Lizheng**: *sighs* There is always trouble around New Years.

这一声并非常见鸟雀扑扇翅膀，而是真正庞大的野外猛禽旋临的声响。\
Suddenly, there comes a loud fluttering of wings. This sound is not like one of common birds flapping, but is rather a droning hazardous sound the kind of a titanic bird of prey approaching.

**里正**：……嗯？\
**Lizheng**: Hmm?

一个长着翅膀的影子，覆盖了桌面的画像。\
A winged shadow covers the portrait on the desk.

里正转头看清来者，面上只剩下愕然与发自内心的疑惑。\
Lǐzhèng turns his head to see the visitor clearly, meeting it with a look of shock and heart-shaking doubt on his face.

**里正**：是你……？！\
**Lizheng**: You?!

来者正是画像上的巨鸟，或者说羽人。\
The visitor is no less than the very giant bird or feathered man depicted in that portrait.

他飞进来的动作，若入无人之境一般流畅自然，就连职祠的护卫也未被惊动。\
He glides in as smoothly and naturally as if he were entering an open glade. It seems as though the guards of the Zhící were unaware of his arrival entirely.

**？？？**：你便是……掌事之人？\
**???**: You … Are you responsible for this place?

**？？？**：可上次我所见的明明是……另一人……\
**???**: It was ... someone else when I last visited.

**？？？**：……唉。\
**???**: *sighs*

**？？？**：罢了，我有要事相告。若是再不阻止，万事休矣。\
**???**: No matter. I have an urgent matter to discuss, or it will be too late.

不待里正反应，一只模样前所未见的马就跟在他身后闯进来了。\
Without waiting for Lǐzhèng to react, a bizarre horse, or something like it, rushes in behind him.

这马的鬃毛与尾巴都是红色，身上亦有虎皮一样的纹路，颇为罕见。\
The horse's mane and tail are both red, and it bears a tiger-stripe pattern along its body, the combination of which produces a truly incomparable sight.

**斑纹马？**：咴——\
**Striped Horse?**: *neighs*

它踏步上前，使里正能够更清楚地看见自己，动作间似乎有着某种灵性。\
It steps forward, allowing Lǐzhèng to see it clearly. It suggests a great sort of intelligence in its movements.

而羽人——羽人只是并拢翅膀降落。狭窄的方室令他颇有些无处伸展的感觉。\
As for the feather man—he simply folds his wings and lands. The narrow space forces him to pinch himself tightly into the cramped room.

里正也因此觉察到对方的一丝局促。\
Lǐzhèng notices a hint of embarrassment in his visitor as a result.

**葛天**：我乃葛天。此行是为告知，那酒坊娘子以术法使人变为鹿蜀形貌，需得尽快阻止，以免贻害更广。\
**Getian**: I'm Gětiān, and I'm here to advise caution. The lady owner of the tavern can turn people into Lùshǔ. She needs to be stopped, or more people will suffer.

**葛天**：她骨相过轻，形状尚在生长，也因此作为不定，恐为祸患。\
**Getian**: She has extremely light bones, which means she's still in the stage of development. She might be unstable, hence a danger to keep in the city.

**里正**：——你指的，难道是曲娘？\
**Lizheng**: You are referring to ... Jiǔ Niángzǐ?

**葛天**：正是。\
**Getian**: Precisely.

**里正**：骨相……难道，你是可识骨相的骊山姥？但你的身形，分明不似黎山老母……\
**Lizheng**: Bones ... Are you the Goddess of Lí Mountain that can read one's bones? But you don't look like her at all ...

**葛天**：……\
**Getian**: ...

短暂的沉默表示了葛天对话题转变速度预计不足的错愕。\
The brief silence conveys Gětiān's astonishment at the unexpected change in topic.

**葛天**：我自然并非骊山姥。\
**Getian**: I am no Goddess of Lí Mountain.

**里正**：那这些言辞从你口中说来，岂不无人相信。你还不若声称自己是骊山姥。\
**Lizheng**: Then your words have no weight at all. You should have claimed to be her.

**里正**：而且……“骊山姥”啊，且看看周围吧。\
**Lizheng**: Besides, "Goddess of Lí Mountain," take a look around you.

虽然疑惑，葛天还是依言环视四周，只看到了一些画了相同鸟类图腾的纸张。部分纸张上面甚至墨迹未干，显然是新落的手笔。\
Though puzzled, Gětiān looks around as advised, only to find some paper with the same bird totems painted on it. Some of the papers even bear ink stains yet to dry, indicating their recentness.

**葛天**：你说的是……这些门笺？\
**Getian**: You mean ... these paper-cutouts?

**葛天**：人面，鸟身，红尾。你们画这些——\
**Getian**: A man-faced bird with a red tail. You're drawing me ...

就算辨认出画上的形象，他也并不认为这些图画的“供奉”有任何必要。\
Even though he recognizes the image in the painting, the idea of being "worshipped" through such artwork comes across as quite unnecessary.

**斑纹马？**：咴？\
**Striped Horse?**: *neighs*

马蹄不耐地点了点地，似乎急急催促着两人的对话。只可惜此刻无人在意。\
Horseshoes impatiently clank on the ground, seeming to urge a sense of haste. This prompting though goes unnoticed.

**葛天**：我并非祥瑞，此类筹措或祈祷，毫无必要。\
**Getian**: But I'm not a Xiángruì. These paper-cuts won't send me your prayers and wishes.

**里正**：……这些并非向祥瑞祈愿的门笺，而是你的通缉令。\
**Lizheng**: They're not paper-cutouts for worshiping the Xiángruì, but wanted posters, and you are wanted.

葛天怔愣一瞬，似乎不能理解里正的话。门笺也好，通缉令也罢，皆是人世间才有的繁杂之物。\
Gětiān is stunned for a moment, as if unable to understand Lǐzhèng's words. Whether paper cuttings or wanted notices, they are complex things found only in the world of the mundane.

所以他决定简单地跳过，继续自己此行的目的。\
As such, he opts to ignore them for now and continue on with the purpose of his journey.

**葛天**：无论如何，现在捉拿曲娘最为要紧。正是她造成了城中的这些失踪案件。\
**Getian**: The most important thing is to find Jiǔ Niángzǐ. She's the culprit of the missing persons cases in the city.

**里正**：呵。\
**Lizheng**: Humph.

**里正**：我还猜想，你是前来自首或交涉。如今看来，却是我想多了。\
**Lizheng**: I thought you came here to confess or make peace, but it seems not.

**里正**：主动前来攀咬曲娘，你是全然不知，自己才是头号疑犯啊。\
**Lizheng**: You come to defame Jiǔ Niángzǐ, while being ignorant of the fact that you're the top suspect.

得知真正被怀疑的对象并非自己指认的曲娘，葛天陷入了更深的疑惑。\
Upon learning that the culprit is not in fact the one he identified as Jiǔ Niángzǐ, Gětiān falls into an even deeper confusion.

人世的许多事情都超出了他的理解范围。\
Many things outside the mountains are beyond his understanding.

**葛天**：这与我何干？\
**Getian**: How am I related to this?

**里正**：我们数次收到人口失踪上报，次次与你现身于城内，携动物来到职祠的时日关联。\
**Lizheng**: Every time a disappearance was reported, you were witnessed bringing animals to the Zhící.

**葛天**：不，这是污蔑。当时那位执礼应知晓我的来意。\
**Getian**: No, the nature of my visit has been taken wrongly. The Zhílǐ there knew what I came for.

**里正**：呵，当我们赶往职祠时，你早已只身离去，不见踪影。\
**Lizheng**: Humph. When we arrived at the Zhící, you had already fled without a trace.

**里正**：无人为她作证，她自是被法曹视为胡言乱语，现已回乡去也。\
**Lizheng**: No one could testify in front of the Fǎcáo for her, so her words were considered nonsense. Now, she has returned to her hometown.

听到此处，葛天反而认为事情明了，舒出一口气来。\
Upon hearing this, Gětiān breathes a sigh of relief.

**葛天**：若非此事突然，我本就不会来到城中，自然没有久留的道理。\
**Getian**: I wouldn't have shown up in the city if not for the urgent matters. What's the purpose of lingering around when my business is done here?

**葛天**：况且，咽下神秘术随性施为的苦果，本应是职祠之责。\
**Getian**: Besides, the Zhící allowed arcane skills to be cast without restrictions in the city, so it is your responsibility to bear the consequences of such negligence.

**里正**：好啊，你伶牙俐齿……\
**Lizheng**: You're very articulate ...

**里正**：昨日正有两位胡商来到沛城，向我们提供了一些线索。\
**Lizheng**: But how can you explain the testimony provided by the two foreign merchants?

**里正**：而这些线索，都指向你。\
**Lizheng**: All roads are leading to you.

**葛天**：……\
**Getian**: ...

**葛天**：是，正是那两位胡人。\
**Getian**: Yes. The two foreigners.

**里正**：……你认罪了？\
**Lizheng**: ... Do you confess?

**葛天**：这是我此行要告知你的另一件事。\
**Getian**: They are the other reason why I'm here.

**葛天**：那两人其中之一，现下就在此处。她可以向你解释。\
**Getian**: One of the two is here with us. She can explain to you.

葛天侧身，让出身旁的红鬃马驹，示意给里正。\
Gětiān leans over and asks the red-maned horse beside him to signal to Lǐzhèng.

**斑纹马？**：咴咴——\
**Striped Horse?**: *neighs*

被冷落许久的奇异马驹，好像知道自己终于能够派上用场一般，迈开蹄子走上前去。\
The strange horse, after being ignored for a long time, seems to acknowledge that it can now finally make itself useful and steps forward on proud hooves.

**里正**：等等，你说它是谁？\
**Lizheng**: Wait, you mean she is ...

不等里正反应，葛天便挥动翅膀，将案上茶水掀翻在地。\
Before Lǐzhèng can react, Gětiān flaps his wings, causing the tea on the table to flip onto the ground.

红鬃的马驹闻声再次迈步，转向石砖被打湿的位置。\
The red-maned horse takes another step forward and turns to the spot where the stone bricks have been wetted.

浑浊的茶水很快滑入室内石砖的缝隙之中，马驹的倒影在水渍汇集最多的部分闪现。\
The tea seeps out over the interior stone, forming a pool in a small indentation. There the reflection of the horse appears in a flash.

**葛天**：稍待，请看这茶水泼过的地方。\
**Getian**: I ask for your patience. Please look at the water on the floor.

**里正**：嗯？\
**Lizheng**: Hmm?

里正也看向葛天视线所在的地方。那里仍然是地砖与逐渐消失的马驹倒影。\
Lǐzhèng looks towards the spot Gětiān's line of sight indicates, where the fading reflection remains.

水痕只是更快向室内低洼不平的位置汇集，最后隐没在石砖下方。\
But the liquid drains out along the low-lying and uneven floor, and eventually disappears into the crevices of the stone bricks.

显然，茶水只是茶水。\
The tea, it seems, is just tea.

**葛天**：……\
**Getian**: ...

**里正**：……这是何意？\
**Lizheng**: What is this for?

**里正**：难道因为我没有恭敬待你，邀你坐下，再向你奉茶？\
**Lizheng**: Is this a demonstration of your discontent, because I didn't treat you as a guest, offer you a seat, and give you a cup of tea?

**葛天**：不是……\
**Getian**: No ...

**葛天**：这不应当。\
**Getian**: This should not be.

他几乎是喃喃自语着转向身边的红尾马驹，语带疑惑。\
He appears to murmur to himself and turns to the red-tailed horse beside him, his words muddled with confusion.

**葛天**：为何——为何你未像先前那样，使出神秘术来？\
**Getian**: Why ... why didn't your arcane skill work this time?

**葛天**：……不。还是说，需得干净的水才行？\
**Getian**: Or must it be clean water to reflect it?

**葛天**：可河水不洁，应当没有这样的限制。你之前究竟是怎样做到的？\
**Getian**: No. The water in the river was no cleaner. How did you do it earlier?

经历了先前的一系列荒诞对峙，即使是见识广博如里正也已完全失去耐心。\
Having now weathered this series of absurd confrontations to his limits, the cultured manner of Lǐzhèng breaks along with his patience.

**里正**：……\
**Lizheng**: ...

**里正**：来人——\
**Lizheng**: Guards!

**里正**：将他拿下！\
**Lizheng**: Catch him!

葛天被突如其来迅速的脚步声吓得立刻飞了起来。\
Gětiān is startled by the sudden and rapid footsteps, and immediately flies upward.

狭窄的方室之中，他翅膀的影子显得异常庞大，连红鬃的马驹也向阴影范围之外退去。\
Within the narrow chamber, the shadow of his wings appears unusually large, and even the red-haired horse retreats beyond the shadow's range.

**葛天**：你这是何意！\
**Getian**: What is the meaning of this?!

**里正**：你是疑犯。因此——\
**Lizheng**: You're a suspect. That's ...

**葛天**：我所知，已倾数相告，你们不去捉拿曲娘，反而在这里纠缠于我？\
**Getian**: What I know, I told you truthfully. Why are you troubling me instead of going after Jiǔ Niángzǐ?

**葛天**：找干净的水来，我再证明给你——\
**Getian**: Find some clean water. I will prove it to you ...

**里正**：不必。束手就擒即可。\
**Lizheng**: That's enough. Surrender now.

**葛天**：……我不会同你们动手，但你们也抓不得我。\
**Getian**: I will not fight you. But neither will you have me.

**里正**：唉。\
**Lizheng**: *sighs*

**里正**：注意保护那红尾的马，那可能是受害者。\
**Lizheng**: Be careful not to hurt that horse. It might be one of the victims.

葛天振翅飞出，逃到院中。\
Gětiān flaps his wings and flies out, escaping to the courtyard.

但他并未直接离开，而是不断躲避着攻击，在院中徘徊。即使这冲突已经令他负伤。\
He does not leave immediately, instead deftly avoiding the attacks of the guards as he flits around the courtyard. Despite the fact that this brief conflict has already left him injured.

**里正**：你的力气总会耗尽的。\
**Lizheng**: Your strength will eventually run out.

**葛天**：何须走到这一步？\
**Getian**: Is this necessary?

**葛天**：仅仅找来清水与我，我就能向你证明曲娘的过错。\
**Getian**: Find me the clean water, and I will show you what Jiǔ Niángzǐ has done.

**里正**：我又如何知道，你的“证明”，不是你用神秘术伪造的结果呢？\
**Lizheng**: How will I know if you're using your arcane skill to fake the result?

**里正**：说到底，我们了解你指认的“罪魁”曲娘，却对你一无所知。\
**Lizheng**: The truth is, we know the girl very well, but nothing about you.

**葛天**：……\
**Getian**: ...

**里正**：甚至于在城内有人失踪前，你都未曾入过沛城。\
**Lizheng**: No one had gone missing in Pèi City before you showed up.

**里正**：我们又要从何处判断你的话语，真实与否？\
**Lizheng**: So how can we trust you or your "proof"?

葛天轻轻摇头，垂下了翅膀。\
Gětiān gently shakes his head and lowers his wings.

**里正**：更何况，你说自己并非祥瑞——\
**Lizheng**: And you have denied that you're a Xiángruì ...

**葛天**：……呼。\
**Getian**: *sighs*

**葛天**：的确，我并非祥瑞，此前也从未来到城中。\
**Getian**: It is true that I am not a Xiángruì, nor have I ever visited here.

**葛天**：因为我本就不愿下山。\
**Getian**: I never wanted to leave the mountain.

他的动作令翅膀上的伤痕被明确地展示。一种代表休战相谈的姿态。\
His movements make the wounds on his wings visible. His stance is low and reverent, suggesting his willingness to discuss a truce.

里正也因这动作而犹疑，抬手叫停了涌上来的职祠护卫。\
Lǐzhèng hesitates and, as a result, raises his hand to stop the storming advance of the guards.

**里正**：你却还是做了这样的事。\
**Lizheng**: But you still left.

**葛天**：为何我一定要来到人世当中呢？\
**Getian**: I really shouldn't have come to the human world.

**里正**：……你这话是什么意思？\
**Lizheng**: What do you mean?

**葛天**：我的那些同族都已下过山了。为了你们，放弃姓名，放弃族人，放弃性命，放弃……\
**Getian**: My people have left the mountain and come to help you. They renounced their names, families, and even lives for you ...

**葛天**：放弃一切，成为一个符号，一个图腾。变得谁也不是。\
**Getian**: They gave up everything so that you would have gods to worship. They became symbols, totems ... except themselves.

**里正**：羽人，你究竟在说什么？\
**Lizheng**: What are you talking about, feather man?

**葛天**：我告知过，可以怎样称呼我。“羽人”并非我的名字。\
**Getian**: I told you my name. I'm not a "feather man."

**里正**：……\
**Lizheng**: ...

**葛天**：“眼前羽人或许非我族类，并无以名相称之必需。”\
**Getian**: "This feather man is not one of us. No need to call him by name."

不是读心，只是答案很容易便能猜想。\
It isn't any sort of prescience. It's only that the answer is a simple deduction.

**里正**：——!\
**Lizheng**: !

**葛天**：……看来尔等确乎忘矣。\
**Getian**: ... Seems like my people have been long forgotten.

**葛天**：忘了过去那些下山的葛天氏，亦曾是建城之人、筑桥之人、抵御洪水之人……只记得一个久不存在，从未回应的摄提神。\
**Getian**: You forgot the Gětiāns who left the mountain, the city-builders, the bridge-masters, the flood-fighters ... They all faded into oblivion. You only remember the Gods of Shètí, who never answered to your prayers!

**葛天**：所以我不愿……\
**Getian**: That's why I'm discouraged ...

**葛天**：不愿下山。不愿相助之后，却又这样被猜忌或忘却。\
**Getian**: ... by the idea of leaving the mountain like my people. I don't want to face such suspicion and disbelief after giving you all the help.

**里正**：——你、你究竟是谁？\
**Lizheng**: Who-who are you?

**葛天**：现今看来，桥断，乃是必然，一如在我之后再无葛天。\
**Getian**: Now that I see it, the destruction of the bridge was inevitable. It was bound to happen, like I was bound to be left in the mountain and be the last of us.

**里正**：“桥断”？你与断桥又有何关联——羽人，你说清楚！\
**Lizheng**: The bridge? Did you have something to do with the broken bridge? Feather man, tell us!

**葛天**：就这样罢。你们尽可以来擒住我了。\
**Getian**: Question no more. You can have me, if that's what you want.

葛天话语和动作传递出的信息，一时之间，令在场所有人都屏住了呼吸。\
The message conveyed by Gětiān's words and actions forces those present to hold their breath.

他放弃了反抗，在以一段语焉不详的指控，勾连出断桥的过往后。\
He gives up his resistance and sees the connection between the broken bridge and this vague allegation.

每个人都在怀疑：这是否只是缓兵之计？\
Though the onlookers wonder whether this might be merely a stalling tactic.

**曲娘**：——里正！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Lǐzhèng!

而先前从酒坊出发，向职祠前进的另外两人，此刻正要迎面赶上一场对峙的终结。\
The two who set off from the tavern, heading toward the Zhící, arrive in time to witness the end of the standoff.

别斯米尔原本一路紧跟曲娘，却在职祠门前停下了脚步。\
Bessmert had been following Jiǔ Niángzǐ closely all the way, but now stops just short of the Zhící's gates.

**别斯米尔**：……曲娘小姐，先不要过去。\
**Bessmert**: Ms. Jiǔ Niángzǐ, please wait.

她的确看不见。之所以停下来，只是敏锐地察觉到前方紧绷的气氛。\
Even without the ability to see it, she stops to analyze the tense atmosphere ahead.

**里正**：不要过来！\
**Lizheng**: Come no further!

**曲娘**：咦？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Huh?

**葛天**：……\
**Getian**: ...

几乎所有人的目光都汇集到院中的葛天身上，警惕着他可能还会有的反应。没有人相信他会真的就这样束手就擒。\
The gaze of almost everyone in the courtyard converges now on Gětiān, wary of any possible movement.No one present believes that he would just surrender like this.

而在无人注意的角落，红尾马驹灵巧地绕过所有人，一路狂奔——\
And in an unnoticed corner, the red-tailed horse deftly bypasses them all before running off in agitation.

**斑纹马？**：咴——！\
**Striped Horse?**: *neighs*

马驹飞快地窜进人群，又迅速窜出，目的竟是将别斯米尔从曲娘的身后掠走。\
The horse that had rushed into the crowd then just as immediately weaves back out, seeming to aim to snatch Bessmert out from behind Jiǔ Niángzǐ.

**别斯米尔**：……啊！\
**Bessmert**: Ah!

并且它成功了。\
And it succeeds.

## NS-14 往日鎏金 / The Old Days

**曲娘**：什么……刚才跑出去的是什么？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: What, what just ran out of there?

**曲娘**：那东西还带走了和我一起来的那位娘子，这——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: That "thing" took away the lady. What's going on?!

曲娘话音落下，众人都齐齐望向院子中央的葛天。多数目光都饱含质疑、猜忌和恐惧。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ's words dissipate in the air without stirring a response. The eyes of all stare at Gětiān in the center of the courtyard. Most of these are filled with doubt, suspicion, and fear.

伴随城外异客的身影远去，那骨杖所带来的神秘术似乎也逐渐消散。\
As the strange horse and its unwilling rider disappear in the distance, the communication arcane skill cast by the bone wand also seems to dissipate.

**里正**：现在我们又失去了一名证人。难道这也在你的计划之中？\
**Lizheng**: Now we lost another witness. Did you plan this?

**葛天**：我的术杖，昨日便已遗落在她的酒坊。你一问便知。\
**Getian**: I left my wand in her tavern yesterday. Ask her. You will know.

**里正**：曲娘？是这样吗？\
**Lizheng**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ, is that so?

**曲娘**：在院子里是发现了一根骨头，但那东西现在正在被掳走的胡人娘子身上。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: We did find a bone in the yard, but it's with that foreign lady now.

**里正**：……\
**Lizheng**: ...

**里正**：先把他捆起来。你还有什么要说的？\
**Lizheng**: Tie him up first. Do you have more to say?

**葛天**：该说的，我都已说了。若再不制止，便是真的祥瑞来了也无力回天。\
**Getian**: Everything I need to tell you, I have spoken it all. Catch her now, or even a real Xiángruì cannot save you from the disaster.

**里正**：你究竟为何执着于指认曲娘为凶手？\
**Lizheng**: Why are you so obsessed with calling Jiǔ Niángzǐ the "culprit"?

**曲娘**：什么？你——我——我是凶手？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: What? You ...? I ...? I am the culprit?!

**曲娘**：我是什么凶手？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: What kind of culprit am I?

**里正**：曲娘，无妨。我们都知道，你与失踪案无关……\
**Lizheng**: It's fine, Jiǔ Niángzǐ. We all know you have nothing to do with the missing persons cases ...

**曲娘**：而且他还说什么——什么真祥瑞也没办法……我看他才是假的！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: And he said ... said that ... "Even a real Xiángruì cannot save you." He is more of a fake one to me!

曲娘气愤地冲向葛天，三步并作两步来到他跟前，临了却又丢失了言语的能力。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ rushes angrily toward Gětiān, striding forward until she stands just before him, but in her rush of emotion, she loses her ability to speak.

**曲娘**：你——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: You ...

**葛天**：……\
**Getian**: ...

**里正**：曲娘，不必激动。现下只能暂且将他关押在职祠，我自去告知法曹。\
**Lizheng**: Stay calm. We will hold him in detention in Zhící for now. I'll report this to the Fǎcáo.

**里正**：现在要紧的，是派人去追回马和那位胡人娘子……\
**Lizheng**: The first thing to do is catch up with the horse and the foreign lady ...

**里正**：需得找到他的术杖，才可溯源。\
**Lizheng**: And find his wand to figure out his arcane skill.

人群依着里正的指挥快速行动起来，逐渐离开了中庭。\
The crowd quickly moves according to Lǐzhèng's command and exits the courtyard in an orderly fashion.

院中只剩下一些零星的护卫，与位于中央，静默的三人。\
Only a few scattered guards remain in the courtyard, along with the three figures located in the center.

葛天原本也应被带走，却由于里正并未直接发话，没有人敢上前。即使已经束手就擒，他巨大的翅膀与趾爪看上去仍然有着相当的威慑力。\
At this point, it would seem obvious that Gětiān must be taken away, but as Lǐzhèng has not yet ordered anything to that effect, no one dares step forward. For though subdued, his huge wings and claws still serve as effective deterrents.

**里正**：……把他也带下去吧。其它人都散了。\
**Lizheng**: Take him away. Everyone else dismissed.

**里正**：曲娘，你随我来。我有事与你商议。\
**Lizheng**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ, follow me. There is something we need to talk about.

**曲娘**：羽人，你到底想做什么？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: What do you want, feather man?

**里正**：曲娘？\
**Lizheng**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ?

**曲娘**：你明明看上去就像祥瑞，为什么要说这样的话？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: You look like a decent Xiángruì. Why did you say something like that?

**曲娘**：而且，就算你不是祥瑞，你难道——难道不怕……不怕真的祥瑞降责于你吗？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Even-even if you're not, aren't you afraid that ... the real Xiángruì will blame you for doing the wrong thing?

对于里正的话语，少女看上去恍若未闻。她问句中的疑惑透过近乎呢喃的语气传递出来。\
The girl appears as though she has not heard Lǐzhèng's words. The doubt in her questions is conveyed in an almost whispered tone.

而葛天连头也没抬。一动不动，仿佛一尊兀然的塑像。\
Gětiān doesn't even lift his head. He remains motionless, like a statue.

**葛天**：……\
**Getian**: ...

**里正**：曲娘。须知他早前未与我们有所接触，的确并非此地祥瑞，城中也已失庇护久矣。\
**Lizheng**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ. It is true that he is not the Xiángruì of our city. The Xiángruì, who once protected our city, has been long lost.

曲娘蓦地转过头来，似乎并不理解里正这一论断的逻辑。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ turns her head, failing to connect the logic behind Lǐzhèng's statement.

**曲娘**：可是——可是大家都以为，山上的羽人就是祥瑞！单单是他的样貌，就能让旁的人觉得他是祥瑞。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: BUT! But everyone thinks the feather man on the mountain is the Xiángruì! Just, just look at him! How could people not take him as a Xiángruì by his look?

**曲娘**：执礼离开前跟我说过，羽人长得像“句芒”，就像画册里走出来的一样，好像这能解释一切。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: The former Zhílǐ told me that the feather man looks like a Gōumáng, just like what was depicted in a picture book. *Gōumáng: the God of Spring in ancient Chinese mythology, in charge of agriculture, with wings and claws.

**曲娘**：句芒可是画在书上的祥瑞啊！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: A Gōumáng is a confirmed Xiángruì recorded in a book!

**里正**：曲娘……\
**Lizheng**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ.

**曲娘**：但他当然不是祥瑞了，不像句芒，或者灭蒙鸟……他连，呃，“绝迹易，无行地难”的道理都不明白。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: But this man? Of course, he is not a Xiángruì! He isn't like the Gōumáng nor the Mièméng ... He doesn't even understand the saying of, um, "One can remove the footsteps, but not the path one walketh on."

**里正**：……\
**Lizheng**: ...

**里正**：“绝迹易，无行地难。”唉，道理确是如此。只要做错了事，必然会留下痕迹。\
**Lizheng**: "One can remove the footsteps, but not the path one walketh on." ... That's fair. One cannot commit wrongdoing without leaving a trace.

**里正**：即使他试图嫁祸于你，我们在尚未找到术杖和证人之前，也不能轻易假定他为凶手。\
**Lizheng**: However, we can't convict him without definitive evidence, such as witnesses and his wand.

**里正**：我们还没有找到足够确证的“痕迹”，曲娘。\
**Lizheng**: The trace he left is yet to be found.

曲娘蓦然，在葛天的身前蹲下来。她执着于去看着对方的眼睛说话，似乎这样就能从中判断话语与感情的真伪。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ squats down in front of Gětiān in a sudden inexplicable movement. Then stares unwaveringly into his eyes as she speaks, as if she is to judge the authenticity of his words and expressions by doing so.

**曲娘**：羽人……什么叫作“真的祥瑞”？你知道它在哪里？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Feather man. Do you know what is a "real Xiángruì"? Do you know where it is?

**曲娘**：你又为什么要带走别人的同伴，却来这里指认我？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Why did you take people's friends away and accuse me of being the culprit?

但葛天似乎已经打定主意沉默。他低着头，好像突然对观察伤口上的血珠有了兴趣。——一种消极的抵抗。\
But Gětiān seems to have made up his mind to remain silent. He lowers his head, taking a feigned interest in observing the blood dripping from his wounds. An act of passive resistance.

**葛天**：……\
**Getian**: ...

一滴血渗入羽毛的时间已足够女孩整理措辞，继续提问。\
A drop of blood seeps into his feathers, the moment passes long enough for the girl to organize her words and continue her barrage of questions.

**曲娘**：你……这样的形貌……嗯，是天道赋予的，就不应该因为自身的好恶得失而偏离了这形貌应有的本性。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: You, um, your appearance is given by heaven. So you should not act against the nature of your look just because of your personal preference.

**曲娘**：你明明可以变得像说书先生说的、像画册上画的那样好，那样受人们喜爱……就像大家所期望的那样。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: You could have become a much-loved spirit, like in the stories and picture books ... as everyone expects you to be.

**曲娘**：但你……你把胡人小娘子，和她的同伴带走的时候，都没有考虑过人们的心情。那不是他们想要分离的时刻。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: But you ... when you took away that foreign lady's teammates, you didn't care about their feelings. They didn't want to be separated.

**曲娘**：你令人伤心了，这不是祥瑞该做的事。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: You disappointed people. That's not what a Xiángruì should do.

**里正**：……好了，曲娘。就到这里吧。\
**Lizheng**: Alright, Jiǔ Niángzǐ. That's enough.

**里正**：你们先把他带下去。\
**Lizheng**: Take him away.

**曲娘**：我……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I ...

曲娘眼瞧着葛天被带走的方向。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ watches coldly as Gětiān is taken away.

**曲娘**：他也什么都没有告诉我。大家都是一样的。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: He didn't tell me anything. Nor did he tell anyone.

**里正**：虽然，我知晓你一直以来都对“祥瑞”十分着迷，但羽人今日来到职祠，言语中已经透露了他实则并非祥瑞的事实。\
**Lizheng**: I know you're chasing after anything that could be a Xiángruì, but the feather man has clearly claimed that he is not one.

**里正**：甚至，我以为他的态度，更像是说他自身并非祥瑞，也从未想过要成为祥瑞。\
**Lizheng**: To be honest, judging from his attitude, he has never had the intention to be one.

**曲娘**：我不明白……他怎么能不想呢？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I don't understand ... How could he not want to be one?

**里正**：并非人人都对祥瑞的传说如此趋之若鹜。\
**Lizheng**: Not everyone is so interested in the legend of Xiángruì.

**里正**：沛城的确曾在祥瑞的庇护下有过不错的时光。但此去经年，那段旧日只能在神话典籍中查阅。甚至我也不敢论断，真正的祥瑞是否还存在。\
**Lizheng**: The Pèi City did have a good era under the protection of the Xiángruìs. But after all these years, no one can recall that time without the help of mythologies and history books. Even I can't be sure if there is a real Xiángruì.

**里正**：但是曲娘，你应该知道。现在，我们也已不需要祥瑞了。\
**Lizheng**: But, Jiǔ Niángzǐ, you should know that we don't need a Xiángruì anymore.

**曲娘**：……我们不需要吗？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: We don't need it?

**里正**：现在没有祥瑞，甚至也没有了行之有效的问卜。但你看，我们失去了与渊庙的沟通，城中依然秩序井然……\
**Lizheng**: With no Xiángruì, no Divination, we cannot arrive at the Yuān Temple, but this is still an orderly city.

**里正**：度朔节也依然热闹非凡，可见祥瑞并不是一城立足之必需。\
**Lizheng**: The Dùshuò Festival is as vibrant as ever. You can tell that a Xiángruì is not necessary for a city to prosper.

**曲娘**：是这样吗……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Is that so ...

曲娘捏住了随身携带的小包。包上绣着搭配奇特的艳诗，她不懂那些字的意思，此刻却正如自己被搅乱的心情。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ grasps the small bag she carries with her. The bag is embroidered with a peculiar combination of love poems. Though, she has never really understood the meaning of the words, in some way, they now mirror her own confused mind.

**里正**：不过，今日看来，原来你是识字的？\
**Lizheng**: By the way, turns out you can read, can't you?

**曲娘**：嗯？你知道我不会写字的，里正。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Hmm? You know that I can't, Lǐzhèng.

**里正**：“绝迹易，无行地难”——\
**Lizheng**: "One can remove the footsteps, but not the path one walketh on."

**曲娘**：哦！不，不是的。我只是听道士说过太多次，所以记住了。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Oh, that's not what it seems to be. I heard it from the Daoist countless times, so I remembered it.

**里正**：哪位道士？是城中的道人吗？\
**Lizheng**: Which Daoist? In the city?

曲娘摇摇头，否认了里正的猜想。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ shakes her head to refute Lǐzhèng's assumptions.

**曲娘**：是我来到城里之前，曾经与一个道士同行过一段时日。他会重复一些话，我总是听不明白，但心里牢牢地记着。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: No. It was a Daoist I traveled with before I came to Pèi City. The Daoist said many different things over and over again. I couldn't understand, but I remembered them.

**里正**：听起来，你曾有一位贤师。毕竟你入城以后，一向与人为善，走上了一条与葛天不同的道路。\
**Lizheng**: Sounds like you had a distinguished teacher. Since you came here, you've been treating people nice and kindly, exactly the opposite of what Gětiān has done.

**曲娘**：啊，原来他叫葛天。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Ah, so his name is Gětiān.

**里正**：是啊，葛天……但你刚才还是同他说得太多了。\
**Lizheng**: Yes, Gětiān ... You said too many things to him.

**里正**：他并不是你一直在寻找，心中所向往的祥瑞。\
**Lizheng**: He is not the Xiángruì you're looking for.

**里正**：真正的祥瑞不会毫无理由做出这样冒犯的事，他或许只是一个……久居山上的大妖。\
**Lizheng**: A real Xiángruì would never be so rude. It is very possible that he is only a ... Yāo that has been living on the mountain for too long.

她低着头，似乎很难接受这样的变故。\
Her head lowers, seeming to find it difficult to accept such a change in thought.

**曲娘**：可他究竟为什么要指认我呢？我……我不明白。是我做错了什么吗？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: But why did he accuse me like that? I-I don't get it. Did I do something wrong?

**里正**：可以想见，因为你是执礼。\
**Lizheng**: Because you're the Zhílǐ.

曲娘茫然地望向里正，脸上写满了疑惑和探寻。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ looks at Lǐzhèng, her face caught between doubt and curiosity.

提出观点的老者则摸着胡子笑起来，仿佛对女孩的反应感到无奈。\
Having presented his point of view, the old man rubs his beard and laughs, knowingly helpless to influence the girl's reaction.

**里正**：前任执礼已因他之故，回乡去了。他见此法奏效，或是想要故伎重施。\
**Lizheng**: The former Zhílǐ left because of what he said and did. Now he wants to play the same trick on you.

**里正**：况且，今日他闯入职祠时，见我似乎相当惊讶。由此不难推断一二。\
**Lizheng**: What's more, when he got here and saw me but not you, he acted quite surprised. You can tell from the details.

**曲娘**：……唔……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Hmm ...

她的眼神越发困惑，这样的心机处事，于她而言似乎太过复杂。\
The thoughts behind her eyes grow more muddled, such deceitful scheming felt too complicated for her to comprehend.

**曲娘**：啊，对了！还有那被掳走的胡人娘子，她——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Oh, and that captured foreign lady, she ...

**里正**：放下心吧，已派人出去搜寻了。我们现在也该去商定一下明早走吉与跃桥的事项。\
**Lizheng**: Don't worry. There are people searching for them now. As for us, we should confirm the details for tomorrow's Fortune Walk and Bridge Leap.

**曲娘**：噢，跃桥。是的，还有这件事……要是断桥能够修复就好了，就不用年节动物，也不用跳桥了。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Right, Bridge Leap, I almost forgot ... If only the broken bridge could be fixed, and we wouldn't need those Festive Animals, nor to jump over the bridge ...

**曲娘**：刚才我问葛天，可是他什么都不回答的时候，我就在想……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: During Gětiān's silence, I was thinking that ...

**曲娘**：如果我能直接问执徐呢？去渊庙。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: What if I can go to the Yuān Temple and ask Zhíxú the Guardian?

**曲娘**：如果是真正的问卜，那我想了解的事情，也一定会有答案吧。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: If the legend of The Divination is real, then whatever the question is, Zhíxú will answer me, right?

**里正**：……是啊。\
**Lizheng**: I guess so.

两人向室内走去，交谈的话音伴随脚步声，逐渐消失在庭院中。\
The two of them walk indoors, their conversation disappearing from the courtyard under the sound of footsteps on hard stone.

齐整的官府室内，两道身影交换着连日来的信息，以商定下一步行动。\
Within the pristine government office, two figures exchange information from their past few days so they might agree on their next step course of action.

**里正**：……事情就是这样，葛天现下暂时收押在职祠地牢，曲娘也还在那边。\
**Lizheng**: That is the whole story. Gětiān is now detained in Zhící's dungeon. Jiǔ Niángzǐ is there as well.

**里正**：两个时辰前，我与执礼曲娘商议后，决定保留走吉与跃桥的仪式。\
**Lizheng**: Four hours ago, after discussing with the new Zhílǐ, we decided to keep the ceremonies of Fortune Walk and Bridge Leap.

**里正**：只是那些生有异色的动物，确实不便再用，规模相较以往执徐值年，有所缩减。\
**Lizheng**: But no colored animals are used this time. The number of animals will be less than those in previous years of Zhíxú.

**里正**：此为人员名录与各类筹措明细，我令人摹写了几份，已经送到各坊去了。\
**Lizheng**: Here is the list of ceremony members and funds. I've asked people to deliver the copies to all the streets.

里正从案上抄起一叠纸页递出去。\
Lǐzhèng picks up a stack of papers from the desk and hands them out dutifully.

**？？？**：您辛苦。\
**???**: Thank you, Sir.

**里正**：应当的。还有葛天一事，按照法规，需得度朔节后再升堂会审。\
**Lizheng**: This is my duty. As for Gětiān, we shall put him on hold untill after the Dùshuò Festival according to the law.

**？？？**：我还有一问。证据追回来了没有？\
**???**: One more thing. Have we found the horse and the proof?

**里正**：……尚未追回。掠走胡人娘子的红尾马驹，大抵还是受了葛天的控制，等我们的人追到郊外，已经在雨中消失得无影无踪。\
**Lizheng**: Not yet. The horse taking that foreign lady away might still be under the control of Gětiān. There was no trace of them when our people chased them out of the city.

**？？？**：辰时郊外急雨，行路困难，可以理解。只能等此次雨停后再行搜索了。\
**???**: I understand, given the road conditions in the morning rain. Looks like we will have to continue with the search after it stops.

**？？？**：不过，一马驹携一盲眼女子，应当走不出太远。待到雨停，我会亲自带队前去。\
**???**: But I don't think a horse carrying a blind woman can go far enough to escape. I'll lead the search squad myself next time.

**里正**：劳烦法曹。\
**Lizheng**: Thank you, Fǎcáo.

背对门厅的威武身影，习惯性压下腰间的短剑，调整了别剑姿势，才又一挥手表示不必在意。\
The imposing figure, with his back to the entryway, habitually presses down on the short sword at his waist, adjusting the position of the blade. Then waves his hand again to show that he doesn't need to concern himself with such matters.

**法曹**：分内事罢了。执礼呢？\
**Facao**: I'm only doing my job. Where is the Zhílǐ?

**里正**：嗯？法曹是问曲娘，还是先前的那位？\
**Lizheng**: Are you referring to Jiǔ Niángzǐ, or the former one?

**法曹**：回乡的那位。\
**Facao**: The one who went back to her hometown.

**里正**：大概需得等到度朔节后，才有消息。我尚未收到她的回信。\
**Lizheng**: We haven't heard anything from her yet. Perhaps it will come after the Dùshuò Festival.

**法曹**：好。曲娘毕竟年轻，在回乡那位执礼传来消息之前，还需得您多多看着职祠些。\
**Facao**: Noted. Jiǔ Niángzǐ is still green, so please help me take care of the Zhící before the former one comes back.

**里正**：她足够良善，也正因此我才会向职祠贸然举荐。若曲娘行事出了差池，自然也是我的责任。\
**Lizheng**: I will. She is kind-hearted. That's why I recommended her for this position. It will be my responsibility if she makes any mistakes.

**法曹**：话虽如此，年节事项繁多，难免有所疏漏，也不必太过苛责。\
**Facao**: Well, there are so many things to do before the New Year. It's fine, even if she makes a mistake or two. Don't push her too hard.

**里正**：正是。若你寻回了证据和那两位胡商，也劳烦派人知会一声。\
**Lizheng**: That's what I thought. If you find any evidence or the two foreigners, please let me know.

法曹一边将文书折叠一边利落起身，预备告辞，却被里正抬手拦下。\
Fǎcáo rises nimbly while folding the documents, as he prepares to bid his farewell, he is stopped by Lǐzhèng's raised hand.

**里正**：稍待，还有一事，是今夜岁除宴。法曹若是愿意，可携亲眷来曲娘的酒坊度过。\
**Lizheng**: Oh, another thing, the New Year's Feast tonight. You're welcome to Jiǔ Niángzǐ's tavern with your relatives.

**法曹**：酒坊？那可是金市街坊都去？\
**Facao**: The tavern? Are the people around the merchants hub going too?

**里正**：是啊。她宴请乡邻，理由也不难猜。\
**Lizheng**: Yes. She is hosting a feast for the neighbors.

**里正**：岁除守夜。翻过年去，便是度朔节的第一天。\
**Lizheng**: It is the New Year's Eve Vigil, followed by the first day of Dùshuò Festival.

**里正**：往年酒坊也是设宴的。\
**Lizheng**: It is an annual tradition at the tavern.

**法曹**：朔日，新年……\
**Facao**: Shuòrì, the New Year ...

**里正**：是啊，新的一年，又是执徐生辰……\
**Lizheng**: Right, another year of the Zhíxú ...

**里正**：希望供奉着执徐的渊庙，亦能传来好消息。\
**Lizheng**: Hopefully, the Yuān Temple, which worships the Zhíxú, will bring us good news.

话音落下，仅余一阵沉默。两人望向窗外，断桥与渊庙的飞檐，在雨中蒙雾里忽隐忽现。\
Having said his piece, leaving only a moment of silence. The two of them look out the window, toward the eaves of the broken bridge and the temple flickering in the misty rain.

## NS-15 空心眼 / Hollow Eyed

红鬃的“斑纹马”驮着别斯米尔冲进急雨。\
The striped horse with its red mane charges through the pouring rain, carrying Bessmert.

它一路狂奔，似乎恐惧于身后可能的追捕，也为了防止背上的人在减速中跳下去。\
All the way, it runs with wild abandon, as if afraid of possible pursuers behind them, and perhaps to prevent the person on its back from jumping off should it slow down.

**别斯米尔**：停——停下——！\
**Bessmert**: Halt ... Halt!

**别斯米尔**：——你能听见吗？\
**Bessmert**: Do you hear me?

马只是继续向前奔跑。它甚至轻松地越过几处凹陷的浅滩，继续往前。\
The horse runs onward still, even striding several shallow depressions with ease before continuing forward.

人的语言无用，别斯米尔试图按照驯马的方式让它减速。\
Seeing her words taking little effect, Bessmert attempts to slow it down using her prior experience with horses.

**别斯米尔**：呼……呼……\
**Bessmert**: *deep breaths*

深呼吸之后，她松开一开始就紧紧抓住的，作为着力点的鬃毛，改为一只手扶在颈脖之前，另一只手则在奔跑的节奏中一下一下抚摸它两旁的皮毛。\
As she releases her breath, she lets go of the mane and replaces one hand in front of the creature's neck, while the other hand caresses the fur on both sides, adjusting to match the rhythm of its gallop.

**别斯米尔**：放松……放松……\
**Bessmert**: Easy ... easy now ...

**别斯米尔**：好孩子……\
**Bessmert**: Good child ...

**别斯米尔**：呼——呼——\
**Bessmert**: *deep breaths*

深呼吸之后，她抓住这机会从马背上翻身，摔了下来。\
After taking another deep breath, she seizes the opportunity to vault herself off the horse and tumble down in a quick movement.

别斯米尔“如愿”跌在浅滩里。\
Bessmert falls into the shallows, just as she intended.

**别斯米尔**：呃！\
**Bessmert**: Ugh!

**斑纹马？**：咴——！\
**Striped Horse?**: *neighs*

**别斯米尔**：嘶呃……\
**Bessmert**: Hiss ...

**斑纹马？**：咴！咴！\
**Striped Horse?**: *neighs*

马停在了不远处，而且正在掉头回来。\
The horse stops not far from where she lands and turns back.

顾不上新伤旧伤叠加，别斯米尔从水泊中爬起来，手却陷入了浅滩柔软的泥土里。\
Ignoring the accumulated pain of new and old injuries, Bessmert clambers out of the water, but her hands sink into the soft mud along the shallow shore.

不像沼泽那般黏着，也同样让她一时无法站立。\
Though not as sticky as the swamp, for a while, she finds it impossible to stand.

**斑纹马？**：别斯米尔女士！\
**Striped Horse?**: Madam!

**别斯米尔**：……什么……\
**Bessmert**: What ...

**别斯米尔**：是你吗？小叶尼塞？\
**Bessmert**: Is it you, Yenisei?

**别斯米尔**：你在哪儿？\
**Bessmert**: Where are you?

熟悉的声音近在咫尺，别斯米尔却无论如何也摸索不到准确的方向。\
The familiar voice is certainly within earshot, but Bessmert cannot place its direction, no matter how hard she strains.

她努力将自己从泥地中撑起，又再次跌下去。\
She struggles to lift herself out of the mud and falls again.

**小叶尼塞**：对不起，您摔伤了吗？\
**Yenisei**: I'm sorry. Are you hurt?

**小叶尼塞**：是我太着急了，我们不能被追上……\
**Yenisei**: I was so anxious. We must not let them catch us ...

**别斯米尔**：还好。还好——你是怎么——\
**Bessmert**: I'm alright. I'm good ... How did you ...

**小叶尼塞**：我现在是在水里和您说话，您快回到我的背上来。\
**Yenisei**: I am talking to you through the water. Please hurry up and get back on me!

**别斯米尔**：……你也变成了斑纹马？！\
**Bessmert**: You've turned into a striped horse, too?!

**别斯米尔**：难道说，这是你的神秘术……\
**Bessmert**: Or, is this your arcane skill? ...

**小叶尼塞**：女士，这不是斑纹马，这是鹿蜀！虽然都是神秘动物，但不一样——哦，是的，这是我的神秘术。\
**Yenisei**: I am not a striped horse, Madam. I'm a Lùshǔ! Both of them are arcane creatures, but not the same kind ... And yes, that's my arcane skill.

**小叶尼塞**：我能通过水中显影传声，经过图拉的沼泽时，您曾经见过的，记得吗？\
**Yenisei**: I can show images and diffuse sounds through water. I cast it once when we passed by the swamp in Tula, remember?

**别斯米尔**：那“鹿蜀”呢？鹿蜀是什么？是“葛天”把你带走了，变成这样——\
**Bessmert**: What about the "Lùshǔ"? What are they? Did Gětiān take you away and turn you into this?

被带走前听到的陌生名词突兀地出现在脑海中，别斯米尔很快将它与现状关联起来。\
That strange term she heard before all this began suddenly reappears in her mind. Bessmert quickly associates it with her current situation.

**小叶尼塞**：雨太大了，我听不见后面的声音，也听不清您——\
**Yenisei**: The rain is making too much noise. I can't hear you or the surroundings ...

**小叶尼塞**：您快上来吧！我不确定他们离这儿还有多远。\
**Yenisei**: Get on my back! I'm not sure how far they are from us.

**别斯米尔**：……\
**Bessmert**: ...

**别斯米尔**：我还没有听见成年人的脚步声。孩子，你得过来些，拉我一把。\
**Bessmert**: I don't hear any footsteps from grown men. Come here, child. Help me up.

小叶尼塞于是跨得更近过去，把别斯米尔从下陷的浅滩中拱出来。\
Yenisei then steps closer and scoops Bessmert out of the sinking shallows.

**别斯米尔**：谢谢。所以究竟发生了什么……？我们遇到的情况似乎越来越复杂了。\
**Bessmert**: Thank you. So ... What happened? The situation is getting trickier and trickier.

**小叶尼塞**：我们弄错了。葛天并没有对我下手，与此相反，恰恰是他救了我。\
**Yenisei**: We made a mistake. Gětiān didn't turn me into a horse. On the contrary, he saved my life.

**别斯米尔**：那是谁？是谁能把你变成这样？\
**Bessmert**: Then who was it? Who did this to you?

**小叶尼塞**：……昨晚您没有喝水，对吗？在您上楼之后，我与曲娘在楼下闲谈，还喝了不少她赠予的水。\
**Yenisei**: You didn't drink any water last night, did you? But I did, quite a lot. After you went into the room, Jiǔ Niángzǐ and I had a chat downstairs, and she gave me the water.

**小叶尼塞**：这就是差别。葛天说曲娘的神秘术就在酒或者水这类液体之中。\
**Yenisei**: This is the difference. Gětiān said her arcane skill was cast through liquids like water and liquor.

**别斯米尔**：天哪，孩子……\
**Bessmert**: My poor child ...

**小叶尼塞**：在那之后，我也来到楼上。您大概是累极了，睡得很安稳，可我却一点也睡不着，只好再次下楼。\
**Yenisei**: I went upstairs after the chat. You must have been too tired to notice me at the time. I stayed in the room but couldn't sleep at all, so I went downstairs again.

**小叶尼塞**：就在下楼的途中，我听见了歌声。\
**Yenisei**: That was when I heard someone singing.

**小叶尼塞**：那是一首……我从没听过的歌。歌词我也无法理解，只记得旋律轻柔，还有些奇特——\
**Yenisei**: That song ... I'd never heard it before, and I had no idea what the lyrics were about. All I remember is that the melody was soft and a bit unusual ...

**小叶尼塞**：直到我发现这首歌是一群木头人在唱。那是一群很小的，会融化在酒水中的木头人。\
**Yenisei**: Then I found that "someone" was a group of wooden dolls. They were small and would melt when they touched liquor.

小叶尼塞把那段惊吓的旅程从头脑中掘起，又努力用平静的语气讲述。\
Yenisei extracts the frightening journey from her mind, trying as best she can to narrate it back in a calm tone.

**小叶尼塞**：而且，院子里的马，好像也在随木头人哼唱旋律。它有红色的鬃毛和尾巴，就像我现在的样子。\
**Yenisei**: And there were horses in the yard, also humming the melody. They had red manes and red tails, just like what I look like now.

**小叶尼塞**：现在我知道，原来那就是鹿蜀。它的斑纹，会在月光下泛着银光。\
**Yenisei**: I didn't know they were Lùshǔs until now. Their stripes glowed under the moon.

**别斯米尔**：可是，昨晚你们在楼下时，你没有看到那只鹿蜀长什么样吗？\
**Bessmert**: But didn't you have a closer look at the Lùshǔ last night?

**小叶尼塞**：说实话，我没有仔细看。上楼之前，我和曲娘甚至聊得……聊得很好。当时一切都很让人安心，我不明白……\
**Yenisei**: I had no time to see it clearly, to be honest. Anyway, that chat I had with Jiǔ Niángzǐ was ... quite good. Everything felt so comforting at the time, so I don't understand ...

**别斯米尔**：那为什么——为什么尤利恩先生他们变成的动物，和你不一样？你只说过他们有斑纹不是吗？\
**Bessmert**: Then, why are you different from the animals turned from Mr. Jurien and the others? You told me they only have stripes on them, right?

**小叶尼塞**：的确不一样。关于这个，我有一些猜想，但现在还没办法确证。\
**Yenisei**: Yes. I have an assumption about that, but I can't verify it now.

**别斯米尔**：什么样的猜想？\
**Bessmert**: What is it?

倒影中的小叶尼塞也沉默了，片刻后才回答了别斯米尔。\
Yenisei falls into silent reflection for a moment before answering Bessmert.

**小叶尼塞**：曲娘后院打水的地方，正靠近城内母河的支流。或许我们遇上的，是它的下游，活水又分割了滞留其中的神秘术。\
**Yenisei**: Remember the river our team found? Perhaps that was the lower course of the main river, and it included Jiǔ Niángzǐ's arcane power because the stream across her yard is near one of its branches. The running water might have diluted the arcane power in there.

**小叶尼塞**：通常情况下，活水就像自足的聚落，会自发排斥外来者的痕迹，就连我也被拒斥过许多次。\
**Yenisei**: Usually, a stream of running water is like an independent settlement. It rejects outsiders by nature. Even I have been rejected more than once.

**小叶尼塞**：尤利恩先生他们的情况，或许只是神秘术施展不完全而导致的意外。\
**Yenisei**: The striped horses our teammates turned into could be an accident caused by an incomplete arcane skill.

**别斯米尔**：那职祠中那些其他的斑纹马，难道也是——\
**Bessmert**: Those other striped horses in the Zhící, are they too ...

**小叶尼塞**：……也许曲娘根本就没有意识到，她所释放的神秘术，以残余的形态流入了河中。\
**Yenisei**: Perhaps Jiǔ Niángzǐ had no idea at all that she somehow leaked her arcane skill into the river.

**小叶尼塞**：而我饮用的，则是她亲手所制的……\
**Yenisei**: As for the water I had, she must have made it on purpose ...

两人都陷入了难堪的沉默。\
Both of them sink into a silence made awkward by the revelation.

**别斯米尔**：唉……那么葛天又是怎样出现的呢？\
**Bessmert**: *sighs* Then, how did Gětiān get involved in all this?

**小叶尼塞**：就在昨晚，在他打退突然开始围攻我的木头小人之后。\
**Yenisei**: Last night, after he saved me from the wooden dolls ...

重新拾起的回忆话题，被急雨骤停打断，小叶尼塞抬起头去确认落雨的情况。\
The topic of their recollections, only just resumed, is again interrupted, this time by the sudden stopping of the rain. Yenisei looks up as if to confirm it has really ended.

雨真的停了。这也意味着她们需要去往其他地方，以免被找到。\
If the rain has stopped for good, this also means they'll need to keep moving to avoid being found.

**小叶尼塞**：雨停了。\
**Yenisei**: The rain has stopped.

**小叶尼塞**：女士，我们得换个安全的地方。\
**Yenisei**: We need to find shelter, Madam.

**别斯米尔**：不，孩子，我不明白葛天为什么唯独把你带走。如果当时我也在那里呢？\
**Bessmert**: No, child. I don't see why he had to take you away. What if I was there with you?

**小叶尼塞**：我只知道，他当时就是为了来带走我们两个，他是来救我们的。\
**Yenisei**: All I know is, he was there to take us out of the danger.

**小叶尼塞**：而且现在葛天已经负伤了。在职祠时，他一直没有出手还击，我怀疑有什么原因让他不能伤害那些人。\
**Yenisei**: And he's injured now. When we confronted the people at the Zhící, he didn't fight back at all. I think he didn't hurt them for a reason.

**小叶尼塞**：如果这是真的，那我们得去救他。\
**Yenisei**: If he really meant to help us, we must go save him.

**别斯米尔**：……孩子。\
**Bessmert**: ... Child.

**别斯米尔**：你突然这样相信他，是不是因为他还做了些什么？\
**Bessmert**: All of a sudden, you seem to trust this creature entirely. Did he do anything else for you?

**别斯米尔**：按照现在的情况，在我看来，他们全都不对劲。葛天是，里正和曲娘也是。\
**Bessmert**: Based on what we know, Gětiān, Lǐzhèng, and Jiǔ Niángzǐ ... they all seem strange.

**小叶尼塞**：女士，请相信我。我曾经也这样觉得，他或许只是装作救人，实则把我们耍得团团转。\
**Yenisei**: Please trust me, Madam. I used to think this way, too. "Maybe he's fooling us with a fake rescue."

**小叶尼塞**：但他不是那样的。他为了使我相信，还使用了一种神秘术，就像是……读我的骨头。\
**Yenisei**: But he's not. He even showed me his arcane skill to win my trust. Yes, he read my bones.

**别斯米尔**：……！\
**Bessmert**: ...!

**小叶尼塞**：您能想象吗？他靠从我骨头上获取的信息，说出了我自己都不确定的事。\
**Yenisei**: Can you imagine that? He gained information by reading my bones, and then he actually told me something I didn't even know about myself.

## NS-16 见我所见 / See What I See

**小叶尼塞**：——放开我！你带我去哪儿？！\
**Yenisei**: Let me go! Where are you taking me?!

**小叶尼塞**：你——\
**Yenisei**: You ...

**？？？**：我现下放开，你摔落便是死路一条。\
**???**: If I let go, you will fall, and death will be your end.

**？？？**：惜命些吧。你们比自己能想象的还要脆弱许多。\
**???**: Hold your life dear. You are a lot more vulnerable than you can imagine.

**小叶尼塞**：下面就是一条河，你不用吓唬我。\
**Yenisei**: Quit threatening me. It's a river down there.

**？？？**：是。可你不知，这河上甚至无法漂浮河灯。\
**???**: Yes. But you don't know how shallow it is. Even a lantern can't float on it!

**？？？**：它在逐渐死去，与你们在来路上所见支流不同。\
**???**: It's dying, unlike the other branches you saw outside the city.

**小叶尼塞**：所以呢？你抓走我，就是为了告诉我这个？\
**Yenisei**: So what? Does that explain why you captured me?

**小叶尼塞**：好，这条河在死去。而我被一个鸟人抓住，摔下去也会死，什么都做不了。\
**Yenisei**: Fine. The river is dying; I'm held by a bird man in mid-air; I'll fall and die if I struggle. There's nothing I can do.

**？？？**：……\
**???**: ...

**？？？**：是的。自知之明，在少年人身上是种难能可贵的品质。\
**???**: Yes. It's a rare wisdom for a girl of your age to know her limits.

**小叶尼塞**：……\
**Yenisei**: ...

**？？？**：不过，我并非鸟人，而是妖。\
**???**: But I am not a bird man. I'm a Yāo.

**？？？**：我名为葛天。\
**???**: My name is Gětiān.

小叶尼塞放弃在半空中挣扎，思索着划下一个“等式”。\
Yenisei gives up on her midair struggle, pondering over his name and identity.

**小叶尼塞**：你会用神秘术。你是一个神秘学家。\
**Yenisei**: You can use arcane skills. You're an arcanist.

**葛天**：若你说是，那便是。\
**Getian**: If you say so, then it is so.

**葛天**：飞出许多里了，我会在不远处将你放下，此地浅滩之后即是草地。\
**Getian**: We have gone for miles. I will leave you here. Beyond the ford, you will see the steppe.

葛天如他所言减缓速度，片刻后将小叶尼塞轻轻放到地上。\
Gětiān slows down, just as he said he would, and after a moment, he gently places Yenisei on the ground.

小叶尼塞并未预料到这种优待。\
Given her situation, she had not anticipated such gentle treatment.

**小叶尼塞**：……我不明白。你到底想做什么？\
**Yenisei**: I don't understand. What on earth is your purpose?

**小叶尼塞**：为什么要把人变成马？我觉得，你能做比这严重得多的事情。\
**Yenisei**: Why did you turn humans into horses? I believe you can commit much worse crimes if you want to.

**小叶尼塞**：难道你以此为乐吗？\
**Yenisei**: Are you doing it for fun?

葛天停在一旁，一棵弯曲生长，像桥一样架过了浅溪的树藤上，神情似乎思索。\
Gětiān stops to the side of a curved tree growing like a bridge over the vines of a shallow stream, face heavy with a look of contemplation.

**葛天**：多问多错。\
**Getian**: The more you ask, the more mistakes you make.

**小叶尼塞**：问题哪来的对错？\
**Yenisei**: There's no such thing as a wrong question.

**葛天**：……但我会答你一问。关于……我为何要将人，变为马。\
**Getian**: I will answer one of the questions, regarding ... why I turned people into horses.

**葛天**：答：我未有此举，亦未有此意。\
**Getian**: The answer is, I didn't do it. Neither did I have that intention.

**小叶尼塞**：哈。真有意思，那谁能做到？\
**Yenisei**: Hah, interesting. Who did it then?

**葛天**：酒坊娘子。\
**Getian**: The lady owner of the tavern.

**小叶尼塞**：曲娘？\
**Yenisei**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ?

**葛天**：正是。\
**Getian**: Precisely.

小叶尼塞摇了摇头，显然并不轻信。\
Yenisei shakes her head, not believing his words.

**小叶尼塞**：如果这是真的，你却还让别斯米尔女士留在那里——你指望我在亲眼看见你带走被变形的人之后，还能草率相信你口说无凭的指认吗？\
**Yenisei**: If that's the case, why did you leave Madam Bessmert there alone? Do you really think I would buy your nonsense after I saw you take my teammates away?

**葛天**：你方才见了院中那红尾红鬃的“马”，是也不是？\
**Getian**: You saw the "horse" in the yard, with the red tail and the red mane. Did you not?

**小叶尼塞**：……是，我看见了。\
**Yenisei**: Yes, I saw ...

**葛天**：那并非是“马”，而是鹿蜀。至少，它的形貌是。\
**Getian**: It's not a "horse." It's a Lùshǔ, or at least, it looks like one.

**小叶尼塞**：鹿蜀……我从来没有听过这种东西。听起来像是东方特有的神秘生物。\
**Yenisei**: Lùshǔ ... I have never heard of it before. It sounds like an arcane creature native to the East.

葛天并未对此作出回应，而是继续抛出惊人的话题。\
Gětiān doesn't respond. He only continues to contribute yet more astonishing information.

**葛天**：它是鹿蜀，也是曲娘。\
**Getian**: It is a Lùshǔ, and also Jiǔ Niángzǐ herself.

**小叶尼塞**：什么？那是曲娘？？\
**Yenisei**: What? That thing is Jiǔ Niángzǐ?!

**葛天**：你今夜所见，的确并非真正意义上的鹿蜀。它们不过徒有鹿蜀的半分形貌。\
**Getian**: What you saw tonight was not real Lùshǔ. Those "horses" merely resembled half of them.

**葛天**：我言下之意，是说曲娘或为鹿蜀，一种妖。也即你方才所说的神秘生物。\
**Getian**: I speak of the fact that Jiǔ Niángzǐ might be a Lùshǔ, a kind of Yāo, or, as you would put it, an arcane creature.

**小叶尼塞**：唉，你说的话比这城里其他人还要更难懂。\
**Yenisei**: *sighs* Your words sound even more complicated than those in the city.

**小叶尼塞**：难道这是因为你同鹿蜀一样是神秘生物，还是这是某种我不能理解的纯血神秘学家怪癖？\
**Yenisei**: Is it because you are also an arcane creature like the Lùshǔ? Or, you have a thing only the pure-blooded can understand?

**葛天**：……我与她并不相似。鹿蜀天然地是一种瑞兽，红鬃白首，身披虎纹。\
**Getian**: We are nothing alike. Lùshǔs are Xiángruìs, born with red manes and white faces, covered with tiger's markings.

**葛天**：总之，据载，古时鹿蜀会役使名为“存想”的神秘术。曲娘也正是经由此术，才可将其他人变为鹿蜀。\
**Getian**: In the books, Lùshǔs are capable of casting an arcane skill named The Shape of Will. It could be the same skill that Jiǔ Niángzǐ uses to turn others into Lùshǔs.

**葛天**：如此解释，能使你明白吗？\
**Getian**: Do you understand?

**小叶尼塞**：哈。我试着理解吧。\
**Yenisei**: Yes ... I'll try.

**葛天**：记载中，“存想”之术隐秘而危险。鹿蜀炼血为火，点石成金，皆依靠此术。\
**Getian**: The Shape of Will is a dangerous and secret skill, as written in the books. The Lùshǔs use it to transform blood into fire and stone into gold.

**小叶尼塞**：也许……就像是炼金术？\
**Yenisei**: So ... it's like alchemy?

**葛天**：我并不了解你所说的“炼金术”，不过……\
**Getian**: I'm unfamiliar with what you said, but ...

**葛天**：曲娘似乎受到了其他术法的限制，她无法像真正的鹿蜀般俯身为妖，身负伟力。与其说她是鹿蜀，更不如说她是天生的半妖。\
**Getian**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ's power seems to be restricted. She cannot fully transform into a Lùshǔ like a Yāo could, nor does she possess great power. She's closer to a Half Yāo.

**葛天**：她的“存想”，需要通过一定媒介才可施展，并不如记载中的鹿蜀那般直截、高效。由此，她相较于真正的鹿蜀，更为难辨。\
**Getian**: Unlike other Lùshǔs, she requires a certain medium to cast her skill, The Shape of Will. This is also why people did not recognize her. She's harder to identify.

**小叶尼塞**：曲娘……半妖……“半妖”难道是指拥有不纯神秘血统的神秘学家？\
**Yenisei**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ ... "Half Yāo" ... Is that another name for the mixed-blood?

**小叶尼塞**：不过，假设你说的都是真的，但这些信息，你又是怎么知道的？\
**Yenisei**: Anyway, even if you're telling the truth, how did you know that?

**葛天**：天赋而已。就像你以水为媒卜出前路，我亦读骨识人。\
**Getian**: It is within my bloodline. Like you find your direction through the water, I read people through their bones.

**小叶尼塞**：……！你怎么知道我——\
**Yenisei**: ...! How did you know my ...

**小叶尼塞**：等等，你说你能看骨头辨识人？这太离奇了，从生理结构上又能看出什么？\
**Yenisei**: Wait, you mean you can read people through their bones? That makes no sense. What can one's physical condition tell you?

**葛天**：许多。许多见识，许多音声。即使我并不曾亲身历经。\
**Getian**: Many. Many stories, many sounds. Even if I was never there with them.

**葛天**：例如你。你骨纹织缠，形似漏网，一方兜首，三面延伸，是自曾经栖居的无水之地离开，迄今为止仍在游荡。\
**Getian**: Such as you. The markings on your bones resemble an open net, yet it captures nothing. You are away from the waterless land where you once lived, and to this day you're still wandering.

**小叶尼塞**：什么……\
**Yenisei**: What ...

少女瞪大了眼睛，显然是不可置信。\
The girl's eyes widen with astonished disbelief.

**葛天**：你此后一生，也将有无数出走与无数归回，譬如……鹘鸠。\
**Getian**: You will travel far many times in life and turn homeward, like the migratory birds.

**葛天**：直至寻到属于你的水域。\
**Getian**: Until you find your lake.

**小叶尼塞**：你究竟在说什么——\
**Yenisei**: What on earth are you talking about ...

**葛天**：我所言有误？应当不会……\
**Getian**: Have I mistaken anything? I should hope not.

**葛天**：抱歉，我已久未读过他人骨相，且诉诸言语了。\
**Getian**: Forgive me. I have long since stopped reading others' bones and put them into words.

**葛天**：或许白口讲来，与所见有些微偏差，但大体上应是没错。\
**Getian**: Perhaps I did not tell it in the most precise way, but it should be generally accurate.

**小叶尼塞**：好，停。\
**Yenisei**: Alright, stop.

**葛天**：嗯？\
**Getian**: Hmm?

**小叶尼塞**：我需要……\
**Yenisei**: I need ...

**小叶尼塞**：我需要一些时间，来理解你刚才说的……\
**Yenisei**: I need some time to digest your words ...

一阵影绰的响动很快就夺走了小叶尼塞的话头。\
A bizarre spectral sound cuts off Yenisei's reply.

**葛天**：——当心！\
**Getian**: Careful!

圆球一样拖着长尾的生物，自两人身后的林中猛然蹿出。\
Strange creatures that resemble balls dragging long tails suddenly leap out from the trees behind the two of them.

它们尖叫着，目标明确地冲向小叶尼塞。\
They shriek and charge towards Yenisei, who is most evidently their target.

**烛夜**：咕吱——吱——\
**Zhuye the Monster**: Squeak!

**烛夜**：吱吱吱！\
**Zhuye the Monster**: Squeak! Squeak! Squeak!

**小叶尼塞**：呃！\
**Yenisei**: Ugh!

**小叶尼塞**：——又是这些东西——我曾经在闹市上见过它们！\
**Yenisei**: These things again ... They already attacked me once in the street!

**烛夜**：吱——吱吱！！\
**Zhuye the Monster**: Squeak!!

**小叶尼塞**：唉，这群奇形怪状的鸟！\
**Yenisei**: *sighs* These stupid birds!

紧随其后的，还有一只与其他圆球有着显著不同的神秘生物。\
Following closely behind is a mysterious creature markedly different from the other feathered balls.

**小叶尼塞**：……怎么还有一只这么亮！别围着我转了，走开！\
**Yenisei**: This one is shining bright! Get out of my way, out!

它通体明亮异常，形态颀长，几乎照亮了眼前整片浅溪的水面。\
It is indeed exceptionally bright and long, illuminating the shallow stream in front of them on both sides.

葛天注视着被打散的烛夜们奔命逃窜的方向，心下有了一些考量。\
Gětiān stares in the direction the scattered Zhúyè ran off, his mind burdened with thought.

**葛天**：你是否……喝过曲娘给你的酒？\
**Getian**: Have you drunk the liquor ... offered by Jiǔ Niángzǐ?

**小叶尼塞**：没有，我只喝过她给我的水。为什么这么问？\
**Yenisei**: No, but I had the water from her. Why?

**葛天**：这些烛夜，或许是闻酒香而来。它们以烛夜花为食，此花可酿酒，其蕊气如酒糟。\
**Getian**: These Zhúyè might be attracted here by the scent of liquor. They feed on the flowers of Zhúyè, which can be used to make liquor and smell of lees.

**葛天**：因此，酒香也会吸引它们。可若你未曾饮酒……它们又是如何会缠上你？\
**Getian**: They could be here because they smelt the liquor. But you only had the water. What else could attract them?

小叶尼塞冥思苦想。\
Yenisei thinks back to the preceding events.

**小叶尼塞**：如果是酒，那或许是因为那群木头小人。我看见它们泡在酒碗里，后来又攻击了我，也许是在我躲避时不小心沾上了它们的气味。\
**Yenisei**: If they were attracted by the scent of liquor, I think it was the wooden dolls' fault. They soaked themselves in the liquor before they attacked me. I might have gotten their scent during the battle.

**葛天**：若真如此，仅身上沾上一些，未曾流入脾胃，应当不会有事。\
**Getian**: The scent of liquor stains is not strong enough to attract them here. It would have taken a proper consumption of liquor for them to notice.

**葛天**：在我来看，那酒水恐怕正是使人变为鹿蜀的媒介。当然，这仅是我的预估，除非你所饮下那水，亦有此作用——\
**Getian**: I worry that liquor is the medium for her transformation skill, but that is only my speculation. If the water you drank also exerts the same effect on you ...

似乎言出法随，变故就在他话语落下的时刻发生。\
As though his words hold the power of execution, the change happens the very moment he speaks.

**小叶尼塞**：呃……\
**Yenisei**: Emm ...

**葛天**：怎么，你——\
**Getian**: What? You ...

小叶尼塞跪了下去，身体逐渐发生变化，一如她的同胞们先前在草原上的境况。\
Yenisei kneels down and her body transforms, just as her companions transformed on the steppes before her.

**葛天**：怎会如此——！\
**Getian**: How so ...!

尽管葛天可以说是对此刻早已有所预料，却仍被这奇异的转变过程惊得振翅飞起。\
Although Gětiān had already anticipated this moment, he cannot help but be startled by this strange process and flaps his wings involuntarily.

本能令他想要离开。\
His instincts tell him to flee.

入夜，雨停，河滩湿润而柔软。\
Night falls. The rain has stopped, and the riverbank is moist and soft.

法曹带队，搜寻着红鬃马驹与胡人娘子的踪迹，终于来到郊外靠近河边的地界。\
Fǎcáo leads his team in search of the red-haired horse's trail, finally arriving at the edge of the river.

而此地正是前一夜葛天与小叶尼塞曾经停留的地方。\
The exact spot where Gětiān and Yenisei stayed the night before.

**巡防兵**：……\
**Guard**: ...

**法曹**：结果如何？\
**Facao**: Find anything?

**巡防兵**：有人来过，足迹似一高挑女子，与一匹马。\
**Guard**: Someone was here. Seems like a horse, with a female, tall and thin.

**法曹**：不是马，是马驹。脚印还要更浅更小，且看仔细些。\
**Facao**: Not a horse, but a foal. Look carefully. The footsteps are smaller and shallower than a horse's.

**法曹**：这些脚印消失在何处？\
**Facao**: Where are the ends of the tracks?

**巡防兵**：前方浅滩，从这里数过去十尺之后就没有痕迹了，无从知晓他们离开的方向。\
**Guard**: The river beach ahead. The tracks stopped three meters away. We couldn't tell where they went.

**法曹**：……不应当。\
**Facao**: That can't be.

法曹大步过去，仔细观察着脚印最后出现地点的残余痕迹。\
Fǎcáo strides over to inspect the traces near where the trail of footprints ends.

**巡防兵**：如果是说脚印消失，急雨接连几场，是有可能冲刷了河滩的。\
**Guard**: It rained a couple of times. The rain could have washed away the footprints.

**法曹**：不。这里不应当还有其他痕迹。\
**Facao**: If that's the case, there shouldn't be other tracks here.

**法曹**：例如此处。树藤的边缘，禽类爪印。\
**Facao**: Like this. A bird's claw marks at the edge of the rotten wood.

**法曹**：猛禽，相当有力的趾爪大小，和甲尖的锋锐程度。更早的时候曾在此落脚。\
**Facao**: It was a bird of prey. And judging from the size and the sharpness, it's quite strong.

**巡防兵**：真的……\
**Guard**: It's true ...

**巡防兵**：啊，这附近还有两组脚印！\
**Guard**: Hey, I found another two sets of footprints!

**巡防兵**：浅而窄，是年轻女子的脚印。\
**Guard**: They are shallow and narrow, possibly from the same person, a young woman.

**法曹**：此处，如此低矮，靠近河面的中空树藤，通常不是普通禽类的理想落脚点。\
**Facao**: The wood lies on the ground near the river. It's not a good spot for birds of prey to roost on.

**法曹**：来过的，是更大的东西。\
**Facao**: What stopped here was something even bigger.

**法曹**：……年轻女子，与如此庞大的猛禽狭路相逢，四周却没有血迹。\
**Facao**: A young woman met a huge bird of prey here, yet there is no bloodstain at all.

**法曹**：也许那失踪胡商的真相，与羽人所说仍有偏差。\
**Facao**: Perhaps the truth behind the foreign merchant's disappearance is different from the feather man's statement.

**法曹**：我们须得回去一趟职祠。\
**Facao**: We need to go back to the Zhící.

草地上，一只鹿蜀替代了原本站立于此的少女，甚至连葛天也因为受到惊吓而飞上了半空。\
On the steppes, a Lùshǔ stands in place of a girl. The fright of this transformation sends Gětiān up into the air.

**鹿蜀**：咴——！\
**Lushu**: *neighs*

**葛天**：……来不及了。\
**Getian**: Too late.

**葛天**：如此看来，即使仅饮下那娘子所予茶水也会发生异变，需得报给官府。\
**Getian**: So it seems her tea can also transform people. I must report this to the authorities.

**葛天**：你就在此处，不要走动。\
**Getian**: Stay here.

**小叶尼塞**：不。不，你不能走！\
**Yenisei**: No, no. You must not leave!

**葛天**：你——你能在水中说话？\
**Getian**: You ... can speak through the water?

**小叶尼塞**：你知道我的神秘术！但我维持不了太久了，刚才驱散烛夜已经耗费了我太多的力气——\
**Yenisei**: You know what my arcane skill can do! But I can't maintain it for long. I spent too much energy fighting the Zhúyès ...

**葛天**：……我须得走了。\
**Getian**: I must take leave.

**小叶尼塞**：你去哪儿？你要去救别斯米尔女士！\
**Yenisei**: Where are you going? You need to save Madam Bessmert!

**小叶尼塞**：不，我请求您！我请求您去救她。她看不见，一个人在酒坊，非常危险……\
**Yenisei**: Please, please, I'm begging you! Please save her. She can't see, and she's still alone in the tavern. She must be in great danger now ...

**葛天**：我曾想过的，我的术杖也遗落在了酒坊。但若此时再去，必将打草惊蛇。\
**Getian**: I have thought about it, given that my wand was also left in that tavern. But should I return, Jiǔ Niángzǐ might be alerted.

**葛天**：我观曲娘其人，本性非恶，除将他人变为鹿蜀以外，再无旁的行迹。你的友人应该暂时安全。\
**Getian**: I sense kindness in that girl. She hasn't done anything evil except for turning people into Lùshǔs. Your friend should be safe with her for the moment.

**葛天**：现下更要紧的是，在曲娘能够有所应对之前，揭穿她。\
**Getian**: The more urgent matter is to spread the word before she further repeats her mistake.

**葛天**：我须得去找能够全权处理此事之人。\
**Getian**: I must go find someone to handle this properly.

**小叶尼塞**：您一定得带上我。\
**Yenisei**: Please take me with you.

**小叶尼塞**：他们现在认为你是失踪案的凶手，你这样过去简直就是自首。\
**Yenisei**: They believe you are the one behind the missing persons cases now. You'll be turning yourself in if you go alone.

葛天一愣，似乎从未料想过这样的情状。\
Gětiān is startled, having never thought such an outcome might occur.

**葛天**：……原是如此。我实在不应下山的。\
**Getian**: I see. The world outside the mountains is indeed not meant for me to step into.

**小叶尼塞**：但你已经在了。而且——而且我们因为先前不知道详情的缘故，已经向里正指认了你……\
**Yenisei**: But you are already involved. Besides, we gave Lǐzhèng a drawing of you when I was not clear of the truth ...

**葛天**：无妨，我自会与他分辩清楚。\
**Getian**: No matter. I will reason with him.

**小叶尼塞**：那你也要带我去。我的神秘术，你看，这不就是最好的证明吗？\
**Yenisei**: Even so, you will need me there. Look at my arcane skill. It will be the best proof, right?

**小叶尼塞**：证明曲娘才是把人变成斑马，变成“鹿蜀”的元凶。\
**Yenisei**: So they will know that Jiǔ Niángzǐ is the real culprit who turned the people into horses, I mean, "Lùshǔs."

**葛天**：还需这般复杂吗？\
**Getian**: Is that really needed?

**小叶尼塞**：你已经被怀疑了！如果你真的没做那些事，就还必须用有百倍说服力的证据，证明给他们看。\
**Yenisei**: You need to know that you are a suspect! Even though I know you are innocent, you need something absolutely persuasive to prove it.

**小叶尼塞**：所以，你需要带我去。我的神秘术可以为你证明。\
**Yenisei**: All in all, you must take me with you. My arcane skill will vindicate you.

## NS-17 舍玉求石 / Jade or Stone

会在岁除的夜晚游荡于街市之上的，只有无家可归者与异乡人。\
Only vagrants and outsiders wander the streets on the eve of the Dùshuò Festival.

各户门前，燃着火星的庭燎与黑夜中张开的结彩，隔着落雨后尚未干燥的沙石道路遥遥相望。\
In front of each threshold, sparking fires burn below colorful decorations laid out in the dark night, peering out at each other from across sandy gravel roads that have not yet dried from the rain.

别斯米尔与小叶尼塞，就在这样寂静柔和的光亮中，继续向职祠前进着。\
Bessmert and Yenisei continue their advance toward the Zhící in the quiet, gentle light.

**别斯米尔**：这里……\
**Bessmert**: This place ...

**别斯米尔**：和白天不一样，街上几乎没有人，没有声音。\
**Bessmert**: ... looks so different than it does in the daytime. It's so quiet and empty.

**别斯米尔**：……简直就像正等着我们过去一样。\
**Bessmert**: As if it's waiting for us.

小叶尼塞停下来，在一处水泊中显影，试图安抚年长者。\
Yenisei stops to cast her reflection into a puddle of water, attempting to comfort Bessmert.

**小叶尼塞**：现在是晚上，他们至少还点燃了火盆。那些彩色的布匹被照得发亮。\
**Yenisei**: It's nighttime now. They have lit the braziers. There is cloth of different colors around them.

**小叶尼塞**：就像我们在新年时也点燃柏油桶，在房子上做各种装饰。您记得吗？\
**Yenisei**: Remember our New Years? We put up tar barrels and made festive fires. There were also decorations on the houses.

**别斯米尔**：是的，我记得。\
**Bessmert**: Yes, I remember that.

**别斯米尔**：也许，在这样的夜晚，人们都呆在家中，就像我们会在一年当中的最后一天晚上，与家人共同度过一样？\
**Bessmert**: Perhaps people here also stay with their families at this time of year, like we do on New Year's Eve.

**别斯米尔**：就像是一种习惯，一种温暖的常态。\
**Bessmert**: A heartwarming custom.

**小叶尼塞**：是啊……\
**Yenisei**: Yeah ...

**别斯米尔**：嘘，不要出声。\
**Bessmert**: Shush, quiet.

别斯米尔停住脚步，仔细听着声响。片刻后，一列巡夜兵从前面拐角处走过。\
Bessmert stops to listen carefully to the sound. A moment later, a line of night patrolmen pass by from the corner ahead.

他们面上松快，脚步不停，显然是正要换班回家的一批人。\
They march at ease without stopping, clearly ready for their shift change and the chance to get home.

等到他们的身影完全消失，小叶尼塞的身影才再次从水洼中显现。\
It isn't until they disappear completely that Yenisei's figure reappears in the puddle.

**小叶尼塞**：这些守卫倒是比新年的近卫军要更尽责，至少他们没有在这个时候就醉醺醺的。\
**Yenisei**: The guards here are more reliable than ours in the empire. At least they don't get drunk on New Year's Eve.

**小叶尼塞**：别斯米尔女士，职祠就在前面了——\
**Yenisei**: Madam, we are close to the Zhící.

**别斯米尔**：除了这些瓶子，我们什么准备也没有。你现在暂时不要使用神秘术了，保存些精力。一会儿说不定还会遇上些什么——\
**Bessmert**: We didn't prepare anything other than these bottles. Don't cast any skills for now. You need to rest. We don't know what's ahead of us ...

**别斯米尔**：等等。又有脚步声。\
**Bessmert**: Hold on. I heard something.

与先前巡防兵整齐的步履不同，这次从远处响起的，是更缓慢、疲惫的脚步声。\
Unlike the neat footsteps of the previous patrol, the distant sound they hear this time is of slower and wearier footsteps.

一人一鹿蜀都匆匆闪入一旁屋檐的荫蔽下。\
The woman and the Lùshǔ hurriedly dart into the shadow of the nearby eaves.

**别斯米尔**：脚步声很不均衡，一深一浅，没有固定的节奏。像是刚刚摔过跤，或喝多了酒的醉汉。\
**Bessmert**: Staggering footsteps, almost limping. Sounds like this person just tripped and fell, or drunk.

小叶尼塞循着别斯米尔描述的声音所在望去。\
Yenisei follows the sound described by Bessmert and looks around.

**小叶尼塞**：……奇怪，怎么会是曲娘？\
**Yenisei**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ? What is she doing here?

不远处，正是曲娘在跌跌撞撞地走着。一步一顿，两步一顿，最终在即将拐入狭窄巷中时停下。\
Not far from them, Jiǔ Niángzǐ hobbles along. She takes one step, then pauses, two steps, then pauses, and finally stops as she prepares to turn down a narrow alley.

她形容落魄，看上去像是与人刚刚打过一架，又或许只是真的醉了酒。\
She looks completely broken down, as though she has just been in a fight, or perhaps she's just drunk.

**曲娘**：……为什……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Why ...

暗处两人都能听到的自言自语，断续话音回响在空旷的除夜街道上。\
They can hear her talking to herself in the darkness, her voice echoing intermittently against the silently festive street.

**曲娘**：为什么……总是没有答案……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Why ... no answers for me ...

**曲娘**：……要等到什么时候……才能……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: How long do I have to wait ... before I ...

**小叶尼塞**：她在说什么？我听不懂，女士，您能——\
**Yenisei**: What is she saying? I don't understand at all. Madam, what about you ...

**别斯米尔**：嘘。\
**Bessmert**: Shh.

**曲娘**：呜……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: *sobbing*

看不清是否落泪，只能听见近似呢喃的哭声。\
They cannot see whether she's crying or not, but there is a soft sobbing that comes out like a whisper.

即使如此，她还是手中握拳，似乎紧紧攥着什么东西。\
Even so, she clenches her fists, as if tightly gripping something.

**曲娘**：是不是……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Is this ...

**曲娘**：错了……？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: ... a mistake?

**曲娘**：……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: ...

默然的泣音中，曲娘垂手。一个长条形的物件自她手中坠落，落入地面水洼。\
Amid her silent sobbing, Jiǔ Niángzǐ relaxes her hand. A long object falls from it and into a puddle on the ground.

**小叶尼塞**：啊……她扔下了一个东西。然后走了。\
**Yenisei**: Oh ... She dropped something and left.

**别斯米尔**：去了哪里？\
**Bessmert**: Where did she go?

**小叶尼塞**：我分辨不出她是不是往酒坊的方向，但确实已经离开了巷口。我们得去看看她究竟丢下了什么。\
**Yenisei**: I don't know if she's going to the tavern, but she has left the port. That's for sure. We should go find out what she dropped.

小叶尼塞的身影从水泊中消失。她迈出两步，回头咬住别斯米尔的衣角，半是拖拽地引导她，朝巷子入口拐角的明暗交界处走去。\
Yenisei's figure disappears from the puddle. She takes two steps, turns around and bites on Bessmert's hem, half dragging, half guiding her toward the corner of the alley's entrance, where the light and darkness intersect.

走近水泊，她才放开别斯米尔，绕到另一边。小叶尼塞低下头以饮水的姿势，从水坑里准确地叼出一根木片。\
Approaching the water, she finally lets go of Bessmert and goes around to the other side. Yenisei then lowers her head as though to drink from the puddle, and deftly removes a piece of wood from it.

她把木片上的水甩干，凑向别斯米尔手边，直至这东西被她握住。\
She shakes the water off the wooden slab and leans toward Bessmert's hand until her friend can grasp it.

**别斯米尔**：这是……一根木头长片。有些粗糙，上面还有刻痕。是写了字吗？\
**Bessmert**: It is ... a wooden chip. Rough surface, and some carvings on it. Is this an inscribed text?

**小叶尼塞**：也许是。请您拿好，让我看看另一面。\
**Yenisei**: Maybe. Please hold it. I'll check the other side.

**小叶尼塞**：从圆的那头开始，最上面刻着一个——唔——像是一个人。中间是一个人拿着碗，下面……\
**Yenisei**: Starting from the round end, there is a ... mmm ... a person, I guess, at the top; then there is another person holding a bowl in the middle ...

**小叶尼塞**：……唔……\
**Yenisei**: Hmm ...

**别斯米尔**：中间是一个人拿着碗，然后呢？\
**Bessmert**: A person holding a bowl in the middle, and ... and then?

**小叶尼塞**：最下面刻着一匹看上去有纹路的……马？\
**Yenisei**: Then there is a striped ... horse? At the bottom?

**小叶尼塞**：……这是什么意思？\
**Yenisei**: What does it mean?

**别斯米尔**：有纹路的马……\
**Bessmert**: A striped horse ...

**别斯米尔**：还记得葛天告诉你，鹿蜀有红色的鬃毛，老虎的纹路。\
**Bessmert**: Gětiān once said that a Lùshǔ has a red mane and the markings of a tiger.

**小叶尼塞**：您是想说，这上面画的是鹿蜀？上面可看不出颜色。\
**Yenisei**: You mean this is a Lùshǔ? But it has no colors.

**小叶尼塞**：不过……就算真的是鹿蜀，她又为什么要哭泣呢？\
**Yenisei**: Even if it is a Lùshǔ, why was she crying?

**小叶尼塞**：就我个人与她的接触来说……曲娘本性并不坏，只是她似乎一直背负着某种不为人知的枷锁。\
**Yenisei**: From my perspective, Jiǔ Niángzǐ is not a bad person. I think she did all these things for a reason—some kind of burden only known to herself.

**别斯米尔**：枷锁？\
**Bessmert**: Burden?

**小叶尼塞**：感觉而已。鉴于我们都没有听清她在说什么，或许怎么猜都是错的，女士。\
**Yenisei**: I'm only guessing. Since we didn't catch her words clearly, there is no conclusion, Madam.

话音落下，两人几乎一同沉默下来。自从入城，前途未卜的乌云就如影随形。\
That being said, the two of them fall into a shared silence. Since entering the city, the dark cloud of their uncertain future has followed them like a shadow.

**别斯米尔**：唉，不明白的事总是存在。我们还是先找到葛天先生，再做打算吧。\
**Bessmert**: Well, there's no easy answer to any question here. We should meet with Mr. Gětiān before making any further arrangements.

**小叶尼塞**：……嗯。\
**Yenisei**: Sure.

一人与一鹿蜀，都快步向前走去。\
The woman and the Lùshǔ walk forward at pace.

两人加快速度，在被另一队巡夜兵发现之前，抵达职祠灰色的院墙之外。\
The two increase their speed, arriving outside the gray walls of the Zhící courtyard before they might be discovered by another team of night patrollers.

这地方的街道，院墙四面总是修得较高，从旁走过去的人，除了院墙与墙砖之外，什么也看不见。\
The streets in this area are built with high walls surrounding their homes on all sides, so that people walking by can see nothing but stacked bricks.

**别斯米尔**：停。我听见了——\
**Bessmert**: Stop here. I hear ...

葛天就是在这个时候从职祠的院墙中飞出来的。\
It is at this moment that Gětiān flies over the Zhící courtyard's walls.

他的翅膀挥动的方式比前几次更轻，更轻，并且在发现墙脚下的人影之前，并没有打算停留。\
His wings flutter lighter—lighter than the previous few times, and he has no intention of stopping until he notices the figure at the foot of the wall.

**别斯米尔**：——！\
**Bessmert**: ...!

**别斯米尔**：葛天先生？\
**Bessmert**: Mr. Gětiān?

或者说，他原本没有打算停留，直到听见了别斯米尔的声音。\
Or perhaps, he had no intention of staying until he heard Bessmert's voice.

**葛天**：……是你？\
**Getian**: It's you?

葛天落到路旁的树上，抓紧了才生出些寒叶的枝杈。树影晃动，他没有出声，却因为认出了两人而停留。\
Gětiān perches on a tree by the roadside, tightly clutching branches bearing leaves that have only just begun to wither. The tree's shadow sways. But he goes silent, only stopping as he recognizes the two figures below.

附近地面平坦，缺少水洼。小叶尼塞只能衔住别斯米尔的衣角轻拽，确认她的猜想。\
The ground nearby is flat and long dried. Without a puddle, Yenisei can only grab hold of Bessmert's hem and tug on it lightly to confirm her guess.

别斯米尔于是理解了。她听着声音向侧前方走去，急切地来到树下。\
Bessmert, though, quickly understands. She listens to the sound and walks forward and to one side, eagerly reaching around beneath the tree.

**别斯米尔**：葛天先生——\
**Bessmert**: Mr. Gětiān ...

**葛天**：你们为何来此？\
**Getian**: Why are you here?

**别斯米尔**：您被放出来了？那曲娘呢？刚才她还在街上——\
**Bessmert**: Did they let you go? Have you seen Jiǔ Niángzǐ? She was on the street just now ...

**葛天**：无论你的猜测如何，我都会离开。\
**Getian**: Whatever speculation you are making, I am leaving.

**别斯米尔**：您说要走，是要去找曲娘对峙吗？\
**Bessmert**: Leaving? Are you going after her?

**葛天**：不。我本就不应下山，如今回去，也只是顺势而为。\
**Getian**: No. I was not meant to be here in the first place. It's only natural that I should return to the mountain.

**别斯米尔**：回去？但是曲娘的事还没得到解决，还有小叶尼塞，她和其他人都仍然是鹿蜀……\
**Bessmert**: Return? But we're not done with Jiǔ Niángzǐ yet. Yenisei and the others are still in the shape of Lùshǔ ...

**别斯米尔**：您难道不是看着她变成鹿蜀的吗？\
**Bessmert**: She was turned into a Lùshǔ in front of you. Are you going to just let her be?

**葛天**：她已全数告知与你。\
**Getian**: She has told you everything.

**别斯米尔**：当然！现在只有您能说服其他人，追究曲娘……我们两个，作为异乡人，是做不到这点的。\
**Bessmert**: Yes, she did! Now you're the only one who can persuade others to go after Jiǔ Niángzǐ ... We are foreigners here. People won't listen to us.

**葛天**：……我亦无可奈何。就连今日职祠之事，是我自愿被俘，你们才得以逃走。\
**Getian**: I am left with no other options. Today, at the Zhící, none of us would have gotten away if I hadn't surrendered.

这是事实，小叶尼塞作为全程的旁观者，是无法否认的。\
This is a fact that, as an observer of the entire scene, Yenisei cannot deny.

**葛天**：我若仍固执与那娘子为难，除被他们视作更大威胁之外，毫无用处。\
**Getian**: They will only see me as a greater threat if I insist on raising doubts about her.

**葛天**：而这一切，只因这些人都与曲娘相识已久。意即在此前提下，我与你们并无不同，都只是……\
**Getian**: They have known her for a long time but know nothing about me. My words have no greater effect than yours, for I'm also ...

**葛天**：异乡人。\
**Getian**: A foreigner here.

他的声音很轻，像夜色一样晦暗。\
His voice is light, but as gloomy as the night.

**别斯米尔**：即使是这样，您还没有用尽办法，就要放弃吗？\
**Bessmert**: Still, you're going to just give it all up before exhausting every possible way to end this?

一阵树影的晃动，是葛天防备地飞了起来。他似乎真的打定主意离开。\
A wave of swaying tree shadows causes Gětiān to fly up on alert. He seems to have finally made up his mind to leave.

**葛天**：……不必激我。无论葛天氏，抑或灭蒙鸟，都不欠你们任何东西。\
**Getian**: You need not prick my pride. Gětiāns and Mièméngs are never meant to get involved in this.

不待反应，整齐的脚步声就纷至沓来。\
Before a response is issued, the sound of rhythmic footsteps sounds, one after another.

无论来的是巡防兵还是其余人员，都足以令在场者立刻警惕。\
Whether it is the patrol or some other city personnel, it is enough to immediately alert the vigilant trio.

**小叶尼塞**：——！\
**Yenisei**: ...!

葛天却并未一走了之，表现更是与他的“口舌之快”不相符合。\
Gětiān though, does not leave. His actions are seemingly not in line with his tongue.

**葛天**：有人来了。你们——\
**Getian**: There are people coming. You ...

**？？？**：果真如此。\
**???**: I knew it.

一个威严的声音在人群牵头的地方响起。\
A bold and imposing voice sounds out from the spot the footsteps had been moving toward.

**法曹**：你们原本就是一伙的，胡商不过是进城的托词。\
**Facao**: You two are in it together. The merchant identity was only an excuse you made up to enter the city.

**法曹**：是也不是？\
**Facao**: Isn't that so?

**别斯米尔**：不，不是这样——\
**Bessmert**: No, please listen to me ...

**法曹**：你两人告给里正的说法，本就漏洞百出，现在竟然还敢堂而皇之，前来劫狱。\
**Facao**: The stories you told Lǐzhèng made no sense at all. How dare you come back like you did nothing and break into the jail?!

**葛天**：……你们先行一步。\
**Getian**: You go first.

**别斯米尔**：葛天先生！\
**Bessmert**: Mr. Gětiān!

别斯米尔直觉自己不应就这样逃走，此时唯一能助她确认决定的只剩下葛天。\
