Bessmert intuits that she shouldn't just run away. At that moment, the only one who can help her confirm her assumption is Gětiān.

被求助的对象却并未出声。他从树上俯冲下来，展开翅膀就像是给猎物覆下一片巨大的阴影。\
The one being sought for help does not make a sound. He dives from the tree, spreading his wings to cast an immense shadow over the scene.

他飞至巡防兵与别斯米尔中间，背对她们，双翅伸展更开，直到完全挡住了身后人的视野。\
He flies between the patrol and Bessmert, turning his back to them, then spreads his wings even wider until they completely block the view of those behind him.

在这种时刻，他才真正好似猛禽。\
At this moment, he truly seems like a bird of prey.

**葛天**：鹿蜀日行千里。先骑上她，快些走，我随后赶来。\
**Getian**: Lùshǔs are fleet-footed creatures. Get on her back and leave. I will join you shortly.

**葛天**：——走！\
**Getian**: Go!

**法曹**：哪里逃——抓住他们！\
**Facao**: Don't you run! Catch them!

得益于葛天的殿后，两人成功跑出坊市，来到小叶尼塞曾两次驻足的郊外浅滩处。\
Thanks to Gětiān's cover, the two successfully run from the neighborhood and arrive at the shallow shore on the city outskirts, where Yenisei has now stopped twice before.

此刻夜色更浓，天幕之中没有半点星子，只有微弱的月光散落河滩。\
At this moment, the night seems to have become even darker, without a single star to light the sky, and only faint moonlight trails scattered across the riverbank.

**小叶尼塞**：……感觉已经很久了，他不会——\
**Yenisei**: It's been quite a while. Is he ...

小叶尼塞显然是想起了葛天早上在职祠的遭遇。\
Yenisei cannot help but think of Gětiān's experience at the Zhící that same morning.

**别斯米尔**：相信他吧，孩子。既然能够自己出逃，就说明他并非毫无抵抗之力。\
**Bessmert**: Have faith in him, child. He is able to defend himself, since he managed to escape without others' help.

**别斯米尔**：甚至或许……\
**Bessmert**: I believe ...

**别斯米尔**：先前他为了解救你，连武器都可以抛掷，或许只是不愿意动武而已。\
**Bessmert**: I believe he is not aggressive. He left his wand behind when he tried to save you.

惴惴的等待中，一阵挥动翅膀的声音终于逐渐靠近。\
A long period of waiting, pregnant with anxiety, is finally broken by the sound of flapping wings.

**别斯米尔**：……！\
**Bessmert**: ...!

**小叶尼塞**：女士——！\
**Yenisei**: Madam!

葛天越过她们，停在扭曲生长的树藤上，收拢翅膀，趾爪紧紧扣住树木边缘。\
Gětiān crosses over them and stops along the twisted vines, folding his wings and tightly gripping the edges of the tree with his talons.

他头上的披挂一定在先前的冲突中散开过，才会在此刻让那下面原本被遮盖的，不解而紧绷的表情，完全显露出来。\
The garment on his head must have split during his fight, and now fully reveals his previously covered expression, one both baffled and tense.

**别斯米尔**：先生，您来了！\
**Bessmert**: You're here!

**别斯米尔**：您听起来没事——您还是要走吗？或者说，您改变主意了——\
**Bessmert**: You seem fine. Do you still intend to leave? Or, have you changed your mind?

别斯米尔循着动静，朝葛天落下的方向殷切地转过头去。\
Bessmert follows the sound of movement, turning her head toward where Gětiān landed.

**葛天**：……并非如此。我来，是为着最后一事。\
**Getian**: No. I'm here for one last thing.

**葛天**：在职祠牢中时，我听闻今夜曲娘设宴，那法曹亦会到场。\
**Getian**: When I was imprisoned in Zhící, I heard that Jiǔ Niángzǐ would hold a banquet at the tavern tonight, and the Fǎcáo was also invited.

**葛天**：趁此机会，我可将那些不完全的鹿蜀都从职祠带出，交还你们——\
**Getian**: I'll take the opportunity and get those half Lùshǔs out of there.

**别斯米尔**：等等，请等一下，先生。\
**Bessmert**: Please wait a second, Sir.

**葛天**：怎么？\
**Getian**: Yes?

**别斯米尔**：我们不会走的。他们都还没有变回来，我们至少还需要尝试去解除这个神秘术。\
**Bessmert**: We're not going anywhere. We must release them from the arcane skill and bring them back.

**葛天**：……你们若再不离开，怕是今夜之后，就再也来不及了。\
**Getian**: If you don't flee tonight, I'm afraid there will be no better chance for you to leave.

**葛天**：尽管我不知她究竟意欲何为，但仅是顺理推断的结果也足够可怖。\
**Getian**: Though her true intention is beyond my speculation, I fear the consequences of her action will be severe.

**别斯米尔**：这些事您都明白。\
**Bessmert**: You know full well the consequences.

**葛天**：嗯？我自然明白。\
**Getian**: Mm? Certainly.

**别斯米尔**：可您不愿阻止曲娘。\
**Bessmert**: But you won't help us stop her.

**葛天**：非我之祸，我已仁至义尽了。\
**Getian**: That is not my problem to address. I have done my part.

**别斯米尔**：那您为什么刚才要救我们，还提出要帮我们最后一件事？\
**Bessmert**: Then why did you help us get rid of the soldiers and offer to help again?

这话令葛天讶然，似乎从没想过。他抬起翅膀，形成一个类似人们掩面的姿势，又仿佛沉思。\
This question surprises Gětiān. He had never thought about it until that moment. He lifts his wings, forming a posture similar to cupping his face, sinking into contemplation.

片刻之后，他才思忖出解释。\
After a moment, he conjures up an explanation.

**葛天**：……我救人，不代表仍会继续参与此事。\
**Getian**: It doesn't suggest my further involvement in this matter.

**别斯米尔**：说实在的，您的行为与您的话语相矛盾了，先生。\
**Bessmert**: You are contradicting your own words, Sir.

葛天低头望向逐渐干涸的浅滩，和一片平静的河面。\
Gětiān lowers his head and looks towards the drying earth near the embankment out across the river's calm surface.

**葛天**：好，不若这样说吧。你们应当留意到，今夜街市之上行人寥寥。\
**Getian**: Very well. I will put it differently. Look at the street. It is empty tonight.

**葛天**：曾几何时，城中之人还会于除夜漂河灯祈愿。即使最朴实的圆灯，也相当明亮。\
**Getian**: There was a time when people sent lanterns down the river on New Year's Eve. Even the simplest lantern would glow like the moon on the water.

**葛天**：承载心愿的河灯，沿水带，顺水流，一路朝前。漂去愈远，愿望成真的希望便愈多。\
**Getian**: Those lanterns, carrying people's wishes, floated down the river. The further they went, the more wishes were granted.

**葛天**：但即使上方附着了能在激流之中卫护烛火的神秘术，多数河灯，都仍会在地形高差变化间失去踪迹。\
**Getian**: Some would cast arcane skills on their lanterns to keep them from getting wet. But most of the lanterns still disappeared in the depths of the mountains or at the waterfalls.

**葛天**：当我……仍在山上时，岁岁自山顶下望，最终如愿汇入下游与支流的那些河灯，在黑夜中如同光带一般醒目。\
**Getian**: I used to look down at the city from the mountain top, watching those lanterns float down the streams and merge into a light belt in the dark.

**葛天**：它们较这城中所谓彻夜通明的庭燎更亮，更具生命力。\
**Getian**: They were more brilliant and vibrant than the bonfires that were lit up all night in this city.

**别斯米尔**：……\
**Bessmert**: ...

鹿蜀也顺着葛天的目光，向河面看去，入目只有光秃狭窄，仿佛溪涧一样的“河水”。\
The Lùshǔ follows Gětiān's gaze and looks towards the river, only to see the bare and narrowing "river" looking more and more like a stream in her eyes.

这现实令她难以想象葛天话语里那样的光景，即使怀念已经几乎自他的语气中满溢。\
This sad reality of the present makes it difficult to imagine the scene described in Gětiān's words, despite the nostalgia overflowing from his tone.

别斯米尔也感受到了，但同伴的安危还始终牵系着她。\
Bessmert feels it too, but the safety of her companions remains a constant concern in her mind.

**别斯米尔**：对不起，我不知道您究竟想说什么，我们的时间已经不多了——\
**Bessmert**: I'm sorry. I don't understand what you mean. Time is against us ...

**葛天**：如今……河流干涸，活水失活。降雨却始终短暂急促，难以扭转水源的消逝。\
**Getian**: Now, the river has dried up, and the water no longer has vitality. Rainfall is getting scarce, accelerating the dying process.

**葛天**：所得不偿所失，自然无人放灯，河灯之俗废弛，成为必然。\
**Getian**: What was given does not compensate for what was lost. So, people no longer show up by the river and send their wishes at night.

**葛天**：我亦许久不曾得见那样的光带。\
**Getian**: And I have lost my opportunity to watch the light belt.

**葛天**：且事已至此，我却仍未悟得此身下山的缘由。也曾以为是因目睹途经山下之人，遭逢变形这等无妄之灾……\
**Getian**: Even so, to this day, I haven't fully understood why I was impelled to leave the mountain. I once thought I couldn't bear the sight of those humans being turned into other creatures.

**别斯米尔**：而您现在却觉得这个理由还不够，是吗？\
**Bessmert**: And now you think it's no longer worth the effort to put things back in order?

**葛天**：是。你们毕竟仅仅经过，如同河灯，有或无，皆与我无关。\
**Getian**: Yes. You people are no more than passengers in my life, drifting past me like those lanterns in the river.

**葛天**：更何况，若此事连他们所奉的摄提神都不关切，纵使我有再多作为，岂不都是多余？\
**Getian**: What's more, what is my purpose here if the Gods of Shètí they serve don't intend to intervene?

葛天的话语听上去竟然疑惑到近乎痛苦。他提问如同割肉饲虎，明知抛出之后不会有任何回报，却仍然坚持。\
Gětiān's words are so full of perplexity that they are almost painful. He poses questions like cutting meat to feed a tiger, knowing that there will be no reward after throwing them out, but still he insists.

一旁，沉默已久的小叶尼塞似乎理解这样的心情。于是她继续沉默，只去注视漆黑的河面。\
Yenisei, who has been silent on one side for a long time, seems to understand his feelings. And so she continues to remain silent, only looking at the pitch-black surface of the river.

河面也以寂静回望。\
The river too looks back with its own quieting babble.

**葛天**：况且，无论如何，那光亮都不再有了。\
**Getian**: The lights in the river are gone, and there will be no more in the future.

小叶尼塞注视着自己属于鹿蜀的倒影。\
Yenisei gazes at her reflection of Lùshǔ.

直到葛天说完“不再有”一句，她才突然抬起蹄子，踏进死寂的河水中。\
It isn't until Gětiān says "there will be no more" that she suddenly lifts her hooves and steps into the silent river.

**葛天**：——嗯？她要做什么？\
**Getian**: Mm? What is she doing?

别斯米尔当然也听见了声音，但她只摇了摇头。\
Of course, Bessmert can also hear the sound of her entering the water, but she only shakes her head.

她知道那女孩要做些什么。这恰好是她能够帮忙的时刻。\
She knows what the girl is going to do. The moment has arrived for her to offer her assistance.

**葛天**：即使水浅亦有危险，这——\
**Getian**: Even shallow water could also be dangerous. She ...

**别斯米尔**：相信她吧。这孩子知道自己在做什么。\
**Bessmert**: Trust her. She knows what she's doing.

水位逐渐吞没了小叶尼塞的半个身子。同时，歌声响起。\
The water begins to engulf half of Yenisei's body. At the same time, her song begins.

**葛天**：她究竟要做什么？\
**Getian**: What is this?

灯彩一般的光点从眼前狭窄如同溪流的河上蓦地燃起，像烈烈的火焰烧灼水面。\
Colorful dots of light suddenly ignited in the narrow river in front of them, burning like intense flames along the water's surface.

而后，与这歌声一起，光点沿柔软的河滩一路蜿蜒，如同时间长河上匆匆旅人，步履不停。\
Then, the dots of light meandered to the soft riverbank, drifting with the song, like travelers on the long river, journeying without end.

这光所经之处，比坊市的结彩，比数年经过山下的河灯，都要更亮。\
The place where the light passes through now shines brighter than all the decorations in the city streets, more than many years worth of river lanterns that had passed through the mountains.

**别斯米尔**：您瞧，河灯。虽然我无法清晰地看到色彩，但我能感觉到它的明亮。\
**Bessmert**: There are river lanterns, yes? I can't see them, but I can feel the light.

**别斯米尔**：而您能真切地看到这一切，不是吗？\
**Bessmert**: Are you appreciating them with your own eyes?

**葛天**：……我，不……\
**Getian**: I ... don't ...

在这样的景象面前，葛天已经近乎哑然。他从骨相上能读出小叶尼塞的神秘术渊源，却无法想象现在这一幕的发生。\
Faced with such a scene, Gětiān is struck dumb. He can sense Yenisei's arcanist origins in her bones, but he cannot even begin to imagine what is happening at this moment.

**别斯米尔**：葛天先生……\
**Bessmert**: Mr. Gětiān ...

**别斯米尔**：真正的既成事实是……因为您已经下山，已经见过了那些原本不必留意的人。\
**Bessmert**: The fact is ... you've seen too many people and grown attached to too many things since you left the mountain.

**别斯米尔**：他们停留在您的心中，就像那些您曾经见过的，耀眼的河灯。\
**Bessmert**: They float in your mind, glistening like the river lanterns.

**别斯米尔**：而您不愿像再也看不见河灯的光亮一样，再也看不见他们。\
**Bessmert**: And you're saddened by the idea that they will be gone one day, like the lanterns drifting away from your sight.

**葛天**：——！\
**Getian**: ...!

**别斯米尔**：但您从来没有想过，那些绚丽的，灵动的，带着企盼的光，是可以再亮起来的。\
**Bessmert**: But have you thought that those bright, agile, and hope-rising flakes of light would gleam once again?

**别斯米尔**：命运从来不是一成不变的。\
**Bessmert**: The path of destiny is not always a dead end.

**葛天**：……\
**Getian**: ...

**别斯米尔**：现在放弃，还太早了，葛天先生。\
**Bessmert**: It's too soon to give up, Mr. Gětiān.

**别斯米尔**：以及……这是您的骨杖。请您收好，且再考虑一下吧。\
**Bessmert**: Here ... It is your wand. Put it away, and please give this another thought.

## NS-18 除夜宴 / New Year's Eve

入夜的酒坊院中，天色仍是有雨将落未落的低沉，雾气缭绕在所有人头顶。\
In the tavern courtyard at night, the sky is still gloomy with the promise of rain yet to fall, and mist shrouds the heads of all present.

但欢庆的酒宴氛围似乎并未受到影响，湿润的水雾轻易被喧嚷人气冲散。\
But the festive atmosphere of the banquet seems unaffected, and the damp mist is easily dispersed by the clamor and high spirits.

**曲娘**：……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: ...

**城中居民Ⅰ**：呀，曲娘。今年知道要在门口迎了。\
**Citizen I**: Oh, Jiǔ Niángzǐ, you are welcoming us at the door this year.

**曲娘**：因为里正说过……啊！欢迎，欢迎，你们都来啦。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Because Lǐzhèng said ... Oh, welcome, guys! You're all here.

**城中居民Ⅰ**：怎么了？瞧着魂不守舍的。\
**Citizen I**: What's going on? You seem absent-minded.

**城中居民Ⅰ**：给，这是烛夜花苗。想着若是你，定不要别家酿的酒。\
**Citizen I**: Here, Zhúyè flower seeds. I know this is the only flower you would use to make liquor.

**城中居民Ⅰ**：这儿呢，还有我自己绣的结彩——两匹不多，对鹿纹，好不好也寻个地方挂起来，不比去岁你送的纸马差。\
**Citizen I**: And here are two festoons with auspicious deer patterns. Not a fancy kind, but I made the pattern myself. Put it on the wall if you want. It would look as lovely as the horse paper-cutouts you gave me last year.

**曲娘**：呀，当然！这……这太贵重了，我马上去挂起来——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Oh, dear, this is too much. I'll hang them up right away!

**曲娘**：谢谢你们！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Thank you so much!

**城中居民Ⅰ**：哪里的话。你这就知道站在门口迎客了，我还想着偷偷地来，喝光酒再同你打招呼呢。\
**Citizen I**: Don't worry! To be honest, I didn't see that you would be welcoming us at the door. I thought I could sneak in and empty the jars before you showed up.

本应在各自家中守岁的邻里，在曲娘的盛情邀请下，都会聚在这摆上了庭燎金彩与珍馐美酒的一方院落中。\
Most had intended to spend the festival at home, but now they gather here at the generous invitation of Jiǔ Niángzǐ. The golden colors of the courtyard displayed for all to see, punctuated by the delicacies and fine liquor on offer.

几乎各处都坐满了人，像戈壁上的石砾一样散落。抛开身份，抛开年纪，毫不拘礼。\
Almost every corner is filled with people, who scattered about like sand in the desert, with status and age set aside and all notions of formality cast to the wind.

**曲娘**：一个，两个，三个，四个……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: One, two, three, four ...

**里正**：曲娘。\
**Lizheng**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ.

**曲娘**：七个，八个，九个……啊，啊？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Seven, eight, nine ... Huh, hmm?

**里正**：大家都入座了。\
**Lizheng**: Everyone is here.

**曲娘**：也许还有人没到……我还没数清楚呢。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I'm not sure about that. I haven't counted them up yet.

**里正**：那么，也许是法曹未到。他的妻儿早已落座，只是尚未得见他本人。\
**Lizheng**: That might be Fǎcáo. His family is here, without him.

**曲娘**：这么晚了，他还在巡逻吗？是不是还在寻找胡人娘子她们？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Is he still patrolling? This late? Is he still looking for the foreign ladies?

**里正**：应当是。我们就这样让其他人等着，不大妥当。\
**Lizheng**: Perhaps. But it is not polite to keep other guests waiting.

**曲娘**：这样……那，那我们先开始吧。我会给他留酒的。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I see ... Then, let's start the party first. I'll save him his liquor.

**里正**：好，诸位——\
**Lizheng**: Alright, everyone!

**里正**：主人家有祝酒辞要唱，烦请听过。\
**Lizheng**: The hostess has a toast to make. Please pay attention.

**曲娘**：感谢您。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Thank you.

曲娘在人群中站起来，以期能让大家都瞧见自己。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ stands up above the crowd, hoping that everyone can see her.

尽管头脑中仍是一片空白，有些心里话却在底下殷殷的眼神鼓舞之中，自然流露。\
Although her mind begins blank, some heartfelt words bubble up, brought to the fore by the encouraging gazes below.

**曲娘**：咳……咳！大家都知道，我不识字，也说不出来什么子丑寅卯。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: A-ahem! Everyone here knows that I can't read and can't say some sweet words like toasting ...

**城中居民Ⅴ**：随便说点吧！\
**Citizen V**: Just say whatever you want!

**城中居民Ⅳ**：死相，别打断人家！\
**Citizen IV**: Don't interrupt her, you imbecile!

**曲娘**：哦，嗯？好，哈哈，我刚才说到哪里了……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Oh, alright? Well, haha, where was I ...

**里正**：祝酒辞。\
**Lizheng**: A toast.

**曲娘**：嗯，对。祝酒辞！我哪会自己写呀，所以只好从职祠的书上看了一句，我觉得很好听，是叫——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Right. A toast! But I can't do it myself, so I copied a line from the book at the place where I work now. I like how it sounds!

**曲娘**：“劝君金屈卮，满酌不须辞。”\
**Jiu Niangzi**: "I bid thee all to drink and be merry, do not stay thy hand from thine cup."

**曲娘**：希望我没有念错，“劝君金屈卮，满酌不须辞”……是说劝大家喝酒，有更多的酒喝，不许推辞！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Hope I didn't pronounce it wrong. It means ... people should drink, and drink more, so you shouldn't say no to it!

**城中居民Ⅲ**：真是这个意思吗？\
**Citizen III**: Is that so?

**曲娘**：——哎，不管啦！总之……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Well, whatever! Anyhow ...

不待在座各人有所反应，她仰头，将自己碗中的东西一饮而尽。\
Without waiting for everyone present to react, she looks up and drinks her bowl dry in a single gulp.

酒碗微倾，表示已经空掉。曲娘的目光从每个人脸上一一滑过，最后快活地笑了起来。\
Her bowl is now slightly tilted, indicating that it has been emptied. Jiǔ Niángzǐ's gaze glides over each face, one by one, and finally she laughs with glee.

**曲娘**：满酌不辞，再卷白波，会饮千岁！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Bottoms up, and fill your cups. Cheers!

很快，“千岁”应和声连连响起，节节拔高，似乎连屋檐上的结彩都被震动。\
Soon, the cry of "cheers" begins to echo through the courtyard, one after another, rising wave by wave, until even the festoons on the eaves are shaking.

**人群**：千岁！！\
**Crowd**: Cheers!

**曲娘**：打从我入城起，乡邻们待我就很好，很亲切。除夜设宴是我能为大家做的为数不多的好事情。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: You've always been nice and warm to me since I came here. I can't do anything in return but host this feast.

**曲娘**：愿大家畅饮美酒，除夜平安，朔日……心想事成。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Hope you enjoy the liquor and the dinner. I wish you a Peaceful New Year's Eve. May all of your wishes come true in the coming Shuòrì.

**曲娘**：呃，里正，您要不要再说些什么？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Er, Lǐzhèng, do you have anything else to say?

**里正**：我这老人家，今日只需说一句“除夜平安”，就够了。\
**Lizheng**: A "Peaceful New Year's Eve" would be enough.

**城中居民Ⅴ**：除夜平安——\
**Citizen V**: Peaceful New Year's Eve ...

**城中居民Ⅱ**：除夜平安！\
**Citizen II**: Peaceful New Year's Eve!

**城中居民Ⅲ**：除夜平安。\
**Citizen III**: Peaceful New Year's Eve.

里正坐在人群中，就像一位普通的老者一样。\
Lǐzhèng sits among them, like a kindly old man from their neighborhood, rather than an imposing governor.

人群在他发言后的片刻便再次松散下来，碰杯拈筷的声音此起彼伏。\
The crowd loosens up once again shortly after he finishes speaking, the sound of clinking cups and tapping chopsticks continuing to rise and fall.

**城中居民Ⅳ**：曲娘，这说得不是挺好吗，看来把人家写给你的情诗粘在墙上，朝夕相对还是有些耳濡目染的用处——\
**Citizen IV**: You did a good job with the toast, Jiǔ Niángzǐ. Looks like you've learned something from those love poems. You must have read them unconsciously after you stuck them on the wall ...

**城中居民Ⅰ**：瞧你说的，我们金市早就不兴贴诗在墙上啦！\
**Citizen I**: Oh, please, that custom is no longer popular in our neighborhood!

**城中居民Ⅰ**：不如说，现今都学曲娘把诗铰成帕子做包，但凡带着出门，人人都羡慕好奇呢！\
**Citizen I**: I'd rather transfer the poem onto a kerchief and make a purse out of it, just like Jiǔ Niángzǐ did. It draws so much attention on the street!

**曲娘**：其实，他们写的东西，我还是看不懂……但字都是很好看的。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Actually, I still can't read what they write on the purse. But the characters seem beautiful!

**城中居民Ⅴ**：那今天这几句，说得这么流利，谁教你的呀？\
**Citizen V**: What about the one you recited during the toast? You sounded really fluent. Who taught that to you?

**曲娘**：噢，哈哈，是前任执礼教的！就是回乡去的那位执礼，她教给我的。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Oh, haha, that's from the former Zhílǐ, the one who went back to her hometown. She taught me that.

**城中居民Ⅲ**：说到这儿，她还回来吗？\
**Citizen III**: Speaking of her, is she going to come back?

**曲娘**：我不知道呀……不过她这会儿，应该也已经在家乡吃上除夜饭了吧。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I didn't know any better ... But by now, she should be at home, having New Year's Eve dinner.

**城中居民Ⅰ**：曲娘得了她的信？这若是不回来了，你真做执礼，那酒坊要怎么办？\
**Citizen I**: Did you hear from her? If she doesn't come back, you'll have to work as the official Zhílǐ. Who will take care of the tavern by then?

**城中居民Ⅰ**：这酒坊主人隔些日子就换来换去，要不是你来了，完全是个烂摊子。\
**Citizen I**: The tavern has never had a reliable owner before you. It would have still been run down if you hadn't taken over it.

**里正**：曲娘为人正直，识大体，有仁善之心。这样的心性，无论做酒坊主人，还是做执礼，都应付得来。\
**Lizheng**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ is kind and warm-hearted. Such a girl of integrity can perform well in both running a tavern and being a Zhílǐ.

**城中居民Ⅰ**：评价这样高，不是偏心，就是确有其事。\
**Citizen I**: You have a high regard for her, Lǐzhèng. Are you telling the truth or showing partiality?

**里正**：自然是确有其事。几个时辰前，她在职祠的一番话，仍使我记忆犹新。\
**Lizheng**: The truth, of course. What she said in the Zhící a few hours ago is still vivid in my mind.

**里正**：学无止境，大抵如此。\
**Lizheng**: I once again realized that it's never too late to learn.

**曲娘**：没有，没有你说的那样好，里正。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: No, no, no, I'm not as good as you say.

**城中居民Ⅰ**：什么话？\
**Citizen I**: What did she say?

**里正**：什么“绝迹易，无行地难”，“道与之貌，天与之形，无以好恶内伤其身”……手到拈来的引用。\
**Lizheng**: Things like "One can remove the footsteps, but not the path one walketh on," "Act not against the nature of thy flesh, for through it all things were made." ... She made it sound easy.

人群发出了一阵子大惊小怪的呼声。\
The crowd erupts in a series of alarmed cries.

**城中居民Ⅴ**：真有这事？\
**Citizen V**: Really?

**里正**：自然。曲娘即使不识字，也一直在摸索着修习，对典籍名句，亦有自己的理解。\
**Lizheng**: Absolutely. She is indeed illiterate, but she keeps learning and interprets the classic sayings in her own way.

**里正**：当时若有旁的书生在，也一定会为她的话语所撼动，挑不出错处来。只可惜，当时她面对的是妖，而非人。\
**Lizheng**: Even if there were other scholars, they would be convinced by her powerful speech. Sadly, the one she confronted was not a human but a Yāo.

**城中居民Ⅰ**：在职祠，面对妖……莫非，曲娘与那羽人对峙了？\
**Citizen I**: Confronted a Yāo in the Zhící ... Was that the feather man?

**里正**：她以为那羽人是祥瑞，所以问了些问题。\
**Lizheng**: She thought the feather man was Xiángruì and asked him some questions.

**城中居民Ⅴ**：你竟然还问他话！你就不怕他将你也变成有斑纹的怪马吗？\
**Citizen V**: You actually asked him questions?! He could have turned you into another striped horse!

**曲娘**：呃，我当时，想不了那么多……我第一次见到形貌那么像画上祥瑞的妖，所以就——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Um, I didn't think of that back then ... This is the first time I've ever been so close to a Yāo. He looks so similar to the ones in the books! So I ...

**法曹**：曲娘——\
**Facao**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ ...

**法曹**：曲娘，曲娘在何处？\
**Facao**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ, where are you?

一阵急促的脚步声踏来，为首的身影两三步便跨进了酒坊中。\
The rapid sound of footsteps approaches, and their leader's figure steps into the tavern in several broad and forceful steps.

粗嘎而匆忙的声音将院中的热闹直接掐断。\
The abrupt sound severs the excitement in the courtyard.

**曲娘**：什么——怎么了？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Wh-what happened?

**城中居民Ⅰ**：这是……？\
**Citizen I**: What is ...?

**法曹**：曲娘在何处？\
**Facao**: Where is Jiǔ Niángzǐ?

**曲娘**：这儿，我在这儿！这是怎么啦？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Here, I'm here! What's happening?

**法曹**：那两个胡人原来与葛天早有勾结。她们助葛天越狱，现已用神秘术躲进了郊外。\
**Facao**: Turns out those foreign ladies have been in league with Gětiān the whole time. They helped him break out of jail and hid themselves in the wild with their arcane skills.

**法曹**：假使不久还要落雨，河边滩险，她们不在外面久留，一定会过来找你。\
**Facao**: I'm sure it will rain again soon and it will be dangerous to stay in the wild. By then, they will come to you.

**法曹**：因为你正是那羽人的目标。\
**Facao**: Because you are the feather man's target.

院中，人群的视线对法曹紧追不放，而法曹的眼睛则直盯曲娘，似乎知道有些拒绝的话，此刻就在她的舌苔底下。\
In the courtyard, the crowd's gaze follows Fǎcáo closely, while Fǎcáo's own eyes are fixed on Jiǔ Niángzǐ. They realize now that some word of resistance is on her tongue.

**里正**：这——曲娘，你——\
**Lizheng**: What ... Jiǔ Niángzǐ, you ...

**里正**：——你须得离开这里，不可留在酒坊。\
**Lizheng**: You must leave here. You can't stay in the tavern.

**曲娘**：酒坊——酒坊是我的酒坊！我为什么要离开这里？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: But it's-it's my tavern! Why am I leaving my own place?

**法曹**：你现在处于危险之中，为了保证你的安全，须得随巡防兵移步官府。既然葛天能够越狱，职祠亦不可靠。\
**Facao**: You are in danger. Since Gětiān was able to break out of jail, he'll for sure be able to break into the Zhící. For your safety, I will have my soldiers escort you to the government office.

**法曹**：我们只剩下官府一个选择。\
**Facao**: That's the only safe place now.

**曲娘**：不，我不能走。他既不是祥瑞，也不是什么大妖……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: No, I'm not leaving. He is neither a Xiángruì nor a strong Yāo ...

**曲娘**：我们不用怕他呀！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Why are we afraid of him?

翅膀划破空气的声响将曲娘话音的末尾覆盖。\
The sound of wings cutting through the air overlaps the end of Jiǔ Niángzǐ's question.

来者展翅，如同阴云遮盖了满院结彩与庭燎光华。\
The new arrival spreads his wings, like a dark cloud blanketing the courtyard's colorful decorations and dazzling lights.

**城中居民Ⅲ**：当心！\
**Citizen III**: Watch out!

**城中居民Ⅰ**：啊！\
**Citizen I**: Waaah!

**葛天**：的确如此。\
**Getian**: She's right.

**葛天**：因为你们更需要惧怕的，是酿酒的这娘子。\
**Getian**: You need not fear me. This lady owner of the tavern is the bigger concern here.

**法曹**：列队——！\
**Facao**: Formation One!

巡防兵训练有素地将酒坊包围，跑走踢踏的声音响彻院落。\
The well-trained guards surround the tavern, and the sound of running, trampling feet echoes through the courtyard.

**法曹**：我就知道你会来找她。\
**Facao**: I knew you would come for her.

**法曹**：你的同伙呢，她们让你来打前锋？\
**Facao**: Where are your accomplices? Are you the vanguard of the team?

**葛天**：曲娘，你现在悔改，仍有机会。\
**Getian**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ, it's not too late for you to stop.

**葛天**：不要再将人变为鹿蜀了，失踪者已是太多。\
**Getian**: No more turning people into a Lùshǔ. Too many people have gone missing because of you.

对多数人来说尚算新鲜的信息，像石子投进水中一样在人群中泛起阵阵涟漪。\
This information, unknown present, hits like a stone cast into water.

一些窃窃的疑问与私语。\
Questions and whispers begin to circulate through the crowd like ripples in a pond.

**城中居民Ⅴ**：人变成鹿蜀？通缉令上不是说，失踪者变成的是斑纹怪马吗？\
**Citizen V**: Turn people into a Lùshǔ? But the wanted poster says those are striped horses.

**城中居民Ⅳ**：他究竟在说什么？\
**Citizen IV**: What is he talking about?

曲娘抬头望向空中，坦然直视着居高临下的葛天。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ looks up into the air and stares straight at the looming figure of Gětiān above her.

**曲娘**：你在说什么？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: What are you talking about?

**曲娘**：你根本不了解鹿蜀。而且，失踪者和我有什么关系？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: You know nothing about Lùshǔs. Besides, what do I have to do with the missing people?

**城中居民Ⅰ**：曲娘……他在胡说，是不是？\
**Citizen I**: He's talking nonsense, right, Jiǔ Niángzǐ?

**法曹**：不必与他多说。\
**Facao**: Save the talk.

**法曹**：先捉住他。\
**Facao**: Catch him first.

## NS-19 如愿 / A Wish Come True

不速之客并不愿出手攻击民众。一场单方面的较量，仅仅躲避的一方会落败，简直再自然不过。\
The uninvited guest is not willing to attack, even in his own defense. So a one-sided battle ensues. It is only natural that the side resigned to only evading will eventually lose.

**法曹**：认输吧，然后解除你的神秘术，将失踪者变回来。\
**Facao**: Surrender, and dispel your arcane skill. Turn the victims back to who they were.

此时，异乡人也赶到了包围圈之外。她们携带的神秘术使落到耳中的话语，再次悄然改变。\
At this moment, Bessmert and Yenisei rush to the edge of the encirclement. The communication arcane skill that Gětiān cast on them earlier is quietly translating the words for people.

**法曹**：让我们在朔日前了结此事。\
**Facao**: We will put an end to it before the Shuòrì.

**葛天**：可我并不能使人变形，自然也无法……解除它。\
**Getian**: But I don't possess the power to transform people from one shape to another, and thus, cannot turn them back.

**葛天**：能应许你所求者，另有其人。\
**Getian**: You're asking the wrong one.

葛天勉力支撑，堪堪停在檐上，依然意有所指地望向曲娘。\
Gětiān struggles to hold on and rests on the eaves, still looking directly at Jiǔ Niángzǐ with some hidden meaning.

但曲娘全不在意，只是坦然而愤怒地回望。那一眼用力到几乎是在瞪着了。\
But Jiǔ Niángzǐ shows no hint of understanding, simply looking back with a placid anger. Her look is so forceful that it is almost a glare.

**曲娘**：你究竟为什么这么执着于栽赃给我？我从没有见过那些失踪的人……我真的不明白你在说什么！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Why do you have to blame this on me? I've never met those missing people. And I have no idea what you're talking about!

**曲娘**：难道、难道我以前……曾经和你结过什么仇吗？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Is-is this because ... Did you have a grudge against me or something?

**葛天**：无仇无怨。我此行，只为阻止事态更加恶化。\
**Getian**: Nothing of that sort. I'm here only to prevent an unwanted escalation.

**葛天**：毕竟，今夜我若就此离去，你们亦无可奈何。于我自身，更是毫无损失，左不过换一地栖息。只是那些被变成残缺鹿蜀之人……\
**Getian**: I could have just walked away, and there's nothing you can do. I could have gone to other mountains, and life would have continued as it has always been. But for those who have been turned into half Lùshǔs ...

**葛天**：就当真回天乏力了。\
**Getian**: No one can get them out of this trouble.

曲娘在他眼前怔住，片刻后才挣扎出一些疑问的词句，声音却微微颤抖了。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ stands stunned before him. After a moment, she struggles out an accusatory remark, but her voice trembles slightly.

**曲娘**：残缺——残缺鹿蜀？你的意思是……我后院里，职祠内的……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: "Been turned into half Lùshǔs"? Are you saying that the animals in my backyard, and those in the Zhící ...

**曲娘**：——它们，都是失踪者吗……？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Are they all the missing people?

**曲娘**：可是，它们只是鹿蜀。我很清楚，我从遇到它们第一眼，我就知道——它们和我很像，是……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: But, but I thought they were just Lùshǔs. The first time I saw them, it was clear that we were alike. We're just some ...

**曲娘**：有残缺的瑞兽。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: ... half divine beasts.

人群哗然。她充耳不闻，只是愣愣地望着葛天。\
The crowd is thrown into a commotion. She turns a deaf ear to them and once again stares blankly at Gětiān.

**曲娘**：它们不可能是人。我也从来没有对它们做过任何——任何能让它们变形的事情！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: So they must not be humans! I've done nothing to-to transform them!

**曲娘**：我只是很好地照料它们，想知道它们都从哪里来……以及能不能带我……回家。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I'm just taking good care of them, so that they can tell me where they're from, and if they can ... take me home.

震颤的尾音落下，了解她已经有所动摇的葛天只能叹息。他似乎已经开始看清事情的全貌了。\
Her trembling words usher in a silence. Gětiān, who knows she has already begun to waver, can only sigh. It seems he is starting to see the whole picture for what it is.

**葛天**：……\
**Getian**: ...

**葛天**：“杻阳之山，有兽焉，其状如马而白首，其文如虎而赤尾，其音如谣，其名曰鹿蜀。”\
**Getian**: "The Niǔyáng Mountain shelters the beasts. The beasts have white heads, red tails, the bodies of horses, and the markings of tigers. When they neigh, the sound becomes music. The name is Lùshǔ."

**葛天**：你院中那些身带斑纹的“马”，即为残缺的鹿蜀。在月色下，火光中，它们哀叫声同歌谣，毛色也一如传说。\
**Getian**: The "striped horses" you keep in the yard are half Lùshǔs. They look like what's told in the tales, and they cry like humming songs in the moonlight.

**葛天**：你亲手所制的木人，能附酒水以“存想”之力，将人变为鹿蜀，或残缺的鹿蜀。而那些木人——曾在沛霖川支流中浸泡过，是也不是？\
**Getian**: And the wooden dolls infuse your arcane skill, The Shape of Will, into the liquor, which turns people into Lùshǔs, or, half Lùshǔs. As for the dolls, they were once soaked in the water of Pèilín River, were they not?

**曲娘**：……后院的河……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: The stream runs through the backyard ...

**曲娘**：不——不可能！它们只是会去那里玩耍，仅仅只是浸泡……不应该，会……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: No, no way! They went there just for fun or a bath! They should not ... should not ...

在巡防兵组成的包围圈外，别斯米尔透过声音判断着进程。\
Beyond the encirclement formed by patrolling troops, Bessmert judges the course of events through the sound of people's voices.

曲娘沉默了。怀疑的种子已经种下，证人也是时候走入舞台。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ falls silent. The seeds of suspicion have been planted, and it is now time for witnesses to take the stand.

**斑纹马？**：咴——\
**Striped Horse?**: *neighs*

藏于人群之中的小叶尼塞猛地撞开两旁的士兵。\
Hidden in the crowd, Yenisei crashes into the soldiers on both sides of her.

剑戟的锋锐从她属于鹿蜀的皮肉上划过，但她仿佛全然未觉，径直冲向水缸所在的方向。\
Sharp swords and spears brush over her Lùshǔ skin, but she seems completely unfazed, charging straight toward the direction of the water jar.

**法曹**：什——谁放它进来的？\
**Facao**: What ... Who let it in?

**法曹**：逮住它——\
**Facao**: Catch it!

缸中漏出的水，在庭院里深浅不一的地面积起块块水洼。虽然不多，但也足够支撑片刻。\
The water leaking from the jar creates puddles in the crevices of the courtyard. Although it isn't much, it is still enough to buy some time.

**小叶尼塞**：停下！\
**Yenisei**: Wait!

**里正**：——是你？！\
**Lizheng**: It's you?!

里正立即抬头望向葛天，似乎要从他静止的身形上看出刚刚释放神秘术的痕迹，只一无所获。\
Lǐzhèng immediately looks up at Gětiān, as though wishing to catch a glimpse of the arcane skill cast from his still figure, only to find nothing there.

**法曹**：老虎的斑纹，红色的鬃毛……与羽人的描述一致，可倒影里却是人。\
**Facao**: The markings of a tiger and a red mane ... Exactly what the feather man said. But its reflection is a woman.

人群里发出一阵倒吸凉气的声音。\
A gasp sounds out from the crowd.

**城中居民Ⅰ**：天哪，那倒影里的，不是前日街上那位小娘子吗？\
**Citizen I**: Oh my, that reflection. Is that the foreign lady from the street earlier?

曲娘望向小叶尼塞的眼神中亦是不解。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ also casts a bewildered gaze toward Yenisei.

**曲娘**：你是——你是鹿蜀。你现在真的已经是鹿蜀了。这才是……鹿蜀。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: You-you are a Lùshǔ. You're a real Lùshǔ now. This ... is what a Lùshǔ should be.

**曲娘**：……可为什么，你还在这里？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: But, but why are you still here?

**小叶尼塞**：我不明白你的意思，曲娘小姐。\
**Yenisei**: I don't see what you mean, Ms. Jiǔ Niángzǐ.

**曲娘**：你受伤了。而且你不应该在这里的，这不对。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: You're hurt. And you shouldn't be here. It's not right.

她轻轻用手点了一下水泊，仿佛在安抚一个看不见的自己的倒影。\
She lightly taps the pool of water with her hand, as if soothing the invisible reflection of herself.

**曲娘**：我以为，你已经能认出自己的同伴，早就和他们一起离开了。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I thought you were able to recognize your teammates and had already left here.

**小叶尼塞**：噢，天哪。\
**Yenisei**: Wait, what ... GOSH!

**小叶尼塞**：——我、我明白了。\
**Yenisei**: I ... I get it!

就连小叶尼塞在水中的倒影，也因这恍然大悟而波动了。\
Even Yenisei's reflection in the water ripples in response to this sudden realization.

**小叶尼塞**：曲娘，你以为让我变成鹿蜀，就能从那些动物里认出我的同伴了，是吗？那晚你说过，你想帮我，你会帮我。原来是这样……\
**Yenisei**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ, you turned me into a Lùshǔ because you thought that would help me find my teammates, didn't you? Last night, you said you would help me, so this is how you ...

**小叶尼塞**：可那并不是在向你求助，只是某种感慨，或者倾述，总之——我当时并不想从你身上得到什么。\
**Yenisei**: But I was not asking for help! I was only being emotional or pouring out my troubles. Anyway, I was not asking for anything from you.

**小叶尼塞**：那个晚上……我能感受到你是发自内心地待我。你很恳切，那不会是作假的。\
**Yenisei**: From the talk, I could feel the sincerity from the bottom of your heart. It was too real to be fake.

**小叶尼塞**：这就足够了，我能理解的。\
**Yenisei**: I understand you were trying to help, and that was enough.

**曲娘**：可是——可是我不理解啊！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: But-but I don't understand!

**曲娘**：……道士说过，能够造福一方的，保护一方之民的，才是祥瑞。如果你有能力，却不这样做，那就是错的。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: The Daoist said, "The one who can protect and benefit the people shall be a Xiángruì." If you can, but you don't, that would be wrong.

**曲娘**：我一直做得都不好。我不像那样威风，也全没有画册上祥瑞的形貌……我甚至无法变成一只真正的鹿蜀！这怎么可能就足够了呢？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I've done a terrible job. I'm not that majestic, nor do I look like any Xiángruìs in the book ... I can't even turn into a real Lùshǔ! How is that enough?

她猛地摇头后退两步，直到退无可退地撞上纹丝不动的巡防兵。\
She shakes her head and takes two steps back, until she can retreat no longer and collides with a motionless patrol guard.

**里正**：……曲娘，我认为你需要将来龙去脉说清。\
**Lizheng**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ, I think you need to tell us everything.

而一直伫立于不远处的里正，语气正逐渐冷凝。\
Lǐzhèng, who has been standing nearby, now speaks, his tone intensifying as he goes on.

**里正**：你是否真的将人变为鹿蜀，有过这样的行径？\
**Lizheng**: Have you ever transformed people into Lùshǔs?

曲娘转过头去，却只发觉所有人的视线都是刀刃调转，朝着自己刺来。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ turns her head, only to find that everyone's gaze has now shifted toward her, needling her with probing eyes.

**里正**：回答我们！\
**Lizheng**: Answer us!

**曲娘**：我——我发誓，我是在帮你们……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I-I swear, I was trying to help ...

**曲娘**：为了让所有人得到他们想要的。就像执礼想要回乡，我就请她喝酒，送她回去了那样。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: ... to help everyone get what they want. Just like the former Zhílǐ—she wanted to go back to her hometown, so I offered her a drink and sent her back.

**法曹**：曲娘，你可明白你所说的话，都是什么意思吗？\
**Facao**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ, do you understand what you are saying?

**曲娘**：每一句话我都清楚！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I understand every word I say!!

她的反应早已胜过任何直接的承认。\
Her reaction says more than any confession.

每一句。每一句都是陈述，每一句也都像是疑问。\
Every sentence. Every sentence is a declaration—every sentence is an interrogation.

**里正**：……曲娘，你到底做了什么？\
**Lizheng**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ, what have you done?

**葛天**：你该早些问出这句话来。\
**Getian**: You should have asked this a lot earlier.

**里正**：你对执礼做了什么？？\
**Lizheng**: What did you do to the Zhílǐ?!

**曲娘**：我……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I ...

面对从来信任自己的里正，表现出这样前所未有的愤怒，曲娘的反应是抓紧自己的手臂。\
With Lǐzhèng, who had always trusted her, turning on her in anger, Jiǔ Niángzǐ's reaction is to grab her own arm tightly as if for protection.

她想要再次后退，令自己远离那种激烈的情感，却没有地方能让她离开。\
She wants to step back again, to keep herself away from the intense emotion, but there is nowhere left for her to go.

她只能回答。\
All she can do now is answer.

**曲娘**：她……她先前来到酒坊，同我抱怨，说自己的话不被你们理解，在考虑是不是应该接受意见，回乡休息。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: She-she came to my tavern and complained that you didn't understand her at all, and that she was considering going back to her hometown.

**曲娘**：可她口中的家乡，离沛城好像很远，她又那样难过和疲惫，不知道该怎么选择。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: But it seemed far away from Pèi City. She looked sad and tired, and didn't know what to do.

**里正**：所以你——所以你就——\
**Lizheng**: So, so you ...

**曲娘**：我必须回应她的心愿，不是吗……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I must grant her wish, mustn't I?

**曲娘**：道士说过，鹿蜀可以轻松日行千里。若是快些，再快些，日行万里也不在话下。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: The Daoist said, a Lùshǔ can easily go a thousand miles within a day. If they start running, go faster, that will be over ten thousand miles.

**曲娘**：如果我能帮助她，当然就要这样做啊！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: If that's how I can help her, I should definitely do that!

**里正**：你——\
**Lizheng**: You ...

曲娘垂下眼睛，试图为这剖白寻找更合适的词句，可不解与难过毕竟能轻易哽住咽喉。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ lowers her eyes, trying to find more suitable words for her confession, but in the end, only a knot of confused sadness fills her throat.

**曲娘**：就像——就像现在。若是沛霖川干涸，你们无处可去……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Just like-like now. If the Pèilín River dries out, you have nowhere to go ...

**曲娘**：如果都能变成鹿蜀，就不会这样了。鹿蜀想去哪里都可以。去北方，去南方，无论哪里。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Just turn into Lùshǔs, and then you won't suffer. Lùshǔs can go anywhere they want. To the north, to the south, wherever they want.

**曲娘**：就算我没办法让沛霖川的水重新涨起，也能换个方法，完成你们的愿望。我想，自由自在的远走是个不错的选择，可结果……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I can grant your wish differently, even if I can't recover the river from drought. I was thinking going away freely might be a good choice. But, in the end ...

**曲娘**：……结果，这是不好的吗？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: But, in the end, in the end, what I'm doing is ... wrong?

一时间，几乎所有人都不知道怎样应对这样的剖白。每一句似乎都错得离谱，但每一句话被说出时的语气又那样恳切。\
For a moment, almost everyone is at a loss for how to deal with this revelation. Every sentence seems to them to be absurdly wrong, but the tone with which she speaks is completely sincere.

无论怎样的剖白都只昭告着，失踪案的罪魁祸首竟然真是曲娘。\
Yet no matter what explanation she might offer, it only reveals that the true culprit of the disappearances was in fact Jiǔ Niángzǐ herself.

**里正**：……曲娘，你……\
**Lizheng**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ, you ...

所有熟识曲娘的人都理应无法料到此刻。在合该属于团圆与欢乐的岁除夜，发觉曲娘竟真的以小兽般的稚气闯下大祸。\
No one familiar with Jiǔ Niángzǐ anticipated this moment. That on the eve of the festival, a time of joy and reunion, they had to come to grips with a colossal disaster caused by such a simple act of childishness.

**曲娘**：如果不这样做，那我又应该……怎么办呢。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: But if not by doing this, then ... what else can I do?

这事实在早春的夜里这样令人胆寒，也这样令人心碎。\
This matter is too chilling and heartbreaking for an early spring night.

许久不作声的小叶尼塞向前迈了一步。\
Yenisei, who has remained silent for a long time, takes a step forward.

**小叶尼塞**：曲娘，还记得昨晚你和我说过的话吗？\
**Yenisei**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ, remember what you said to me last night?

**小叶尼塞**：酒有那样多的名字，却都还是酒。\
**Yenisei**: Liquor has many different names, but they are still "liquor."

**小叶尼塞**：即使你换了一件颜色不一样的衣服，你也仍然是曲娘。\
**Yenisei**: You can put on many different clothes, but you will still be the same Jiǔ Niángzǐ.

**小叶尼塞**：无论你把我变成马，变成驴，还是变成鹿蜀……我都只是小叶尼塞而已。\
**Yenisei**: Likewise, whether you turn me into a horse, a donkey, or a Lùshǔ, I will still be the same Yenisei.

**小叶尼塞**：你并不需要……强求自己变成人们想象中的祥瑞，我认为那只是一个缥缈的符号。\
**Yenisei**: You don't have to force yourself to become the people's Xiángruì. I think it's only an unreachable symbol.

**小叶尼塞**：我能看到的，是竭尽所能地为所有人排忧解难的曲娘。尽管它的结果不如人意，但你的初衷，和我来到这里了解到的祥瑞，已经没有差别。\
**Yenisei**: What matters is that the Jiǔ Niángzǐ I know would do whatever she could to help others. That's just what a Xiángruì does, as far as I know. Even though some results turned out to be not so satisfying, your sincerity is as valuable as the Xiángruì itself.

**小叶尼塞**：所以现在……你只需要把大家变回来就好。\
**Yenisei**: So now, you just need to turn us all back.

**葛天**：的确如此。穷途孑立，亦可回返。在尚可挽回时，挽回即可。\
**Getian**: Yes. So turn back, when no path lies before you. It's never too late to return.

见一旁失语已久的里正也点头，曲娘脸上惴惴的神色才逐渐焕发希望。\
Seeing Lǐzhèng, who has been silent for a while now, nodding, Jiǔ Niángzǐ's worried expression begins to stifle a few beams of hope.

**曲娘**：好……我会努力的——我会尽我的全力……！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I-I will. I will do my best!

曲娘回身吹了一声哨。紧接着，木头的踢踏声就接续哨声末尾，逐渐在院落四周响起。它们围了过来，沉默不语地在曲娘身旁蹦跳。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ turns around and whistles. Immediately after, the sound of wooden footsteps follows and gradually echoes around the courtyard. They circle in and silently jump around her.

**曲娘**：好了，你们现在可以说话了，没关系——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Alright! You can talk now. It's okay ...

**木头小人**：困住你，他们。\
**Wooden Doll**: They, trapped you.

**木头小人**：我们会救你。\
**Wooden Doll**: We, save you.

**曲娘**：什——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: What?

**里正**：……人造物件，却会言语……\
**Lizheng**: These handicrafts are able to talk ...

**里正**：曲娘，你竟是为它们所操纵。\
**Lizheng**: How could you be manipulated by them, Jiǔ Niángzǐ.

**木头小人群**：救你，救你——！\
**Wooden Dolls**: Save you. Save you!

**曲娘**：不是，不是的！不用救我！你们误会了！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: No-no! You're getting it wrong! Don't save me!

**曲娘**：里正，我没有被操纵，它们、它只是木头！虽然也是我的朋友——不，这不是我想说的，但——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Lǐzhèng, I'm not manipulated! They're just wood! Well, they're indeed my friends ... No, no, no, that's not for now ...

**曲娘**：它说话一直都断断续续的，不是完整的意思！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: They just talk like that! That's not what they mean!

长者的耐心早已濒临耗尽，背负的责任迫使他沉下心来等待这场闹剧的结尾。\
The elder's patience teeters now on the verge of exhaustion, yet his responsibilities force him to stay calm and wait patiently for the end of this farce.

**里正**：……我便，最后信你一次。询问它们将人复原的方法吧，我且等着。\
**Lizheng**: This shall be the last time I put my trust in you. Ask them how to transform people back.

**里正**：若是不能……\
**Lizheng**: But if you can't ...

曲娘知道，此刻已经没有“不能”这个选项。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ knows that there can be no "can't" allowed at this juncture.

她转头看向包围着整个院落的巡防兵，与面有惧色的邻里，最后晃晃脑袋，好将多余的情绪都清出脑海，专注于一件事。\
She turns her head to look at the patrolmen surrounding the entire courtyard, and the locals with their fearful faces. Finally, she shakes her head to clear her mind of any unnecessary emotions and focuses on just one thing.

**曲娘**：你们……都听见了吧？现在，我想知道怎样让他们都变回去。可以告诉我方法吗？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: You-you heard him. Now, please tell me how to turn them back into humans, will you?

**曲娘**：如果也需要你们跳进酒里，那我现在去找酒来——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: If it requires liquor, I'll get it for you ...

**木头小人**：方法，没有。酒，起效。收回，无效。\
**Wooden Doll**: Way. No way. Once turned, no turning back.

**木头小人**：白毛道士和花黄，你忘了。\
**Wooden Doll**: The white-haired Daoist. The yellow drawing, on forehead. You forgot.

**曲娘**：道士？我没有忘！而且，你……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: The Daoist? I didn't forget anything! And you ...

**曲娘**：对，你在捉弄我，报复我，因为今天早上我讲话的态度不好，是吗？可现在不是耍脾气的时候了，我真的很需要——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I see. You must be messing with me, because I treated you badly this morning. This is your revenge, right? It's not the time for it. I really need you to ...

**木头小人**：没有。\
**Wooden Doll**: No way.

**曲娘**：不可能没有，不会的！我不可能……不可能连解术都做不到……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: No, no! There must be a way! I must-I must be able to dispel my own craft ...

苍白的言语到了最后，声音渐渐弱了下去。一种意识到无路可走的标志。\
At the end of her somewhat lackluster speech, her voice weakens to a whimper—an acknowledgment that there is no way out.

**法曹**：看来……曲娘，你随我回职祠。我们再看如何解决这件事。\
**Facao**: You must come to the Zhící with me, Jiǔ Niángzǐ. We'll see what we can do.

他示意巡防兵上前，要将曲娘带走。曲娘此刻却不再配合，反而再次后退了一步。\
He signals to the patrol soldiers to come forward and take her away. At this moment, Jiǔ Niángzǐ no longer seems willing to cooperate and instead takes another step back.

**曲娘**：对不起，对不起。但是，我要……我能解决这件事。这是我闯下的大祸，我必须要……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I'm sorry. I'm sorry. But I must fix it. I can fix it! This is all because of me. I need to ...

她做出了一个术法手势，试图最后再尝试一次。\
She makes a ritual gesture, attempting one final desperate act of self-salvation.

**曲娘**：我——呃——会好好想一想，之前是怎么做的——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I, um, I will think carefully, think of what I did before ...

**曲娘**：我能做到的。不需要它们，我也能做到……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I can do it. I can do it without them ...

**木头小人**：不，不。很疼。会疼。刀剜在骨头上。\
**Wooden Doll**: No. It hurts. Very. Writhing pain.

**曲娘**：……呃啊！\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Urgh!!

她的额头上散出一道幽暗的光，像月色，也像夜半时分，鹿蜀身上泛起的银纹。\
A dim light emanates from her forehead, like moonlight or the silver stripes on the Lùshǔ's skin in the dead of night.

**木头小人群**：救你——我们救你！\
**Wooden Dolls**: Save you! We save you!

**木头小人群**：——救你！\
**Wooden Dolls**: SAVE YOU!

更多木头人狂乱跳动的声音响起。它们自院中各处角落里涌现，以意想不到的力道撞开巡防兵与居民组成的包围圈，向着曲娘直直奔去。\
The sound of more wooden dolls leaping wildly rings out. They emerge from various corners of the courtyard, breaking through the encirclement of patrol soldiers and locals with unexpected force, heading straight toward Jiǔ Niángzǐ.

小小的，低矮的木头造物，终于在因突然爆发的痛苦而委顿下去的曲娘面前，开始以扭曲的方式迅速成长。\
The miniature wooden creations begin to grow rapidly in a twisted transformation before Jiǔ Niángzǐ, who is now overwhelmed by a sudden burst of pain.

——自人形，变为了奇异而巨大的兽类。此前种种，几如谶语。\
They shift from a human form into strange, enormous beasts. To this point, everything has proceeded almost exactly like the prophecy.

曲娘瘫坐在木头人被众人合力击碎的残骸中，痛苦已从她脸上褪去，仅余颓然。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ sits slumped in the debris of the wooden dolls smashed through everyone's joint efforts, the pain fading from her face leaves only a desperate look of despair.

她捧着木头的碎片，无助得好像又是闹市上那个柔弱而慌张的女孩儿了。\
She holds the fragments of wood, helpless—as though she were that weak and panicked girl in the bustling marketplace once more.

**曲娘**：……看来，它们说的是真的。我做不到。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Seems what they said is true. I can't do it.

**曲娘**：我只是想回去，让一切都变回去。就连这样也不可以吗？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I just want everything to be back to normal. Is that too much?

**葛天**：有施术，就应当有解术。可如今的情况，却是连我也看不明晰了。\
**Getian**: There should have been ways to undo it. But now even I am confounded.

**葛天**：你这痛苦，亦不似作伪，那究竟是……\
**Getian**: Your pain is real. Then ...

**别斯米尔**：……\
**Bessmert**: ...

破碎的水缸旁，小叶尼塞望向别斯米尔。女人似有所感，从呆滞的巡防兵手下轻轻挣脱出来。\
Beside the broken water jar, Yenisei looks toward Bessmert, who seems to feel something and gently breaks free from the stupefied patrol soldiers.

这静止的院落就像一场沉默的戏剧，别斯米尔是在台上随意行走的唯一一人。\
This static courtyard is like a frozen scene, and Bessmert is the only actor walking freely on stage.

她什么也看不见，或许也因此才更加坦然。\
Not being able to see the danger gives her an unworldly calm.

**别斯米尔**：是“做不到”，而不是不能做，不愿做。对不对？\
**Bessmert**: You said you "can't do it," not that you "don't want to." Right?

**别斯米尔**：有所限制的神秘术，仅能释放，不可收回。\
**Bessmert**: The arcane skill with conditions cannot be taken back once it is cast.

**别斯米尔**：就像在萨满仪式中已经说出口的诅咒与誓言。\
**Bessmert**: Just like the irretrievable curses and vows in Siberian shamanism.

**葛天**：……我观此女，头骨上确有后天刻印的纹路，图样乃是某种镇符，不可溯源。关于她“存想”能力之限，此前我亦有所猜测。\
**Getian**: I can see some markings on this girl's skull, like an unknown seal. I've been speculating about what caused the limitation of her power.

**葛天**：或许，这也是为何方才她看上去那样痛苦。能够改变骨纹的永久封印，即使短暂挣脱也并非易事。\
**Getian**: This may be the reason why she is in pain. A seal powerful enough to change one's marking on the bones is not to be easily broken.

**曲娘**：头骨……？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Skull ...?

曲娘抬手，摸了摸自己的额头。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ raises her hand and touches her forehead.

上面的花黄理应被潦草的动作擦去一块，变成一道彩色的印记，或者别的什么，可它却没有。\
The yellow drawing upon it should have been swept away by this sudden movement, forming a colorful mark, or something else, but it doesn't.

**曲娘**：我不知道你们在说什么……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I don't know what you're talking about ...

摸索无果，曲娘疲惫地收回手，放弃了深究与挣扎。\
Her exploration bearing no fruit, Jiǔ Niángzǐ wearily withdraws her hand and gives up her investigation.

**曲娘**：我做不到。我能将他们变成鹿蜀，但却不能将他们变回人。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I can't. I can turn them into Lùshǔs, but not the opposite way.

**曲娘**：或许，我根本就不能成为祥瑞，没有那样的本领。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Maybe-maybe I can't be a Xiángruì at all. I'm not qualified.

故事至此，走进了无解的死胡同。\
At this point, the story has entered an unsolvable impasse.

**别斯米尔**：……好吧。那么，还有一个被忽略的问题。\
**Bessmert**: Alright. There's one more question that seems to be overlooked by us all.

**别斯米尔**：在场的人，有多少已经喝了曲娘的酒——\
**Bessmert**: How many people have drunk Jiǔ Niángzǐ's liquor ...

**别斯米尔**：——在节日氛围的鼓动之下？\
**Bessmert**: ... in the merry festival spirit?

## NS-20 别春山 / Farewell to the Past

异乡人话音落下，时辰亦至。饮下酒的众人，在混乱的嘶鸣与尖叫中脱胎换骨，尽数变成了鹿蜀。\
When the voice of this outsider fades, the fated hour also arrives. Those among the crowd who drank the liquor undergo a transformation amidst chaotic screams, as each and every one of them becomes a Lùshǔ.

曲娘眼看这无可挽回的一幕，毫无觉察间，泪水已经簌簌落下。\
As Jiǔ Niángzǐ watches this irreversible scene, she is unaware that tears are already flowing down her face.

……自己竟然从来没有太大的长进，一切都与莽撞无教的数年前别无二致。\
She has made no progress at all. Everything is no different now than it was a few years ago, when she was even more reckless and naive.

**曲娘**：道士告诉我，我的母亲是从古至今第九只鹿蜀。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: The Daoist told me that my mother was the ninth Lùshǔ from the very beginning of time.

**曲娘**：似乎很伟大，却也很遥远。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Great, though, distant.

**曲娘**：毕竟，除了她离开时从人变回妖模样的那瞬间之外——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: After all, except for the moment she turned from a human into a Yāo when she was leaving ...

**曲娘**：我不太记得她。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I don't quite remember her.

**道士**：你母亲，是庇护一方的祥瑞。\
**Daoist**: Your mother was the Xiángruì, the people's guardian.

**小曲娘**：什么是祥瑞？\
**Jiu Niangzi (Child)**: What is a Xiángruì?

**道士**：生而有灵，选择造福一方，保护一方之民的大妖。就像你的母亲。\
**Daoist**: The spirit of auspiciousness, the great Yāo who protects and benefits people, like your mother once did.

**道士**：但祥瑞不应有私情。因这私情，她为你而陨落。你须得记住。\
**Daoist**: But a Xiángruì is not supposed to have any personal feelings. She fell because of you, because of the personal feeling. Remember that.

**小曲娘**：“私情”又是什么？\
**Jiu Niangzi (Child)**: What is a "personal feeling"?

**道士**：她不应有的东西，你也不需要了解。\
**Daoist**: It's something she shouldn't have had, for you, either.

**道士**：但……她没能走下去的路，你却应当继续走。\
**Daoist**: But you shall keep to the path she left.

**小曲娘**：什么路？\
**Jiu Niangzi (Child)**: What path?

**小曲娘**：是这样的泥土路，还是像那些房子外面的石板路？\
**Jiu Niangzi (Child)**: Is it like the dirt path we're walking on, or, or the stone path around the house?

**道士**：都不是。\
**Daoist**: Neither.

**道士**：留在城里，成为他们的庇护者，成为祥瑞。\
**Daoist**: Stay in this city. Be their guardian. Be a Xiángruì.

**道士**：终有一日，你会知晓。\
**Daoist**: You shall understand when the day comes.

**曲娘**：……道士带走我，却又离开我。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: The Daoist brought me here, and left me here.

**曲娘**：曾是祥瑞的母亲也同样如此，于是我以为，分离是步入人间必须付出的代价。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: That's exactly what my mother, the former Xiángruì, did to me as well. So I took departure as the price of living in the human world.

**曲娘**：将我关入沛城前，道士也曾经允诺我——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Before I came into Pèi City, the Daoist guaranteed me that ...

**曲娘**：“成为祥瑞，便能理解她，触及她。”\
**Jiu Niangzi**: "Be a Xiángruì, and then you will understand her."

**曲娘**：这话很诱人，于是我就留了下来。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: How alluring was that! That's why I chose to stay here.

**曲娘**：起初，我日夜不停地咀嚼这句话，却实在不知道应该怎么做。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: At first, I couldn't stop thinking about what the Daoist said, but I had no idea how.

**曲娘**：因为道士也从未指点我应该怎么做。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Because I was never taught how by anyone.

**曲娘**：可我也没有其他的选择，于是……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I didn't have any other choice, so ...

**曲娘**：于是我开始从那些散落的话语，从不同的画册里，从不可触及的传奇中，试着拼凑起一个母亲，一个祥瑞。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: So I started to recall my mother by piecing together the scattered words and descriptions from books and legends, to recall what a Xiángruì is.

**曲娘**：然后学着成为它，学着取代它。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I tried to be her, tried to replace her.

**曲娘**：——却也是为了再次见到她。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Just to meet her, once again.

**曲娘**：我想问问她，你是怎样想的呢？\
**Jiu Niangzi**: If I got to meet her, I would ask her, "What was on your mind?"

**曲娘**：若是知道我这祥瑞，做得这样好，会不会有哪怕一点的后悔呢？后悔离开我，后悔将我一人留下。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: If only you could see me doing such a great job as a Xiángruì, would you feel even the slightest twinge of guilt? For deserting me, for leaving me alone.

**曲娘**：……好吧。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Well.

**曲娘**：现在看来，我其实从未真正理解过她，也没有真正理解过“祥瑞”。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Looks like I've neither truly understood her, nor a Xiángruì.

院中廊下站立着两人。在沉默的雨幕中，一个抉择已经被定下。\
Between the two people standing in the courtyard walkway in the silent rain, a decision is made.

**法曹**：曲娘，你难道真的要……\
**Facao**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ, are you really going to ...

作为一个从来意志坚定的人，他难得犹疑了，不知应该摘撷何种词句才能向眼前人强调此事的危险，又或是一切言语在她的选择前都显得苍白。\
As someone who has always been steadfast in his will, he rarely hesitates. He doesn't know which words to use to emphasize the danger of this matter to the person in front of him, or whether all words are powerless before her final choice.

所以他最终还是沉默了。\
And so, ultimately, he remains silent.

**曲娘**：我知道，从来都没有人真的跳过去了。里正为了告诫我，还讲过许多故事。一些不适合用来告诫孩童的故事。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: It's fine. I know there's no one who could jump over it. In order to stop me, Lǐzhèng even told me some stories, and they were ... not very suitable for children.

**曲娘**：可我一定得去。因为只有这个方法了。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: But I have to, because there is no other way ...

**曲娘**：只有问卜——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Only The Divination.

**曲娘**：而且，朔日本就应该有问卜。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Well, you can't talk about Shuòrì without The Divination, right?

**曲娘**：……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: ...

**曲娘**：谢谢您愿意放我走，甚至还替我取来了衣服。虽然执礼不在，我都不知道怎么穿它才对……\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Thank you for letting me go. You even brought me the clothes. But the Zhílǐ is not here. I'm not sure if I'm wearing it right ...

**曲娘**：但没关系。新衣服始终是新衣服，不会因为我穿得不好，就变了味道。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: But it's ok. Even if it's wrong, it still looks new and colorful.

她毫无目的地拍了拍裙边，又翻折了一下袖口，最后将披帛重新拢起来。直至再也找不到可以做的事，道别的话也正好走到舌尖。\
She pats the hem of her skirt aimlessly, then folds the cuffs, and finally folds back the silk drapes once more. When she cannot find anything else to fix, her farewell rises to the tip of her tongue.

**曲娘**：……谢谢，真的谢谢您。那我这就——\
**Jiu Niangzi**: Thank you. Thank you so very much. I-er, I ...

**曲娘**：嗯，我走了。\
**Jiu Niangzi**: I'm leaving, then.

说完，曲娘后退两步，将双手以掌心贴手背的方式交叠，置于额下。她向此刻站在廊下的法曹，和已经变为鹿蜀的里正鞠躬告别。\
Jiǔ Niángzǐ steps back and places her hands beneath her forehead, palm to back. She bows farewell to Fǎcáo in the hallway and the Lùshǔ turned from Lǐzhèng.

是感谢，也是歉意。她从来没有行过这样的礼，这是第一次也是最后一次。\
A gesture of gratitude and an apology. She has never performed such a ritual before—this will be the first and last time.

**法曹**：……也许，我们会找到其他法子。你不必——\
**Facao**: Perhaps we will find another way. You don't have to ...

他没有说完。因为这显然并非实话，甚至是幸存者对元凶不必要的宽慰。\
He doesn't finish. Because anything he wants to say would be untrue, an example of unwarranted comfort from a survivor toward their aggressor.

所以曲娘也没有说话。她摇了摇头，仿佛没有听到这个提议一般后退，退进雨中，然后转身向着职祠之外迈去。\
And so, Jiǔ Niángzǐ says nothing. She shakes her head as if she hadn't even heard his proposal, retreating into the rain, and then turns around and walks towards the outside of the Zhící.

她的脚步从未如此松快，步子越走越急，到最后几乎变为了奔跑。\
Her footsteps have never been so relaxed before, with each step becoming faster and faster, almost evolving into a sprint toward the end.

——她向着城外奔去，却并不是为了逃离这里。\
She runs toward the outside of the city, but not to escape.

这雨从昨夜起就再没停下过。\
The rain has not stopped since the previous night.

城外，别斯米尔同小叶尼塞站在断桥这头，眺望雾气缭绕的对岸。\
Outside the city, Bessmert and Yenisei stand at the end of the broken bridge, gazing at the misty bank opposite to them.

葛天停在她们头顶的树上。他一直在，来得比所有人都要早。\
Gětiān is perched on the tree above their heads. He has been here all along, arriving earlier than the others.

**别斯米尔**：葛天先生，我们……\
**Bessmert**: Mr. Gětiān, we ...

**别斯米尔**：我们只能在这里，对着断桥祈祷了，对吗？\
**Bessmert**: We are left with only one option, which is to stand here and pray for her, correct?

**别斯米尔**：祈祷那个“所求必应”，或者说问卜，能够灵光一闪地实现。\
**Bessmert**: Pray that the Ask and Acquire, or The Divination, will answer us and give us what we want in a flash.

**别斯米尔**：——说实在的，这有可能吗？\
**Bessmert**: But is it really possible?

**葛天**：……\
**Getian**: ...

**葛天**：并无可能，还是放弃罢。\
**Getian**: I think not. We should go.

别斯米尔听着周围越来越多的脚步声，来自那些朝断桥走来，仍记挂着朔日走吉的人们。\
Bessmert listens to the advancing footsteps around her, emanating from all those who are walking toward the broken bridge, still remembering the auspicious significance of this New Year's Day.

一开始她还尝试去分辨法曹他们可能身处其中的声音，直到雨越来越大，才终于放弃。\
At first, she tries to distinguish the voices that might be Fǎcáo and the others, but as the rain grows heavier and louder, she finally gives up.

**别斯米尔**：我听见他们说，今天是度朔节的第一天，也是岁朝春。\
**Bessmert**: I heard today is a special day for the locals, known as "Suìzhāochūn."

**别斯米尔**：葛天先生，什么是“岁朝春”？\
**Bessmert**: Mr. Gětiān, what is Suìzhāochūn?

别斯米尔把淋湿的额发别向一边，油伞也朝小叶尼塞倾斜而去。\
Bessmert holds her wet fringe to one side, and tilts the oiled umbrella towards Yenisei.

鹿蜀沉默着靠近，使潮湿紧贴着潮湿。\
The Lùshǔ silently approaches and leans against her tightly.

**葛天**：“百载难逢岁朝春。”\
**Getian**: It comes from an ancient proverb, "Bǎizǎi Nánféng Suìzhāochūn."

**葛天**：既是朔日，也是立春。\
**Getian**: It's the first day of a new year and the first day of spring.

**葛天**：立春，艮位坎卦下，应乘春令。\
**Getian**: Lìchūn, the beginning of spring, corresponds to the lower trigram of Kǎn in the direction of Gèn. It is the season of life.

**葛天**：……气清而温阳。\
**Getian**: A time when the weather is clear and Yáng fills the air.

**别斯米尔**：听起来很厉害。\
**Bessmert**: They are pleasing to the ears.

**别斯米尔**：但这些句子合在一起，我什么也没听明白。\
**Bessmert**: But I don't know what to make of it when all these are put together.

**葛天**：……立春是一个节气，表明春季将临。\
**Getian**: Lìchūn is one of the 24 solar terms. It signifies the beginning of spring.

**葛天**：岁朝春则是立春与度朔节第一日重叠，百年不遇，实为难得。\
**Getian**: Suìzhāochūn is how people would call it when the first day of the Dùshuò Festival and the first day of spring happen to be the same day. It is a once-in-a-century good sign.

**别斯米尔**：听起来是很难得的日子，还是新年的第一天，这很好。\
**Bessmert**: Indeed. It's also the first day of a new year. I like the coincidence.

**葛天**：但你的同伴，或许都无法变回来了。即使如此，你也认为很好？\
**Getian**: Do you still find it equally pleasing if your teammates are not coming back?

**别斯米尔**：那我就这样带他们回去，再做打算。\
**Bessmert**: Then, I will take them home as they are now and see what I can do.

**葛天**：……\
**Getian**: ...

**别斯米尔**：没必要用沉默来回应我。这只是目前看来的最佳选择。\
**Bessmert**: I know the words are hidden behind your silence, but this is the best option for now.

**别斯米尔**：毕竟，您也说了，光靠祈祷是不能让他们都变回去的。\
**Bessmert**: After all, as you just said, prayers are not enough to bring them back.

**葛天**：曾经是可以的。\
**Getian**: They could, for a time.

**别斯米尔**：但您同时也说了，那是以前。从前总是有好时光的。\
**Bessmert**: But that's only what happened in the past, as you just said. Good days only exist in our memories.

**葛天**：是在那场洪水之前……我原以为那洪水造成的破坏，并不会遗留至今。\
**Getian**: That was before the flood. The aftermath of that disaster lasted longer than I thought.

**葛天**：显然，我错了。\
**Getian**: I was so wrong to think it was over.

别斯米尔仰起头。一滴雨正好坠在她用以遮盖眼睛的布料上。随后是更多更多，逐渐湿濡了整块纺面。\
Bessmert looks up. A drop of rain falls right onto the fabric she uses to cover her eyes. Then more falls, and more, gradually wetting the entire weaved surface.

她听着，且不打算发表评价。\
She listens without intending any comment.

**葛天**：……起先是……不可回流到上游的汹涌洪水。少许水波的变化，声音细微，因此无人注意。\
**Getian**: It all began with the unstoppable flood. At first, it was just a few unusual tides that no one noticed.

**葛天**：然后是洪水肆虐后，无可修复的断桥。\
**Getian**: Then the flood came, followed by the destruction of the bridge.

**葛天**：紧接着，才是失去香火的山上渊庙，和无人应答的问卜习俗。\
**Getian**: The temple on the mountain thus lost its connection to its pilgrims. The prayers were no longer answered.

**葛天**：关于这些，我无从知晓原因。那些下了山，对这一切施以援手，了解真相的同族，也都没有再回来。\
**Getian**: I do not understand what caused all these things. My people left the mountain to help with the situation, but they never came back.

**葛天**：而现在……\
**Getian**: And now ...

**葛天**：连下方这条河，也将如隐入雾气之中的渊庙一般失落了。\
**Getian**: Even this river beneath us is gone, just like the Yuān Temple, forever lost in the fog.

**葛天**：……\
**Getian**: ...

几人身后，逐渐有普通的城中居民走上前来，像往年一样在手中的木签上，刻下问卜之辞。\
Behind them, the city residents gradually approach and carve words of divination onto the wooden sticks in their hands, just as they had in previous years.

他们对这问卜无人应答的事实早有准备，却对其中原因一无所知。\
They are prepared for the fact that there may not be an answer to their questions, but they know nothing of the reason why.

别斯米尔望着越来越多的人。他们聚拢去，在雨中刻写，久久做着无用功。\
Bessmert feels the weight of the growing crowd. They gather and write in the rain, working tirelessly for a long time.

明知不可为而为之，这是人类与神秘学家亘古不变的常态吗？\
Is it the eternal fate of humans and arcanists to act upon desires they know cannot be realized?

**葛天**：白费力气。祂听不见，也看不到。\
**Getian**: It's useless. The god won't hear us, nor will It see us.

**别斯米尔**：……我不知道这样问，是不是一种冒犯。\
**Bessmert**: Please know that I don't mean to offend you with this question.

**葛天**：请讲。\
**Getian**: Please.

**别斯米尔**：难道您不能带着那些人到对岸去吗？\
**Bessmert**: Can't you take those people to the other end of the bridge?

**别斯米尔**：如果现在问卜能得偿所愿的条件，是跃过断桥——\
**Bessmert**: If the condition of The Divination is to go across the broken bridge ...

**葛天**：的确，你才是天真的外乡人。\
**Getian**: Though we are both outsiders in this place, you're more naive than I am.

**别斯米尔**：嗯……？\
**Bessmert**: Emm ...?

**葛天**：自然只有自己走过去，或者跃过去，才可作数，即使那要以付出仅此一次的生命为代价。\
**Getian**: One can only meet the condition by going over the bridge oneself, even if the price is their life.

**葛天**：或许你会揣测，这是否太过残酷。可若真如你所说，祂所求必应，然却随手可得，毋需付出……\
**Getian**: You might think it's cruel. But what good would it do if people were easily given what they asked for without paying a price?

**葛天**：那此地一切生灵的困苦，不都如同笑话一般吗？\
**Getian**: Wouldn't it make others' suffering a joke?

**别斯米尔**：……\
**Bessmert**: ...

葛天低头去看别斯米尔，和一旁没有动静的小叶尼塞，认为对方并没有相信自己的话。\
Gětiān lowers his head to look at Bessmert and the quiet Yenisei beside him, thinking that they perhaps do not believe his words.

他很少需要在几日之内与其他人说这么多。但既然已经起了头，不如将对子作完。\
He rarely needs to say so much to others in such a short space of time. But since he has already started, he might as well finish.

**葛天**：你不信我的话。\
**Getian**: You don't believe me.

**别斯米尔**：我是……在尝试理解。\
**Bessmert**: I'm ... trying to understand.

**葛天**：并无不同。我能够带你飞往对岸，但你应当做好这毫无用处的准备。\
**Getian**: It's all the same. I can take you to the other side of the bridge, but you must not be disappointed if it ends up fruitless.

**别斯米尔**：……什么？\
**Bessmert**: Pardon?

**葛天**：我可以带你飞过去。\
**Getian**: I can take you there.

**别斯米尔**：为什么？为什么您突然改变了主意？\
**Bessmert**: Why? Why the change of mind?

**葛天**：嗯？我从未提起过吗？\
**Getian**: Mm? Haven't I mentioned it before?

**别斯米尔**：提起什么？\
**Bessmert**: Mentioned what?

**葛天**：你的骨相。你的骨相是我所见之人当中，唯一不可堪识的。\
**Getian**: Your bones. Among all the others, you are the only one for whom I do not recognize the markings on your bones.

## NS-21 天堑亦通途 / Another Way Out

一个全新的发现，轻易将别斯米尔的注意力从飞跃断桥上全部吸引过去。\
This new discovery swiftly draws Bessmert's attention away from the broken bridge.

**别斯米尔**：嗯？这是什么意思？\
**Bessmert**: Mm? What is that supposed to mean?

**葛天**：从骨相不可识读这点看来，你不是妖，也不是人。精怪？亦不相同。\
**Getian**: Judging from the fact that you have unreadable bones, you're certainly neither a Yāo, nor a human. A grumkin? No.

**别斯米尔**：噢，我也是一位神秘学家。\
**Bessmert**: Oh, I'm also an arcanist.

**葛天**：直觉告诉我，应在看到你的那一刻，就逃去天涯海角……\
**Getian**: My instinct told me that I should flee to the end of the world the moment I saw you.

**别斯米尔**：我记得，您的确这样做了，带着我那些被变成鹿蜀的，可怜的同伴们。\
**Bessmert**: You did run away, along with my poor teammates, who were turned into Lùshǔs.

**葛天**：……\
**Getian**: ...

**葛天**：总之，我本难以想象，应当怎样与无法看透骨相之人相处。\
**Getian**: I could not have imagined being around someone with unreadable bones.

**葛天**：如今看来，也不过如此而已。\
**Getian**: Turns out it wasn't as strange as I thought it would be.

**别斯米尔**：没有什么区别，对吗？就像我至今还很惊讶，这座城里的人，竟然认为神秘学家与人类并无不同。\
**Bessmert**: Not much difference, you mean? Like the people here believe that there's no difference between humans and arcanists, which makes me very surprised.

**葛天**：就我所见骨相来说，大约确有不同。不过……\
**Getian**: Based on the bones I've seen, they are different. It's just that ...

**别斯米尔**：不重要，是不是？\
**Bessmert**: Doesn't make a difference, right?

**别斯米尔**：在有所求，有所问的时候，我们也没有什么不同。\
**Bessmert**: We are the same when we desire something.

别斯米尔把脸转向人们走来的方向。\
Bessmert turns her face toward where the people are moving.

她明明看不见，却像是在坚定地望着什么。\
She holds her face as if firmly staring at something, despite her lack of sight.

**别斯米尔**：……不如说，我刚才提出借助外力，飞跃断桥的那个问题，也并不是为了质疑你，或者你们说的“渊庙”。\
**Bessmert**: I wasn't questioning you or the temple when I asked you about flying to the other side.

**别斯米尔**：甚至也不是在质疑这个古老神秘术的施放条件。\
**Bessmert**: I wasn't even questioning the strange condition of this arcane skill.

**葛天**：那你是何意？\
**Getian**: What do you mean?

**别斯米尔**：只是……走投无路。我想。\
**Bessmert**: I was ... running out of options, I guess.

**别斯米尔**：像所有已经走投无路，却不理解自己究竟是怎样走到这一步的人，都会想做的一些无用功。\
**Bessmert**: It was just some futile effort I made when I realized this was a dead end, but I have no idea how it got to this point.

别斯米尔做了一个决定。她把油伞举起来，卡在头顶的树杈之间，自己则从那下面离开，走向雨中正在刻下问卜木签的人们。\
Bessmert makes her decision. She lifts the oiled umbrella and sticks it between the branches above her head. Walking out from beneath its cover, heading toward the people carving sticks in the rain.

小叶尼塞也没有停留。她跟在别斯米尔身后，从最早出发时就是如此，现在也一样。\
Yenisei does not stop either. She follows behind Bessmert—just as she has been doing since their departure.

**葛天**：你往哪里去？\
**Getian**: Where are you going?

**别斯米尔**：我也有话想问。\
**Bessmert**: I have questions to ask.

**葛天**：即使没有答案？\
**Getian**: Even if there're no answers?

**别斯米尔**：是的。我相信这些人……他们也都知道。\
**Bessmert**: Yes. I think ... it is the same for all these people.

**别斯米尔**：没有答案，可他们依然在问。\
**Bessmert**: They keep asking, even though they hear no answers.

别斯米尔往前走去，几乎都要走上断桥，直到小叶尼塞衔住她的袖子。\
Bessmert walks forward, almost reaching the broken bridge, until Yenisei grabs her sleeve.

**别斯米尔**：没关系，我明白。\
**Bessmert**: It's okay. I know what you're going to say.

小叶尼塞在雨中显影。水泊的表面被雨点打得隐隐绰绰，她的面庞也在其中不断晃动。\
Yenisei reveals her image in the rain. The surface of the water is lightly pattered by raindrops, and her face is rippled by their falling.

好在她的内心已经不再如倒影一样摇摆不定。\
Fortunately, her heart is no longer swaying like her reflection.

**小叶尼塞**：您想怎么做？我们没有那样的木签。\
**Yenisei**: How are you going to do it? We don't have any wooden chips like that.

**别斯米尔**：用手指，用泥水，就在地面。\
**Bessmert**: I will use my finger, mud, and water, on the ground.

**别斯米尔**：你也问吧，不必拘泥于形式。\
**Bessmert**: You can ask, too, whatever means you use.

**小叶尼塞**：我的问题……\
**Yenisei**: What I want to know ...

别斯米尔蹲下身来，以食指戳在松软的泥水中，写下几个西里尔字母。而后是一些和另一些。\
Bessmert crouches down and pokes her index finger into the soft mud, writing a few Cyrillic letters. Then, others, and then still more.

当她写完整个问题时，前面的字母已经被大雨冲刷而去，就像海水会卷走沙滩上的所有痕迹。\
By the time she finishes writing the entire question, the first letters have already been eaten by the heavy rain, like seawater washing away etchings on a beach.

**别斯米尔**：孩子，你的问题呢？你可以说出来的。\
**Bessmert**: Child, what's your question? Say it if you like.

**小叶尼塞**：……我还是写下来吧。\
**Yenisei**: I think I will write it down.

小叶尼塞并不认为这样做会有任何的意义。但她无法拒绝别斯米尔。\
Yenisei doesn't believe that doing so will have any purpose. But she cannot refuse Bessmert.

注视着自己在水泊中的面容，她再次发动了神秘术，同时问出心中一直以来的疑问。\
As she gazes at her face in the pool of water, she once again activates her arcane skill and asks the question that has been waiting in her heart.

很快，眼前的水泊中，红发的女孩消失了。取而代之的是澄澈水面上，由暖色光点组成的一行西里尔字母。\
The red-haired girl suddenly disappears from the pool of water in front of her. Instead, a line of Cyrillic letters composed of warm-colored dots appears on the clear water's surface.

女孩望着水面，意识到那行字甚至不需要去仔细辨认。\
The girl looks at the water and realizes that the line of words doesn't even need to be fully legible.

雨点捶打，波光浮动。水面颤抖出一个问句。\
Rain pounds and waves rise. The water trembles with her question.

«Где мои воды?»<“我的水域在哪里？”>\
"Where is my water?"

突然出现的更多动物的脚步声，令小叶尼塞没来得及陷入更深的思索。\
The sudden emergence of more animal footsteps prevents Yenisei from becoming lost in deeper thought.

红发女孩重新出现在水泊中，语气如往常一样毫不留情。\
The red-haired girl reappears in the water, her tone as unsparing as usual.

**小叶尼塞**：他们难道还没放弃走吉——\
**Yenisei**: Are they still going to carry out the Fortune Walk?

小叶尼塞猛地回过头去。\
Yenisei turns around.

既不是鹿蜀，也不是斑纹马的人们，从城中无人看管的职祠离开，却不约而同地来到这里。\
These animals, neither Lùshǔs nor striped horses, have left the city's unattended Zhící and coincidentally arrived here.

他们赤裸，疲惫，未被驱赶，也没有穿着任何年节的装饰。\
They are stood there naked and tired, unadorned in any festive decorations.

那些第一天小叶尼塞曾从闹市上见过的绸带与花朵都消失了。它们在这里毕竟不合时宜。\
The ribbons and flowers Yenisei had seen on that first day in the bustling market have disappeared. Not suitable for the present situation, after all.

**小叶尼塞**：……\
**Yenisei**: ...

**小叶尼塞**：……他们……衔着木签……\
**Yenisei**: They are ... carrying wooden chips in their mouths ...

**别斯米尔**：他们都来了，是吗？\
**Bessmert**: They're all here, right?

**小叶尼塞**：……是的。\
**Yenisei**: Yes.

**小叶尼塞**：衔着木签。他们为问卜而来。\
**Yenisei**: With the wooden chips. They are here for The Divination.

**小叶尼塞**：但那上面是空白的。\
**Yenisei**: But the chips are empty.

**别斯米尔**：他们只能在心里发问了。\
**Bessmert**: They will have to ask in their minds.

**小叶尼塞**：您想让我做什么？\
**Yenisei**: What would you like me to do?

**别斯米尔**：……\
**Bessmert**: ...

**别斯米尔**：你可以——\
**Bessmert**: You can ...

**别斯米尔**：成为他们的口、手、眼。\
**Bessmert**: You can be their mouths, hands, and eyes.

**别斯米尔**：或者什么也不做。\
**Bessmert**: You can also do nothing.

**别斯米尔**：就像我们后面的那位先生。\
**Bessmert**: Just like the good sir waiting behind us.

葛天还留在树上，也因此得见了一切。\
Gětiān remains in the tree and thus sees everything.

他的翅膀因淋雨而变得潮湿和沉重，头上的布巾也浸透了雨水，滞重地压着，像是要使他回到地上，回到泥层里，回到世界之初会有的那些地方去。\
His wings have become damp and heavy from the rain, and the cloth on his head is soaked, pressing down heavily as if dragging him back down to the ground, back into the mud, back to the place where the world began.

他没有动作，沉默着将树下发生的一切纳入眼中。\
He doesn't move, silently taking stock of everything that happened under that tree.

**小叶尼塞**：我知道了。如果他们都是来问卜……\
**Yenisei**: I see. If they are here for The Divination ...

**小叶尼塞**：我会帮忙。\
**Yenisei**: I will help.

不平的地面上有许多水洼。短暂的光点闪烁后，水中逐渐显现出一些形色各异的人的面庞。\
There are many puddles on the uneven ground. After a brief flicker of light, faces begin to appear in the water.

那些面庞很快出现，又很快消失，接连浮现的，是或长或短的方块字句子。小叶尼塞无法读懂。这就是她能做的所有了。\
They fade again one by one, forming in long or short sentences. Though Yenisei cannot understand them. This is all she can do.

她继续望了一会儿，选择转头去寻找别斯米尔。\
She continues to look for a while, then forces herself to turn around and search for Bessmert.

**小叶尼塞**：女士，等回去后——\
**Yenisei**: Madam, after we go back ...

别斯米尔笑起来，轻轻摇头，止住女孩的话。\
Bessmert smiles, shakes her head gently, and halts the girl's words.

年长者转过身去，似乎朝向葛天所在的方向，也像是在对着众人来时城门的位置。\
Bessmert turns around, seeming to be facing Gětiān's direction, back to the city gates from which everyone came.

尽管她什么也看不见，却能察觉到某处有着源源不断的生的气息，正朝此处奔涌而来。\
She can sense a steady stream of energy flowing toward some destination.

**别斯米尔**：……你错了。祂能听到的。\
**Bessmert**: You're wrong. "It" can hear us.

葛天在树上，像雨燕那样抖落翅膀上所有会令其过分潮湿的缘由。\
Gětiān is in the tree, shaking off his wings like a swallow—shaking off the reasons for making him feel so excessively damp.

他清楚别斯米尔并非在对着自己说话，盲眼的神秘学家只是继续做着无用功。\
He knows that Bessmert must not be talking to him, as the blind arcanist continues to work in vain.

——但他又一次错了。\
But then he is wrong yet again.

**葛天**：……那是——何人？\
**Getian**: Who is ... that?

所有在场者都能听见的声音，在除了雨声一无所有的寂静中越发响亮，以至于一切活物都应声回头——\
The sound everyone present can hear becomes louder and louder against the breaking silence, accompanied now by nothing but the patter of the rain, to the point where they all turn back in response—

只见一袭红衣飞快地越过所有人。\
All they see is a red dress swiftly passing over them all.

是曲娘。\
It is Jiǔ Niángzǐ.

那是曲娘，熟知或不熟知的人们都很快意识到。\
Both those familiar and unfamiliar with her quickly realize her identity, despite the change.

她为什么要这样做？她真的跃过断桥了吗？跃过去之后会怎么样？\
Why did she do it? Did she really jump over the broken bridge? What could possibly have happened to her after doing so?

无数个问题盘旋在目睹一切之人的脑海中。\
A myriad of questions hovers in the minds of the confounded witnesses.

**小叶尼塞**：——！\
**Yenisei**: ...!

**别斯米尔**：……是她。刚才的声音……是曲娘，对吗？\
**Bessmert**: It was her. The noise I heard ... It was Jiǔ Niángzǐ, right?

**别斯米尔**：我听到了非同寻常的动静，就在她跃过去的那一瞬间。\
**Bessmert**: It was an unusual disturbance when she jumped over the bridge.

**城中居民Ⅰ**：刚才那是——是曲娘——？！\
**Citizen I**: That-that was Jiǔ Niángzǐ?

**城中居民Ⅰ**：柳郎，你看见了吗？？\
**Citizen I**: Mr. Liǔ, did you see that??

**城中居民Ⅲ**：是，我看见了。是她——是她。天啊，她居然办到了，她飞过去了……！\
**Citizen III**: Yes! That's her, that's really her. High heaven, she did it, she jumped over!

震惊之中，有人向断桥的对岸急急探出头去，却又在崖边停住收回。\
In shock, someone hurriedly pokes their head toward the opposite bank of the broken bridge, but stops and withdraws at the cliff's edge.

他们追求着一个笃定的答案，却仍然畏惧于悬崖的陡峭与高远，自然也想不到——\
They are seeking a definite answer, but fear the steepness and height of the cliff. Naturally, they never imagined someone might cross it—

**城中居民Ⅰ**：这，这——\
**Citizen I**: This ... That ...

**小叶尼塞**：没错，没错，是曲娘……我看到她变成了鹿蜀……女士，她真的成为了鹿蜀！\
**Yenisei**: That's right. It's Jiǔ Niángzǐ ... I saw her turn into a Lùshǔ ... Madam, she turned into a real Lùshǔ!

**城中居民Ⅰ**：——呜呜……马都变回来了，河也——\
**Citizen I**: *sobs* The people are back, and the river ...

**城中居民Ⅴ**：天哪，河水——沛霖川涨水了——！\
**Citizen V**: The river! Ah, the Pèilín River is rising!

悬崖之下已经不再是峡谷和低矮的河水，而是涌动着不断向上的湍流。\
Beneath the cliff no longer lies a canyon or a low river, but a constantly rising torrent.

**城中居民Ⅴ**：不对，我能说话了，我的身体也……怎么回事！！\
**Citizen V**: Wait, I can talk! My body is ... What's happening?!

人们终于反应了过来。\
The people finally react.

他们奋袂地张望着彼此，脸上浮现着红光，如同除夜廊下耀眼的庭燎，更像是河上曾经的光带。\
They look at each other excitedly, a red light illuminating their faces like the dazzling courtyard fires beneath the festival walkways—or the strip of light that appeared on the river before.

问卜应验了。\
Their divine wishes have been granted.

**小叶尼塞**：等等，我——\
**Yenisei**: Wait. I ...

**小叶尼塞**：我也变回来了？\
**Yenisei**: My body is back?

小叶尼塞几乎要跳起来拥抱别斯米尔。\
Yenisei almost leaps into the air to embrace Bessmert.

**小叶尼塞**：曲娘——曲娘跳过去了！她竟然以人身的样子……跃过去了……！\
**Yenisei**: Jiǔ Niángzǐ ... She jumped over the bridge! She jumped over ... in the human form!

**小叶尼塞**：她没有坠下去，甚至在半空中的时候，我以为是我眼花了……似乎有一瞬间，她真的变成了鹿蜀。\
**Yenisei**: She didn't fall! I'm not sure if I saw it clearly ... I think, for an instant, she turned into a real Lùshǔ.

**小叶尼塞**：难道这就是问卜，是“所求必应”……\
**Yenisei**: Is this the power of The Divination, the magic of "Ask and Acquire"?

**小叶尼塞**：对了！这些城中的人都变回来了，说不定——\
**Yenisei**: Oh, wait! The people in the city have come back, so maybe ...

许久未闻的声音也在身旁响起。\
A voice now long unheard also sounds from beside them.

**克罗利克**：什么……这……？\
**Krolik**: What ... the?

**克罗利克**：啊，这到底是怎么了？头痛欲裂……\
**Krolik**: Ugh, what's going on? Ah! My head hurts ...

**小叶尼塞**：……克罗利克先生！\
**Yenisei**: Mr. Krolik!

人群之中，同伴失而复得。\
In the crowd, all the companions they once had lost are now returned to them.

**尤利恩**：天哪……难道我是做了一场怪梦吗……\
**Jurien**: Oh, dear ... I had the strangest dream ...

**小叶尼塞**：还有——尤利恩先生他们——\
**Yenisei**: And Mr. Jurien, everyone!

**小叶尼塞**：他们都在那边！别斯米尔女士，我们也过去吧！\
**Yenisei**: They are over there! Madam, let's go see them!

不等回答，小叶尼塞远远招手示意，随即奔向他们。\
Without waiting for an answer, Yenisei waves from a distance and immediately runs toward them.

**小叶尼塞**：这里，我们在这边——\
**Yenisei**: Here! We are here ...

**别斯米尔**：……“百载难逢岁朝春”……\
**Bessmert**: Bǎizǎi Nánféng Suìzhāochūn.

**别斯米尔**：的确难得。\
**Bessmert**: It's indeed a rare occasion.

## NS-22 “所求必应” / Ask and Acquire

**说书先生**：上回说到——\
**Storyteller**: Previously, we were at ...

**城中居民Ⅵ**：说到祥瑞鹿蜀人间历劫，幡然悔悟！\
**Citizen VI**: Lùshǔ the Xiángruì came to the human world to go through the god's test, but she repented!

**说书先生**：正是。且说那鹿蜀，衔草结环，除夜叩拜了先生开解之恩，自城中一别，独往断桥去也。\
**Storyteller**: Exactly. She had been troubled by the repentance until the New Year's Eve. That night, her tutor straightened her out, and she was very grateful. After that, she bid him goodbye and went to the broken bridge alone.

**说书先生**：须知今岁朔日亦交春，端的是百年难遇，云中却狂雨乱坠，异象频生——！\
**Storyteller**: However, ladies and gentlemen, the Shuòrì this year happened to be the beginning of spring. Such a coincidence happens only once every 100 years. On this peculiar day, the thunderstorm was raging, and all the strangest things happened!

**说书先生**：即使那崖岸上是致人晕眩之雾气，崖下是去不可返之深渊，鹿蜀身负了众人期望，决意跃过这无人可征之断桥，为它所庇佑者，寻觅重启龟甲问卜之法——\
**Storyteller**: The cliff was shrouded in confusing fog, and below was a bottomless abyss! No one had ever jumped over the bridge successfully, yet the Lùshǔ decided to make an attempt, for the sake of the people who believed in her! She was determined to retrieve the tortoise shell divination ...

**城中居民Ⅵ**：你说错啦！是木签，不是龟甲！\
**Citizen VI**: That's not it! She used the wooden chip! Not the tortoise shell!

**说书先生**：这……\
**Storyteller**: Emm ...

**城中居民Ⅱ**：这故事我们都听过好几遍了，这也讲错，您确实糊涂了。\
**Citizen II**: You've told this story for many times, and still getting it wrong? You have to admit you're not young anymore.

**说书先生**：说故事，总有疏漏或再编，劳烦各位听过的，就当作是没听过一般，权且忘了罢……\
**Storyteller**: Well, there is no such thing as a perfect story. Adaptations are always allowed, right? Please pretend you didn't hear me and forget about it ...

**城中居民Ⅶ**：这说书的，怎么又开始了？原先我还记着他说不会再讲了，抢过他最后一场的坐堂票呢——\
**Citizen VII**: Give me a break. He's telling that story again? I thought he'd be done with it after last time. I even bought a ticket!

**城中居民Ⅴ**：原先？你这一觉睡得……原先是哪个原先？翻过年以前？\
**Citizen V**: "Last time"? When, last year? Did you sleep for a whole year?

**说书先生**：堂后蓝衣公子之问，我可全数听说了。\
**Storyteller**: I hear you, gentleman in blue.

**城中居民Ⅶ**：耳朵这么好使……\
**Citizen VII**: Now he's listening ...

**说书先生**：我这回来，就像你，可是这鹿蜀传奇的一部分。\
**Storyteller**: You know, you're part of the story, just like me.

**城中居民Ⅶ**：我？什么意思？\
**Citizen VII**: Me? What do you mean?

**说书先生**：鹿蜀跃桥，唤醒渊庙，复生河流。沛霖川恢复往日充盈，人们年节走动频繁，于是我便重拾旧业了。\
**Storyteller**: Listen and you'll know. So the Lùshǔ jumped over the bridge, awakened the Yuān Temple, and revived the Pèilín River. As a result, more and more people come to the Pèi City at festivals, so I start telling stories again.

**说书先生**：至于你——\
**Storyteller**: As for you ...

**说书先生**：那鹿蜀收了你的酒馆，将你变为它类，原是你自己卖酒时缺斤少两坏了名声，却怪时节收成不良，营生不易。\
**Storyteller**: The Lùshǔ took over your tavern and turned you into her kind because you were an unscrupulous profiteer. You gave short weight to the people. That caused the decline of your business, yet you blamed it on the poor harvest.

**说书先生**：这鹿蜀，可算是解了你的困境！替你经营酒坊，还令你好好睡上一觉，醒来呀，坐享其成便是——\
**Storyteller**: But I think the Lùshǔ saved you from the plight! She ran the tavern for you, and you had a good sleep during that time. In a word, you did nothing good, but things ended up well for you!

**城中居民Ⅵ**：还有这样的美事！\
**Citizen VI**: What? No way!

**城中居民Ⅵ**：我也想睡一觉起来，就有人帮我写了策论！\
**Citizen VI**: I want that, too. If only somebody could finish my essay when I fall asleep!

**说书先生**：小小年纪便习写策论，年少有为，年少有为啊……\
**Storyteller**: Already writing a political essay at this age? You have a promising future, young man ...

**说书先生**：不过，还是早些回去，洗洗睡了，明日里起来温书要紧。\
**Storyteller**: But I think you should go home now and get some sleep. You need to rest well, so you can continue with your studies tomorrow.

**说书先生**：听故事可写不来策论，是不是？\
**Storyteller**: After all, the essay matters much more than the story, right?

节日热闹的喧嚷之外，一场话别正在城门前酝酿。\
Amidst the festive hustle and bustle, a farewell brews in front of the city gates.

人们从这里进入，也从这里离开。\
This is the place from which people come, and people go.

**别斯米尔**：这次的素材相当充足，足够我写上一本恰到好处的游记了。\
**Bessmert**: I have so many things to write about this time, enough for me to write a travel note.

**别斯米尔**：这本游记，应该叫什么好……《东方游记》？《沛城游记》？\
**Bessmert**: What should I call it? Travel in the East? Journey to Pèi City?

**小叶尼塞**：……听上去都不太对。\
**Yenisei**: Neither of them sounds good.

**小叶尼塞**：写“游记”的人已经太多了，女士。我认为，您是与他们不同的，所以……\
**Yenisei**: There are already too many Travels and Journeys. I think you are different from those authors, Madam, so ...

葛天将一行人送到城门外不远处，道路便分开两边。一边是上山的路，一边是下山的路。\
Gětiān escorts the group to a spot near the city gate, where the road splits into two. On one side lies the road up the mountain, and on the other lies the road down.

他停下来，缓缓落到地上，略有不适地站稳。\
He slowly descends to the ground, standing still, stiff and slightly uncomfortable.

两位神秘学家的人类同伴都警惕而畏惧地向后退去。\
The human companions of the two arcanists retreat in caution and fear from the strange bird creature.

**葛天**：是不同。两位皆得了始终。\
**Getian**: Indeed. Unlike others, the two of you have experienced it in its entirety.

**小叶尼塞**：这是什么意思？\
**Yenisei**: What do you mean?

**葛天**：有始有终，不忘来时心念，便是得出始终。\
**Getian**: There was a beginning, and now here is an end. Forget not where you came from at the end—this is entirety.

**葛天**：有福之人亦如此。\
**Getian**: Thus, happiness is found.

**别斯米尔**：很遗憾，我还是没有听懂。\
**Bessmert**: I'm sorry that I still don't understand your riddles.

**葛天**：无妨。\
**Getian**: That's no matter.

**克罗利克**：我们……我们能走了吗？很抱歉打扰你们，但我真的很想回家……\
**Krolik**: Emm ... Sorry to interrupt you. Can we go? I really want to go home right away ...

**别斯米尔**：啊，那我们——\
**Bessmert**: Ah, then we shall ...

**葛天**：烦请稍待。我还有一事相问。\
**Getian**: Please wait. There's one more thing.

**别斯米尔**：那么，您请说。\
**Bessmert**: Certainly, please.

**葛天**：两位所问，是否都已得到解答？\
**Getian**: The questions you asked—have you had the answers?

**小叶尼塞**：……\
**Yenisei**: ...

**别斯米尔**：我不清楚。\
**Bessmert**: I'm not sure.

**葛天**：不清楚？\
**Getian**: What do you mean?

**别斯米尔**：那天曲娘跃过断桥之后，小叶尼塞告诉我，在我先前写下了问题的地方，出现了一个图像。\
**Bessmert**: When Jiǔ Niángzǐ jumped over the bridge, Yenisei saw a pattern being formed where I wrote my question.

**别斯米尔**：我们看不明白，也没太在意，因为我的问题或许本身就没有解答——\
**Bessmert**: We didn't understand it. It didn't bother us either, perhaps because there was no answer to my question ...
