**葛天**：问卜之问，问卜之卜。前者提出问题，后者卜筮解答。你们得到的，应是卦象，而非卦辞。\
**Getian**: A question is asked, and a divination is made. What you saw might be a Hexagram, not the interpretation of it.

**葛天**：还记得那个图形，长什么模样吗？\
**Getian**: Do you still remember what it looks like?

小叶尼塞思索着，用地质锤的把手在沙地上划下歪歪扭扭，中间偶有断开的几条线。\
Yenisei thinks for a moment and uses a rock hammer handle to draw crooked and twisted lines in the sand, with occasional breaks in the middle of them.

**小叶尼塞**：它变化了一下……最后是这样。\
**Yenisei**: It changed a little ... and ended up like this.

**葛天**：水火既济。\
**Getian**: The Hexagram of Water and Fire.

**葛天**：我猜，这卦应属年长之人。你又如何？\
**Getian**: I'd assume this belongs to an elderly person. What about yours?

小叶尼塞愣住片刻，又划下几横，到最后已经有些潦草，以至于支出去一节。\
Yenisei is stunned for a moment, then draws a few more lines. By the end of it, her offering is already rather messy, so much so that she stretches out a section of it.

所幸葛天尚能辨认。\
Fortunately, Gětiān can still read it.

**葛天**：此为……需卦。虽不知变卦几何……\
**Getian**: This is ... Xū, the Hexagram of waiting. Though I don't know what could be derived from it ...

**葛天**：不过需卦本真简明。上为水险，是龙困浅滩，未到时机。下为刚健，遇凶亦可化险为夷。\
**Getian**: The interpretation is simple. Above is Water, the stranding dragon, advising patience. Below is uprightness, which means you will smooth away the obstacles.

**小叶尼塞**：什么意思？\
**Yenisei**: Which means ...?

**葛天**：你会找到那片水域，只是需得等待时机。\
**Getian**: You will find your water. All you need to do is wait.

**小叶尼塞**：……说了跟没说一样。\
**Yenisei**: Yes, thank you. I didn't know that.

**葛天**：至于“既济”……\
**Getian**: As for your Hexagram ...

**葛天**：既已渡河，那便已做出选择。\
**Getian**: You have gone across the river. A decision has been made.

**别斯米尔**：原来是这样。\
**Bessmert**: I see.

**小叶尼塞**：所以这问卜其实一点用也没有。\
**Yenisei**: Turns out The Divination doesn't help at all.

**葛天**：信则有。\
**Getian**: It does, if you believe in it.

**别斯米尔**：不，我知道了。\
**Bessmert**: No. I know what you mean.

**别斯米尔**：这与我现在所想的一样。谢谢您，葛天先生。\
**Bessmert**: It is exactly how I expected it to be. Thank you, Mr. Gětiān.

**葛天**：不必言谢。\
**Getian**: No need.

**别斯米尔**：您呢？您问了吗？有解答了吗？\
**Bessmert**: And what about you? Have you learned your answer?

**葛天**：它令我顺其自然。\
**Getian**: It told me to let things be.

**葛天**：所以我决定……既然已经下山，那便从心而为了。\
**Getian**: Since I have left the mountain ... I should follow what's inside my mind.

葛天转过头去，以翅膀指向上山的道路。\
Gětiān turns his head and points his wings toward the path up the mountain.

**葛天**：我仍记得，河灯曾经漂向的沛霖川尽头，远远立着一栋宏伟的楼宇。\
**Getian**: I remember that at the end of the Pèilín River, where the lanterns float, stands a great building.

**葛天**：或真实，或虚幻。即使是数次亲眼所见，我却从未心念往去，一探究竟。\
**Getian**: It might be real or illusional. I have seen it many times, yet I have never thought of going there.

两人也随着葛天所指方向看过去，只看到曲娘消失的那片丛林，再看不到更远更多。\
The two of them look in the direction pointed out by Gětiān, only seeing the jungle into which Jiǔ Niángzǐ disappeared, and nothing more.

**小叶尼塞**：那里什么也没有。\
**Yenisei**: There's nothing there.

**葛天**：我仍会前去。\
**Getian**: I will go anyway.

**小叶尼塞**：……\
**Yenisei**: ...

**小叶尼塞**：那……\
**Yenisei**: Then ...

**小叶尼塞**：……曲娘呢？她也过去了。但她是不是，不会再回来了？\
**Yenisei**: What about Jiǔ Niángzǐ? She jumped over the bridge. Is she never coming back?

葛天没有回答，摇了摇头。小叶尼塞只能征询地望向别斯米尔。\
Gětiān doesn't answer, he only shakes his head. All Yenisei can do is glance over to Gětiān filled with unspoken inquiries.

别斯米尔也看着远处的山崖与丛林，许久没有说话。\
Bessmert turns toward the distant cliffs and jungle, standing without speaking for a long while.

片刻后，她才开口。\
Until at last she breaks her silence.

**别斯米尔**：也许……\
**Bessmert**: Perhaps ...

**别斯米尔**：也许在别的地方，会再见到的。\
**Bessmert**: Perhaps we will meet again one day.

## NS-23 他日再逢 / We Will Meet Again

队伍沿着河流走了许久也没有迎来黑夜。\
The party journeys along the river for a long time, but the night never falls.

多数人都着急赶路，想要离开这里的相同念头前所未有地强烈，以至于成为了一种足以保证队伍和谐的共识。\
Most of them are in a hurry to leave—the same desire as before, but now much stronger than ever before, more than enough to bring the long-awaited harmony of a common purpose to the team.

没有人再提及先前的经历。\
And no one dares mention their experiences for the rest of the trip.

**克罗利克**：我们在走出草原之后再扎营休息，可以吗？\
**Krolik**: Let's make camp after we get out of the forest. What do you say?

**别斯米尔**：我没有异议。尤利恩先生，您感觉怎么样？\
**Bessmert**: I'm fine with it. How are you feeling, Mr. Jurien?

**尤利恩**：我也没有问题。\
**Jurien**: I'm fine with that.

**小叶尼塞**：……\
**Yenisei**: ...

只有少数人仍保有一种迟疑的好奇，忍耐许久，终于还是在途中回过头去，想要再看一看那山腰的古城，是否还在视线之中。\
A few still harbor a lingering curiosity, one they endure for a long time, and until unable to resist, they turn around to see if the ancient city on the mountainside is still in sight.

这并非只要回头便变为盐柱的故事，但也确实再也找不到一丝那奇异城市曾经存在的痕迹。\
But while this is not a story where those who look back might turn into pillars of salt, there remains no trace of the strange city that should have still been in view.

甚至，连同他们一路沿着走下来，被称为“沛霖川”的复生河流，也一起变了模样。\
And as they walk onward, the revived river known as the Pèilín too has changed its appearance.

**小叶尼塞**：……！！！\
**Yenisei**: ...!

**小叶尼塞**：女士，这条河——它——\
**Yenisei**: Madam, the river ...

一条原本宽阔的大河，不知不觉间竟在人们身后分裂为数道纤细的支流，如同绳网一般，安静盘踞在春季茂盛的草甸上。\
The once-wide river invisibly splits into slender tributaries behind them, spread out across the lush spring meadows like a rope net.

即使想找，也再也辨不清回去的那支。\
Even if they wanted to find it, they might never distinguish the one that would lead them back.

**别斯米尔**：怎么了？\
**Bessmert**: What is it?

**考察队员Ⅱ**：——指南针！指南针能用了！\
**Team Member II**: The compass is working!

**考察队员Ⅱ**：好极了——\
**Team Member II**: Great!

同行者激动地抬起双手，短暂阻隔了小叶尼塞回望别斯米尔的视线。\
Their fellow traveler excitedly raises his hands, briefly blocking Yenisei's gaze from Bessmert.

女孩顺势收回未能出口的话，转而轻轻摇头。\
The girl takes advantage of the situation and withdraws the words she cannot say. She only gently shakes her head.

**小叶尼塞**：……没什么，女士。我们继续走吧。\
**Yenisei**: Nothing. Let's move.

**小叶尼塞**：指南针可以使用的话，地图也能重新派上用场。\
**Yenisei**: The compass is working, which means we can rely on the map again.

**别斯米尔**：哦，是的。另外关于这本游记……\
**Bessmert**: Oh, that's good. As for the book I'm going to write ...

**小叶尼塞**：嗯？您想好名字了？\
**Yenisei**: Yes? Have you decided the title?

**别斯米尔**：没错。我想，我会叫它——\
**Bessmert**: Yes. I will call it ...

**别斯米尔**：“朔日手记”。\
**Bessmert**: "Notes on Shuòrì."

**小叶尼塞**：《朔日手记》……\
**Yenisei**: Notes on Shuòrì ...

**小叶尼塞**：是的，是这个名字。\
**Yenisei**: Yes, that's the title.

她将手稿翻过一页，继续读着。\
She flips over a page and continues reading.

**小叶尼塞**：“这名字对一本以地理探索与发现为主要内容的书籍来说，其实算不上一个良好的选择。”\
**Yenisei**: "The title is actually not a good choice for a book on geographical discoveries."

**小叶尼塞**：“一方面，‘朔日’对本书未来潜在的读者来说，实在是一个晦涩难懂的名词。”\
**Yenisei**: "On one hand, there is no doubt that 'Shuòrì' is a difficult word for the target readers of this book."

**小叶尼塞**：“而另一方面，‘手记’常见于称呼随笔性质的文章合集。这种合集常常是职业作家夜话笔录的结果，其中饱含思想的碰撞与灵感的曙光。”\
**Yenisei**: "On the other hand, the word 'Notes,' in most cases, is used to describe the collections of informal essays. They usually record the daily talks of professional writers, and thus include a variety of ideas and inspirations."

**小叶尼塞**：“作为并不专精文字的地理研究者，我的文学素养显然还没有到达那样高深的程度。更遗憾的是，负责为我记录文字的助手同样如此……”\
**Yenisei**: "As a geographer, however, I don't possess enough knowledge of literature to write the real 'Notes,' nor does the assistant who takes dictations from me, unfortunately ..."

**小叶尼塞**：哈哈……\
**Yenisei**: Haha ...

**小叶尼塞**：“……但无论如何，我们还是定下了这个名字。批注：这一决定，也见于寄给《祖国纪实》月刊编辑和书报审查部门的初稿中。”\
**Yenisei**: "Even so, we have decided to use these words for the title. Postscript: The title has also been included in the first draft we sent to the editors of Motherland Documentary and the Department of Publication Review."

**小叶尼塞**：缺页。之后是——\
**Yenisei**: The next page is missing. Let me see ...

**小叶尼塞**：找到了。\
**Yenisei**: Oh, found it.

**小叶尼塞**：“六月四日，天气晴。我从未想过，在与助手从叶堡出发后，竟然直到次年六月才终于回到鄂木斯克……”\
**Yenisei**: "June 4, sunny. I never knew the journey back to Omsk would take so long. My assistant and I set off from Yekaterinburg last year, and we didn't arrive until now ..."

**小叶尼塞**：“在那里，我们与总督再次面谈，为感谢当地科学研究协会的帮助，我留下了一部分《朔日手记》的草稿供他们使用。”\
**Yenisei**: "In Omsk, we met the governor again. I left him some drafts of this book in return for the help from the local Scientific Research Association."

**小叶尼塞**：“其中包含大部分鄂木河周边草原生态的详细记录，例如在抵达鄂木斯克以前，我们曾跟随一群尾部有显著毛绒结团症状的绵羊涉水渡河。”\
**Yenisei**: "Those drafts have recorded the steppe ecosystem around the Om River in detail. For example, before we arrived in Omsk, we followed a herd of sheep across the river. The wool on their tails was apparently matted."

**小叶尼塞**：“之所以着重记述这一点，是因为那简直是种神迹似的景象。众所周知，绵羊极易溺水，它们厚重的毛在遇水时只是负担。”\
**Yenisei**: "I recorded this detail because the way they crossed the water was almost a miracle. It is known to all that sheep can be easily drowned because their thick wool holds them back in water."

**小叶尼塞**：“然而这群绵羊却与众不同。在当地牧民的训练下，它们渡河的动作极快且轻，几乎像是漂在河上的数团棉花一样自在，甚至……”\
**Yenisei**: "Yet things seemed different for those sheep. They had been trained by the local herders and were able to cross the river swiftly, as if they were only several balls of cotton floating on the water ..."

**无线电小姐**：“……甚至直到它们靠岸，你才会发现，原来它们还长着被切掉一块的蛋糕似的蹄子。”\
**Ms. Radio**: "... When they came to the shore, I noticed that their hooves were in the shape of a round cake with one slice missing."

**维尔汀**：……唔……\
**Vertin**: Hmm ...

**无线电小姐**：“靠岸之后，那些绵羊用蛋糕蹄子攀爬上去，稳当地甩落一身潮湿，继续向着水草丰茂的地方走去，从不瞻前顾后。”\
**Ms. Radio**: "They climbed out of the water with their little cake hooves, shook themselves dry, and continued on to the next pasture, never hesitant to go forward, never looking back."

**无线电小姐**：“见过了这一切之后，我认为，这也将是我日后所有旅程的目标……”\
**Ms. Radio**: "Seeing all these, I hope I will be as determined as these sheep in my future journey ..."

**无线电小姐**：“今日电台选段，来自圣洛夫基金会远东分部收藏地理学手稿——《朔日手记》。记录员：小叶尼塞。”\
**Ms. Radio**: "Today's article was an extract from a geographic manuscript from St. Pavlov Foundation Far East Branch, recorded by Yenisei."

**无线电小姐**：“现在，将进行今日新闻播报……”\
**Ms. Radio**: "Next is the news broadcast ..."

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：呃……\
**Vertin**: Mmm ...

**维尔汀**：无线电小姐？\
**Vertin**: Ms. Radio?

**无线电小姐**：您好，我在。\
**Ms. Radio**: Yes, I'm here.

**维尔汀**：现在——现在是什么时候了？\
**Vertin**: I ... What time is it now?

**无线电小姐**：下午四点十五分。\
**Ms. Radio**: It's 4:15 p.m.

**维尔汀**：……看起来，我睡了一个漫长的午觉。\
**Vertin**: The nap went on a little longer than I thought.

**无线电小姐**：是的，您感觉如何？\
**Ms. Radio**: Yes. How are you feeling?

**维尔汀**：我觉得我做了梦。有好多动物在跳过一个断掉的木桥。\
**Vertin**: Think I had a dream. Many animals were jumping over a broken bridge.

**无线电小姐**：在先前的推送中，我为您阅读了一个包含斑马和绵羊的故事。\
**Ms. Radio**: I read you a story which has zebras and sheep in it.

**维尔汀**：斑马，绵羊？\
**Vertin**: Zebras and sheep?

**维尔汀**：不，我好像也记不清了……\
**Vertin**: I don't remember that ...

**维尔汀**：嗯？\
**Vertin**: Hmm?

**？？？**：——请问，司辰在吗？\
**???**: Excuse me. Is Timekeeper in the room?

**维尔汀**：我在。\
**Vertin**: I am.

**？？？**：我可以进来吗？有些事情需要征询您的意见——\
**???**: May I come in? There is something I need to confirm with you ...

**维尔汀**：抱歉，请问你是？\
**Vertin**: I'm sorry, who's that?

**十四行诗**：嗯？是我，十四行诗。\
**Sonetto**: Hmm? It's me, Sonetto.

**维尔汀**：……这个午觉可能的确太漫长了。没事，请进吧。\
**Vertin**: I might have taken too long a nap. Never mind, please come in.

**十四行诗**：司辰，您看上去有些恍惚……您感觉还好吗？\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper, you don't look very well. Are you alright?

**维尔汀**：还好，只是做了奇怪的梦。\
**Vertin**: It's ok. I had a weird dream.

**维尔汀**：怎么了？\
**Vertin**: What's going on?

**十四行诗**：啊，是基金会来信。日前有一位来自俄罗斯分部的同事调职到总部，她对能够长期外出调查的工作表达出了强烈的意愿……\
**Sonetto**: Oh, it's a letter from the Foundation. A colleague from the Russian branch was transferred to the headquarters today. She has shown a strong willingness to perform long-term field missions ...

**十四行诗**：所以总部倾向于将她也编入司辰小队，您要不要见一下她？据说她有丰富的地理探索和野外应急处理经验，也许能成为很好的助力。\
**Sonetto**: Thus, the headquarters intends to transfer her to the Timekeeper Squad. Would you have a meeting with her? It is said that she is experienced in geographical exploration and survival in the wilderness. She could be a great helper.

**维尔汀**：地理探索？她叫什么名字？\
**Vertin**: Geographical exploration? What's her name?

**十四行诗**：请稍等，她的资料在这里。\
**Sonetto**: Please hold on. Let me check her file here.

**十四行诗**：名字是——\
**Sonetto**: And her name is ...

**十四行诗**：——小叶尼塞。\
**Sonetto**: Yenisei.
